# SESSION 08: UNSICHERHEITS-LAYER
**Modul:** `jarvis/models/uncertainty.py`
**Tests:** `tests/unit/models/test_uncertainty.py`
**Abhaengigkeiten:** S01, S06, S07
**Zeit:** 80-100 min

## SCOPE
Vollstaendige sigma^2-Zerlegung + Meta-Unsicherheit U mit System-Level-Zustandssteuerung

## INFORMATION QUALITY SCORE (mu) WISSENSCHAFTLICHE HAERTUNG

### Regime-Adaptive Learned Weights

```python
from typing import Dict
import numpy as np
from sklearn.model_selection import TimeSeriesSplit

class InformationQualityEstimator:
    """
    Berechnet mu (Informationsqualitaet) via regime-adaptive learned weights.
    Ersetzt heuristische Gewichtung durch Cross-Validation-optimierte Gewichte.
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        # Regime-spezifische Feature-Gewichte (learned via CV)
        self.regime_weights: Dict[str, np.ndarray] = {}
        self.cv_scores: Dict[str, float] = {}
        self.weight_stability: Dict[str, float] = {}
    
    def learn_weights(
        self,
        features: np.ndarray,
        outcomes: np.ndarray,
        regime_labels: np.ndarray,
        n_splits: int = 5
    ) -> Dict[str, np.ndarray]:
        """
        Lernt regime-spezifische Feature-Gewichte via Time Series Cross-Validation.
        
        Args:
            features: (N, F) Feature-Matrix
            outcomes: (N,) Ground Truth Outcomes
            regime_labels: (N,) Regime-Labels (0-4)
            n_splits: Anzahl CV-Folds
        
        Returns:
            Dict mapping Regime -> optimale Feature-Gewichte
        """
        from sklearn.linear_model import Ridge
        
        regime_weights = {}
        
        for regime_id in range(5):  # 5 Regimes
            # Daten fuer dieses Regime filtern
            regime_mask = regime_labels == regime_id
            X_regime = features[regime_mask]
            y_regime = outcomes[regime_mask]
            
            if len(X_regime) < 100:
                # Nicht genug Daten fuer dieses Regime
                regime_weights[f"regime_{regime_id}"] = np.ones(features.shape[1]) / features.shape[1]
                continue
            
            # Time Series Cross-Validation
            tscv = TimeSeriesSplit(n_splits=n_splits)
            fold_weights = []
            fold_scores = []
            
            for train_idx, val_idx in tscv.split(X_regime):
                X_train, X_val = X_regime[train_idx], X_regime[val_idx]
                y_train, y_val = y_regime[train_idx], y_regime[val_idx]
                
                # Ridge Regression fuer Feature Importance
                model = Ridge(alpha=1.0, random_state=42)
                model.fit(X_train, y_train)
                
                # Gewichte = absolute Koeffizienten (normiert)
                weights = np.abs(model.coef_)
                weights = weights / max(np.sum(weights), 1e-10)
                
                fold_weights.append(weights)
                fold_scores.append(model.score(X_val, y_val))
            
            # Mittelung ueber Folds
            regime_weights[f"regime_{regime_id}"] = np.mean(fold_weights, axis=0)
            self.cv_scores[f"regime_{regime_id}"] = np.mean(fold_scores)
        
        self.regime_weights = regime_weights
        return regime_weights
    
    def compute_mu(
        self,
        features: Dict[str, float],
        regime: int,
        data_quality: float
    ) -> float:
        """
        Berechnet mu via weighted Feature-Importance.
        
        mu = data_quality * weighted_feature_score
        
        Args:
            features: Feature-Dict
            regime: Aktuelles Regime (0-4)
            data_quality: Datenqualitaet von Layer 1 [0, 1]
        
        Returns:
            mu in [0, 1]
        """
        regime_key = f"regime_{regime}"
        
        if regime_key not in self.regime_weights:
            # Fallback auf gleichmaessige Gewichtung
            return float(np.clip(data_quality, 0.0, 1.0))
        
        weights = self.regime_weights[regime_key]
        feature_values = np.array(list(features.values()))
        
        # Gewichteter Feature-Score
        weighted_score = float(np.dot(weights, feature_values))
        weighted_score = np.clip(weighted_score, 0.0, 1.0)
        
        # mu = Produkt aus Datenqualitaet und gewichtetem Feature-Score
        mu = float(data_quality * weighted_score)
        mu = np.clip(mu, 0.0, 1.0)
        
        return mu
    
    def sensitivity_analysis(self, regime: int) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """
        Analysiert Sensitivitaet von mu gegenueber Feature-Perturbationen.
        
        Returns:
            Dict[feature_name -> sensitivity_score]
        """
        regime_key = f"regime_{regime}"
        if regime_key not in self.regime_weights:
            return {}
        
        weights = self.regime_weights[regime_key]
        
        # Sensitivitaet = normierte Gewichte
        sensitivities = {
            f"feature_{i}": float(w) 
            for i, w in enumerate(weights)
        }
        
        return sensitivities
    
    def weight_stability_check(self, window_size: int = 1000) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """
        Prueft Stabilitaet der gelernten Gewichte ueber Zeit.
        
        Returns:
            Dict[regime -> stability_score] wobei stability_score in [0, 1]
            (1.0 = vollstaendig stabil, 0.0 = hochgradig instabil)
        """
        from collections import deque
        
        if not hasattr(self, 'weight_history'):
            self.weight_history = {f"regime_{i}": deque(maxlen=window_size) for i in range(5)}
        
        stability_scores = {}
        
        for regime_key, weights in self.regime_weights.items():
            history = self.weight_history[regime_key]
            history.append(weights)
            
            if len(history) < 10:
                # Noch nicht genug Historie
                stability_scores[regime_key] = 1.0
                continue
            
            # Stabilitaet = 1 - (std dev ueber Zeit)
            weight_matrix = np.array(list(history))
            weight_std = np.mean(np.std(weight_matrix, axis=0))
            stability = float(1.0 - np.clip(weight_std, 0.0, 1.0))
            
            stability_scores[regime_key] = stability
        
        self.weight_stability = stability_scores
        return stability_scores

class InformationGainOptimizer:
    """
    Alternative Methode: Information Gain Optimization fuer Feature-Gewichtung.
    """
    
    def compute_information_gain(
        self,
        feature_subset: List[str],
        full_features: Dict[str, float],
        outcomes: np.ndarray
    ) -> float:
        """
        Berechnet Information Gain fuer Feature-Subset.
        
        IG(Y|X) = H(Y) - H(Y|X)
        
        wobei H = Entropie
        """
        from scipy.stats import entropy
        
        # Entropie der Outcomes
        outcome_counts = np.bincount(outcomes.astype(int))
        outcome_probs = outcome_counts / max(np.sum(outcome_counts), 1)
        H_Y = entropy(outcome_probs)
        
        # Conditional Entropie (vereinfacht)
        # In Praxis: via Decision Tree oder Mutual Information berechnen
        H_Y_given_X = H_Y * 0.5  # Platzhalter - in echt via sklearn.feature_selection.mutual_info_classif
        
        return float(H_Y - H_Y_given_X)
```

### Weight Derivation Documentation

Die Feature-Gewichte werden via folgender Methodik abgeleitet:

1. **Data Collection:** Historische Daten (min. 10k Samples pro Regime)
2. **Cross-Validation:** 5-Fold Time Series Split
3. **Model Training:** Ridge Regression pro Regime (alpha=1.0 fuer Regularisierung)
4. **Weight Extraction:** |coefficients| normiert auf Summe=1
5. **Validation:** Out-of-Sample R^2 Score >= 0.3 erforderlich
6. **Stability Check:** Weight-Stabilitaet >= 0.7 ueber 1000-Sample-Window

### Sensitivity Analysis

Pro Regime wird Sensitivitaet jedes Features getrackt:
- **High Sensitivity (>0.1):** Feature stark einflussreich auf mu
- **Medium Sensitivity (0.05-0.1):** Moderater Einfluss
- **Low Sensitivity (<0.05):** Geringer Einfluss, Kandidat fuer Removal

### Stability Across Regimes

Gewicht-Stabilitaet wird via Rolling-Window-Std-Dev gemessen:
- **Stability Score = 1 - mean(std(weights_over_time))**
- **Target:** Stability >= 0.7 pro Regime
- **Action:** Bei Stability < 0.5 -> Retraining triggered

---

## UNSICHERHEITSTYPEN (nach Systemvertrag D(t))
```python
from dataclasses import dataclass
from jarvis.core.system_state import GlobalSystemState, SystemMode

@dataclass
class UncertaintyBreakdown:
    """
    sigma^2 = sigma^2_alea + sigma^2_epist_model + sigma^2_epist_data
    Diese Zerlegung ist NICHT vereinfachbar (Systemvertrag).
    """
    aleatoric: float           # sigma^2_alea ? Irreduzibler Noise
    epistemic_model: float     # sigma^2_epist_model ? Modellunsicherheit
    epistemic_data: float      # sigma^2_epist_data ? Datenunsicherheit
    distributional: float      # Verteilungsshift-Beitrag
    meta: float                # U ? Unsicherheit ueber Unsicherheit
    total: float               # sigma^2 gesamt

    def __post_init__(self):
        """Konsistenzpruefung."""
        expected_total = self.aleatoric + self.epistemic_model + self.epistemic_data
        if abs(self.total - expected_total) > 1e-6:
            raise ValueError(
                f"sigma^2-Zerlegung inkonsistent: total={self.total:.8f}, "
                f"Summe={expected_total:.8f}"
            )

@dataclass
class Intervals:
    ci_50: tuple
    ci_90: tuple
    ci_95: tuple
```

## ALEATORIC UNSICHERHEIT
```python
import numpy as np

def compute_aleatoric(predictions: List[Prediction]) -> float:
    """
    Durchschnittliche Vorhersagevarianz (irreducible noise).
    PFLICHT: Epsilon-Floor fuer Division.
    PFLICHT: Ergebnis muss >= 0 sein.
    """
    n = max(len(predictions), 1)  # Division durch 0 verhindern
    result = sum(p.sigma**2 for p in predictions) / n  # sigma^2 statt sigma
    return float(max(result, 0.0))
```

## EPISTEMIC UNSICHERHEIT
```python
def compute_epistemic(predictions: List[Prediction]) -> tuple:
    """
    Gibt (sigma^2_epist_model, sigma^2_epist_data) zurueck.
    Modell: Varianz der Ensemble-Mittel.
    Daten: Aus Feature-Drift-Score des LatentState.
    PFLICHT: Beiden Komponenten sind immer >= 0.
    """
    n = max(len(predictions), 1)
    means = [p.mu for p in predictions]
    avg = sum(means) / n
    sigma_sq_model = sum((m - avg)**2 for m in means) / n
    return float(max(sigma_sq_model, 0.0))
```

## META-UNSICHERHEIT (U aus D(t)) MIT SYSTEM-LEVEL-ZUSTANDSSTEUERUNG
```python
class MetaUncertaintyEstimator:
    """
    Berechnet U = Meta-Unsicherheit.
    U steuert den globalen Systemzustand ? keine lokale Behandlung.
    """

    def estimate(
        self,
        uncertainty: float,
        calibration_error: float,
        stability: float,
        system_state: GlobalSystemState
    ) -> float:
        """
        U = sqrt(ECE^2 + (1 - Stabilitaet)^2)
        PFLICHT: U in [0, 1] geclippt.
        PFLICHT: Zustandsaenderung wenn Schwellenwerte ueberschritten.
        """
        import math
        import numpy as np

        # Epsilon-Floor fuer Stabilitaet
        stab = float(np.clip(stability, 1e-6, 1.0))
        ece = float(np.clip(calibration_error, 0.0, 1.0))

        raw_u = math.sqrt(ece**2 + (1 - stab)**2)
        u = float(np.clip(raw_u, 0.0, 1.0))

        # SYSTEM-LEVEL ZUSTANDSSTEUERUNG (unveraenderliche Schwellenwerte)
        self._apply_meta_uncertainty_state(u, system_state)

        return u

    def _apply_meta_uncertainty_state(
        self,
        u: float,
        system_state: GlobalSystemState
    ) -> None:
        """
        SYSTEM-LEVEL ZUSTANDSAeNDERUNGEN basierend auf U.
        Dies ist eine Systemzustandsaenderung, keine lokale Behandlung.
        Schwellenwerte aus META_U_* Konstanten (hash-gesichert).
        """
        from jarvis.utils.constants import (
            META_U_RECALIBRATION, META_U_CONSERVATIVE, META_U_COLLAPSE
        )

        if u > META_U_COLLAPSE:
            # U > 0.7 -> Konfidenz-Kollaps: Alle Vorhersagen deaktiviert
            system_state.mode = SystemMode.CONFIDENCE_COLLAPSE
        elif u > META_U_CONSERVATIVE:
            # U > 0.5 -> Konservativer Modus: Confidence-Multiplikator reduziert
            system_state.mode = SystemMode.CONSERVATIVE
        elif u > META_U_RECALIBRATION:
            # U > 0.3 -> Rekalibrierung ausloesen
            system_state.mode = SystemMode.RECALIBRATION
```

## KONFIDENZINTERVALLE
```python
class UncertaintyLayer:
    def compute_intervals(
        self,
        pred: Prediction,
        uncertainty: UncertaintyBreakdown
    ) -> Intervals:
        """
        PFLICHT: sigma = sqrt(sigma^2_total) fuer Intervallberechnung.
        """
        import math
        sigma = math.sqrt(max(uncertainty.total, 0.0))
        return Intervals(
            ci_50=(pred.mu - 0.67 * sigma, pred.mu + 0.67 * sigma),
            ci_90=(pred.mu - 1.65 * sigma, pred.mu + 1.65 * sigma),
            ci_95=(pred.mu - 1.96 * sigma, pred.mu + 1.96 * sigma)
        )

    def decompose(self, predictions: List[Prediction], data_drift: float) -> UncertaintyBreakdown:
        """
        Vollstaendige sigma^2-Zerlegung.
        PFLICHT: Alle Komponenten separat, nicht zusammenfuehren.
        """
        sigma_sq_alea = compute_aleatoric(predictions)
        sigma_sq_epist_model = compute_epistemic(predictions)
        sigma_sq_epist_data = float(max(data_drift**2, 0.0))
        total = sigma_sq_alea + sigma_sq_epist_model + sigma_sq_epist_data

        return UncertaintyBreakdown(
            aleatoric=sigma_sq_alea,
            epistemic_model=sigma_sq_epist_model,
            epistemic_data=sigma_sq_epist_data,
            distributional=sigma_sq_epist_data,  # Alias
            meta=0.0,  # Wird von MetaUncertaintyEstimator befuellt
            total=total
        )
```

## PERFORMANCE-GARANTIEN
- Unsicherheitsberechnung: < 5ms
- Meta-Unsicherheit: < 10ms
- **Kalibrierungsstabilitaets-Std: < 0.02** (ueber Perioden)
- OOD False Positive Rate: kontrolliert (< 15%)
- Degradierungslatenz: begrenzt (< 1 Minute)
- **Logging-Integritaet: 100%** (keine stillen Ausfaelle)

## ? KALIBRIERUNGS-HARDGATE (DEPLOYMENT-BLOCK)

```python
class CalibrationHardGate:
    """
    Deployment ist BLOCKIERT wenn:
    - Regime-gemittelter ECE >= 0.05
    - Per-Regime ECE-Drift > 0.02
    - Brier-Score-Verschlechterung erkannt

    KEINE WARNUNGEN. NUR HARD EXCEPTION.
    """

    def enforce(self, metrics: 'CalibrationMetrics', system_state: 'GlobalSystemState') -> None:
        from jarvis.utils.constants import ECE_HARD_GATE, ECE_PER_REGIME_DRIFT
        from jarvis.core.integrity_layer import CalibrationGateViolation

        if metrics.ece >= ECE_HARD_GATE:
            raise CalibrationGateViolation(
                f"ECE {metrics.ece:.4f} >= {ECE_HARD_GATE} ? Deployment blockiert"
            )

        if metrics.ece_regime_drift > ECE_PER_REGIME_DRIFT:
            raise CalibrationGateViolation(
                f"ECE-Drift {metrics.ece_regime_drift:.4f} > {ECE_PER_REGIME_DRIFT} ? Deployment blockiert"
            )

        if metrics.brier_score_degraded:
            raise CalibrationGateViolation(
                "Brier-Score-Verschlechterung erkannt ? Deployment blockiert"
            )
```

## ECE-BERECHNUNG (Adaptive Binning)
```python
def compute_ece_adaptive(preds: List[Prediction], outcomes: List[float]) -> float:
    """
    ECE via Equal-Frequency Binning (10 Bins).
    PFLICHT: Epsilon-Floor fuer bin_weight Division.
    """
    n_bins = 10
    n = max(len(preds), 1)  # Division-Guard
    sorted_pairs = sorted(zip(preds, outcomes), key=lambda x: x[0].confidence)
    bin_size = max(n // n_bins, 1)  # Mindestens 1

    ece = 0.0
    for i in range(n_bins):
        bin_data = sorted_pairs[i * bin_size : (i + 1) * bin_size]
        if not bin_data:
            continue
        bin_n = len(bin_data)
        bin_conf = sum(p.confidence for p, _ in bin_data) / bin_n
        bin_acc = sum(o for _, o in bin_data) / bin_n
        bin_weight = bin_n / n  # Relativ zur Gesamtzahl
        ece += bin_weight * abs(bin_conf - bin_acc)

    return float(ece)
```

## OOD MEASUREMENT FORMALISIERUNG

### Ground Truth Definition
OOD-Ground-Truth wird via historischer Krisen-Labeling definiert:

```python
from dataclasses import dataclass
from datetime import datetime
from typing import List

@dataclass
class CrisisLabel:
    """Historische Krisen-Labels fuer OOD-Ground-Truth."""
    start_time: datetime
    end_time: datetime
    crisis_type: str  # "BLACK_SWAN", "REGIME_SHIFT", "LIQUIDITY_CRISIS", "FLASH_CRASH"
    severity: float   # 0.0 - 1.0
    confirmed: bool   # True wenn von Expert verifiziert

class HistoricalCrisisLabeler:
    """
    Definiert Ground Truth via bekannter Krisen-Perioden:
    - Bitcoin Flash Crash (Mai 2021)
    - Terra/Luna Kollaps (Mai 2022)
    - FTX Kollaps (Nov 2022)
    - Silikon Valley Bank Run (Maerz 2023)
    - Binance CZ Ruecktritt (Nov 2023)
    """
    
    KNOWN_CRISES: List[CrisisLabel] = [
        CrisisLabel(
            start_time=datetime(2021, 5, 19, 0, 0),
            end_time=datetime(2021, 5, 20, 0, 0),
            crisis_type="FLASH_CRASH",
            severity=0.9,
            confirmed=True
        ),
        CrisisLabel(
            start_time=datetime(2022, 5, 9, 0, 0),
            end_time=datetime(2022, 5, 13, 0, 0),
            crisis_type="BLACK_SWAN",
            severity=1.0,
            confirmed=True
        ),
        # ... weitere Krisen
    ]
    
    def label_timepoint(self, timestamp: datetime) -> bool:
        """True wenn timestamp in bekannter Krisen-Periode liegt."""
        for crisis in self.KNOWN_CRISES:
            if crisis.confirmed and crisis.start_time <= timestamp <= crisis.end_time:
                return True
        return False
```

### Precision and Recall Definition

```python
@dataclass
class OODMetrics:
    """OOD-Detector Performance Metriken."""
    true_positives: int    # Korrekt als OOD klassifiziert
    false_positives: int   # Faelschlich als OOD klassifiziert
    true_negatives: int    # Korrekt als In-Distribution klassifiziert
    false_negatives: int   # Verpasste OOD-Faelle
    
    @property
    def precision(self) -> float:
        """Precision = TP / (TP + FP)"""
        denom = self.true_positives + self.false_positives
        return self.true_positives / max(denom, 1) if denom > 0 else 0.0
    
    @property
    def recall(self) -> float:
        """Recall = TP / (TP + FN). MUSS >= 0.90 sein (HARD GATE)."""
        denom = self.true_positives + self.false_negatives
        return self.true_positives / max(denom, 1) if denom > 0 else 0.0
    
    @property
    def f1_score(self) -> float:
        """F1 = 2 * (Precision * Recall) / (Precision + Recall)"""
        p, r = self.precision, self.recall
        return 2 * p * r / max(p + r, 1e-10)

def evaluate_ood_detector(
    detector: 'OODEnsemble',
    test_data: List[Dict],
    labels: List[bool]
) -> OODMetrics:
    """
    Evaluiert OOD-Detector gegen Ground Truth.
    PFLICHT: Recall >= 0.90 (OOD_RECALL_MINIMUM)
    """
    from jarvis.utils.constants import OOD_RECALL_MINIMUM
    
    tp = fp = tn = fn = 0
    for data, is_ood_true in zip(test_data, labels):
        result = detector.detect_ood(data['features'])
        is_ood_pred = result.is_ood
        
        if is_ood_true and is_ood_pred:
            tp += 1
        elif is_ood_true and not is_ood_pred:
            fn += 1
        elif not is_ood_true and is_ood_pred:
            fp += 1
        else:
            tn += 1
    
    metrics = OODMetrics(tp, fp, tn, fn)
    
    # HARD GATE Enforcement
    if metrics.recall < OOD_RECALL_MINIMUM:
        raise OODRecallViolation(
            f"OOD Recall {metrics.recall:.3f} < {OOD_RECALL_MINIMUM} - Deployment blockiert"
        )
    
    return metrics
```

### False Positive Tolerance Policy

```python
class FalsePositiveController:
    """
    Kontrolliert False Positive Rate basierend auf Risiko-Kontext.
    
    Toleranz-Levels:
    - DEFENSIVE Modus: FPR < 10% akzeptabel (Sicherheit > Effizienz)
    - NORMAL Modus: FPR < 5% Ziel
    - AGGRESSIVE Modus: FPR < 2% erforderlich (Effizienz wichtig)
    """
    
    FP_TOLERANCE = {
        "DEFENSIVE": 0.10,
        "NORMAL": 0.05,
        "AGGRESSIVE": 0.02
    }
    
    def check_fp_rate(self, metrics: OODMetrics, mode: str) -> bool:
        """True wenn FP-Rate innerhalb Toleranz."""
        fp_rate = metrics.false_positives / max(
            metrics.false_positives + metrics.true_negatives, 1
        )
        return fp_rate <= self.FP_TOLERANCE.get(mode, 0.05)
```

### OOD Drift Tracking

```python
from collections import deque

class OODDriftTracker:
    """
    Tracked OOD-Score-Drift ueber Zeit.
    Erkennt schleichende Verteilungsverschiebungen.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, window_size: int = 1000):
        self.window_size = window_size
        self.score_history: deque = deque(maxlen=window_size)
        self.baseline_mean: float = 0.0
        self.baseline_std: float = 0.0
    
    def update(self, ood_score: float) -> 'DriftResult':
        """
        Tracked neuen OOD-Score und detektiert Drift.
        
        Returns:
            DriftResult mit Drift-Statistiken
        """
        self.score_history.append(ood_score)
        
        if len(self.score_history) < 100:
            # Noch nicht genug Daten
            return DriftResult(drift_detected=False, drift_magnitude=0.0)
        
        current_mean = np.mean(list(self.score_history))
        current_std = np.std(list(self.score_history))
        
        # Baseline setzen wenn noch nicht gesetzt
        if self.baseline_mean == 0.0:
            self.baseline_mean = current_mean
            self.baseline_std = current_std
        
        # Drift-Magnitude berechnen
        drift_magnitude = abs(current_mean - self.baseline_mean) / max(self.baseline_std, 1e-6)
        
        # Drift erkannt wenn > 2 Sigma Verschiebung
        drift_detected = drift_magnitude > 2.0
        
        return DriftResult(
            drift_detected=drift_detected,
            drift_magnitude=float(drift_magnitude),
            current_mean=current_mean,
            baseline_mean=self.baseline_mean
        )
```

## SENSOR 1: Maximum Softmax Probability
```python
def detect_msp(prediction: Prediction) -> float:
    """Hoher Score = wahrscheinlich OOD."""
    import numpy as np
    return float(np.clip(1.0 - prediction.confidence, 0.0, 1.0))
```

## SENSOR 2: Mahalanobis-Distanz
```python
def detect_mahalanobis(
    features: Dict[str, float],
    train_mean: List[float],
    train_cov_inv: List[List[float]],
    threshold: float
) -> float:
    """
    Mahalanobis-Distanz normiert auf [0,1].
    PFLICHT: Tikhonov-regularisierte Inverse fuer train_cov_inv verwenden.
    PFLICHT: Ergebnis auf [0, 1] clippen.
    """
    import numpy as np
    x = np.array(list(features.values()))
    mean = np.array(train_mean)
    cov_inv = np.array(train_cov_inv)
    diff = x - mean
    dist_sq = float(diff @ cov_inv @ diff)
    dist_sq = max(dist_sq, 0.0)  # Numerische Stabilitaet
    normalized = float(np.clip(dist_sq / max(threshold, 1e-10), 0.0, 1.0))
    return normalized
```

## SENSOR 3: Wasserstein-Distanz
```python
def detect_wasserstein(
    current_window: List[float],
    reference_window: List[float],
    threshold: float
) -> float:
    """Earth Mover's Distance normiert auf [0,1]."""
    from jarvis.utils.helpers import wasserstein_distance
    dist = wasserstein_distance(current_window, reference_window)
    return float(min(dist / max(threshold, 1e-10), 1.0))
```

## SENSOR 4: Ensemble-Varianz
```python
def detect_ensemble_variance(
    predictions: List[Prediction],
    threshold: float
) -> float:
    """Varianz der Ensemble-Vorhersagen normiert auf [0,1]."""
    n = max(len(predictions), 1)
    means = [p.mu for p in predictions]
    avg = sum(means) / n
    variance = sum((m - avg)**2 for m in means) / n
    return float(min(variance / max(threshold, 1e-10), 1.0))
```

## AGGREGATION MIT KONSENS-VOTING
```python
# Gewichte: MSP=0.25, Mahal=0.20, Wasser=0.20, Varianz=0.20, Rekon=0.15
SENSOR_WEIGHTS = [0.25, 0.20, 0.20, 0.20, 0.15]

# Threshold fuer "Sensor sagt OOD"
SENSOR_DETECTION_THRESHOLD = 0.5

def aggregate_ood(
    sensor_scores: Dict[str, float],
    system_state: 'GlobalSystemState'
) -> OODResult:
    """
    Zwei-Stufen-Klassifikation:
    1. Gewichteter Score fuer Schwere
    2. Konsens-Voting fuer is_ood
    """
    scores = list(sensor_scores.values())
    ood_score = sum(w * s for w, s in zip(SENSOR_WEIGHTS, scores))

    # Konsens: Wie viele Sensoren sagen OOD?
    consensus_count = sum(
        1 for s in scores if s > SENSOR_DETECTION_THRESHOLD
    )

    if ood_score > 0.8:
        severity = OODSchwere.KRITISCH
    elif ood_score > 0.6:
        severity = OODSchwere.HOCH
    elif ood_score > 0.4:
        severity = OODSchwere.MITTEL
    else:
        severity = OODSchwere.NIEDRIG

    result = OODResult(
        score=ood_score,
        severity=severity,
        sensor_scores=sensor_scores,
        consensus_count=consensus_count,
        is_ood=(consensus_count >= OOD_CONSENSUS_MINIMUM)  # >= 3/5 PFLICHT
    )

    # System-Level-Zustandsaenderung
    _update_ood_system_state(result, system_state)
    return result

def _update_ood_system_state(
    result: OODResult,
    system_state: 'GlobalSystemState'
) -> None:
    from jarvis.core.system_state import OODStatus
    if result.severity == OODSchwere.KRITISCH:
        system_state.ood_status = OODStatus.CRITICAL
    elif result.is_ood:
        system_state.ood_status = OODStatus.DETECTED
    else:
        system_state.ood_status = OODStatus.CLEAR
    system_state.ood_consensus_score = result.consensus_count
```

## UNKNOWN-UNKNOWN HANDLER
```python
from enum import Enum

class OODAktion(Enum):
    VORHERSAGEN_DEAKTIVIEREN = "vorhersagen_deaktivieren"
    MAX_UNSICHERHEIT         = "max_unsicherheit"
    UNSICHERHEIT_ERHOEHEN    = "unsicherheit_erhoehen"
    KEINE                    = "keine"

def handle_unknown_unknown(ood_result: OODResult) -> OODAktion:
    if ood_result.severity == OODSchwere.KRITISCH:
        return OODAktion.VORHERSAGEN_DEAKTIVIEREN
    elif ood_result.severity == OODSchwere.HOCH:
        return OODAktion.MAX_UNSICHERHEIT
    elif ood_result.severity == OODSchwere.MITTEL:
        return OODAktion.UNSICHERHEIT_ERHOEHEN
    return OODAktion.KEINE
```

# SESSION 09.5: AUTO-RECALIBRATION (NEU - PHASE 1 OPTIMIZATION)

**Modul:** `jarvis/models/auto_recalibrator.py`
**Tests:** `tests/unit/models/test_auto_recalibrator.py`
**Zeit:** 20-30 min
**Prioritaet:** WICHTIG fuer ECE-Stabilitaet

## AUTOMATISCHE REKALIBRIERUNG BEI DRIFT

Problem: ECE kann im Laufe der Zeit driften (Regime-Shift, Markt-Evolution).

Loesung: Automatische Rekalibrierung wenn ECE-Drift erkannt wird.

```python
# jarvis/models/auto_recalibrator.py

from dataclasses import dataclass
from datetime import datetime
import numpy as np

@dataclass
class RecalibrationTrigger:
    """Grund fuer Rekalibrierung."""
    triggered: bool
    reason: str
    current_ece: float
    threshold: float
    timestamp: datetime

class AutoRecalibrator:
    """
    Automatische Rekalibrierung bei ECE-Drift.
    
    Trigger:
    - ECE >= 0.05 (Hard Gate)
    - ECE-Drift > 0.02 zwischen Perioden
    - Regime-Shift erkannt
    """
    
    ECE_THRESHOLD = 0.05
    ECE_DRIFT_THRESHOLD = 0.02
    MIN_SAMPLES = 100
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.last_ece = 0.0
        self.sample_buffer = []
        self.is_recalibrating = False
    
    def check_and_recalibrate(
        self,
        current_ece: float,
        calibration_layer: 'CalibrationLayer'
    ) -> RecalibrationTrigger:
        """
        Prueft ob Rekalibrierung noetig und triggert sie.
        
        Waehrend Recalibration:
        - Predictions werden blockiert
        - System switched zu HOLD
        """
        # Check 1: ECE Hard Gate
        if current_ece >= self.ECE_THRESHOLD:
            self._trigger_recalibration(calibration_layer, "ECE >= 0.05")
            return RecalibrationTrigger(
                triggered=True,
                reason=f"ECE {current_ece:.4f} >= {self.ECE_THRESHOLD}",
                current_ece=current_ece,
                threshold=self.ECE_THRESHOLD,
                timestamp=datetime.utcnow()
            )
        
        # Check 2: ECE Drift
        if self.last_ece > 0:
            drift = abs(current_ece - self.last_ece)
            if drift > self.ECE_DRIFT_THRESHOLD:
                self._trigger_recalibration(calibration_layer, f"ECE-Drift {drift:.4f}")
                return RecalibrationTrigger(
                    triggered=True,
                    reason=f"ECE-Drift {drift:.4f} > {self.ECE_DRIFT_THRESHOLD}",
                    current_ece=current_ece,
                    threshold=self.ECE_DRIFT_THRESHOLD,
                    timestamp=datetime.utcnow()
                )
        
        self.last_ece = current_ece
        
        return RecalibrationTrigger(
            triggered=False,
            reason="ECE within limits",
            current_ece=current_ece,
            threshold=self.ECE_THRESHOLD,
            timestamp=datetime.utcnow()
        )
    
    def _trigger_recalibration(
        self,
        calibration_layer: 'CalibrationLayer',
        reason: str
    ):
        """
        Triggert Rekalibrierung.
        WICHTIG: Blockiert Predictions waehrend Recalibration!
        """
        from jarvis.core.logging_layer import EventLogger
        
        logger = EventLogger()
        logger.log_event("RECALIBRATION_TRIGGERED", {"reason": reason})
        
        # Blockiere System
        self.is_recalibrating = True
        
        # Rekalibriere
        if len(self.sample_buffer) >= self.MIN_SAMPLES:
            calibration_layer.recalibrate(self.sample_buffer)
        
        # Entsperre System
        self.is_recalibrating = False
        
        logger.log_event("RECALIBRATION_COMPLETED", {"reason": reason})
    
    def add_sample(self, prediction: float, outcome: float):
        """
        Fuegt Sample zu Buffer hinzu fuer spaetere Recalibration.
        """
        self.sample_buffer.append((prediction, outcome))
        if len(self.sample_buffer) > 1000:
            self.sample_buffer.pop(0)
    
    def should_block_predictions(self) -> bool:
        """
        True wenn Predictions blockiert werden sollen.
        """
        return self.is_recalibrating

# INTEGRATION:
# auto_recal = AutoRecalibrator()
# trigger = auto_recal.check_and_recalibrate(current_ece, cal_layer)
# if trigger.triggered:
#     # Switch to HOLD mode
#     strategy = "HOLD"
```

# SESSION 11: QUALITAeTS-SCORER
**Modul:** `jarvis/systems/quality_scorer.py`
**Tests:** `tests/unit/systems/test_quality_scorer.py`
**Abhaengigkeiten:** S01, S08
**Zeit:** 60-80 min

## SCOPE
Berechnet mu (Informationsqualitaet) aus Systemvertrag D(t).
mu ist KEIN beliebiger Score ? es ist die formale Qualitaetsgroesse des Systemvertrags.

## FORMEL (Systemvertrag, Whitepaper 2.2)
```
mu = w_cal ? (1 - ECE) +
    w_conf ? confidence +
    w_stab ? stability +
    w_data ? data_quality +
    w_regime ? regime_confidence

wobei: ?(w_i) = 1.0 (erzwungen)
       mu in [0, 1]
```

## IMPLEMENTIERUNG
```python
from dataclasses import dataclass
import math
import numpy as np

@dataclass
class QualityScore:
    """
    Vollstaendiges mu-Objekt aus Systemvertrag D(t).
    Alle Komponenten muessen vorhanden sein.
    """
    total: float                        # mu in [0, 1]
    calibration_component: float
    confidence_component: float
    stability_component: float
    data_quality_component: float
    regime_component: float

    def __post_init__(self):
        """Numerische Validierung."""
        for name, val in [
            ("total", self.total),
            ("calibration_component", self.calibration_component),
            ("confidence_component", self.confidence_component),
            ("stability_component", self.stability_component),
            ("data_quality_component", self.data_quality_component),
            ("regime_component", self.regime_component),
        ]:
            if math.isnan(val) or math.isinf(val):
                raise ValueError(f"QualityScore.{name} enthaelt NaN/Inf: {val}")
            if not 0.0 <= val <= 1.0:
                raise ValueError(f"QualityScore.{name} ausserhalb [0,1]: {val}")

class QualityScorer:
    WEIGHTS = {
        "calibration":  0.35,
        "confidence":   0.25,
        "stability":    0.20,
        "data_quality": 0.10,
        "regime":       0.10
    }

    def __init__(self):
        # Gewichts-Konsistenzpruefung
        total_w = sum(self.WEIGHTS.values())
        assert abs(total_w - 1.0) < 1e-9, f"Gewichte summieren nicht zu 1.0: {total_w}"

    def compute_quality(
        self,
        prediction: 'Prediction',
        state: 'LatentState',
        data: 'MarketData'
    ) -> QualityScore:
        """
        Berechnet mu in < 5ms; Bereich [0, 1].
        PFLICHT: Alle Komponenten auf NaN/Inf pruefen.
        PFLICHT: Ergebnis auf [0, 1] clippen.
        """
        cal = float(np.clip(1.0 - data.quality_score, 0.0, 1.0))
        conf = confidence_score(prediction.sigma)
        stab = stability_score(self._recent_mus)
        dq = data_quality_score(
            valid_feature_count=len([v for v in data.features.values() if not math.isnan(v)]),
            total_features=len(data.features),
            age_seconds=0,
            source_reliability=data.quality_score
        )
        reg = float(np.clip(state.regime_confidence, 0.0, 1.0))

        # Gewichtete Summe
        total = (
            self.WEIGHTS["calibration"] * cal +
            self.WEIGHTS["confidence"] * conf +
            self.WEIGHTS["stability"] * stab +
            self.WEIGHTS["data_quality"] * dq +
            self.WEIGHTS["regime"] * reg
        )

        # NaN-Guard
        if math.isnan(total) or math.isinf(total):
            total = 0.0  # Minimum-Qualitaet bei Fehler

        return QualityScore(
            total=float(np.clip(total, 0.0, 1.0)),
            calibration_component=cal,
            confidence_component=conf,
            stability_component=stab,
            data_quality_component=dq,
            regime_component=reg
        )
```

## KOMPONENTEN
```python
def calibration_score(ece: float) -> float:
    import numpy as np
    return float(np.clip(1.0 - ece, 0.0, 1.0))

def confidence_score(sigma: float) -> float:
    """
    Konfidenz aus Unsicherheit.
    PFLICHT: Epsilon-Floor fuer Division.
    """
    return float(1.0 / (1.0 + max(sigma, 0.0)))

def stability_score(recent_mus: List[float]) -> float:
    """
    Letzte 20 Vorhersagen; niedrige Varianz = hohe Stabilitaet.
    PFLICHT: Epsilon-Floor fuer Division.
    """
    if len(recent_mus) < 2:
        return 0.5
    n = len(recent_mus)
    avg = sum(recent_mus) / n
    variance = sum((m - avg)**2 for m in recent_mus) / n
    return float(1.0 / (1.0 + max(variance, 0.0)))

def data_quality_score(
    valid_feature_count: int,
    total_features: int,
    age_seconds: float,
    source_reliability: float
) -> float:
    completeness = valid_feature_count / max(total_features, 1)
    freshness = max(0.0, 1.0 - (age_seconds / 300))
    return float((completeness + freshness + source_reliability) / 3)
```

## ZIELE
- Berechnung: < 5ms
- Bereich: [0, 1]
- Korrelation mit tatsaechlichem Ergebnis: >= 0.70

## IMPORT IN ANDEREN MODULEN
```python
from jarvis.systems.quality_scorer import QualityScorer, QualityScore
```

```python
    ergebnis: Ergebnis
    konfidenz: float
    timestamp: datetime

    prediction_id: str

    vorhersage_fehler: float
    timestamp: datetime

@dataclass
class Label:
    wert: float
    unsicherheit: float
```

## HYBRIDES LABELING
```python
class HybridesLabeling:
    def create_label(
        self,
        benutzer_fb: BenutzerFeedback,
        markt_fb: MarktFeedback
    ) -> Label:
        """
        Kombiniert Benutzer- und Markt-Feedback gewichtet.
        PFLICHT: Gewichte summieren zu 1.0.
        """
        gewicht_benutzer = 0.6 if benutzer_fb.konfidenz > 0.8 else 0.4
        gewicht_markt = 1.0 - gewicht_benutzer

        benutzer_score = self._score_benutzer_feedback(benutzer_fb)
        markt_score = self._score_markt_feedback(markt_fb)

        label_wert = gewicht_benutzer * benutzer_score + gewicht_markt * markt_score
        label_unsicherheit = self._compute_label_unsicherheit(benutzer_fb, markt_fb)

        return Label(wert=label_wert, unsicherheit=label_unsicherheit)

    def _score_benutzer_feedback(self, fb: BenutzerFeedback) -> float: ...
    def _score_markt_feedback(self, fb: MarktFeedback) -> float: ...
    def _compute_label_unsicherheit(self, bf, mf) -> float: ...
```

## ONLINE-KALIBRIERUNGS-UPDATE
```python
class OnlineLearner:
    update_schwellenwert: int = 100

    def __init__(self):
        self._puffer: List[Label] = []

    def process_feedback(
        self,
        benutzer_fb: BenutzerFeedback,
        markt_fb: MarktFeedback
    ) -> None:
        """
        Akkumuliert Samples; loest Rekalibrierung bei Schwellenwert aus.
        PFLICHT: Nach Rekalibrierung CalibrationHardGate pruefen.
        """
        label = HybridesLabeling().create_label(benutzer_fb, markt_fb)
        self._puffer.append(label)

        if len(self._puffer) >= self.update_schwellenwert:
            self._rekalibrieren(self._puffer)
            self._puffer.clear()

    def _rekalibrieren(self, labels: List[Label]) -> None:
        """
        Nach Rekalibrierung: CalibrationHardGate.enforce() aufrufen.
        Wenn Gate versagt: Exception propagieren (kein stilles Weiter).
        """
        ...
```

# SESSION 13: DEGRADATIONS-CONTROLLER
**Modul:** `jarvis/systems/degradation_ctrl.py`
**Tests:** `tests/unit/systems/test_degradation_ctrl.py`
**Abhaengigkeiten:** S01, S02, S10
**Zeit:** 70-90 min

## SCOPE
Kontrollierte Degradation ueber 8 Systemmodi.
Alle Modi muessen mit dem GlobalSystemState synchronisiert sein.

## SYSTEMMODI
```python
from enum import Enum

class SystemModus(Enum):
    NORMAL           = "normal"
    KONSERVATIV      = "konservativ"
    ERHOEHTE_WACHSAMKEIT = "erhoehte_wachsamkeit"
    KRISE            = "krise"
    MINIMAL          = "minimal"
    NOTFALL          = "notfall"
    REKALIBRIERUNG   = "rekalibrierung"
    KALTSTART        = "kaltstart"
    KONFIDENZ_KOLLAPS = "konfidenz_kollaps"  # NEU: Meta-U > 0.7
```

## MODUSUeBERGAeNGE (mit GlobalSystemState)
```python
@dataclass
class SystemZustand:
    ece: float
    ood_score: float
    datenverlust_ratio: float
    entscheidungs_count: int
    aktive_rekalibrierung: bool
    meta_unsicherheit_u: float  # NEU: Aus UncertaintyLayer

class DegradationsController:
    def evaluate_system_health(
        self,
        zustand: SystemZustand,
        global_state: 'GlobalSystemState'
    ) -> SystemModus:
        from jarvis.utils.constants import META_U_COLLAPSE, ECE_HARD_GATE

        if zustand.entscheidungs_count < 1000:
            return SystemModus.KALTSTART
        if zustand.meta_unsicherheit_u > META_U_COLLAPSE:
            # Muss mit GlobalSystemState synchronisiert werden
            global_state.mode = SystemMode.CONFIDENCE_COLLAPSE
            return SystemModus.KONFIDENZ_KOLLAPS
        if zustand.aktive_rekalibrierung:
            return SystemModus.REKALIBRIERUNG
        if zustand.ece > ECE_HARD_GATE:  # 0.05
            return SystemModus.KONSERVATIV
        if zustand.ood_score > 0.8:
            return SystemModus.KRISE
        if zustand.datenverlust_ratio > 0.3:
            return SystemModus.MINIMAL
        if zustand.ood_score > 0.6:
            return SystemModus.ERHOEHTE_WACHSAMKEIT
        return SystemModus.NORMAL
```

## MODUS-KONFIGURATIONEN
```python
@dataclass
class ModusKonfiguration:
    vorhersagen_aktiv: bool
    konfidenz_multiplikator: float
    deep_path_erzwungen: bool
    warnungen_prominent: bool
    rekalibrierung_ausloesen: bool

MODUS_KONFIGURATIONEN = {
    SystemModus.NORMAL:                ModusKonfiguration(True,  1.0, False, False, False),
    SystemModus.KONSERVATIV:           ModusKonfiguration(True,  0.8, False, False, True),
    SystemModus.ERHOEHTE_WACHSAMKEIT:  ModusKonfiguration(True,  0.6, True,  False, False),
    SystemModus.KRISE:                 ModusKonfiguration(True,  0.3, True,  True,  False),
    SystemModus.MINIMAL:               ModusKonfiguration(True,  0.4, False, True,  False),
    SystemModus.NOTFALL:               ModusKonfiguration(False, 0.0, False, True,  False),
    SystemModus.REKALIBRIERUNG:        ModusKonfiguration(True,  0.7, False, False, False),
    SystemModus.KALTSTART:             ModusKonfiguration(True,  0.5, False, True,  False),
    SystemModus.KONFIDENZ_KOLLAPS:     ModusKonfiguration(False, 0.0, False, True,  True),
}
```

```python
def test_kontrollierte_degradation():
    """Muss alle 9 Modi korrekt ausloesen."""
    ctrl = DegradationsController()
    for modus in SystemModus:
        zustand = inject_failure_for_modus(modus)
        result = ctrl.evaluate_system_health(zustand, mock_global_state())
```

```python
from fastapi import WebSocket

async def stream_predictions(websocket: WebSocket, symbol: str) -> None:
    """Echtzeit-Vorhersage-Stream per WebSocket."""
    await websocket.accept()
    try:
        while True:
            data = await fetch_latest_data(symbol)
            # GlobalSystemState pruefen
            if not global_state.is_deployment_safe():
                await websocket.send_json({"error": "System nicht einsatzbereit", "state": str(global_state.mode)})
                continue
            prediction = await predict_async(data)
            await websocket.send_json(prediction)
    except Exception:
        await websocket.close()
```

## PYDANTIC MODELLE

```python
from pydantic import BaseModel, validator
from typing import Optional
from datetime import datetime

class VorhersageAnfrage(BaseModel):
    symbol: str
    timeframe: str
    use_deep_path: bool = False

class UnsicherheitsOutput(BaseModel):
    """Vollstaendige sigma^2-Zerlegung ? alle Felder Pflicht."""
    total: float
    aleatoric: float
    epistemic_model: float      # sigma^2_epist_model
    epistemic_data: float       # sigma^2_epist_data
    meta: float                 # U

class VorhersageOutput(BaseModel):
    richtung: str
    konfidenz: float
    qualitaets_score: float     # mu
    unsicherheit: UnsicherheitsOutput
    Q: float                    # Kontextuelle Kohaerenz
    S: float                    # Systemstabilitaet
    R: float                    # Regime-Konfidenz

class VorhersageAntwort(BaseModel):
    vorhersage: VorhersageOutput
    regime: str
    system_modus: str
    ood_score: float
    ood_consensus_count: int    # 0-5
    latenz_ms: float
    prediction_id: str
    timestamp: datetime
```

## SCOPE

## ? SYNTHETISCHER STRESS-TEST ALS DEPLOYMENT-GATE

Das System darf NICHT in Produktion, es sei denn:

```python
STRESS_ZERTIFIZIERUNG = {
    "kategorien": 5,           # Pflicht: 5 Kategorien
    "schweregrade": 3,         # Mindestens: 3 Schweregrade pro Kategorie
    "erkennungs_min": 0.90,    # >= 90% Erkennungsrate
    "regime_shift_min": 0.95,  # >= 95% Regime-Shift-Erkennung
}
```

Alle 5 Kategorien mit mind. 3 Schweregraden muessen >= 90% Erkennungsrate zeigen.
Unterschreitung = **Deployment-Block** (keine Ausnahmen, kein Soft-Fail).

## VALIDIERUNGSTESTS

### 1. ECE Walk-Forward Validierung
```python
def test_ece_walk_forward():
    """16 Walk-Forward-Perioden; ECE < 0.05 in mindestens 14/16."""
    from jarvis.validation.validators import create_walk_forward_periods
    from jarvis.models.calibration import CalibrationHardGate

    perioden = create_walk_forward_periods(n_perioden=16, train_size=5000, test_size=1000)

    ece_results = []
    for periode in perioden:
        predictions = [models.predict(x) for x in periode.test]
        outcomes = [get_outcome(x) for x in periode.test]
        ece = compute_ece_adaptive(predictions, outcomes)
        ece_results.append(ece)

    passed = sum(1 for e in ece_results if e < 0.05)
    assert passed >= 14, f"ECE < 0.05 nur in {passed}/16 Perioden"

    # KALIBRIERUNGS-STABILITAeTS-STD CHECK
    import statistics
    stabilitaets_std = statistics.stdev(ece_results)
    assert stabilitaets_std < 0.02, (
        f"Kalibrierungs-Stabilitaets-Std {stabilitaets_std:.4f} >= 0.02"
    )
```

### 2. Per-Regime ECE Validierung
```python
def test_ece_per_regime():
    """ECE < 0.05 in ALLEN 5 Regimes. Drift < 0.02 zwischen Regimes."""
    from jarvis.core.state_layer import Regime
    from jarvis.utils.constants import ECE_HARD_GATE, ECE_PER_REGIME_DRIFT

    ece_pro_regime = {}
    for regime in Regime:
        data = load_regime_data(regime)
        predictions = [models.predict(x) for x in data]
        outcomes = [get_outcome(x) for x in data]
        ece_pro_regime[regime] = compute_ece_adaptive(predictions, outcomes)
        assert ece_pro_regime[regime] < ECE_HARD_GATE, (
            f"Regime {regime}: ECE {ece_pro_regime[regime]:.4f} >= {ECE_HARD_GATE}"
        )

    # Drift-Check
    max_ece = max(ece_pro_regime.values())
    min_ece = min(ece_pro_regime.values())
    drift = max_ece - min_ece
    assert drift <= ECE_PER_REGIME_DRIFT, (
        f"ECE-Drift {drift:.4f} > {ECE_PER_REGIME_DRIFT}"
    )
```

### 3. Historische Krisen-Erkennung
```python
def test_historische_krisen():
    """OOD-Score >= 0.6 fuer alle historischen Krisen."""
    from jarvis.validation.stress_tests import HISTORISCHE_KRISEN
    from jarvis.utils.constants import OOD_CONSENSUS_MINIMUM

    for name, config in HISTORISCHE_KRISEN.items():
        data = load_crisis_data(config["datum"])
        ood_result = ood_ensemble.detect_ood(data)
        assert ood_result.score > 0.6, (
            f"{name}: OOD-Score {ood_result.score:.2f} zu niedrig"
        )
        # Konsens-Pruefung
        assert ood_result.consensus_count >= OOD_CONSENSUS_MINIMUM, (
            f"{name}: Nur {ood_result.consensus_count}/5 Sensoren erkannt "
            f"(Minimum: {OOD_CONSENSUS_MINIMUM})"
        )
```

### 4. Synthetische Stress-Zertifizierung (DEPLOYMENT-GATE)
```python
def test_synthetischer_stress_zertifizierung():
    """
    DEPLOYMENT-GATE: 5 Kategorien x 3 Schweregrade >= 90%.
    Regime-Shift-Erkennung >= 95%.
    KEIN Soft-Fail. Jede Unterschreitung blockiert Deployment.
    """
    from jarvis.validation.stress_tests import SYNTHETISCHER_STRESS

    erkennungen = {}

    for name, config in SYNTHETISCHER_STRESS.items():
        kategorie_erkennungen = []
        for schweregrad in config["schweregrade"]:
            stressed_data = generate_stressed_data(name, schweregrad, clean_data)
            ood_result = ood_ensemble.detect_ood(stressed_data)
            erkannt = ood_result.score > config["erkennungs_schwellenwert"]
            kategorie_erkennungen.append(erkannt)

        erkennungs_rate = sum(kategorie_erkennungen) / len(kategorie_erkennungen)
        erkennungen[name] = erkennungs_rate

        assert erkennungs_rate >= 0.90, (
            f"[DEPLOYMENT BLOCKIERT] Kategorie '{name}': "
            f"Erkennungsrate {erkennungs_rate:.1%} < 90%"
        )

    # Regime-Shift separat pruefen
    regime_shift_rate = erkennungen.get("RegimeShift", 0.0)
    assert regime_shift_rate >= 0.95, (
        f"[DEPLOYMENT BLOCKIERT] Regime-Shift-Erkennung "
        f"{regime_shift_rate:.1%} < 95%"
    )
```

### 6. Systemvertrag-Validierung (D(t))
```python
def test_systemvertrag_vollstaendigkeit():
    """Alle D(t)-Felder {mu, sigma^2, Q, S, U, R} muessen in jedem Output vorhanden sein."""
    from jarvis.models.deep_path import DeepPathEnsemble

    ensemble = DeepPathEnsemble()
    result = ensemble.predict(sample_features, sample_state)

    pflicht_felder = ["mu", "sigma_squared", "Q", "S", "U", "R"]
    for feld in pflicht_felder:
        assert hasattr(result, feld), f"Systemvertrag verletzt: Feld '{feld}' fehlt"

    # sigma^2-Konsistenz
    expected_sum = (
        result.sigma_sq_aleatoric +
        result.sigma_sq_epistemic_model +
        result.sigma_sq_epistemic_data
    )
    assert abs(result.sigma_squared - expected_sum) < 1e-6, (
        f"sigma^2-Inkonsistenz: {result.sigma_squared:.8f} != {expected_sum:.8f}"
    )
```

```python
def test_meta_unsicherheit_zustandsuebergaenge():
    """U-Schwellenwerte muessen System-Level-Zustandsaenderungen ausloesen."""
    from jarvis.models.uncertainty import MetaUncertaintyEstimator
    from jarvis.core.system_state import GlobalSystemState, SystemMode

    estimator = MetaUncertaintyEstimator()
    state = GlobalSystemState(...)

    # U > 0.7 -> CONFIDENCE_COLLAPSE
    estimator.estimate(uncertainty=1.0, calibration_error=0.5, stability=0.1, system_state=state)
    assert state.mode == SystemMode.CONFIDENCE_COLLAPSE

    # U > 0.5 -> CONSERVATIVE
    estimator.estimate(uncertainty=0.5, calibration_error=0.3, stability=0.3, system_state=state)
    assert state.mode == SystemMode.CONSERVATIVE

    # U > 0.3 -> RECALIBRATION
    estimator.estimate(uncertainty=0.3, calibration_error=0.2, stability=0.5, system_state=state)
    assert state.mode == SystemMode.RECALIBRATION
```

### 8. Numerische Stabilitaetsvalidierung
```python
def test_keine_nan_inf_im_system():
    """
    Das gesamte System darf niemals NaN/Inf still propagieren.
    1000 Zufalls-Inputs; kein einziger NaN/Inf in der Ausgabe.
    """
    import math
    import numpy as np

    rng = np.random.RandomState(42)  # Reproduzierbar

    nan_inf_count = 0
    for i in range(1000):
        features = {
            f"feat_{j}": float(rng.randn())
            for j in range(10)
        }
        try:
            result = system.predict(features)
            for name, val in [
                ("mu", result.mu), ("sigma_squared", result.sigma_squared),
                ("Q", result.Q), ("S", result.S), ("U", result.U), ("R", result.R)
            ]:
                if math.isnan(val) or math.isinf(val):
                    nan_inf_count += 1
        except Exception:
            pass  # Exception ist OK ? silentes NaN ist nicht OK

    assert nan_inf_count == 0, f"{nan_inf_count} NaN/Inf in 1000 Inputs gefunden"
```

### 9. Performance-Tests
```python
def test_latenz():
    """Fast Path < 50ms P95; Deep Path < 500ms P95."""
    import time

    fast_latenzen = []
    for _ in range(1000):
        start = time.perf_counter()
        fast_path.predict(sample_features)
        fast_latenzen.append((time.perf_counter() - start) * 1000)

    p95_fast = sorted(fast_latenzen)[int(0.95 * len(fast_latenzen))]
    assert p95_fast < 50, f"Fast Path P95 = {p95_fast:.1f}ms"

    deep_latenzen = []
    for _ in range(200):
        start = time.perf_counter()
        deep_path.predict(sample_features)
        deep_latenzen.append((time.perf_counter() - start) * 1000)

    p95_deep = sorted(deep_latenzen)[int(0.95 * len(deep_latenzen))]
    assert p95_deep < 500, f"Deep Path P95 = {p95_deep:.1f}ms"
```

## PRODUCTION ENGINEERING ADDENDUM

### Operational Stability Layer

```python
# jarvis/production/stability_controller.py
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, Optional
import time
from enum import Enum

class StabilityMode(Enum):
    NORMAL = "normal"
    DEGRADED = "degraded"
    CRITICAL = "critical"
    EMERGENCY = "emergency"

@dataclass
class SLAMetrics:
    """Service Level Agreement Metrics."""
    target_latency_p50: float = 100.0  # ms
    target_latency_p95: float = 200.0  # ms
    target_latency_p99: float = 500.0  # ms
    target_availability: float = 0.999  # 99.9%
    target_error_rate: float = 0.001   # 0.1%
    
    current_latency_p50: float = 0.0
    current_latency_p95: float = 0.0
    current_latency_p99: float = 0.0
    current_availability: float = 1.0
    current_error_rate: float = 0.0
    
    def is_within_sla(self) -> bool:
        """True wenn alle SLA-Metriken erfuellt."""
        return all([
            self.current_latency_p95 <= self.target_latency_p95,
            self.current_availability >= self.target_availability,
            self.current_error_rate <= self.target_error_rate
        ])

class StabilityController:
    """
    Kontrolliert operative Stabilitaet und reagiert auf Degradation.
    """
    
    # Circuit Breaker Thresholds
    ERROR_THRESHOLD = 0.05      # 5% Fehlerrate
    LATENCY_THRESHOLD_MS = 1000 # 1 Sekunde
    CONSECUTIVE_FAILS = 5       # Consecutive Fails fuer Circuit Break
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.mode = StabilityMode.NORMAL
        self.sla_metrics = SLAMetrics()
        self.consecutive_fails = 0
        self.circuit_open = False
    
    def check_stability(self) -> StabilityMode:
        """
        Prueft System-Stabilitaet und bestimmt Mode.
        """
        # Latenz Check
        if self.sla_metrics.current_latency_p95 > self.LATENCY_THRESHOLD_MS:
            if self.mode == StabilityMode.NORMAL:
                self.mode = StabilityMode.DEGRADED
            elif self.mode == StabilityMode.DEGRADED:
                self.mode = StabilityMode.CRITICAL
        
        # Error Rate Check
        if self.sla_metrics.current_error_rate > self.ERROR_THRESHOLD:
            self.consecutive_fails += 1
            if self.consecutive_fails >= self.CONSECUTIVE_FAILS:
                self.circuit_open = True
                self.mode = StabilityMode.EMERGENCY
        else:
            self.consecutive_fails = 0
            if self.circuit_open:
                # Recovery check
                if self.sla_metrics.current_error_rate < self.ERROR_THRESHOLD / 2:
                    self.circuit_open = False
                    self.mode = StabilityMode.DEGRADED
        
        return self.mode

class BackpressureHandler:
    """
    Handhabt API-Backpressure und Load Shedding.
    """
    
    MAX_QUEUE_SIZE = 1000
    REJECT_THRESHOLD = 0.9  # Bei 90% Queue-Fuellstand ablehnen
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.queue_size = 0
        self.total_requests = 0
        self.rejected_requests = 0
    
    def should_accept_request(self) -> bool:
        """
        Entscheidet ob Request akzeptiert wird.
        Implementiert Load Shedding bei Ueberlast.
        """
        queue_utilization = self.queue_size / self.MAX_QUEUE_SIZE
        
        if queue_utilization > self.REJECT_THRESHOLD:
            self.rejected_requests += 1
            return False
        
        self.total_requests += 1
        return True
    
    def get_rejection_rate(self) -> float:
        """Gibt aktuelle Rejection Rate zurueck."""
        if self.total_requests == 0:
            return 0.0
        return self.rejected_requests / self.total_requests

class TimeoutManager:
    """
    Verwaltet Timeouts fuer verschiedene Operationen.
    """
    
    TIMEOUTS = {
        'data_fetch': 5.0,      # Sekunden
        'feature_compute': 0.02, # 20ms
        'fast_path': 0.05,      # 50ms
        'deep_path': 0.5,       # 500ms
        'risk_engine': 0.1,     # 100ms
        'api_response': 1.0     # 1 Sekunde
    }
    
    def execute_with_timeout(self, operation: str, func, *args, **kwargs):
        """
        Fuehrt Funktion mit Timeout aus.
        Wirft TimeoutError bei Ueberschreitung.
        """
        timeout = self.TIMEOUTS.get(operation, 1.0)
        start = time.time()
        
        try:
            result = func(*args, **kwargs)
            elapsed = time.time() - start
            
            if elapsed > timeout:
                raise TimeoutError(
                    f"Operation '{operation}' exceeded timeout: "
                    f"{elapsed:.3f}s > {timeout}s"
                )
            
            return result
        except Exception as e:
            elapsed = time.time() - start
            raise RuntimeError(
                f"Operation '{operation}' failed after {elapsed:.3f}s: {e}"
            )

class GracefulDegradationController:
    """
    Kontrolliert graceful degradation unter Last.
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.degradation_level = 0  # 0 = normal, 3 = maximum degradation
    
    def degrade(self, stability_mode: StabilityMode):
        """
        Passt System-Funktionalitaet basierend auf Stabilitaets-Mode an.
        """
        if stability_mode == StabilityMode.NORMAL:
            self.degradation_level = 0
            # Volle Funktionalitaet
        
        elif stability_mode == StabilityMode.DEGRADED:
            self.degradation_level = 1
            # Reduzierte Funktionalitaet:
            # - Deaktiviere Deep Path
            # - Reduziere Feature-Berechnung auf Top 50
            # - Erhoehe Cache-TTL
        
        elif stability_mode == StabilityMode.CRITICAL:
            self.degradation_level = 2
            # Stark reduzierte Funktionalitaet:
            # - Nur Fast Path
            # - Nur Top 30 Features
            # - Aggressive Cache-Nutzung
            # - Reduziere OOD-Checks
        
        elif stability_mode == StabilityMode.EMERGENCY:
            self.degradation_level = 3
            # Minimum-Funktionalitaet:
            # - Cache-Only Mode
            # - Keine neuen Predictions
            # - Nur Monitoring
            # - Reject alle non-critical Requests
    
    def get_feature_count(self) -> int:
        """Gibt erlaubte Feature-Count basierend auf Degradation zurueck."""
        return {
            0: 99,  # Alle Features
            1: 50,  # Top 50
            2: 30,  # Top 30
            3: 0    # Keine neuen Features
        }[self.degradation_level]
```

### Resource Scaling Strategy

```python
# jarvis/production/auto_scaler.py

class AutoScaler:
    """
    Automatisches Resource Scaling basierend auf Load.
    """
    
    # Scaling Thresholds
    CPU_SCALE_UP_THRESHOLD = 0.70      # 70% CPU
    CPU_SCALE_DOWN_THRESHOLD = 0.30    # 30% CPU
    MEMORY_SCALE_UP_THRESHOLD = 0.80   # 80% Memory
    
    # Scaling Parameters
    MIN_INSTANCES = 2
    MAX_INSTANCES = 10
    SCALE_UP_COOLDOWN = 300    # 5 Minuten
    SCALE_DOWN_COOLDOWN = 600  # 10 Minuten
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.current_instances = self.MIN_INSTANCES
        self.last_scale_action = 0
    
    def should_scale_up(
        self,
        cpu_usage: float,
        memory_usage: float,
        request_rate: float
    ) -> bool:
        """Entscheidet ob Scale-Up erforderlich."""
        if self.current_instances >= self.MAX_INSTANCES:
            return False
        
        if time.time() - self.last_scale_action < self.SCALE_UP_COOLDOWN:
            return False
        
        return (
            cpu_usage > self.CPU_SCALE_UP_THRESHOLD or
            memory_usage > self.MEMORY_SCALE_UP_THRESHOLD
        )
    
    def should_scale_down(
        self,
        cpu_usage: float,
        memory_usage: float,
        request_rate: float
    ) -> bool:
        """Entscheidet ob Scale-Down moeglich."""
        if self.current_instances <= self.MIN_INSTANCES:
            return False
        
        if time.time() - self.last_scale_action < self.SCALE_DOWN_COOLDOWN:
            return False
        
        return (
            cpu_usage < self.CPU_SCALE_DOWN_THRESHOLD and
            memory_usage < self.MEMORY_SCALE_UP_THRESHOLD / 2
        )
    
    def scale(
        self,
        cpu_usage: float,
        memory_usage: float,
        request_rate: float
    ) -> int:
        """
        Fuehrt Scaling-Entscheidung aus.
        Returns: Neue Anzahl Instanzen
        """
        if self.should_scale_up(cpu_usage, memory_usage, request_rate):
            self.current_instances = min(
                self.current_instances + 1,
                self.MAX_INSTANCES
            )
            self.last_scale_action = time.time()
        
        elif self.should_scale_down(cpu_usage, memory_usage, request_rate):
            self.current_instances = max(
                self.current_instances - 1,
                self.MIN_INSTANCES
            )
            self.last_scale_action = time.time()
        
        return self.current_instances
```

### Failure Escalation Chain

```python
# jarvis/production/failure_handler.py

from enum import Enum

class FailureSeverity(Enum):
    LOW = "low"           # Log only
    MEDIUM = "medium"     # Alert on-call
    HIGH = "high"         # Page on-call + escalate
    CRITICAL = "critical" # All hands + emergency shutdown

class FailureEscalation:
    """
    Definiert Failure Escalation Chain.
    """
    
    ESCALATION_RULES = {
        # Data Layer Failures
        'data_fetch_timeout': FailureSeverity.MEDIUM,
        'data_validation_failed': FailureSeverity.MEDIUM,
        'data_nan_inf_detected': FailureSeverity.HIGH,
        
        # Model Failures
        'ood_detected': FailureSeverity.MEDIUM,
        'calibration_gate_violation': FailureSeverity.CRITICAL,
        'ece_threshold_exceeded': FailureSeverity.CRITICAL,
        
        # System Failures
        'global_state_corruption': FailureSeverity.CRITICAL,
        'kalman_divergence': FailureSeverity.HIGH,
        'circuit_breaker_open': FailureSeverity.HIGH,
        
        # Resource Failures
        'memory_exhaustion': FailureSeverity.CRITICAL,
        'cpu_saturation': FailureSeverity.HIGH,
        'disk_full': FailureSeverity.CRITICAL,
    }
    
    def escalate(self, failure_type: str, context: Dict):
        """
        Eskaliert Failure basierend auf Typ.
        """
        severity = self.ESCALATION_RULES.get(
            failure_type,
            FailureSeverity.MEDIUM
        )
        
        if severity == FailureSeverity.LOW:
            self._log_failure(failure_type, context)
        
        elif severity == FailureSeverity.MEDIUM:
            self._log_failure(failure_type, context)
            self._alert_oncall(failure_type, context)
        
        elif severity == FailureSeverity.HIGH:
            self._log_failure(failure_type, context)
            self._page_oncall(failure_type, context)
            self._escalate_to_lead(failure_type, context)
        
        elif severity == FailureSeverity.CRITICAL:
            self._log_failure(failure_type, context)
            self._page_all_hands(failure_type, context)
            self._trigger_emergency_shutdown(failure_type, context)
    
    def _log_failure(self, failure_type: str, context: Dict):
        """Loggt Failure."""
        pass
    
    def _alert_oncall(self, failure_type: str, context: Dict):
        """Sendet Alert an On-Call Engineer."""
        pass
    
    def _page_oncall(self, failure_type: str, context: Dict):
        """Paged On-Call Engineer."""
        pass
    
    def _escalate_to_lead(self, failure_type: str, context: Dict):
        """Eskaliert zu Tech Lead."""
        pass
    
    def _page_all_hands(self, failure_type: str, context: Dict):
        """All Hands Page."""
        pass
    
    def _trigger_emergency_shutdown(self, failure_type: str, context: Dict):
        """Triggert Emergency Shutdown."""
        from jarvis.core.global_state import GlobalSystemStateController
        ctrl = GlobalSystemStateController.get_instance()
        ctrl.emergency_shutdown(reason=f"{failure_type}: {context}")
```

# SESSION 15.5: REPRODUCIBILITY CONTROLLER (NEU - PHASE 1 OPTIMIZATION)

**Modul:** `jarvis/systems/reproducibility.py`
**Tests:** `tests/unit/systems/test_reproducibility.py`

**Prioritaet:** KRITISCH fuer Certification

## BIT-FUER-BIT REPRODUZIERBARKEIT

Problem: Float-Operationen koennen auf verschiedenen CPUs/GPUs unterschiedliche Ergebnisse liefern.

Loesung: Explizite Precision-Kontrolle.

```python
# jarvis/systems/reproducibility.py

import numpy as np
from typing import Any

class ReproducibilityController:
    """
    Garantiert Bit-fuer-Bit Reproduzierbarkeit.
    
    Strategie:
    1. Float-Precision auf 15 Dezimalstellen begrenzen
    2. Deterministische Seeds fuer alle RNGs
    3. Single-Threaded Execution fuer kritische Pfade
    4. Verifikation via Hash-Vergleich
    """
    
    FLOAT_PRECISION = 15  # Dezimalstellen
    
    def ensure_reproducible(self, value: float) -> float:
        """
        Rundet Float auf definierte Precision.
        Verhindert CPU/GPU-spezifische Unterschiede.
        """
        if np.isnan(value) or np.isinf(value):
            raise ValueError(f"Cannot make NaN/Inf reproducible: {value}")
        
        return round(value, self.FLOAT_PRECISION)
    
    def ensure_reproducible_array(self, arr: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
        """Wendet Precision auf Array an."""
        return np.around(arr, self.FLOAT_PRECISION)
    
    def verify_reproducibility(
        self,
        run1_output: Any,
        run2_output: Any
    ) -> bool:
        """
        Verifiziert identische Ergebnisse zwischen zwei Runs.
        """
        if isinstance(run1_output, float):
            return abs(run1_output - run2_output) < 1e-14
        
        elif isinstance(run1_output, np.ndarray):
            return np.allclose(run1_output, run2_output, atol=1e-14)
        
        elif isinstance(run1_output, dict):
            if set(run1_output.keys()) != set(run2_output.keys()):
                return False
            return all(
                self.verify_reproducibility(run1_output[k], run2_output[k])
                for k in run1_output
            )
        
        else:
            return run1_output == run2_output
    
    def get_system_fingerprint(self) -> str:
        """
        Erzeugt System-Fingerprint fuer Reproduzierbarkeit.
        """
        import hashlib
        import sys
        import platform
        
        fingerprint = f"{sys.version}_{platform.machine()}_{np.__version__}"
        return hashlib.sha256(fingerprint.encode()).hexdigest()[:16]

# VERWENDUNG in jedem Modul:
# repro = ReproducibilityController()
# result = repro.ensure_reproducible(compute_result())
```

## CERTIFICATION TEST

```python
def test_reproducibility_certification():
    """
    GATE: Reproduzierbarkeit verifiziert
    """
    repro = ReproducibilityController()
    
    # Fuehre identischen Run 2x aus
    np.random.seed(42)
    run1 = full_system_pipeline(test_data)
    
    np.random.seed(42)
    run2 = full_system_pipeline(test_data)
    
    # MUSS identisch sein
    assert repro.verify_reproducibility(run1, run2), \
        "System nicht reproduzierbar!"
```

# SESSIONS 16-20: PROBABILISTIC RISK INTELLIGENCE PLATFORM
# Version: 5.0-final | Dependencies: S01-S15

---

## SYSTEMIDENTITAET (NICHT VERHANDELBAR)

JARVIS IST KEIN SIGNAL-BOT.

JARVIS ist eine:

    Probabilistic Risk Intelligence Platform

Das bedeutet:
- KEINE "Buy/Sell"-Ausgaben
- KEINE fixen Signale
- STATTDESSEN:
  * Confidence-Zonen (Wahrscheinlichkeitsbereiche)
  * Wahrscheinlichkeitsbasierte Entry/Exit-Boxen
  * Risiko-Korridore
  * Regime-abhaengige Strategie-Modi

Jede Ausgabe ist eine Risikowahrscheinlichkeit, KEIN Befehl.
Wer dies aendert, bricht den Systemvertrag.

---

## SESSION 16: CONFIDENCE ZONE ENGINE
**Abhaengigkeiten:** S05 (Regime), S08 (Uncertainty), S09 (Calibration)
**Zeit:** 70-90 min

### Scope

Berechnet keine Kauf-/Verkaufssignale.
Berechnet:
  - Entry Confidence Box: [lower_bound, upper_bound] mit P(entry_valid)
  - Exit Risk Corridor: [soft_exit, hard_exit] mit P(exit_triggered)
  - Expected Move %: Wahrscheinlichkeitsgewichtete Preisspanne
  - Volatility Adjusted Stop: Dynamischer Stop basierend auf Regime-Vol

### Kernformel: Confidence Box

```python
# jarvis/risk/confidence_zone_engine.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import numpy as np
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Optional

@dataclass
class ConfidenceZone:
    """
    Output: KEINE Signale. Nur Wahrscheinlichkeitsraeume.
    """
    entry_lower:      float   # Untere Grenze der Entry-Box
    entry_upper:      float   # Obere Grenze der Entry-Box
    entry_confidence: float   # P(entry gueltig) in [1e-6, 1-1e-6]
    exit_soft:        float   # Soft-Exit-Level (erhoehte Vorsicht)
    exit_hard:        float   # Hard-Exit-Level (Risikogrenze)
    exit_confidence:  float   # P(exit ausgeloest) in [1e-6, 1-1e-6]
    expected_move_pct: float  # Erwartete Bewegung in %
    vol_adjusted_stop: float  # Volatility-adjustierter Stop
    meta_uncertainty:  float  # U aus Systemvertrag D(t)

@dataclass
class ConfidenceZoneRequest:
    current_price:    float
    regime:           str    # TRENDING, RANGING, HIGH_VOL, SHOCK, UNKNOWN
    sigma_sq:         float  # Totale Varianz aus D(t)
    mu:               float  # Informationsqualitaet aus D(t)
    regime_confidence: float # R aus D(t)

class ConfidenceZoneEngine:
    """
    Berechnet Entry/Exit Confidence Zones.
    Output ist IMMER ein Wahrscheinlichkeitsraum, NIEMALS ein Signal.
    """

    REGIME_VOL_MULTIPLIER = {
        "TRENDING":  1.0,
        "RANGING":   0.8,
        "HIGH_VOL":  1.8,
        "SHOCK":     3.0,
        "UNKNOWN":   2.5,
    }

    def compute(self, req: ConfidenceZoneRequest) -> ConfidenceZone:
        """
        Hauptberechnung: Confidence Zone fuer aktuellen Marktkontext.
        Wirft ValueError bei ungueltigem Regime oder NaN-Werten.
        """
        for name, val in [("current_price", req.current_price),
                          ("sigma_sq", req.sigma_sq),
                          ("mu", req.mu)]:
            if not np.isfinite(val) or val < 0:
                raise ValueError(f"Ungaeltiger Wert fuer {name}: {val}")

        vol_mult = self.REGIME_VOL_MULTIPLIER.get(req.regime, 2.5)
        sigma    = float(np.sqrt(max(req.sigma_sq, 1e-10)))
        adjusted_sigma = sigma * vol_mult

        # Entry Box: +/- 1 Sigma, gewichtet mit Informationsqualitaet
        box_width = adjusted_sigma * (1.0 + (1.0 - req.mu))
        entry_lower = req.current_price * (1.0 - box_width)
        entry_upper = req.current_price * (1.0 + box_width)

        # Entry Confidence: Kalibrierte Wahrscheinlichkeit
        raw_entry_conf = req.mu * req.regime_confidence
        entry_confidence = float(np.clip(raw_entry_conf, 1e-6, 1 - 1e-6))

        # Exit Risk Corridor
        soft_mult = adjusted_sigma * 1.5
        hard_mult = adjusted_sigma * 2.5
        exit_soft = req.current_price * (1.0 - soft_mult)
        exit_hard = req.current_price * (1.0 - hard_mult)

        raw_exit_conf = 1.0 - req.mu
        exit_confidence = float(np.clip(raw_exit_conf, 1e-6, 1 - 1e-6))

        # Expected Move %
        expected_move_pct = adjusted_sigma * 100.0

        # Volatility Adjusted Stop
        vol_adjusted_stop = req.current_price * (1.0 - adjusted_sigma * 2.0)

        # Meta-Uncertainty: Gesamtunsicherheit des Systems
        meta_uncertainty = float(np.clip(
            1.0 - (req.mu * req.regime_confidence), 1e-6, 1 - 1e-6
        ))

        return ConfidenceZone(
            entry_lower=entry_lower,
            entry_upper=entry_upper,
            entry_confidence=entry_confidence,
            exit_soft=exit_soft,
            exit_hard=exit_hard,
            exit_confidence=exit_confidence,
            expected_move_pct=expected_move_pct,
            vol_adjusted_stop=vol_adjusted_stop,
            meta_uncertainty=meta_uncertainty,
        )
```

### Kritische Anforderungen

- R1: KEINE Signal-Ausgabe (kein "BUY"/"SELL")
- R2: Alle Wahrscheinlichkeiten geclipt auf [1e-6, 1-1e-6]
- R3: Entry/Exit-Grenzen NIEMALS als absolute Wahrheiten kommuniziert
- R4: meta_uncertainty IMMER sichtbar (Qualitaetskontrolle)

## SESSION 17: RISK ENGINE (KERNKOMPONENTE)

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S05, S08, S09, S16
**Zeit:** 90-110 min

### Prinzip

Top-Systeme optimieren NICHT Profit.
Sie kontrollieren RISIKO.

Der Risk Engine ist der Kern von JARVIS. Keine andere Komponente
darf den Risk Engine bypassen.

### Kernkomponenten

```python
# jarvis/risk/risk_engine.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import numpy as np
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import List, Dict, Optional

from jarvis.core.regime import GlobalRegimeState, MacroRegimeState, CorrelationRegimeState
from jarvis.utils.constants import JOINT_RISK_MULTIPLIER_TABLE

@dataclass
class RiskOutput:
    """
    Vollstaendiger Risk-Assessment-Output.
    Muss Systemvertrag D(t) erweiternd erfuellen.
    """
    expected_drawdown:       float  # Erwarteter Drawdown (0-1)
    expected_drawdown_p95:   float  # 95%-Quantil des Drawdowns
    volatility_forecast:     float  # Vorhergesagte Volatilitaet (annualisiert)
    risk_compression_active: bool   # True wenn Risk Compression Mode aktiv
    position_size_factor:    float  # Adaptive Position Size (0-1)
    exposure_weight:         float  # Confidence-Weighted Exposure (0-1)
    risk_regime:             str    # NORMAL, ELEVATED, CRITICAL, DEFENSIVE


class RiskEngine:
    """
    Zentraler Risk Engine. PFLICHT fuer alle Positions-Entscheidungen.
    Kein direktes Trading ohne Risk Engine Freigabe.
    """

    # Immutable Risk Thresholds (Hash-gesichert in THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json)
    MAX_DRAWDOWN_THRESHOLD  = 0.15   # 15% - Hard Limit
    VOL_COMPRESSION_TRIGGER = 0.30   # 30% ann. Vol -> Risk Compression
    SHOCK_EXPOSURE_CAP      = 0.25   # Max 25% Exposure bei Schock

    def compute_expected_drawdown(
        self,
        returns_history: List[float],
        confidence_level: float = 0.95
    ) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """
        Expected Drawdown Forecast via historischer Simulation.
        Gibt mean und p95 zurueck.
        """
        if len(returns_history) < 20:
            raise ValueError("Mindestens 20 Returns fuer Drawdown-Schaetzung")

        arr = np.array(returns_history, dtype=float)
        if not np.all(np.isfinite(arr)):
            raise ValueError("Returns enthalten NaN/Inf")

        # Kumulative Returns
        cum = np.cumprod(1.0 + arr)
        running_max = np.maximum.accumulate(cum)
        drawdowns = (running_max - cum) / np.maximum(running_max, 1e-10)

        expected_dd   = float(np.mean(drawdowns))
        dd_p95        = float(np.percentile(drawdowns, confidence_level * 100))

        return {"mean": expected_dd, "p95": dd_p95}

    def forecast_volatility(
        self,
        returns: List[float],
        halflife_days: int = 20
    ) -> float:
        """
        EWMA Volatilitaets-Forecast (annualisiert).
        Decay-Faktor = exp(-log(2)/halflife).
        """
        if len(returns) < 5:
            raise ValueError("Zu wenig Datenpunkte fuer Volatilitaets-Forecast")

        arr = np.array(returns, dtype=float)
        if not np.all(np.isfinite(arr)):
            raise ValueError("Returns enthalten NaN/Inf")

        decay = float(np.exp(-np.log(2.0) / max(halflife_days, 1)))
        weights = np.array([decay ** i for i in range(len(arr) - 1, -1, -1)])
        weights /= weights.sum()

        ewma_var = float(np.sum(weights * arr ** 2))
        vol_annual = float(np.sqrt(max(ewma_var, 1e-10) * 252))
        return vol_annual

    def compute_adaptive_position_size(
        self,
        base_size: float,
        volatility: float,
        drawdown_p95: float,
        regime: str,
        meta_uncertainty: float
    ) -> float:
        """
        Adaptive Position Sizing:
        Reduziert bei hoher Vol, hohem Drawdown, hoher Unsicherheit.
        Gibt Faktor in [0.0, 1.0] zurueck.
        """
        vol_factor  = float(np.clip(0.2 / max(volatility, 1e-6), 0.0, 1.0))
        dd_factor   = float(np.clip(1.0 - drawdown_p95 / self.MAX_DRAWDOWN_THRESHOLD,
                                    0.0, 1.0))
        unc_factor  = float(np.clip(1.0 - meta_uncertainty, 0.0, 1.0))

        regime_cap = {
            "NORMAL":    1.0,
            "ELEVATED":  0.7,
            "CRITICAL":  0.4,
            "DEFENSIVE": 0.2,
        }.get(regime, 0.3)

        raw_factor = vol_factor * dd_factor * unc_factor * regime_cap
        return float(np.clip(raw_factor * base_size, 0.0, 1.0))

    def assess(
        self,
        returns_history: List[float],
        current_regime: str,
        meta_uncertainty: float,
        macro_regime: Optional[MacroRegimeState] = None,
        correlation_regime: Optional[CorrelationRegimeState] = None,
    ) -> RiskOutput:
        """
        Vollstaendiger Risk Assessment. Wirft bei Hard-Limit-Verletzung.

        Optional parameters macro_regime and correlation_regime enable the
        Joint Macro x Correlation Risk Multiplier (JRM). If either is None,
        JRM defaults to 1.0 and behavior is identical to prior versions.
        """
        dd_result  = self.compute_expected_drawdown(returns_history)
        vol        = self.forecast_volatility(returns_history)

        # Risk Compression Mode
        risk_compression = (
            vol > self.VOL_COMPRESSION_TRIGGER or
            dd_result["p95"] > self.MAX_DRAWDOWN_THRESHOLD or
            current_regime in (GlobalRegimeState.SHOCK, "CRITICAL")
        )

        # Risk Regime
        if current_regime == GlobalRegimeState.SHOCK or dd_result["p95"] > self.MAX_DRAWDOWN_THRESHOLD:
            risk_regime = "DEFENSIVE"
        elif vol > self.VOL_COMPRESSION_TRIGGER:
            risk_regime = "CRITICAL"
        elif vol > self.VOL_COMPRESSION_TRIGGER * 0.7:
            risk_regime = "ELEVATED"
        else:
            risk_regime = "NORMAL"

        base_exposure = self.SHOCK_EXPOSURE_CAP if risk_compression else 1.0
        position_size = self.compute_adaptive_position_size(
            base_size=base_exposure,
            volatility=vol,
            drawdown_p95=dd_result["p95"],
            regime=risk_regime,
            meta_uncertainty=meta_uncertainty,
        )

        exposure_weight = float(np.clip(
            position_size * (1.0 - meta_uncertainty), 1e-6, 1.0
        ))

        # Joint Macro x Correlation Risk Multiplier (JRM)
        # Applied at final stage only. Does not alter risk_compression or risk_regime.
        # Backward compatible: if either input is None, joint_multiplier = 1.0.
        if macro_regime is not None and correlation_regime is not None:
            joint_multiplier = JOINT_RISK_MULTIPLIER_TABLE[macro_regime][correlation_regime]
        else:
            joint_multiplier = 1.0

        exposure_weight = float(np.clip(
            exposure_weight / joint_multiplier,
            self.SHOCK_EXPOSURE_CAP,
            1.0,
        ))

        return RiskOutput(
            expected_drawdown=dd_result["mean"],
            expected_drawdown_p95=dd_result["p95"],
            volatility_forecast=vol,
            risk_compression_active=risk_compression,
            position_size_factor=position_size,
            exposure_weight=exposure_weight,
            risk_regime=risk_regime,
        )
```

### Hard Requirements

- R1: Risk Engine NIEMALS deaktivierbar
- R2: MAX_DRAWDOWN_THRESHOLD unveraenderlich (Hash-gesichert)
- R3: position_size_factor = 0.0 bei risk_regime == DEFENSIVE erlaubt
- R4: Jeder Risk-Assessment in BUILD_LOG.json geloggt
