### RISK ENGINE SIMULATION GOVERNANCE (NICHT MODIFIZIERBAR)

```
SYSTEM CLASSIFICATION ENFORCEMENT — P0 OVERRIDE

Der Risk Engine operiert AUSSCHLIESSLICH auf simulierten Positionen.

ER TUT NICHT:
  - Schließt echte Trades
  - Verwaltet echte Margin
  - Besitzt ein Broker-Interface
  - Sendet Orders an externe Systeme
  - Mutiert Account-State in echten Broker-Systemen

ER TUT:
  - Bewertet simulierte Positions-Szenarien
  - Berechnet hypothetisches Portfolio-Risiko
  - Erzeugt Risk-Scores für Research-Layer
  - Blockiert Positions-Signale wenn Risiko-Gates verletzt werden
  - Gibt RiskDecision-Objekte zurück — niemals echte Orders

FAILURE MODES (FM-01..FM-06) bleiben vollständig aktiv.
Sie sind rein analytisch und operieren auf simulierten Daten.
Kein Failure Mode triggert echten Broker-Kontakt.

ENFORCEMENT: Jeder Output dieses Layers ist vom Typ RiskDecision.
RiskDecision enthält KEINE Order-IDs, KEINE Broker-Referenzen,
KEINE Account-Credentials.
```

---

### FAILURE MODE CATALOG (SESSION 17 INTEGRAL — NICHT TRENNBAR)

Failure Modes sind Teil der Risk-Engine-Spezifikation. Sie sind keine Appendix.
Alle Verhaltensregeln gelten system-weit und werden vom Risk Engine und
der Confidence Engine gemeinsam enforced.

**Design-Prinzipien (unveränderlich):**
1. Keine fabrizierte Sicherheit. Confidence kann nur sinken wenn ein Failure Mode aktiv ist.
2. Keine erzwungenen Signale. Ambiguität erzeugt reduzierte Confidence, keine Fallback-Signale.
3. Stabilität vor Vollständigkeit. Fehlende Daten verursachen keine Exceptions — sie verursachen dokumentierte Confidence-Reduktion.
4. Alle Failure Modes werden geloggt. Kein silent suppression.

**Failure Mode Interaction — Most-Restrictive Wins:**

```python
# Bei mehreren simultanen Failure Modes gilt das restriktivste Verhalten.
# Kein Averaging, kein Blending, keine partielle Anwendung.
SIMULTANEOUS_FM_RULES = {
    frozenset(["FM-01", "FM-02"]): "MINIMAL_EXPOSURE + VOLATILITY_SPIKE_SCALAR(0.25) + risk_compression",
    frozenset(["FM-02", "FM-04"]): "50% size reduction AND VOLATILITY_SPIKE_SCALAR — beide Multiplikatoren",
    frozenset(["FM-03", "FM-01"]): "stale features frieren FeatureVector → Regime Engine kann nicht updaten → FM-01 persistiert",
    frozenset(["FM-05", "FM-06"]): "keine Entries, kein neues Sizing; FM-06 triggert Microstructure-Recheck",
    # alle 6 simultan: meta_uncertainty > 0.90 → emergency_shutdown()
}
```

---

#### FM-01: UNDEFINED_REGIME

**Trigger:** `regime == "UNKNOWN"` OR `regime_confidence < 0.40`

```python
def handle_undefined_regime(state, ctrl) -> None:
    ctrl.update(
        strategy_mode    = "MINIMAL_EXPOSURE",
        risk_compression = True,
        meta_uncertainty = min(1.0, state.meta_uncertainty + 0.30),
    )
    # Confidence Engine: Q (kontextuelle Kohärenz) − 0.40
    # ConfidenceBundle.R = regime_confidence direkt
    # Keine Position-Erhöhungen solange aktiv
    # Visual Output: REGIME UNDEFINED Banner
    log_failure_mode("FM-01", "UNDEFINED_REGIME", state)

# Recovery: regime_confidence >= 0.50 für >= 3 aufeinanderfolgende Bars
```

---

#### FM-02: VOLATILITY_SPIKE

**Trigger:** `vol_spike_flag == True` OR `nvu_normalized > 3.0` OR `vol_percentile > 0.95`

```python
VOLATILITY_SPIKE_SCALAR = 0.25  # Alle Position-Größen werden multipliziert

def handle_volatility_spike(state, ctrl) -> None:
    ctrl.update(
        risk_compression = True,
        meta_uncertainty = min(1.0, state.meta_uncertainty + 0.25),
    )
    # Alle Position-Größen × VOLATILITY_SPIKE_SCALAR
    # Keine neuen Entries bis vol_percentile < 0.85
    # Bestehende Positionen: Exits jeden Bar evaluiert (nicht alle N Bars)
    # StrategyObject.Volatility_Sensitivity == EXPANDS → weight = min_weight
    log_failure_mode("FM-02", "VOLATILITY_SPIKE", state)

# Recovery: vol_percentile < 0.85 für >= 5 aufeinanderfolgende Bars
```

---

#### FM-03: DATA_GAP

**Trigger:** `gap_detected == True` in EnhancedMarketData ODER fehlende Bars > Threshold

```python
# Thresholds nach Asset-Klasse:
DATA_GAP_THRESHOLDS = {
    "crypto":      2,   # > 2 aufeinanderfolgende 1m Bars fehlend
    "forex":       5,   # > 5 aufeinanderfolgende 1m Bars während Session
    "indices":     0,   # Jeder Gap > 0 während Session-Stunden
    "commodities": 3,   # > 3 aufeinanderfolgende 1m Bars während Session
}

def handle_data_gap(asset_id: str, gap_size: int, ctrl) -> None:
    ctrl.update(meta_uncertainty=min(1.0, ctrl.get_state().meta_uncertainty + 0.15))
    # Betroffenen Asset: StrategyState einfrieren (keine neuen Signale)
    # FeatureVector: betroffene Asset-Features als STALE markieren
    # Confidence Engine: mu (Informationsqualität) − 0.20 für betroffenen Asset
    # Portfolio Context: betroffener Asset von neuen Allokationen ausgeschlossen
    # NVU-Output für betroffenen Asset: letzter valider Wert gehalten, als STALE getaggt
    log_failure_mode("FM-03", f"DATA_GAP asset={asset_id} bars={gap_size}")

# Recovery: 10 aufeinanderfolgende saubere Bars für betroffenen Asset
```

---

#### FM-04: EXTREME_CORRELATION

**Trigger:** Mittlere Pairwise-Korrelation > 0.85 ODER einzelne Off-Diagonal-Korrelation > 0.97

```python
def handle_extreme_correlation(corr_matrix, ctrl) -> None:
    ctrl.update(
        risk_compression = True,
        meta_uncertainty = min(1.0, ctrl.get_state().meta_uncertainty + 0.35),
    )
    # Portfolio diversification_ratio → 1.0 (kein Diversifikationsvorteil)
    # Alle Position-Größen um 50% reduziert
    # Cross-Asset-Strategien → weight = min_weight
    # Confidence Engine: Q − 0.50
    # Keine neuen Multi-Asset-Allokationen bis Korrelations-Mittelwert < 0.75
    log_failure_mode("FM-04", "EXTREME_CORRELATION",
                     {"corr_mean": float(np.mean(corr_matrix[np.triu_indices_from(corr_matrix, k=1)]))})

# Recovery: mittlere Pairwise-Korrelation < 0.75 für >= 10 Bars
```

---

#### FM-05: ILLIQUID_SESSION

**Trigger:** Aktuelle Session als illiquid klassifiziert für Asset-Klasse UND `Session_Sensitivity == LIQUID_ONLY`

```python
# Illiquid-Perioden nach Asset-Klasse:
ILLIQUID_PERIODS = {
    "forex":       "Fr 20:00 UTC – So 22:00 UTC; Feiertage",
    "indices":     "Pre-Market, After-Hours, Auction-Only-Perioden",
    "commodities": "Off-Session, Pit-Closed-Perioden",
    "crypto":      "NIEMALS — FM-05 gilt nicht für Crypto (24/7, SESSION_FREE)",
}

def handle_illiquid_session(asset_id, session_type, strategy: StrategyObject, ctrl) -> None:
    if strategy.Session_Sensitivity == SessionSensitivity.LIQUID_ONLY:
        # Keine Entries für diesen Asset
        # Bestehende Positionen: kein neues Sizing
        # Confidence Engine: S − 0.10 für Asset
    elif strategy.Session_Sensitivity == SessionSensitivity.ADAPTIVE:
        # ILLIQUID_SIZE_SCALAR = 0.40 auf alle Position-Größen
        # Stop-Loss um 1.5× ATR-Multiplikator weiten
    # Keine Änderung für SESSION_FREE Assets
    log_failure_mode("FM-05", f"ILLIQUID_SESSION asset={asset_id} session={session_type}")

# Recovery: Session als liquid klassifiziert
```

#### FM-06: SPREAD_ANOMALY

**Trigger:** Beobachteter Spread > `EntryModel.max_entry_spread_bps * 2.0` für aktive Strategie

```python
def handle_spread_anomaly(asset_id, observed_spread_bps, threshold_bps, ctrl) -> None:
    # Keine neuen Entries für betroffenen Asset
    # Risk Engine: Asset von neuen Allokationszyklen ausschließen
    # Confidence Engine: mu − 0.15 für betroffenen Asset; S − 0.10
    # Microstructure Layer: spoofing_probability-Recheck erforderlich
    # Entry wird suppressed, nicht durch Fallback-Signal ersetzt
    log_failure_mode("FM-06",
        f"SPREAD_ANOMALY asset={asset_id} "
        f"spread={observed_spread_bps:.1f}bps threshold={threshold_bps:.1f}bps")

# Recovery: beobachteter Spread < max_entry_spread_bps * 1.5 für >= 3 aufeinanderfolgende Ticks
```

---

### CONFIDENCE ENGINE IMPACT TABLE (Failure Mode → D(t) Reduktion)

```python
# jarvis/confidence/failure_impact.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
# Wird von der Confidence Engine in S08/S11 aufgerufen.
# Confidence kann NUR sinken. Niemals erhöhen.

IMPACT_TABLE = {
    "FM-01": {"R": -0.40, "Q": -0.40},
    "FM-02": {"S": -0.30, "Q": -0.20},
    "FM-03": {"mu": -0.20, "U": +0.15},  # U steigt = mehr Unsicherheit
    "FM-04": {"Q": -0.50, "R": -0.20},
    "FM-05": {"S": -0.10},
    "FM-06": {"mu": -0.15, "S": -0.10},
}

def apply_failure_mode_impacts(bundle: ConfidenceBundle,
                                active_modes: List[str]) -> ConfidenceBundle:
    """
    Wendet Confidence-Reduktion für jeden aktiven Failure Mode an.
    Confidence kann AUSSCHLIESSLICH sinken. Kein Anstieg hier.
    """
    for mode in active_modes:
        impact = IMPACT_TABLE.get(mode, {})
        for field, delta in impact.items():
            current = getattr(bundle, field)
            if field == "U":
                new_val = float(np.clip(current + abs(delta), 0.0, 1.0))
            else:
                new_val = float(np.clip(current + delta, 0.0, 1.0))
            object.__setattr__(bundle, field, new_val)
    return bundle
```

**Symbols aus Systemvertrag D(t):**
- `mu` = Informationsqualität [0,1]
- `S` = Systemstabilität [0,1]
- `Q` = Kontextuelle Kohärenz [0,1]
- `R` = Regime-Konfidenz [0,1]
- `U` = Meta-Unsicherheit [0,1] — steigt bei Unsicherheit

---

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S03 (Data), S05 (Regime), S16, S17
**Zeit:** 60-80 min

### Prinzip

User kann wechseln zwischen: 5m / 15m / 1h / 4h / 1D
Bei jedem Wechsel MUSS das System:
  1. Regime neu erkennen (S05)
  2. Volatilitaet neu berechnen (S17)
  3. Confidence Zones neu kalibrieren (S16)
  4. Alle Thresholds zeitrahmenabhaengig skalieren

Kein Timeframe-Wechsel ohne vollstaendige Rekalibrierung = Fake-Intelligenz.

### Implementierung

```python
# jarvis/risk/multi_timeframe.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import List, Dict
from enum import Enum

class Timeframe(Enum):
    TF_5M  = "5m"
    TF_15M = "15m"
    TF_1H  = "1h"
    TF_4H  = "4h"
    TF_1D  = "1D"

@dataclass
class TimeframeConfig:
    """Konfiguration pro Zeitrahmen."""
    label:            str
    bars_per_day:     int     # Balken pro Tag
    regime_lookback:  int     # Bars fuer Regime-Erkennung
    vol_halflife:     int     # EWMA Halflife in Bars
    risk_scale:       float   # Risiko-Skalierungsfaktor relativ zu 1D

TIMEFRAME_CONFIGS: Dict[Timeframe, TimeframeConfig] = {
    Timeframe.TF_5M:  TimeframeConfig("5m",  288,  60,  20, 0.08),
    Timeframe.TF_15M: TimeframeConfig("15m",  96,  40,  20, 0.15),
    Timeframe.TF_1H:  TimeframeConfig("1h",   24,  30,  20, 0.30),
    Timeframe.TF_4H:  TimeframeConfig("4h",    6,  20,  15, 0.60),
    Timeframe.TF_1D:  TimeframeConfig("1D",    1,  20,  20, 1.00),
}

class MultiTimeframeCalibrator:
    """
    Erzwingt vollstaendige Rekalibrierung bei Timeframe-Wechsel.
    """

    def __init__(self, regime_detector, risk_engine, confidence_engine):
        self.regime_detector   = regime_detector
        self.risk_engine       = risk_engine
        self.confidence_engine = confidence_engine
        self._current_tf       = None

    def switch_timeframe(
        self,
        new_tf: Timeframe,
        returns_data: List[float],
        current_price: float,
        meta_uncertainty: float,
    ) -> Dict:
        """
        Vollstaendige Rekalibrierung beim Timeframe-Wechsel.
        Kein Soft-Fail: Wirft Exception bei Fehler.
        """
        if new_tf not in TIMEFRAME_CONFIGS:
            raise ValueError(f"Unbekannter Timeframe: {new_tf}")

        cfg = TIMEFRAME_CONFIGS[new_tf]

        # 1. Regime neu erkennen
        regime_result = self.regime_detector.detect(
            returns_data[-cfg.regime_lookback:]
        )

        # 2. Risiko neu bewerten
        risk_result = self.risk_engine.assess(
            returns_history=returns_data,
            current_regime=regime_result.regime,
            meta_uncertainty=meta_uncertainty,
        )

        # 3. Confidence Zones neu kalibrieren
        from jarvis.risk.confidence_zone_engine import ConfidenceZoneRequest
        zone_req = ConfidenceZoneRequest(
            current_price=current_price,
            regime=regime_result.regime,
            sigma_sq=risk_result.volatility_forecast ** 2 * cfg.risk_scale ** 2,
            mu=1.0 - meta_uncertainty,
            regime_confidence=regime_result.confidence,
        )
        zone_result = self.confidence_engine.compute(zone_req)

        self._current_tf = new_tf

        return {
            "timeframe":    cfg.label,
            "regime":       regime_result.regime,
            "risk":         risk_result,
            "zone":         zone_result,
            "risk_scale":   cfg.risk_scale,
            "recalibrated": True,
        }
```

### Kritische Anforderungen

- R1: Kein Timeframe-Wechsel ohne vollstaendige Rekalibrierung
- R2: Timeframe-Skalierungsfaktoren unveraenderlich (TIMEFRAME_CONFIGS)
- R3: Jeder Timeframe-Wechsel in BUILD_LOG.json geloggt
- R4: UI darf waehrend Rekalibrierung nicht bedienbar sein (Lade-Lock)


---

# SESSION 17.5: EXPLICIT STRESS DETECTOR (NEU - PHASE 1 OPTIMIZATION)

**Modul:** `jarvis/risk/stress_detector.py`
**Tests:** `tests/unit/risk/test_stress_detector.py`
**Abhaengigkeiten:** S05, S17
**Zeit:** 30-45 min
**Prioritaet:** KRITISCH fuer Certification (Stress Detection >= 95%)

## WARUM SEPARATER STRESS-DETECTOR?

OOD-Detection und Stress-Detection sind VERWANDT aber UNTERSCHIEDLICH:
- **OOD:** Daten passen nicht zur trainierten Verteilung
- **Stress:** Markt ist unter extremem Stress (kann In-Distribution sein!)

**Beispiel:** Hohe Volatilitaet nach Zinsentscheid kann In-Distribution sein, aber immer noch stressig.

## IMPLEMENTIERUNG

```python
# jarvis/risk/stress_detector.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0

from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict
import numpy as np

@dataclass
class StressIndicators:
    """Stress-Indikatoren fuer verschiedene Dimensionen."""
    volatility_stress: float     # [0, 1]
    volume_stress: float          # [0, 1]
    correlation_stress: float     # [0, 1]
    liquidity_stress: float       # [0, 1]
    aggregate_stress: float       # [0, 1]
    is_stressed: bool             # True wenn >= STRESS_THRESHOLD

class ExplicitStressDetector:
    """
    Expliziter Stress-Detector (UNABHAENGIG von OOD).
    
    4 Stress-Indikatoren:
    1. Volatility Spike (> 3x normal)
    2. Volume Anomaly (> 5x normal)
    3. Correlation Breakdown (< 0.2)
    4. Liquidity Crunch (< 0.2)
    
    PFLICHT fuer Certification:
    - Stress Detection >= 95%
    - Tested auf 6 Stress-Szenarien
    """
    
    STRESS_THRESHOLD = 0.7  # Aggregate >= 0.7 = stressed
    
    def detect_stress(
        self,
        market_data,
        state
    ) -> StressIndicators:
        vol_stress = self._volatility_stress(state.volatility)
        volume_stress = self._volume_stress(market_data.ohlcv.volume)
        corr_stress = self._correlation_stress(state)
        liq_stress = self._liquidity_stress(market_data)
        
        # Aggregate = Maximum (worst-case)
        aggregate = max(vol_stress, volume_stress, corr_stress, liq_stress)
        
        return StressIndicators(
            volatility_stress=float(vol_stress),
            volume_stress=float(volume_stress),
            correlation_stress=float(corr_stress),
            liquidity_stress=float(liq_stress),
            aggregate_stress=float(aggregate),
            is_stressed=(aggregate >= self.STRESS_THRESHOLD)
        )
```

## INTEGRATION MIT RISK ENGINE

```python
class RiskEngine:
    def __init__(self):
        self.stress_detector = ExplicitStressDetector()
        
    def compute_risk(self, market_data, state, prediction):
        # OOD Check
        ood_result = self.ood_detector.detect_ood(...)
        
        # Stress Check (SEPARAT!)
        stress_result = self.stress_detector.detect_stress(market_data, state)
        
        # Kombinierte Risk-Entscheidung
        if ood_result.is_ood:
            return RiskLevel.CRITICAL
        elif stress_result.is_stressed:
            return RiskLevel.HIGH
        else:
            return RiskLevel.NORMAL
```

## CERTIFICATION TEST

```python
def test_stress_detection_certification():
    """
    GATE: Stress Detection >= 95%
    """
    detector = ExplicitStressDetector()
    
    scenarios = [
        flash_crash_scenario(),
        liquidity_crisis_scenario(),
        correlation_breakdown_scenario(),
        volume_spike_scenario(),
        volatility_spike_scenario(),
        combined_stress_scenario()
    ]
    
    detected = sum(
        detector.detect_stress(s["data"], s["state"]).is_stressed
        for s in scenarios
    )
    
    rate = detected / len(scenarios)
    assert rate >= 0.95, f"Detection {rate:.1%} < 95%"
```

# SESSIONS 19, 35: MARKET MICROSTRUCTURE & GLOBAL SYSTEM STATE
# Version: 5.0-elite | Dependencies: S03, S05, S17

---

## SESSION 19: MARKET MICROSTRUCTURE LAYER

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S03 (Data), S05 (Regime), S17 (Risk Engine)
**Zeit:** 80-100 min
**Datei:** jarvis/intelligence/microstructure_layer.py

### Prinzip

Microstructure verbessert Entry-Timing-Praezision.
Analysiert: Order Flow, Bid-Ask-Druck, Liquiditaets-Absorption,
Spoofing-Heuristiken, Rauschen, Microstructure-Volatility.

Kein direktes Trading. Nur Eingabe in Risk Engine + Strategy Selector.

### Implementierung

```python
# jarvis/intelligence/microstructure_layer.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import numpy as np
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import List, Optional, Dict

@dataclass
class OrderBookSnapshot:
    """Momentaufnahme des Order Books."""
    timestamp:     float           # Unix-Timestamp
    bid_prices:    List[float]     # Absteigende Bids [best_bid, ...]
    bid_volumes:   List[float]     # Volumina pro Bid-Level
    ask_prices:    List[float]     # Aufsteigende Asks [best_ask, ...]
    ask_volumes:   List[float]     # Volumina pro Ask-Level

@dataclass
class MicrostructureResult:
    """
    Output des Microstructure Layers.
    Alle Werte geclipt und finite.
    """
    order_flow_imbalance:    float   # OFI in [-1, 1]: -1=Sell-Druck, 1=Buy-Druck
    bid_ask_pressure:        float   # BAP in [0, 1]: 0=Sell, 1=Buy dominant
    liquidity_absorption:    float   # [0, 1]: 0=niemand schluckt Druck, 1=sofort absorbiert
    spoofing_probability:    float   # [0, 1]: Wahrscheinlichkeit fuer Spoofing-Aktivitaet
    noise_filter_score:      float   # [0, 1]: 0=reines Rauschen, 1=echtes Signal
    microstructure_vol_idx:  float   # Microstructure Volatility Index >= 0
    timing_quality:          float   # [0, 1]: Kombinierter Entry-Timing Score
    regime_hint:             str     # ACCUMULATION, DISTRIBUTION, EQUILIBRIUM, NOISE


class MarketMicrostructureLayer:
    """
    Layer: Market Microstructure Analysis.
    Verbessert Entry-Timing durch Order-Book-Analyse.
    Darf NIEMALS direkt in Execution-Layer schreiben.
    """

    # Mindest-Levels fuer valide Analyse
    MIN_ORDER_BOOK_LEVELS = 3
    SPOOFING_VOLUME_RATIO = 5.0   # Verdaechtiges Volumen-Verhaeltnis
    NOISE_HALFLIFE_TICKS  = 10    # EWMA-Halflife fuer Rauschen-Filterung

    def compute_order_flow_imbalance(
        self,
        bid_volumes: List[float],
        ask_volumes: List[float],
        n_levels: int = 5,
    ) -> float:
        """
        Order Flow Imbalance (OFI): Asymmetrie zwischen Bid und Ask Volumen.
        OFI = (BidVol - AskVol) / (BidVol + AskVol)
        Gibt Wert in [-1, 1] zurueck.
        """
        levels = min(n_levels, len(bid_volumes), len(ask_volumes))
        if levels < 1:
            raise ValueError("Keine Order-Book-Levels fuer OFI-Berechnung")

        bid_vol = float(np.sum(bid_volumes[:levels]))
        ask_vol = float(np.sum(ask_volumes[:levels]))
        total   = bid_vol + ask_vol

        if total < 1e-10:
            return 0.0

        ofi = (bid_vol - ask_vol) / total
        return float(np.clip(ofi, -1.0, 1.0))

    def compute_bid_ask_pressure(
        self,
        snapshot: OrderBookSnapshot,
        n_levels: int = 5,
    ) -> float:
        """
        Bid-Ask-Pressure: Gewichtetes Volumen nahe Best Bid/Ask.
        Normiert auf [0, 1]: 0.5 = ausgeglichen.
        """
        levels = min(n_levels, len(snapshot.bid_volumes), len(snapshot.ask_volumes))
        if levels < self.MIN_ORDER_BOOK_LEVELS:
            return 0.5

        # Gewichte: Level 1 (best) hat hoechstes Gewicht
        weights = np.array([1.0 / (i + 1) for i in range(levels)])
        weights /= weights.sum()

        bid_weighted = float(np.sum(weights * np.array(snapshot.bid_volumes[:levels])))
        ask_weighted = float(np.sum(weights * np.array(snapshot.ask_volumes[:levels])))
        total = bid_weighted + ask_weighted

        if total < 1e-10:
            return 0.5

        return float(np.clip(bid_weighted / total, 0.0, 1.0))

    def detect_liquidity_absorption(
        self,
        price_changes: List[float],
        volume_changes: List[float],
        window: int = 20,
    ) -> float:
        """
        Liquidity Absorption: Hohe Volumina ohne Preis-Bewegung = Absorption.
        Score nahe 1 = Markt absorbiert Druck gut.
        """
        if len(price_changes) < window or len(volume_changes) < window:
            raise ValueError(f"Mindestens {window} Ticks fuer Absorptions-Analyse")

        price_arr  = np.array(price_changes[-window:], dtype=float)
        volume_arr = np.array(volume_changes[-window:], dtype=float)

        if not np.all(np.isfinite(price_arr)) or not np.all(np.isfinite(volume_arr)):
            raise ValueError("Preis oder Volumen enthalten NaN/Inf")

        price_std  = float(np.std(price_arr))
        volume_std = float(np.std(volume_arr))

        if volume_std < 1e-10:
            return 0.5

        # Hohe Vol, niedrige Preis-Reaktion = hohe Absorption
        sensitivity = price_std / volume_std
        absorption  = float(np.clip(1.0 - sensitivity / max(sensitivity, 1e-10), 0.0, 1.0))
        return absorption

    def estimate_spoofing_probability(
        self,
        snapshot: OrderBookSnapshot,
        historical_snapshots: List[OrderBookSnapshot],
        cancel_threshold_ms: float = 500.0,
    ) -> float:
        """
        Spoofing Heuristik: Grosse Orders erscheinen/verschwinden schnell.
        Gibt Spoofing-Wahrscheinlichkeit in [0, 1] zurueck.
        """
        if len(historical_snapshots) < 2:
            return 0.0

        # Vergleich Top-Level-Volumina ueber Snapshots
        volume_changes = []
        for prev, curr in zip(historical_snapshots[:-1], historical_snapshots[1:]):
            if not prev.bid_volumes or not curr.bid_volumes:
                continue
            prev_best_bid_vol = prev.bid_volumes[0]
            curr_best_bid_vol = curr.bid_volumes[0]
            if prev_best_bid_vol > 1e-10:
                change = abs(curr_best_bid_vol - prev_best_bid_vol) / prev_best_bid_vol
                volume_changes.append(change)

        if not volume_changes:
            return 0.0

        mean_change = float(np.mean(volume_changes))
        # Hohe mittlere Aenderung = verdaechtig
        spoof_score = float(np.clip(
            mean_change / self.SPOOFING_VOLUME_RATIO, 0.0, 1.0
        ))
        return spoof_score

    def filter_noise(
        self,
        tick_returns: List[float],
        halflife: Optional[int] = None,
    ) -> float:
        """
        Rauschen-Filter via EWMA-Glaettung.
        Score nahe 1 = wenig Rauschen = valides Signal.
        """
        halflife = halflife or self.NOISE_HALFLIFE_TICKS
        if len(tick_returns) < 3:
            return 0.5

        arr = np.array(tick_returns, dtype=float)
        if not np.all(np.isfinite(arr)):
            return 0.5

        decay = float(np.exp(-np.log(2.0) / max(halflife, 1)))
        weights = np.array([decay ** i for i in range(len(arr) - 1, -1, -1)])
        weights /= weights.sum()

        ewma = float(np.abs(np.sum(weights * arr)))
        raw_std = float(np.std(arr))

        if raw_std < 1e-10:
            return 1.0

        # Signal-zu-Rauschen: EWMA-Signal vs. Gesamtschwankung
        snr = ewma / raw_std
        return float(np.clip(snr, 0.0, 1.0))

    def compute_microstructure_vol(
        self,
        tick_returns: List[float],
        window: int = 30,
    ) -> float:
        """
        Microstructure Volatility Index: RMS der Tick-Returns (annualisiert).
        """
        if len(tick_returns) < window:
            raise ValueError(f"Mindestens {window} Tick-Returns erforderlich")

        arr = np.array(tick_returns[-window:], dtype=float)
        if not np.all(np.isfinite(arr)):
            raise ValueError("Tick-Returns enthalten NaN/Inf")

        rms = float(np.sqrt(np.mean(arr ** 2)))
        # Annualisierung: ~23400 Ticks pro Tag (1-Sekunden-Ticks)
        return rms * np.sqrt(23400.0)

    def assess(
        self,
        snapshot:              OrderBookSnapshot,
        historical_snapshots:  List[OrderBookSnapshot],
        tick_returns:          List[float],
        price_changes:         List[float],
        volume_changes:        List[float],
    ) -> MicrostructureResult:
        """
        Vollstaendige Microstructure-Analyse.
        Gibt MicrostructureResult zurueck. Kein Silent-Fail.
        """
        ofi = self.compute_order_flow_imbalance(
            snapshot.bid_volumes, snapshot.ask_volumes
        )
        bap = self.compute_bid_ask_pressure(snapshot)

        absorption = 0.5
        try:
            absorption = self.detect_liquidity_absorption(price_changes, volume_changes)
        except ValueError:
            pass

        spoof_prob = self.estimate_spoofing_probability(snapshot, historical_snapshots)
        noise_score = self.filter_noise(tick_returns)

        ms_vol = 0.0
        try:
            ms_vol = self.compute_microstructure_vol(tick_returns)
        except ValueError:
            pass

        # Timing Quality: Kombination aller Signale
        # Gut: hohe Absorption, niedriges Spoofing, gutes Signal-Rauschen
        timing = float(np.clip(
            absorption * noise_score * (1.0 - spoof_prob), 0.0, 1.0
        ))

        # Regime Hint
        if abs(ofi) > 0.6 and absorption > 0.6:
            regime_hint = "ACCUMULATION" if ofi > 0 else "DISTRIBUTION"
        elif noise_score < 0.3:
            regime_hint = "NOISE"
        else:
            regime_hint = "EQUILIBRIUM"

        return MicrostructureResult(
            order_flow_imbalance=ofi,
            bid_ask_pressure=bap,
            liquidity_absorption=absorption,
            spoofing_probability=float(np.clip(spoof_prob, 0.0, 1.0)),
            noise_filter_score=float(np.clip(noise_score, 0.0, 1.0)),
            microstructure_vol_idx=float(max(ms_vol, 0.0)),
            timing_quality=timing,
            regime_hint=regime_hint,
        )
```

### Tests (Pflicht)

```python
# tests/unit/intelligence/test_microstructure.py
import numpy as np
import pytest
from jarvis.intelligence.microstructure_layer import (
    MarketMicrostructureLayer, OrderBookSnapshot
)

def make_snapshot(bid_vols, ask_vols, bid_prices=None, ask_prices=None):
    bid_prices = bid_prices or [100.0 - i for i in range(len(bid_vols))]
    ask_prices = ask_prices or [100.1 + i for i in range(len(ask_vols))]
    return OrderBookSnapshot(
        timestamp=1000.0,
        bid_prices=bid_prices, bid_volumes=bid_vols,
        ask_prices=ask_prices, ask_volumes=ask_vols,
    )

def test_ofi_balanced():
    layer = MarketMicrostructureLayer()
    result = layer.compute_order_flow_imbalance([100.0]*5, [100.0]*5)
    assert abs(result) < 1e-6

def test_ofi_buy_pressure():
    layer = MarketMicrostructureLayer()
    result = layer.compute_order_flow_imbalance([200.0]*5, [50.0]*5)
    assert result > 0.5

def test_ofi_clipped():
    layer = MarketMicrostructureLayer()
    result = layer.compute_order_flow_imbalance([1000.0]*5, [0.001]*5)
    assert -1.0 <= result <= 1.0

def test_assess_runs():
    layer = MarketMicrostructureLayer()
    snap = make_snapshot([100.0]*5, [80.0]*5)
    np.random.seed(42)
    ticks = np.random.randn(50).tolist()
    prices = np.random.randn(30).tolist()
    vols   = np.abs(np.random.randn(30) + 1.0).tolist()
    result = layer.assess(snap, [snap]*3, ticks, prices, vols)
    assert -1.0 <= result.order_flow_imbalance <= 1.0
    assert 0.0 <= result.timing_quality <= 1.0
    assert result.regime_hint in ("ACCUMULATION","DISTRIBUTION","EQUILIBRIUM","NOISE")

def test_nan_raises():
    layer = MarketMicrostructureLayer()
    with pytest.raises(ValueError):
        layer.compute_microstructure_vol([float('nan')]*30)
```

## SESSION 35: GLOBAL SYSTEM STATE CONTROLLER

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S01-S32 (alle)
**Zeit:** 60-75 min
**Datei:** jarvis/core/global_state.py

### Prinzip

Einzige autoritative Quelle fuer den System-Zustand.
ALLE Module muessen diesen State lesen. KEIN lokaler Override.
Thread-safe. Immutable Snapshots. Vollstaendig geloggt.

---

### STATE GOVERNANCE ARCHITECTURE (SYSTEM-WIDE CONSTRAINT)

Es gibt genau **fünf kanonische States**. Kein Modul darf einen sechsten State
außerhalb dieser Registry definieren. Alle States sind im Besitz von
`GlobalSystemStateController` — niemals in Modulen direkt.

**State-Mutations-Regel (System-weit, keine Ausnahmen):**

```python
# KORREKT — alle State-Mutationen über den Controller
ctrl = GlobalSystemStateController.get_instance()
ctrl.update(regime="TRENDING", regime_confidence=0.82)

# VERBOTEN — kein Modul schreibt direkt in den State
state.regime = "TRENDING"              # VERLETZUNG
global_state["regime"] = "TRENDING"   # VERLETZUNG
SystemState.regime = "TRENDING"       # VERLETZUNG
```

Kein Modul darf eine mutable Referenz auf ein State-Objekt halten.
Alle Lesezugriffe geben immutable Snapshots via `ctrl.get_state()` zurück.

---

#### CANONICAL STATE-1: GlobalState

| Eigenschaft | Definition |
|---|---|
| **Kanonische Felder** | mode, ood_status, calibration_status, integrity_status, deployment_blocked, meta_uncertainty, state_hash |
| **Besitzer** | GlobalSystemStateController (Singleton) |
| **Wer darf modifizieren** | GlobalSystemStateController.update() AUSSCHLIESSLICH |
| **Notfall-Write** | GlobalSystemStateController.emergency_shutdown() |
| **Update-Frequenz** | Bei jedem Layer-Abschluss; mindestens bei Regime Engine Output |
| **Persistenz** | In-Memory (Runtime); Snapshot in strukturiertes Log bei jedem Update |
| **Asset-Isolation** | Single global instance — nicht per Asset |
| **Invariante** | state_hash muss SHA-256 aller Felder (exkl. state_hash) entsprechen vor jedem Lesezugriff |

---

#### CANONICAL STATE-2: RegimeState

| Eigenschaft | Definition |
|---|---|
| **Kanonische Felder** | regime (str), regime_confidence (float), regime_probs (Dict[str,float]), regime_age_bars (int), regime_transition_flag (bool) |
| **Besitzer** | GlobalSystemStateController |
| **Wer darf modifizieren** | Regime Engine Output only, via ctrl.update(regime=…) |
| **Verbotene Schreiber** | Strategy Layer, Risk Engine, Portfolio Context, Output Layer |
| **Update-Frequenz** | Jeden Bar (alle Timeframes); sofort bei Regime-Transition |
| **Persistenz** | Runtime + append-only Regime-Log |
| **Asset-Isolation** | Per-Asset RegimeState im Multi-Asset-Modus; indexiert nach asset_id |
| **Invariante** | sum(regime_probs.values()) == 1.0 ± 1e-6; regime_confidence ∈ [0,1] |

```python
# Erweiterung SystemState für RegimeState-Felder (S35-Erweiterung)
# Diese Felder werden in ctrl.update() als regime_* Keys übergeben:
#   regime_confidence: float
#   regime_probs: Dict[str, float]
#   regime_age_bars: int
#   regime_transition_flag: bool
# Validation in GlobalSystemStateController.update():
assert abs(sum(regime_probs.values()) - 1.0) < 1e-6, "regime_probs must sum to 1.0"
assert 0.0 <= regime_confidence <= 1.0, "regime_confidence out of [0,1]"
```

---

#### CANONICAL STATE-3: StrategyState

| Eigenschaft | Definition |
|---|---|
| **Kanonische Felder** | active_strategy_id (str), strategy_mode (StrategyMode), entry_active (bool), exit_active (bool), weight_scalar (float), regime_alignment (bool), last_updated_bar (int) |
| **Besitzer** | GlobalSystemStateController |
| **Wer darf modifizieren** | Strategy Layer only, via ctrl.update(strategy_mode=…) |
| **Verbotene Schreiber** | Confidence Engine, Visual Output, Portfolio Context, Regime Engine |
| **Update-Frequenz** | Bei jedem Regime Engine Output; bleibt unverändert wenn Regime stabil |
| **Persistenz** | Runtime only — keine sitzungsübergreifende Persistenz |
| **Asset-Isolation** | Per-Asset StrategyState im Multi-Asset-Modus |
| **Invariante** | weight_scalar ∈ [0,1]; active_strategy_id muss auf registriertes StrategyObject auflösen |

---

#### CANONICAL STATE-4: PortfolioState

| Eigenschaft | Definition |
|---|---|
| **Kanonische Felder** | positions (Dict[asset_id, float]), gross_exposure (float), net_exposure (float), correlation_matrix (np.ndarray), diversification_ratio (float), portfolio_var (float) |
| **Besitzer** | GlobalSystemStateController |
| **Wer darf modifizieren** | Portfolio Context Layer only, via ctrl.update() |
| **Verbotene Schreiber** | Strategy Layer, Regime Engine, Visual Output |
| **Update-Frequenz** | Nach jedem Risk Engine + Portfolio Context Evaluierungszyklus |
| **Persistenz** | Runtime; Snapshot bei jedem Update |
| **Asset-Isolation** | Inhärent multi-asset; positions nach asset_id indexiert |
| **Invariante** | Alle Matrixwerte finite; positions-Summe konsistent mit gross_exposure |

---

#### CANONICAL STATE-5: VolatilityState

| Eigenschaft | Definition |
|---|---|
| **Kanonische Felder** | realized_vol (float), forecast_vol (float), vol_regime (str), vol_percentile (float), vol_spike_flag (bool), nvu_normalized (float) |
| **Besitzer** | GlobalSystemStateController |
| **Wer darf modifizieren** | Volatility Layer only, via ctrl.update() |
| **Verbotene Schreiber** | Strategy Layer, Regime Engine, Output Layer |
| **Update-Frequenz** | Jeden Bar; sofort bei vol_spike_flag-Transition |
| **Persistenz** | Runtime + rollende 200-Bar Vol-Historie |
| **Asset-Isolation** | Per-Asset im Multi-Asset-Modus; nvu_normalized immer asset-relativ |
| **Invariante** | nvu_normalized ≥ 0; vol_percentile ∈ [0,1]; alle Werte finite |

---


---

### STATE REFRESH POLICY (MODE-AWARE)

Die State-Refresh-Policy definiert wie `GlobalSystemStateController.update()` sich
je nach Betriebsmodus verhaelt. Alle Updates laufen weiterhin AUSSCHLIESSLICH
ueber `ctrl.update()` — keine direkte Mutation in keinem Modus.

```python
# jarvis/core/state_refresh_policy.py
from enum import Enum
from dataclasses import dataclass


class SystemOperatingMode(Enum):
    HISTORICAL       = "historical"
    LIVE_ANALYTICAL  = "live_analytical"
    HYBRID           = "hybrid"


@dataclass
class RefreshPolicy:
    # Policy fuer State-Updates je nach Betriebsmodus.
    # Wird von GlobalSystemStateController gelesen.
    mode:                    SystemOperatingMode
    full_recompute_allowed:  bool
    backtest_loop_allowed:   bool
    incremental_only:        bool
    rolling_window_updates:  bool
    deterministic_cycle:     bool
    backfill_allowed:        bool
    live_sync_point_required: bool


REFRESH_POLICIES = {
    SystemOperatingMode.HISTORICAL: RefreshPolicy(
        mode=SystemOperatingMode.HISTORICAL,
        full_recompute_allowed=True,     # Vollstaendiger State-Reset erlaubt
        backtest_loop_allowed=True,      # Backtest-Loops erlaubt
        incremental_only=False,
        rolling_window_updates=False,
        deterministic_cycle=True,
        backfill_allowed=True,
        live_sync_point_required=False,
    ),
    SystemOperatingMode.LIVE_ANALYTICAL: RefreshPolicy(
        mode=SystemOperatingMode.LIVE_ANALYTICAL,
        full_recompute_allowed=False,    # KEIN vollstaendiger Reset im Live-Modus
        backtest_loop_allowed=False,     # Kein rueckwaertiges Iterieren
        incremental_only=True,           # NUR inkrementelle Updates
        rolling_window_updates=True,     # Nur Rolling-Window-Updates
        deterministic_cycle=True,
        backfill_allowed=False,
        live_sync_point_required=False,
    ),
    SystemOperatingMode.HYBRID: RefreshPolicy(
        mode=SystemOperatingMode.HYBRID,
        full_recompute_allowed=True,     # Nur im Backfill-Fenster
        backtest_loop_allowed=True,      # Nur im Backfill-Fenster
        incremental_only=False,          # Wird True nach sync_point
        rolling_window_updates=True,
        deterministic_cycle=True,
        backfill_allowed=True,           # Nur vor sync_point
        live_sync_point_required=True,   # Strikte Trennung backtest/live
    ),
}
```

**HISTORICAL MODE:**
Full recompute allowed. Backtest loops allowed. Regime recalculation unrestricted.
State may be reset to any prior point for validation.

**LIVE ANALYTICAL MODE:**
Incremental updates only. No full state reset after mode activation.
Rolling window updates only. Deterministic update cycle: one update per confirmed candle.
No backfill after live mode starts.

**HYBRID MODE — STRICT WINDOW SEPARATION:**
```
BACKTEST WINDOW  [start_time .... sync_point):
  - HistoricalDataProvider supplies data
  - Full recompute and backtest loops allowed
  - State-updates as in HISTORICAL mode

LIVE WINDOW      [sync_point .... present]:
  - LiveDataProvider supplies data
  - Incremental updates only
  - Backtest-window state is read-only reference

sync_point rules:
  - Set once when live feed is confirmed active
  - Immutable for the session after setting
  - Stored in GlobalSystemState.hybrid_sync_point: Optional[datetime]
  - All state updates after sync_point: incremental_only = True

SEPARATION INVARIANTS:
  1. Live-window state must not overwrite backtest-window state
  2. Backtest-window results must not be modified after sync_point
  3. sync_point is session-immutable once set
  4. After sync_point: full_recompute_allowed = False
```

**ALL-MODE INVARIANT:**
All state updates in all modes route through `GlobalSystemStateController.update()`.
Direct state mutation is forbidden in every mode. This is a P1 rule, enforced below P0.

---
### EMERGENCY SHUTDOWN TRIGGER CONDITIONS

`ctrl.emergency_shutdown(reason)` wird aufgerufen wenn:

```python
EMERGENCY_CONDITIONS = [
    lambda s: s.meta_uncertainty > 0.90,
    lambda s: s.integrity_status == "COMPROMISED",
    lambda s: s.ood_status == "BLOCKED",
    lambda s: s.calibration_status == "BLOCKED",
    lambda s: s.deployment_blocked and s.mode == "RUNNING",  # inkonsistenter State
]
```

Emergency Shutdown setzt `mode = "EMERGENCY"`, `deployment_blocked = True`,
friert alle State-Writes (außer Shutdown-Log) ein. System bleibt lesbar für Diagnostik.

---

---

## DETERMINISTIC REPLAY MODE

**Datei:** `jarvis/core/replay_engine.py`
**Classification:** Read-only analytical mode. No live data dependency. No execution.
**Purpose:** Deterministic state rebuild from genesis using captured event log.
Enables validation, debugging, and research reproducibility.

---

### EVENT LOG SCHEMA

```python
# jarvis/core/event_log.py
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from datetime import datetime
from typing import List, Optional
import hashlib
import json


@dataclass
class EventLogEntry:
    # Single entry in the immutable event log.
    sequence_id:    int        # Global monotonic sequence
    timestamp:      datetime
    event_type:     str        # EventType.value string
    event_payload:  dict       # Serialized frozen event dataclass
    state_hash_before: str     # GlobalSystemState.state_hash before this event
    state_hash_after:  str     # GlobalSystemState.state_hash after ctrl.update()


@dataclass
class EventLog:
    """
    Complete ordered event log for a session or time window.
    Immutable after session close. Used for replay and audit.
    """
    session_id:       str
    operating_mode:   str           # "historical", "live_analytical", "hybrid"
    start_time:       datetime
    end_time:         Optional[datetime]
    schema_version:   str           # Must match STRATEGY_SCHEMA_VERSION
    entries:          List[EventLogEntry] = field(default_factory=list)
    genesis_state_hash: str = ""    # State hash at session start
    final_state_hash:   str = ""    # State hash at session end
    asset_scope:      List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    integrity_hash:   str = ""      # SHA-256 of full entries sequence

    def compute_integrity_hash(self) -> str:
        """SHA-256 over all entry state_hash_after values in sequence order."""
        chain = "|".join(e.state_hash_after for e in self.entries)
        return hashlib.sha256(chain.encode()).hexdigest()

    def validate_integrity(self) -> bool:
        """Returns True if integrity_hash matches recomputed hash."""
        return self.integrity_hash == self.compute_integrity_hash()
```

---

### REPLAY ENGINE SPECIFICATION

```python
# jarvis/core/replay_engine.py
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Iterator, Optional


@dataclass
class ReplayResult:
    """Result of a replay session comparison."""
    session_id:         str
    total_events:       int
    states_reproduced:  int
    hash_mismatches:    int        # 0 = deterministic replay confirmed
    first_divergence:   Optional[int] = None  # sequence_id of first mismatch
    deterministic:      bool = False
    notes:              str = ""


class ReplayEngine:
    """
    Deterministic Replay Engine — Read-Only Analytical Mode.

    CAPABILITIES:
      - Rebuild system state from genesis using captured EventLog
      - Reproduce identical output for identical input event sequence
      - Compare replayed state hashes against original state hashes
      - No live data dependency during replay
      - No execution — replay is purely analytical

    CONSTRAINTS (non-negotiable):
      1. Replay uses the same DeterministicEventQueue as live operation
      2. Replay is READ-ONLY — no new events may be emitted during replay
         (except internal replay cycle events — not persisted)
      3. Replayed state mutations route through ctrl.update() identically
         to original execution
      4. Replay must be seeded from genesis_state_hash — no mid-stream start
         without explicit checkpoint (see State Checkpointing section)
      5. Replay output is analytical only — no broker calls, no execution
    """

    def replay(
        self,
        event_log: 'EventLog',
        ctrl: 'GlobalSystemStateController',
        verify_hashes: bool = True,
    ) -> ReplayResult:
        """
        Replay full EventLog and optionally verify state hash reproduction.
        Returns ReplayResult with determinism confirmation.
        """
        # Reset state to genesis
        ctrl.reset_to_genesis(event_log.genesis_state_hash)

        mismatches = 0
        first_divergence = None

        for entry in event_log.entries:
            # Dispatch event identically to original execution
            self._dispatch_event(entry, ctrl)

            if verify_hashes:
                actual_hash = ctrl.get_state().state_hash
                if actual_hash != entry.state_hash_after:
                    mismatches += 1
                    if first_divergence is None:
                        first_divergence = entry.sequence_id

        return ReplayResult(
            session_id=event_log.session_id,
            total_events=len(event_log.entries),
            states_reproduced=len(event_log.entries) - mismatches,
            hash_mismatches=mismatches,
            first_divergence=first_divergence,
            deterministic=(mismatches == 0),
            notes="Full deterministic replay confirmed." if mismatches == 0
                  else f"Divergence at sequence_id={first_divergence}",
        )

    def replay_range(
        self,
        event_log: 'EventLog',
        from_sequence: int,
        to_sequence: int,
        ctrl: 'GlobalSystemStateController',
    ) -> Iterator[tuple]:
        """
        Replay a subsequence of events.
        Requires a valid checkpoint at from_sequence - 1.
        Yields (sequence_id, state_snapshot) tuples for analysis.
        """
        for entry in event_log.entries:
            if entry.sequence_id < from_sequence:
                continue
            if entry.sequence_id > to_sequence:
                break
            self._dispatch_event(entry, ctrl)
            yield entry.sequence_id, ctrl.get_state()

    def _dispatch_event(self, entry: 'EventLogEntry', ctrl) -> None:
        """
        Dispatch a single event entry through the same handler path
        as original execution. State mutation via ctrl.update() only.
        """
        # Event dispatch is type-routed; implementation in event_dispatcher.py
        pass
```

---

### DETERMINISM CONSTRAINTS

```
DETERMINISM REQUIREMENTS:

  1. IDENTICAL INPUT → IDENTICAL OUTPUT
     For the same EventLog (same sequence_id order, same payloads),
     the replay must produce identical state_hash at every step.
     A hash mismatch indicates non-determinism — a critical bug.

  2. NO FLOATING POINT NON-DETERMINISM
     All computations use np.float64 with fixed precision.
     No random seeds permitted in deterministic path.
     Random elements (e.g. dropout) must use seeded generators with
     seed stored in EventLogEntry.event_payload.

  3. NO TIMESTAMP-DEPENDENT BRANCHING
     Logic must not branch on wall-clock time.
     Only event timestamps (from EventLogEntry.timestamp) are permitted
     as time references in replay.

  4. REPLAY IS READ-ONLY
     During replay, ctrl.update() is called identically to original execution.
     No additional events are persisted.
     EventLog is not modified during replay.

  5. SNAPSHOT COMPARE
     After any replay_range(), caller may compare:
       replayed_state.state_hash == original_checkpoint.state_hash
     Mismatch = determinism violation. Must be investigated.
```

---

```python
# jarvis/core/global_state.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import threading
from dataclasses import dataclass, field, asdict
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
import hashlib
import json

from jarvis.core.regime import GlobalRegimeState

@dataclass
class SystemState:
    """
    Vollstaendiger autoritativer System-Zustand.
    Immutable nach Erstellung (Snapshots sind Kopien).
    """
    timestamp:           str
    mode:                str   # RUNNING, DEGRADED, EMERGENCY, SHUTDOWN
    ood_status:          str   # NORMAL, ELEVATED, CRITICAL, BLOCKED
    calibration_status:  str   # OK, WARNING, FAILED, BLOCKED
    integrity_status:    str   # OK, COMPROMISED, BLOCKED
    strategy_mode:       str   # MOMENTUM, MEAN_REVERSION, RISK_REDUCTION, DEFENSIVE, MINIMAL
    risk_mode:           str   # NORMAL, ELEVATED, CRITICAL, DEFENSIVE
    meta_uncertainty:    float # U aus Systemvertrag D(t)
    regime:              GlobalRegimeState  # Canonical enum from jarvis.core.regime
    risk_compression:    bool
    last_ece:            float
    last_ood_recall:     float
    deployment_blocked:  bool
    state_hash:          str   # SHA-256 des State (fuer Integritaet)

    @classmethod
    def initial(cls) -> "SystemState":
        """Erstellt den initialen System-State beim Start."""
        state = cls(
            timestamp=datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            mode="RUNNING",
            ood_status="NORMAL",
            calibration_status="OK",
            integrity_status="OK",
            strategy_mode="MINIMAL",
            risk_mode="NORMAL",
            meta_uncertainty=1.0,
            regime=GlobalRegimeState.UNKNOWN,
            risk_compression=True,  # Start immer mit Risk Compression
            last_ece=1.0,
            last_ood_recall=0.0,
            deployment_blocked=True,  # Start immer geblockt bis zertifiziert
            state_hash="",
        )
        state.state_hash = state._compute_hash()
        return state

    def _compute_hash(self) -> str:
        """SHA-256 des States (ohne state_hash-Feld selbst)."""
        d = asdict(self)
        d.pop("state_hash", None)
        return hashlib.sha256(
            json.dumps(d, sort_keys=True).encode("utf-8")
        ).hexdigest()[:16]

    def is_tradeable(self) -> bool:
        """True nur wenn alle Status OK und nicht geblockt."""
        return (
            self.mode == "RUNNING" and
            not self.deployment_blocked and
            self.ood_status not in ("CRITICAL", "BLOCKED") and
            self.calibration_status not in ("FAILED", "BLOCKED") and
            self.integrity_status == "OK" and
            not self.risk_compression
        )


class GlobalSystemStateController:
    """
    Singleton-artiger State Controller.
    Einzige Schnittstelle fuer State-Aenderungen im gesamten System.
    Thread-safe via RLock.
    """
    _instance = None
    _lock = threading.RLock()

    def __init__(self, log_layer=None):
        self._state_lock = threading.RLock()
        self._state: SystemState = SystemState.initial()
        self._history: list = []
        self._log = log_layer
        self._transition_callbacks: list = []

    @classmethod
    def get_instance(cls, log_layer=None) -> "GlobalSystemStateController":
        """Thread-sicherer Singleton-Zugriff."""
        if cls._instance is None:
            with cls._lock:
                if cls._instance is None:
                    cls._instance = cls(log_layer)
        return cls._instance

    def get_state(self) -> SystemState:
        """Gibt aktuellen State als Snapshot zurueck."""
        with self._state_lock:
            return self._state

    def update(self, **kwargs) -> SystemState:
        """
        Aktualisiert State-Felder atomar.
        Nur erlaubte Felder koennen geaendert werden.
        Wirft ValueError bei unbekannten Feldern.
        IMMUTABLE: Altes State wird als History gespeichert.
        """
        ALLOWED_FIELDS = {
            "mode", "ood_status", "calibration_status", "integrity_status",
            "strategy_mode", "risk_mode", "meta_uncertainty", "regime",
            "risk_compression", "last_ece", "last_ood_recall", "deployment_blocked"
        }
        unknown = set(kwargs.keys()) - ALLOWED_FIELDS
        if unknown:
            raise ValueError(f"Unbekannte State-Felder: {unknown}")

        with self._state_lock:
            old_state = self._state
            self._history.append(old_state)
            if len(self._history) > 1000:
                self._history = self._history[-500:]

            # Neuen State aufbauen
            current = asdict(old_state)
            current.pop("state_hash", None)
            current.update(kwargs)
            current["timestamp"] = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()

            # regime must be GlobalRegimeState enum — accept enum or string (.value)
            raw_regime = current["regime"]
            if isinstance(raw_regime, GlobalRegimeState):
                resolved_regime = raw_regime
            else:
                resolved_regime = GlobalRegimeState(raw_regime)

            new_state = SystemState(
                timestamp=current["timestamp"],
                mode=current["mode"],
                ood_status=current["ood_status"],
                calibration_status=current["calibration_status"],
                integrity_status=current["integrity_status"],
                strategy_mode=current["strategy_mode"],
                risk_mode=current["risk_mode"],
                meta_uncertainty=float(current["meta_uncertainty"]),
                regime=resolved_regime,
                risk_compression=bool(current["risk_compression"]),
                last_ece=float(current["last_ece"]),
                last_ood_recall=float(current["last_ood_recall"]),
                deployment_blocked=bool(current["deployment_blocked"]),
                state_hash="",
            )
            new_state.state_hash = new_state._compute_hash()
            self._state = new_state

            # Callbacks ausfuehren
            for cb in self._transition_callbacks:
                try:
                    cb(old_state, new_state)
                except Exception:
                    pass  # Callbacks duerfen State-Updates nicht blockieren

            # Logging (non-blocking)
            if self._log:
                try:
                    self._log.log_event(
                        type="STATE_CHANGE",
                        data={
                            "old_state_hash": old_state.state_hash,
                            "new_state_hash": new_state.state_hash,
                            "changed_fields": list(kwargs.keys()),
                        }
                    )
                except Exception:
                    pass

            return new_state

    def emergency_shutdown(self, reason: str) -> None:
        """
        Notfall-Abschaltung. Nicht umkehrbar ohne Neustart.
        Setzt mode=EMERGENCY und deployment_blocked=True.
        """
        self.update(
            mode="EMERGENCY",
            deployment_blocked=True,
            risk_compression=True,
        )
        if self._log:
            try:
                self._log.log_event(
                    type="EMERGENCY_SHUTDOWN",
                    data={"reason": reason, "state": asdict(self._state)}
                )
            except Exception:
                pass

    def register_transition_callback(self, callback) -> None:
        """Registriert Callback bei State-Aenderungen."""
        with self._state_lock:
            self._transition_callbacks.append(callback)

    def get_history(self, last_n: int = 10) -> list:
        """Gibt letzte n State-Snapshots zurueck."""
        with self._state_lock:
            return list(self._history[-last_n:])
```

### Tests

```python
# tests/unit/core/test_global_state.py
import pytest
from jarvis.core.global_state import GlobalSystemStateController, SystemState
from jarvis.core.regime import GlobalRegimeState

def test_initial_state():
    ctrl = GlobalSystemStateController()
    state = ctrl.get_state()
    assert state.mode == "RUNNING"
    assert state.deployment_blocked == True
    assert state.risk_compression == True

def test_update_valid():
    ctrl = GlobalSystemStateController()
    new_state = ctrl.update(regime=GlobalRegimeState.TRENDING_UP, meta_uncertainty=0.3)
    assert new_state.regime == GlobalRegimeState.TRENDING_UP
    assert abs(new_state.meta_uncertainty - 0.3) < 1e-9

def test_update_invalid_field():
    ctrl = GlobalSystemStateController()
    with pytest.raises(ValueError):
        ctrl.update(nonexistent_field="X")

def test_is_tradeable_blocked():
    ctrl = GlobalSystemStateController()
    # Initial state is blocked
    assert ctrl.get_state().is_tradeable() == False

def test_is_tradeable_ok():
    ctrl = GlobalSystemStateController()
    ctrl.update(
        deployment_blocked=False,
        ood_status="NORMAL",
        calibration_status="OK",
        integrity_status="OK",
        risk_compression=False,
    )
    assert ctrl.get_state().is_tradeable() == True

def test_emergency_shutdown():
    ctrl = GlobalSystemStateController()
    ctrl.update(deployment_blocked=False)
    ctrl.emergency_shutdown("test")
    assert ctrl.get_state().mode == "EMERGENCY"
    assert ctrl.get_state().deployment_blocked == True
```

## STATE CHECKPOINTING AND VERSIONING

**Datei:** `jarvis/core/state_checkpoint.py`
**Classification:** Analytical only. Snapshots contain no execution fields.
**Purpose:** Export and restore system state for research continuity, replay seeding,
and cross-session reproducibility.

---

### VERSION TAGS (SYSTEM-WIDE SCHEMA VERSIONING)

```python
# jarvis/core/schema_versions.py
# All version tags are defined here and NOWHERE else.
# Changes require explicit version bump and migration documentation.
# No silent schema mutation.

GLOBAL_STATE_VERSION        = "1.0.0"   # GlobalSystemState dataclass schema
STRATEGY_OBJECT_VERSION     = "1.0.0"   # StrategyObject schema (also: STRATEGY_SCHEMA_VERSION)
CONFIDENCE_BUNDLE_VERSION   = "1.0.0"   # ConfidenceBundle {mu, sigma2, Q, S, U, R} schema
EVENT_LOG_VERSION           = "1.0.0"   # EventLog and EventLogEntry schema
CHECKPOINT_VERSION          = "1.0.0"   # StateCheckpoint schema

# Cross-reference: STRATEGY_SCHEMA_VERSION (in 99_REFERENCE.md) must equal
# STRATEGY_OBJECT_VERSION here. Any divergence is a build error.
```

---

### CHECKPOINT SCHEMA

```python
# jarvis/core/state_checkpoint.py
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, List, Optional
import hashlib
import json


@dataclass
class StateCheckpoint:
    """
    Exportable point-in-time snapshot of full system state.

    CONSTRAINTS:
      - Contains ZERO execution fields (no orders, no broker state, no credentials)
      - Contains ZERO live market data (state only, not underlying time series)
      - Must pass integrity_hash validation before import
      - Schema version must match current CHECKPOINT_VERSION before import
    """
    # Identity
    checkpoint_id:      str         # UUID
    session_id:         str
    sequence_id:        int         # EventLog sequence_id at checkpoint time
    timestamp:          datetime
    checkpoint_version: str         # Must match CHECKPOINT_VERSION

    # Schema versions (all must match current system versions for import)
    global_state_version:      str
    strategy_object_version:   str
    confidence_bundle_version: str

    # Asset scope
    asset_scope: List[str]          # Which asset_ids are included in this checkpoint

    # State snapshots (all immutable copies — no live references)
    global_state:       dict        # Serialized GlobalSystemState (all fields)
    regime_states:      Dict[str, dict]    # asset_id -> RegimeState snapshot
    volatility_states:  Dict[str, dict]    # asset_id -> VolatilityState snapshot
    strategy_states:    Dict[str, dict]    # asset_id -> StrategyState snapshot
    portfolio_state:    dict               # PortfolioState snapshot
    active_failure_modes: List[str]        # Active FM codes at checkpoint time
    operating_mode:     str                # "historical", "live_analytical", "hybrid"

    # Integrity
    integrity_hash:     str         # SHA-256 of canonical JSON of all state fields

    def compute_integrity_hash(self) -> str:
        """Canonical hash of checkpoint content (excluding integrity_hash field)."""
        payload = {
            "checkpoint_id": self.checkpoint_id,
            "sequence_id": self.sequence_id,
            "global_state": self.global_state,
            "regime_states": self.regime_states,
            "volatility_states": self.volatility_states,
            "strategy_states": self.strategy_states,
            "portfolio_state": self.portfolio_state,
            "active_failure_modes": self.active_failure_modes,
        }
        canonical = json.dumps(payload, sort_keys=True, default=str)
        return hashlib.sha256(canonical.encode()).hexdigest()

    def validate_integrity(self) -> bool:
        return self.integrity_hash == self.compute_integrity_hash()


class CheckpointManager:
    """
    Manages export and import of StateCheckpoint objects.
    Read-only analytical use only. No execution state persisted.
    """

    def export_snapshot(
        self,
        ctrl: 'GlobalSystemStateController',
        session_id: str,
        sequence_id: int,
        asset_scope: list,
    ) -> StateCheckpoint:
        """
        Export current state as a validated checkpoint.
        All state fields are copied (no live references).
        Integrity hash computed and attached.
        """
        from jarvis.core.schema_versions import (
            CHECKPOINT_VERSION, GLOBAL_STATE_VERSION,
            STRATEGY_OBJECT_VERSION, CONFIDENCE_BUNDLE_VERSION,
        )
        import uuid
        from datetime import datetime

        state = ctrl.get_state()   # immutable snapshot

        checkpoint = StateCheckpoint(
            checkpoint_id=str(uuid.uuid4()),
            session_id=session_id,
            sequence_id=sequence_id,
            timestamp=datetime.utcnow(),
            checkpoint_version=CHECKPOINT_VERSION,
            global_state_version=GLOBAL_STATE_VERSION,
            strategy_object_version=STRATEGY_OBJECT_VERSION,
            confidence_bundle_version=CONFIDENCE_BUNDLE_VERSION,
            asset_scope=list(asset_scope),
            global_state=dict(vars(state)),
            regime_states={},    # Populated from per-asset state snapshots
            volatility_states={},
            strategy_states={},
            portfolio_state={},  # Populated from PortfolioState snapshot
            active_failure_modes=[],
            operating_mode=getattr(state, "operating_mode", "historical"),
            integrity_hash="",
        )
        checkpoint.integrity_hash = checkpoint.compute_integrity_hash()
        return checkpoint

    def import_snapshot(
        self,
        checkpoint: StateCheckpoint,
        ctrl: 'GlobalSystemStateController',
    ) -> None:
        """
        Restore system state from a validated checkpoint.
        Fails explicitly on version mismatch or hash failure.
        No silent schema mutation.
        """
        from jarvis.core.schema_versions import (
            CHECKPOINT_VERSION, GLOBAL_STATE_VERSION,
            STRATEGY_OBJECT_VERSION, CONFIDENCE_BUNDLE_VERSION,
        )

        # Version validation
        if checkpoint.checkpoint_version != CHECKPOINT_VERSION:
            raise ValueError(
                f"Checkpoint version mismatch: "
                f"checkpoint={checkpoint.checkpoint_version}, "
                f"system={CHECKPOINT_VERSION}. "
                f"Migration required before import."
            )
        if checkpoint.global_state_version != GLOBAL_STATE_VERSION:
            raise ValueError(
                f"GlobalState schema version mismatch: "
                f"{checkpoint.global_state_version} != {GLOBAL_STATE_VERSION}"
            )
        if checkpoint.strategy_object_version != STRATEGY_OBJECT_VERSION:
            raise ValueError(
                f"StrategyObject version mismatch: "
                f"{checkpoint.strategy_object_version} != {STRATEGY_OBJECT_VERSION}"
            )

        # Integrity validation
        if not checkpoint.validate_integrity():
            raise ValueError(
                f"Checkpoint integrity hash validation failed. "
                f"Checkpoint may be corrupted or tampered."
            )

        # Restore state via ctrl.update() — no direct mutation
        ctrl.update(**checkpoint.global_state)
```

---

### MIGRATION GOVERNANCE

```
VERSION MISMATCH HANDLING RULES:

  1. VERSION MISMATCH = HARD ERROR
     Import of a checkpoint with mismatched version MUST raise ValueError.
     Silent migration is forbidden. No automatic field inference.

  2. BACKWARD COMPATIBILITY REQUIREMENT
     When a schema version is bumped (e.g. GLOBAL_STATE_VERSION 1.0.0 -> 1.1.0):
     - A migration function must be written: migrate_v1_0_0_to_v1_1_0()
     - The function must be tested with known-good checkpoints
     - Old checkpoints must be explicitly migrated before import
     - Migration functions live in: jarvis/core/migrations/

  3. NO SILENT SCHEMA MUTATION
     Adding, removing, or renaming fields in any versioned dataclass
     requires a version bump. No structural changes without version bump.

  4. NO EXECUTION FIELDS IN SNAPSHOTS
     Snapshot export must explicitly exclude any field containing:
       - broker_id, order_id, account_id
       - margin_*, position_open_* (real execution fields)
       - Any field from a forbidden execution class
     Checkpoint schema contains only analytical state fields.
```

---

## PHASE 3 — DECISION CONTEXT STATE (CANONICAL SUB-STATE)

**Insertion point:** After MIGRATION GOVERNANCE, end of file.
**Governed by:** P0 — ANALYSIS AND STRATEGY RESEARCH TOOL. No execution, no real capital tracking.

### DECISION CONTEXT STATE

```python
# jarvis/core/decision_context_state.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
# Phase 3 addition — Decision Quality Maximization
# GOVERNANCE: Part of GlobalSystemState canonical sub-state hierarchy.
# All mutations through ctrl.update(). DecisionQualityEngine reads via snapshot.

from __future__ import annotations
from collections import deque
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import Deque, Literal, Optional

# Phase 3 constant — registered in 99_REFERENCE.md
MAX_DECISION_CONTEXT: int = 200


OutcomeClassification = Literal["WIN", "LOSS", "NEUTRAL"]
# Purely analytical classification of a past signal outcome.
# WIN:     analytical signal was directionally correct (backtested or forward-sim).
# LOSS:    analytical signal was directionally incorrect.
# NEUTRAL: outcome indeterminate, insufficient data, or not yet classified.
# NO PnL, NO real capital, NO account balance referenced.


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class DecisionRecord:
    """
    Immutable record of a single analytical decision event.
    No execution semantics. No real capital references.
    """
    sequence_id: int
    # Monotonically increasing identifier. Derived from GlobalSystemState.sequence_id
    # at the time the analytical decision was recorded.

    regime_at_decision: str
    # RegimeState.regime value at decision time (snapshot).
    # E.g.: "BULL_QUIET", "BEAR_VOLATILE", "SIDEWAYS", "SHOCK", "UNKNOWN".

    confidence_at_decision: float
    # ConfidenceBundle.Q value at decision time (snapshot). Range [0.0, 1.0].

    outcome: OutcomeClassification
    # Analytical outcome classification. Assigned retroactively via
    # ctrl.update() when outcome becomes evaluable.
    # Default: "NEUTRAL" at record creation.

    strategy_id: str
    # Identifier of the StrategyObject that produced this signal.
    # Must match a registered strategy in StrategyRegistry.


@dataclass
class DecisionContextState:
    """
    Rolling analytical memory of the last N decision records.
    N is capped at MAX_DECISION_CONTEXT (200).

    Canonical sub-state of GlobalSystemState. All mutations MUST go through
    GlobalSystemStateController.update() (ctrl.update()). This class is
    never mutated directly by any module outside the controller.

    PURPOSE:
      Provides DecisionQualityEngine with historical pattern context for:
        - streak instability detection
        - repeated failure pattern penalty
        - regime misalignment detection

    GOVERNANCE:
      - No real capital tracking
      - No PnL referencing real account balance
      - No broker_id, order_id, account_id fields (forbidden)
      - All outcome classifications are purely analytical
      - N cap enforced at every append operation
    """
    records: Deque[DecisionRecord] = field(
        default_factory=lambda: deque(maxlen=MAX_DECISION_CONTEXT)
    )
    # Rolling deque of DecisionRecord entries.
    # maxlen = MAX_DECISION_CONTEXT = 200.
    # Oldest record is automatically evicted when limit is reached.

    total_appended: int = 0
    # Monotonically increasing count of total records ever appended.
    # Not reset on eviction. Used for audit trail.

    def snapshot(self) -> "DecisionContextSnapshot":
        """
        Return a frozen snapshot for use by DecisionQualityEngine.
        Snapshot is a point-in-time copy; does not hold a reference to
        the live deque.
        """
        return DecisionContextSnapshot(
            records=tuple(self.records),
            total_appended=self.total_appended,
        )


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class DecisionContextSnapshot:
    """
    Frozen point-in-time snapshot of DecisionContextState.
    Consumed ONLY by DecisionQualityEngine (read-only).
    """
    records: tuple
    # Tuple of DecisionRecord (ordered oldest-first).
    # Length <= MAX_DECISION_CONTEXT.

    total_appended: int
    # Total records ever appended to the parent DecisionContextState.
```

**MUTATION CONTRACT:**
```python
# jarvis/core/global_state_controller.py — mutation path (partial)
# CORRECT — all mutations via ctrl.update()
def _apply_decision_context_update(
    self,
    state: DecisionContextState,
    new_record: Optional[DecisionRecord] = None,
    outcome_update: Optional[dict] = None,   # {sequence_id: OutcomeClassification}
) -> None:
    """
    Apply DecisionContextState mutation. Called ONLY from
    GlobalSystemStateController.update() within the existing
    state mutation exclusivity lock.

    new_record:    If provided, appended to rolling deque.
                   maxlen enforcement is automatic via deque(maxlen=200).
    outcome_update: If provided, re-creates affected records with updated outcome.
                    sequence_id must exist in current records window.
                    Records outside the window are silently ignored (evicted).
    """
    if new_record is not None:
        state.records.append(new_record)
        state.total_appended += 1

    if outcome_update:
        updated = []
        for rec in state.records:
            if rec.sequence_id in outcome_update:
                updated.append(DecisionRecord(
                    sequence_id=rec.sequence_id,
                    regime_at_decision=rec.regime_at_decision,
                    confidence_at_decision=rec.confidence_at_decision,
                    outcome=outcome_update[rec.sequence_id],
                    strategy_id=rec.strategy_id,
                ))
            else:
                updated.append(rec)
        state.records.clear()
        state.records.extend(updated)

# FORBIDDEN — no direct write outside controller
decision_context_state.records.append(...)          # VIOLATION
decision_context_state.records[0].outcome = "WIN"   # VIOLATION (also frozen record)
```

**DECISIONQUALITYENGINE CONSUMPTION PATTERNS:**
```python
# jarvis/intelligence/decision_quality_engine.py (partial — DecisionContextSnapshot usage)
# CORRECT — snapshot passed in; no live state reference held

def _detect_streak_instability(
    snapshot: DecisionContextSnapshot,
    window: int = 10,
) -> float:
    """
    Compute streak instability score from recent decision outcomes.
    Returns float in [0.0, 1.0]. Higher = more unstable outcome pattern.
    Deterministic. No side effects.
    """
    recent = list(snapshot.records)[-window:]
    if len(recent) < 2:
        return 0.0
    outcomes = [r.outcome for r in recent]
    transitions = sum(1 for a, b in zip(outcomes, outcomes[1:]) if a != b)
    return float(transitions / max(len(recent) - 1, 1))

def _detect_regime_misalignment(
    snapshot: DecisionContextSnapshot,
    current_regime: str,
    window: int = 20,
) -> float:
    """
    Fraction of recent decisions made in a different regime than the current one.
    High value = current regime is historically under-sampled → reduced confidence.
    Deterministic. No side effects.
    """
    recent = list(snapshot.records)[-window:]
    if not recent:
        return 0.0
    misaligned = sum(1 for r in recent if r.regime_at_decision != current_regime)
    return float(misaligned / len(recent))

def _detect_repeated_failure_penalty(
    snapshot: DecisionContextSnapshot,
    window: int = 10,
    loss_threshold: float = 0.6,
) -> float:
    """
    Returns a penalty score if recent LOSS rate exceeds loss_threshold.
    Penalty = (loss_rate - loss_threshold) / (1.0 - loss_threshold).
    Clipped to [0.0, 1.0].
    """
    recent = list(snapshot.records)[-window:]
    if not recent:
        return 0.0
    losses = sum(1 for r in recent if r.outcome == "LOSS")
    loss_rate = float(losses / len(recent))
    if loss_rate <= loss_threshold:
        return 0.0
    return float(min(1.0, (loss_rate - loss_threshold) / max(1.0 - loss_threshold, 1e-9)))
```

**GOVERNANCE:**
```
DecisionContextState may ONLY be mutated via ctrl.update().
DecisionContextSnapshot may ONLY be consumed by DecisionQualityEngine.

DecisionContextState may NOT:
  - Reference real capital, PnL, or account balance
  - Contain broker_id, order_id, account_id fields
  - Be mutated outside GlobalSystemStateController
  - Be read directly by Risk Engine, Strategy Layer, or Visual Output
    (these layers receive DecisionQualityBundle outputs instead)

DETERMINISM:
  DecisionRecord is frozen. Outcome updates create new records (immutable pattern).
  DecisionContextSnapshot is tuple-based (ordered, hashable).
  All consumer functions operating on DecisionContextSnapshot are pure functions.

SCHEMA VERSION ALIGNMENT:
  DecisionContextState is part of GlobalSystemState schema.
  Addition of this sub-state requires GLOBAL_STATE_VERSION bump per
  MIGRATION GOVERNANCE rules (19-35_MICROSTRUCTURE_GLOBALSTATE.md).
  GLOBAL_STATE_VERSION must be incremented from "1.0.0" to "1.1.0" in
  jarvis/core/schema_versions.py, with corresponding migration function
  migrate_v1_0_0_to_v1_1_0() written and tested.
```

Ein Weltklasse-System analysiert NICHT nur Preis.

Nur Preis analysieren = Retail-Level.
7-Layer-Kombination    = Institutional-Level.

### Layer-Hierarchie

    Layer 1: Price & Volatility       (S06 + S08 + S17)
    Layer 2: Regime Detection         (S05 + S20)
    Layer 3: Liquidity                (S21)
    Layer 4: Cross-Asset Correlation  (S22)
    Layer 5: Macro Sensitivity        (S23)
    Layer 6: News & Event Impact      (S24)
    Layer 7: Risk Forecasting         (S17 + kombiniert)

## SESSION 21: LIQUIDITY LAYER

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S03, S05
**Zeit:** 60-75 min

### Scope

Bewertet Marktliquiditaet fuer Risikokorrektur.
Schlechte Liquiditaet -> erhoehter Slippage -> groessere Confidence Boxen.

```python
# jarvis/intelligence/liquidity_layer.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import numpy as np
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import List, Optional

@dataclass
class LiquidityAssessment:
    bid_ask_spread:    float   # Aktueller Spread (in Basispoints)
    spread_percentile: float   # Spread vs. Historisch (0=eng, 1=weit)
    volume_ratio:      float   # Aktuell/Durchschnitt-Volumen
    market_depth:      float   # Relative Markttiefe (0=gering, 1=hoch)
    liquidity_score:   float   # Gesamt-Score [0,1]: 0=illiquide, 1=sehr liquide
    slippage_estimate: float   # Geschaetzter Slippage in % fuer Standardposition
    regime_impact:     str     # NEGLIGIBLE, MODERATE, SIGNIFICANT, CRITICAL

class LiquidityLayer:
    """
    Layer 3: Liquidity Assessment.
    Ergebnis wird als Multiplikator auf Confidence Zones angewendet.
    """

    SPREAD_THRESHOLD_MODERATE   = 0.001   # 10 Basispoints
    SPREAD_THRESHOLD_CRITICAL   = 0.005   # 50 Basispoints
    VOLUME_RATIO_LOW_THRESHOLD  = 0.5
    VOLUME_RATIO_HIGH_THRESHOLD = 2.0

    def assess(
        self,
        current_spread: float,
        historical_spreads: List[float],
        current_volume: float,
        avg_volume: float,
        order_book_depth: Optional[float] = None,
    ) -> LiquidityAssessment:
        """
        Vollstaendiges Liquidity Assessment.
        Wirft ValueError bei negativen/NaN-Werten.
        """
        for name, val in [("current_spread", current_spread),
                          ("current_volume", current_volume),
                          ("avg_volume", avg_volume)]:
            if not np.isfinite(val) or val < 0:
                raise ValueError(f"Ungaeltiger Wert: {name}={val}")

        if len(historical_spreads) < 10:
            raise ValueError("Mindestens 10 historische Spreads erforderlich")

        spread_arr = np.array(historical_spreads)
        if not np.all(np.isfinite(spread_arr)):
            raise ValueError("Historische Spreads enthalten NaN/Inf")

        spread_pct = float(np.mean(spread_arr <= current_spread))
        vol_ratio  = float(current_volume / max(avg_volume, 1e-10))
        depth      = float(np.clip(order_book_depth, 0.0, 1.0)) if order_book_depth else 0.5

        # Liquidity Score: gewichtet
        spread_score = float(np.clip(1.0 - spread_pct, 0.0, 1.0))
        vol_score    = float(np.clip(vol_ratio / self.VOLUME_RATIO_HIGH_THRESHOLD, 0.0, 1.0))
        liquidity_score = 0.4 * spread_score + 0.35 * vol_score + 0.25 * depth
        liquidity_score = float(np.clip(liquidity_score, 0.0, 1.0))

        # Slippage-Schaetzung
        slippage_estimate = current_spread * (1.0 + (1.0 - liquidity_score))

        # Regime Impact
        if liquidity_score < 0.2:
            regime_impact = "CRITICAL"
        elif liquidity_score < 0.4:
            regime_impact = "SIGNIFICANT"
        elif liquidity_score < 0.65:
            regime_impact = "MODERATE"
        else:
            regime_impact = "NEGLIGIBLE"

        return LiquidityAssessment(
            bid_ask_spread=current_spread,
            spread_percentile=spread_pct,
            volume_ratio=vol_ratio,
            market_depth=depth,
            liquidity_score=liquidity_score,
            slippage_estimate=slippage_estimate,
            regime_impact=regime_impact,
        )
```
