## SESSION 22: CROSS-ASSET CORRELATION LAYER

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S03, S05
**Zeit:** 70-90 min

### Scope

Misst Korrelation des Ziel-Assets zu anderen Assets.
Hohe Korrelation zu Risiko-Assets + Markt faellt = erhoehtes Risiko.

```python
# jarvis/intelligence/cross_asset_layer.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import numpy as np
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, List

from jarvis.core.regime import CorrelationRegimeState

@dataclass
class CrossAssetSignal:
    correlations:       Dict[str, float]  # Asset-Name -> Korrelation [-1,1]
    risk_on_exposure:   float             # Exposure zu Risk-On Regime [0,1]
    correlation_regime: CorrelationRegimeState  # DECOUPLED, COUPLED, CRISIS_COUPLING
    systemic_risk:      float             # Systemisches Risiko [0,1]

class CrossAssetLayer:
    """
    Layer 4: Cross-Asset Correlation Analysis.
    Erkennt systemische Risikoverbreitung zwischen Asset-Klassen.
    """

    CRISIS_CORRELATION_THRESHOLD = 0.85

    def compute(
        self,
        target_returns: List[float],
        reference_assets: Dict[str, List[float]],
        window: int = 60,
    ) -> CrossAssetSignal:
        """
        Berechnet rollierende Korrelationen zu Referenz-Assets.
        """
        if len(target_returns) < window:
            raise ValueError(f"Mindestens {window} Returns erforderlich")

        target_arr = np.array(target_returns[-window:])
        if not np.all(np.isfinite(target_arr)):
            raise ValueError("Target returns enthalten NaN/Inf")

        correlations: Dict[str, float] = {}
        for name, ref_returns in reference_assets.items():
            ref_arr = np.array(ref_returns[-window:])
            if len(ref_arr) < window or not np.all(np.isfinite(ref_arr)):
                correlations[name] = 0.0
                continue
            cov_mat = np.cov(target_arr, ref_arr)
            denom   = float(np.sqrt(max(cov_mat[0, 0] * cov_mat[1, 1], 1e-12)))
            corr    = float(cov_mat[0, 1] / denom)
            correlations[name] = float(np.clip(corr, -1.0, 1.0))

        # Risk-On Exposure: Mittelwert der Korrelationen zu Risk-Assets
        if correlations:
            risk_on = float(np.mean(list(correlations.values())))
            risk_on = float(np.clip((risk_on + 1.0) / 2.0, 0.0, 1.0))
        else:
            risk_on = 0.5

        # Correlation Regime
        max_corr = max(abs(v) for v in correlations.values()) if correlations else 0.0
        if max_corr > self.CRISIS_CORRELATION_THRESHOLD:
            corr_regime = CorrelationRegimeState.CRISIS_COUPLING
        elif max_corr > 0.6:
            corr_regime = CorrelationRegimeState.COUPLED
        else:
            corr_regime = CorrelationRegimeState.DECOUPLED

        # Systemisches Risiko
        systemic = float(max_corr * risk_on)
        systemic = float(np.clip(systemic, 0.0, 1.0))

        return CrossAssetSignal(
            correlations=correlations,
            risk_on_exposure=risk_on,
            correlation_regime=corr_regime,
            systemic_risk=systemic,
        )
```

## SESSION 23: MACRO SENSITIVITY LAYER

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S05, S22
**Zeit:** 60-75 min

### Scope

Bewertet Sensitivitaet des Assets zu makrooekonomischen Faktoren.
Zins, Inflation, Waehrung -> Impact auf Asset-Klasse.

```python
# jarvis/intelligence/macro_layer.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import numpy as np
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict

from jarvis.core.regime import MacroRegimeState

@dataclass
class MacroSensitivityResult:
    factor_sensitivities: Dict[str, float]  # Faktor -> Beta
    macro_risk_score:     float             # Gesamt-Makro-Risiko [0,1]
    dominant_factor:      str              # Dominantester Makro-Faktor
    macro_regime:         MacroRegimeState  # BENIGN, UNCERTAIN, ADVERSE

class MacroSensitivityLayer:
    """
    Layer 5: Macro Sensitivity Assessment.
    Bewertet wie stark das Asset auf Makro-Faktoren reagiert.
    """

    MACRO_FACTORS = ["interest_rate", "inflation", "usd_strength",
                     "credit_spread", "vix"]

    def compute(
        self,
        asset_returns: list,
        factor_returns: Dict[str, list],
        window: int = 120,
    ) -> MacroSensitivityResult:
        """
        OLS-Regression: Asset gegen Makro-Faktoren.
        """
        target = np.array(asset_returns[-window:])
        if not np.all(np.isfinite(target)):
            raise ValueError("Asset returns enthalten NaN/Inf")

        betas: Dict[str, float] = {}
        for factor_name, f_returns in factor_returns.items():
            f_arr = np.array(f_returns[-window:])
            if len(f_arr) < window or not np.all(np.isfinite(f_arr)):
                betas[factor_name] = 0.0
                continue
            # Einfache OLS-Beta: Cov(y,x)/Var(x)
            cov    = float(np.cov(target, f_arr)[0, 1])
            var_x  = float(np.var(f_arr))
            beta   = cov / max(var_x, 1e-12)
            betas[factor_name] = float(np.clip(beta, -5.0, 5.0))

        # Makro-Risiko-Score: L2-Norm der Betas normalisiert
        beta_arr = np.array(list(betas.values()))
        macro_score = float(np.clip(
            np.sqrt(np.sum(beta_arr ** 2)) / max(len(betas), 1), 0.0, 1.0
        ))

        # Dominanter Faktor
        dominant = max(betas, key=lambda k: abs(betas[k])) if betas else "NONE"

        # Makro-Regime
        if macro_score > 0.7:
            macro_regime = MacroRegimeState.ADVERSE
        elif macro_score > 0.4:
            macro_regime = MacroRegimeState.UNCERTAIN
        else:
            macro_regime = MacroRegimeState.BENIGN

        return MacroSensitivityResult(
            factor_sensitivities=betas,
            macro_risk_score=macro_score,
            dominant_factor=dominant,
            macro_regime=macro_regime,
        )
```

## SESSION 24: NEWS & EVENT INTELLIGENCE LAYER

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S03, S17
**Zeit:** 80-100 min

### Prinzip

NICHT "Internet lesen".
Stattdessen:
  - Whitelisted Quellen (konfigurierbar, nicht hardcoded)
  - NLP Event Detection
  - Impact-Score pro Event
  - Zeitgestempelte Einbindung in Systemvertrag
  - Shock-Probability Injection

News wird strukturierte Variable, KEIN Chaosfaktor.

```python
# jarvis/intelligence/news_layer.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import numpy as np
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from datetime import datetime
from typing import List, Dict, Optional
import hashlib

from jarvis.core.regime import NewsRegimeState

@dataclass
class NewsEvent:
    """Strukturierter News-Event. Kein roher Text in Systemkern."""
    event_id:        str       # SHA-256 der Headline (Eindeutigkeit)
    source:          str       # Whitelisted Quellen-ID
    timestamp:       datetime
    category:        str       # CENTRAL_BANK, EARNINGS, GEOPOLITICAL, ECONOMIC, OTHER
    headline_hash:   str       # Hash der Headline (kein Originaltext im System)
    sentiment_score: float     # [-1,1]: -1=sehr negativ, 1=sehr positiv
    impact_score:    float     # [0,1]: Einfluss auf Asset-Klasse
    shock_prob:      float     # [0,1]: Wahrscheinlichkeit eines Schock-Events
    processed:       bool = False

@dataclass
class NewsLayerOutput:
    recent_events:          List[NewsEvent]
    aggregate_impact:       float   # Gewichteter Durchschnitt Impact [0,1]
    shock_probability:      float   # P(Schock-Event) in naechster Periode
    news_regime:            NewsRegimeState  # QUIET, ACTIVE, HIGH_IMPACT, SHOCK
    sentiment_drift:        float   # Trend der Stimmung [-1,1]


class NewsIntelligenceLayer:
    """
    Layer 6: News & Event Intelligence.
    Nur whitelisted Quellen. Kontrollierte, strukturierte Verarbeitung.
    """

    # Whitelisted Quellen: NIEMALS dynamisch erweiterbar ohne Config-Aenderung
    WHITELISTED_SOURCES: List[str] = field(default_factory=lambda: [])

    IMPACT_CATEGORIES: Dict[str, float] = {
        "CENTRAL_BANK":  0.9,
        "GEOPOLITICAL":  0.7,
        "ECONOMIC":      0.6,
        "EARNINGS":      0.5,
        "OTHER":         0.2,
    }

    SHOCK_PROB_THRESHOLD = 0.7

    def __init__(self, whitelisted_sources: List[str]):
        if not whitelisted_sources:
            raise ValueError("Mindestens eine whitelisted Quelle erforderlich")
        self.whitelisted_sources = whitelisted_sources

    def process_event(
        self,
        source: str,
        timestamp: datetime,
        category: str,
        headline_text: str,
        raw_sentiment: float,
    ) -> Optional[NewsEvent]:
        """
        Verarbeitet einen News-Event. Gibt None zurueck wenn Quelle nicht whitelisted.
        Speichert NIEMALS den Original-Text im System.
        """
        if source not in self.whitelisted_sources:
            return None  # Nicht-whitelisted Quellen werden ignoriert

        if category not in self.IMPACT_CATEGORIES:
            category = "OTHER"

        # Headline-Hash: kein Original-Text im Systemkern
        headline_hash = hashlib.sha256(headline_text.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()[:16]
        event_id      = hashlib.sha256(
            f"{source}{timestamp.isoformat()}{headline_hash}".encode()
        ).hexdigest()[:16]

        sentiment = float(np.clip(raw_sentiment, -1.0, 1.0))
        base_impact = self.IMPACT_CATEGORIES.get(category, 0.2)
        # Negativer Sentiment erhoht Impact
        impact = float(np.clip(base_impact * (1.0 + max(-sentiment, 0.0)), 0.0, 1.0))

        # Shock-Wahrscheinlichkeit: basierend auf Sentiment und Impact
        shock_prob = float(np.clip(
            impact * max(-sentiment, 0.0), 0.0, 1.0
        ))

        return NewsEvent(
            event_id=event_id,
            source=source,
            timestamp=timestamp,
            category=category,
            headline_hash=headline_hash,
            sentiment_score=sentiment,
            impact_score=impact,
            shock_prob=shock_prob,
            processed=True,
        )

    def aggregate(
        self,
        events: List[NewsEvent],
        lookback_hours: float = 24.0,
        now: Optional[datetime] = None,
    ) -> NewsLayerOutput:
        """
        Aggregiert News-Events zu strukturiertem Layer-Output.
        """
        now = now or datetime.utcnow()

        # Zeitfenster: nur Events der letzten lookback_hours
        cutoff_seconds = lookback_hours * 3600.0
        recent = [
            e for e in events
            if (now - e.timestamp).total_seconds() <= cutoff_seconds
            and e.processed
        ]

        if not recent:
            return NewsLayerOutput(
                recent_events=[],
                aggregate_impact=0.0,
                shock_probability=0.0,
                news_regime=NewsRegimeState.QUIET,
                sentiment_drift=0.0,
            )

        impacts     = np.array([e.impact_score for e in recent])
        shocks      = np.array([e.shock_prob for e in recent])
        sentiments  = np.array([e.sentiment_score for e in recent])

        agg_impact  = float(np.mean(impacts))
        shock_prob  = float(np.clip(np.max(shocks), 0.0, 1.0))
        sent_drift  = float(np.mean(sentiments))

        # News Regime
        if shock_prob >= self.SHOCK_PROB_THRESHOLD:
            news_regime = NewsRegimeState.SHOCK
        elif agg_impact > 0.6:
            news_regime = NewsRegimeState.HIGH_IMPACT
        elif len(recent) > 5:
            news_regime = NewsRegimeState.ACTIVE
        else:
            news_regime = NewsRegimeState.QUIET

        return NewsLayerOutput(
            recent_events=recent,
            aggregate_impact=agg_impact,
            shock_probability=shock_prob,
            news_regime=news_regime,
            sentiment_drift=sent_drift,
        )
```

### Kritische Anforderungen

- R1: KEINE nicht-whitelisted Quellen verarbeiten
- R2: Originaltext NIEMALS im Systemkern gespeichert (nur Hash)
- R3: shock_probability direkt in Systemvertrag als sigma^2-Erweiterung
- R4: Alle verarbeiteten Events in BUILD_LOG geloggt (event_id, timestamp, impact)

## SESSION 25: MULTI-SOURCE MARKET DATA RESEARCH LAYER

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S03
**Zeit:** 50-65 min

### Prinzip

Daten von mehreren Brokern = bessere Datenbasis.
ABER: Execution Layer strikt getrennt.
Kein direkter, ungesicherter Brokerzugriff.

Zweck der Multi-Broker-Schicht:
  - Spread-Vergleich zwischen Brokern
  - Liquiditaetsunterschiede erkennen
  - Datenpunkte cross-validieren
  - Best-of-Data-Feed-Auswahl

```python
# jarvis/intelligence/multi_broker_layer.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import numpy as np
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, List, Optional

@dataclass
class BrokerQuote:
    broker_id:   str
    bid:         float
    ask:         float
    timestamp:   float  # Unix-Timestamp
    volume:      Optional[float] = None

@dataclass
class MultiBrokerAssessment:
    best_bid:        float             # Bester Bid aller Broker
    best_ask:        float             # Bester Ask aller Broker
    avg_spread:      float             # Durchschnittlicher Spread
    min_spread:      float             # Minimaler Spread
    spread_dispersion: float           # Spread-Streuung (Qualitaetsindikator)
    liquidity_map:   Dict[str, float]  # Broker-ID -> Liquiditaets-Score
    preferred_source: str             # Broker mit bestem Spread+Liquiditaet
    data_quality:    float            # Quote-Qualitaet [0,1]


class MultiSourceDataLayer:
    """
    Layer: Multi-Source Market Data Research Aggregation.
    ISOLIERT vom jedem Execution-Layer. Kein Broker-Interface fuer Orders.
    Kein Trade-Routing. Nur Daten-Aggregation und Qualitaets-Analyse.
    Zweck: Spread-Research, Liquiditaets-Forschung, Datenqualitaets-Bewertung.
    """

    MAX_QUOTE_AGE_SECONDS = 10.0  # Quotes aelter als 10s werden ignoriert

    def aggregate(
        self,
        quotes: List[BrokerQuote],
        now_ts: float,
    ) -> MultiBrokerAssessment:
        """
        Aggregiert Broker-Quotes zu strukturiertem Output.
        Ignoriert veraltete Quotes (>MAX_QUOTE_AGE_SECONDS).
        """
        if not quotes:
            raise ValueError("Keine Broker-Quotes vorhanden")

        # Frische Quotes filtern
        fresh = [
            q for q in quotes
            if abs(now_ts - q.timestamp) <= self.MAX_QUOTE_AGE_SECONDS
            and np.isfinite(q.bid) and np.isfinite(q.ask)
            and q.ask > q.bid > 0
        ]

        if not fresh:
            raise ValueError("Keine gueltigen/frischen Broker-Quotes")

        bids = np.array([q.bid for q in fresh])
        asks = np.array([q.ask for q in fresh])
        spreads = asks - bids

        best_bid = float(np.max(bids))
        best_ask = float(np.min(asks))
        avg_spread = float(np.mean(spreads))
        min_spread = float(np.min(spreads))
        spread_dispersion = float(np.std(spreads))

        # Liquiditaets-Map
        liq_map: Dict[str, float] = {}
        for q in fresh:
            spread_score = float(np.clip(
                1.0 - (q.ask - q.bid) / max(avg_spread, 1e-10), 0.0, 1.0
            ))
            vol_score = 0.5
            if q.volume is not None and np.isfinite(q.volume) and q.volume > 0:
                all_vols = [x.volume for x in fresh if x.volume]
                if all_vols:
                    vol_score = float(np.clip(
                        q.volume / max(np.mean(all_vols), 1e-10), 0.0, 1.0
                    ))
            liq_map[q.broker_id] = 0.6 * spread_score + 0.4 * vol_score

        preferred = max(liq_map, key=lambda k: liq_map[k]) if liq_map else "UNKNOWN"

        # Daten-Qualitaet: basierend auf Anzahl frischer Quotes und Spread-Konsistenz
        freshness_score = float(np.clip(len(fresh) / max(len(quotes), 1), 0.0, 1.0))
        consistency     = float(np.clip(
            1.0 - spread_dispersion / max(avg_spread, 1e-10), 0.0, 1.0
        ))
        data_quality = 0.5 * freshness_score + 0.5 * consistency

        return MultiBrokerAssessment(
            best_bid=best_bid,
            best_ask=best_ask,
            avg_spread=avg_spread,
            min_spread=min_spread,
            spread_dispersion=spread_dispersion,
            liquidity_map=liq_map,
            preferred_broker=preferred,
            data_quality=data_quality,
        )
```

### Isolations-Anforderungen (KRITISCH — P0 ENFORCEMENT)

- R1: MultiSourceDataLayer hat KEIN Interface zum Execution Layer und keinen Broker-Order-Kanal
- R2: Kein Trade-Routing. Nur Daten-Aggregation und Qualitaets-Analyse.
- R3: API-Credentials fuer Datenquellen NIEMALS in diesem Layer (nur in gesichertem Vault)
- R4: Veraltete Quotes (>10s) werden ignoriert, nicht als Fehler behandelt
- R5: Outputs gehen NUR an Intelligence Layer (S21-S24) und Feature Registry — niemals an Execution

## PHASE 2 — EPISTEMIC UNCERTAINTY (BLOCK D CROSS-REFERENCE)

**Full implementation in:** `37_SYSTEM_ADDENDUM.md` (Block D section)
**Datei:** `jarvis/intelligence/epistemic_uncertainty.py`

```
EpistemicUncertaintyEngine integrates with Intelligence Layer as follows:

  Input from Intelligence layers:
    - S21 (Liquidity): contributes to data_sparsity_score via thin-market detection
    - S23 (Macro): regime instability observable from macro regime changes
    - S24 (News): n_regime_changes informed by news-driven regime events
    - S25 (Multi-Source Data): n_valid_samples from data quality assessment

  Output to:
    - ConfidenceBundle: total_uncertainty -> sigma^2 (system contract component)
    - WeightPosteriorModel: if total_uncertainty > 0.5, caps posterior_mean at 0.3
    - Visual Output (P9): full UncertaintyBundle breakdown displayed

  UncertaintyBundle is frozen and read-only downstream.
  No layer downstream may modify it.
  No layer uses it to trigger execution.
```

P6 Strategy Layer or P9 Visual Output only. No execution triggers. No stochastic simulation.

### REGIME TRANSITION MATRIX

**Datei:** `jarvis/intelligence/regime_transition.py`

```python
# jarvis/intelligence/regime_transition.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import Dict, List, Tuple
import numpy as np


# Canonical regime ordering — must match REGIME_STATES in 99_REFERENCE.md
CANONICAL_REGIMES: List[str] = ["TRENDING", "RANGING", "HIGH_VOL", "SHOCK", "UNKNOWN"]
N_REGIMES: int = len(CANONICAL_REGIMES)


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class RegimeTransitionMatrix:
    """
    NxN Markov-style transition probability matrix for regime dynamics.
    Frozen: immutable after creation. Deterministic update — no random sampling.

    GOVERNANCE:
      - Rows must sum to 1.0 (validated at construction)
      - Matrix is updated from observed regime sequence — no stochastic generation
      - Output feeds Confidence Engine (P8) and Visual Output (P9) only
      - Must NOT trigger execution or strategy switching directly
    """
    regimes:    Tuple[str, ...]      # Canonical regime labels (N,)
    matrix:     Tuple[Tuple[float, ...], ...]  # NxN transition probabilities
    n_obs:      int                  # Number of observations used to estimate
    version:    str                  # Schema version — must match GLOBAL_STATE_VERSION

    def __post_init__(self):
        m = np.array(self.matrix, dtype=np.float64)
        if m.shape != (len(self.regimes), len(self.regimes)):
            raise ValueError(f"Matrix shape {m.shape} != ({len(self.regimes)}, {len(self.regimes)})")
        row_sums = m.sum(axis=1)
        if not np.allclose(row_sums, 1.0, atol=1e-6):
            raise ValueError(f"Rows must sum to 1.0; got {row_sums}")

    def transition_probability(self, from_regime: str, to_regime: str) -> float:
        """P(to | from) — deterministic lookup from matrix."""
        i = self.regimes.index(from_regime)
        j = self.regimes.index(to_regime)
        return self.matrix[i][j]

    def most_likely_next(self, current_regime: str) -> str:
        """Returns regime with highest transition probability from current."""
        i = self.regimes.index(current_regime)
        row = self.matrix[i]
        return self.regimes[int(np.argmax(row))]


class RegimeTransitionEstimator:
    """
    Estimates RegimeTransitionMatrix from observed regime sequence.
    Deterministic: frequency counting, no randomness.
    """

    def estimate(
        self,
        observed_regimes: List[str],
        regimes: List[str] = None,
        laplace_smoothing: float = 0.1,
    ) -> RegimeTransitionMatrix:
        """
        Compute transition matrix from regime sequence via frequency counting.
        Laplace smoothing ensures no zero-probability transitions.
        """
        from jarvis.core.schema_versions import GLOBAL_STATE_VERSION
        if regimes is None:
            regimes = CANONICAL_REGIMES
        n = len(regimes)
        idx = {r: i for i, r in enumerate(regimes)}

        counts = np.full((n, n), laplace_smoothing, dtype=np.float64)
        n_obs = 0
        for t in range(len(observed_regimes) - 1):
            fr = observed_regimes[t]
            to = observed_regimes[t + 1]
            if fr in idx and to in idx:
                counts[idx[fr], idx[to]] += 1.0
                n_obs += 1

        row_sums = counts.sum(axis=1, keepdims=True)
        matrix_arr = counts / np.maximum(row_sums, 1e-10)

        return RegimeTransitionMatrix(
            regimes=tuple(regimes),
            matrix=tuple(tuple(float(v) for v in row) for row in matrix_arr),
            n_obs=n_obs,
            version=GLOBAL_STATE_VERSION,
        )
```

### VOLATILITY MARKOV MODEL

**Datei:** `jarvis/intelligence/volatility_markov.py`

```python
# jarvis/intelligence/volatility_markov.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, Tuple
import numpy as np


# Volatility state bins — deterministic thresholds from 99_REFERENCE.md
# LOW: nvu_normalized < 1.0, MEDIUM: 1.0-2.0, HIGH: 2.0-3.0, EXTREME: >= 3.0
VOL_STATES: Tuple[str, ...] = ("LOW", "MEDIUM", "HIGH", "EXTREME")


def classify_vol_state(nvu_normalized: float) -> str:
    """Deterministic classification — no randomness."""
    if nvu_normalized < 1.0:
        return "LOW"
    elif nvu_normalized < 2.0:
        return "MEDIUM"
    elif nvu_normalized < 3.0:
        return "HIGH"
    else:
        return "EXTREME"


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class VolatilityTransitionMatrix:
    """
    Markov transition matrix for volatility state dynamics.
    Used ONLY for probability scoring — NOT for stochastic simulation.
    Frozen, deterministic, no random sampling.

    GOVERNANCE: Output used only for:
      - Confidence Engine probability weighting
      - Visual Output volatility transition display
      - Strategy Weight posterior adjustment (read-only input)
    """
    states:  Tuple[str, ...]
    matrix:  Tuple[Tuple[float, ...], ...]  # NxN transition probabilities
    n_obs:   int
    version: str

    def __post_init__(self):
        m = np.array(self.matrix)
        if not np.allclose(m.sum(axis=1), 1.0, atol=1e-6):
            raise ValueError("VolatilityTransitionMatrix rows must sum to 1.0")

    def transition_probability(self, from_state: str, to_state: str) -> float:
        i = self.states.index(from_state)
        j = self.states.index(to_state)
        return self.matrix[i][j]

    def prob_fm02_trigger(self, current_state: str) -> float:
        """P(EXTREME | current) — probability of FM-02 vol spike trigger."""
        return self.transition_probability(current_state, "EXTREME")
```

### BAYESIAN CONFIDENCE UPDATE

**Datei:** `jarvis/intelligence/bayesian_confidence.py`

```python
# jarvis/intelligence/bayesian_confidence.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict
import numpy as np


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class BayesianConfidenceUpdate:
    """
    Result of a Bayesian posterior confidence update.
    Frozen, deterministic. No Monte Carlo, no random sampling.

    FORMULA: posterior = (prior * likelihood) / evidence
    where evidence = sum_over_all_hypotheses(prior_i * likelihood_i)

    GOVERNANCE:
      - posterior_confidence feeds only ConfidenceBundle.Q and Weight_Model
      - May not trigger execution or auto-open positions
      - Spike-up constraint: posterior >= prior only when regime is stable
        AND no active Failure Modes AND data quality > 0.7
    """
    prior_confidence:    float   # ConfidenceBundle.Q before update
    likelihood:          float   # P(data | hypothesis) — deterministic mapping
    evidence:            float   # Normalizing constant
    posterior_confidence: float  # Computed: (prior * likelihood) / evidence
    regime_stable:       bool    # Whether current regime permits spike-up
    fm_active:           bool    # Whether any Failure Mode is active
    update_permitted:    bool    # True if posterior will be applied


# Deterministic likelihood mapping from regime and data quality
LIKELIHOOD_TABLE: Dict[str, Dict[str, float]] = {
    # regime -> data_quality_band -> likelihood
    "TRENDING":  {"high": 0.85, "medium": 0.65, "low": 0.40},
    "RANGING":   {"high": 0.75, "medium": 0.55, "low": 0.35},
    "HIGH_VOL":  {"high": 0.50, "medium": 0.35, "low": 0.20},
    "SHOCK":     {"high": 0.30, "medium": 0.20, "low": 0.10},
    "UNKNOWN":   {"high": 0.25, "medium": 0.15, "low": 0.08},
}


def data_quality_band(quality_score: float) -> str:
    if quality_score >= 0.75:
        return "high"
    elif quality_score >= 0.50:
        return "medium"
    else:
        return "low"


class BayesianConfidenceEngine:
    """
    Computes Bayesian posterior confidence from prior and current market evidence.
    Deterministic — uses LIKELIHOOD_TABLE, no sampling.

    GOVERNANCE:
      - Spike-up (posterior > prior) requires: regime_stable AND NOT fm_active
        AND data quality >= 0.70
      - If constraints not met: posterior = min(prior, computed_posterior)
      - Output feeds ConfidenceBundle.Q only — no other state
    """

    def update(
        self,
        prior_confidence: float,
        regime: str,
        quality_score: float,
        fm_active: bool,
        regime_stable: bool,
        joint_multiplier: float = 1.0,
    ) -> BayesianConfidenceUpdate:
        """
        Compute posterior confidence via Bayesian update.

        Optional parameter joint_multiplier accepts the JRM value from
        RiskEngine / constants.JOINT_RISK_MULTIPLIER_TABLE. When 1.0
        (default), behavior is identical to prior versions.
        L_adjusted = L_base / joint_multiplier reduces the effective
        likelihood under joint macro + correlation stress.
        """
        if not (0.0 <= prior_confidence <= 1.0):
            raise ValueError(f"prior_confidence must be in [0,1]: {prior_confidence}")

        band = data_quality_band(quality_score)
        l_base = LIKELIHOOD_TABLE.get(regime, LIKELIHOOD_TABLE["UNKNOWN"])[band]

        # Joint Macro x Correlation Risk Multiplier: reduces likelihood under stress.
        # joint_multiplier == 1.0 → no change (backward compatible default).
        likelihood = float(np.clip(l_base / max(joint_multiplier, 1e-10), 0.0, 1.0))

        # Evidence: weighted sum over all regimes (simplified closed-form)
        evidence = sum(
            (1.0 / len(LIKELIHOOD_TABLE)) * LIKELIHOOD_TABLE[r][band]
            for r in LIKELIHOOD_TABLE
        )
        evidence = max(evidence, 1e-10)

        raw_posterior = float(np.clip(
            (prior_confidence * likelihood) / evidence, 0.0, 1.0
        ))

        # Spike-up constraint
        spike_up_permitted = regime_stable and not fm_active and quality_score >= 0.70
        if not spike_up_permitted:
            posterior = min(prior_confidence, raw_posterior)
        else:
            posterior = raw_posterior

        return BayesianConfidenceUpdate(
            prior_confidence=prior_confidence,
            likelihood=likelihood,
            evidence=evidence,
            posterior_confidence=float(np.clip(posterior, 0.0, 1.0)),
            regime_stable=regime_stable,
            fm_active=fm_active,
            update_permitted=True,
        )
```

---

### STRATEGY WEIGHT POSTERIOR MODEL

**Datei:** `jarvis/intelligence/weight_posterior.py`

```python
# jarvis/intelligence/weight_posterior.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, List
import numpy as np


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class WeightPosteriorModel:
    """
    Posterior weight distribution over strategy candidates.
    Replaces static weight reinforcement.
    Posterior mean used as input to StrategyObject.Weight_Model.
    Frozen, deterministic.

    GOVERNANCE:
      - posterior_mean is the ONLY field consumed by Weight_Model
      - No adaptive execution behavior
      - May not trigger position changes directly
      - StrategyObject.Weight_Model remains authoritative for actual weights
    """
    strategy_id:       str
    prior_weight:      float             # Prior weight (from previous cycle)
    posterior_mean:    float             # Posterior mean — consumed by Weight_Model
    posterior_std:     float             # Uncertainty in weight estimate
    evidence_count:    int               # Number of observations used
    regime_alignment:  float            # [0,1] — how well strategy fits regime
    confidence_factor: float            # ConfidenceBundle.Q at time of update


class WeightPosteriorEstimator:
    """
    Estimates posterior weight distribution for each strategy candidate.
    Uses regime alignment + Bayesian update + confidence scaling.
    Deterministic — no random sampling.
    """

    def estimate(
        self,
        strategy_id: str,
        prior_weight: float,
        historical_weights: List[float],
        regime_alignment: float,
        confidence_q: float,
        fm_active: bool,
    ) -> WeightPosteriorModel:
        """
        Compute posterior weight estimate.
        If FM active: posterior_mean capped at prior_weight * 0.5 (defensive).
        """
        if len(historical_weights) < 2:
            posterior_mean = prior_weight * regime_alignment * confidence_q
            posterior_std  = 0.5  # High uncertainty with few observations
        else:
            arr = np.array(historical_weights[-20:], dtype=np.float64)  # Last 20 obs
            obs_mean = float(np.mean(arr))
            obs_std  = float(np.std(arr))

            # Bayesian combination: equally weight prior and observation
            posterior_mean = 0.5 * prior_weight + 0.5 * obs_mean
            posterior_mean *= regime_alignment * confidence_q
            posterior_std   = obs_std / max(np.sqrt(len(arr)), 1.0)

        if fm_active:
            posterior_mean = min(posterior_mean, prior_weight * 0.5)

        return WeightPosteriorModel(
            strategy_id=strategy_id,
            prior_weight=float(np.clip(prior_weight, 0.0, 1.0)),
            posterior_mean=float(np.clip(posterior_mean, 0.0, 1.0)),
            posterior_std=float(np.clip(posterior_std, 0.0, 0.5)),
            evidence_count=len(historical_weights),
            regime_alignment=float(np.clip(regime_alignment, 0.0, 1.0)),
            confidence_factor=float(np.clip(confidence_q, 0.0, 1.0)),
        )
```

**PROBABILISTIC MODULE GOVERNANCE:**
```
ALL probabilistic module outputs are subject to the following constraints:

  1. NO EXECUTION TRIGGERS
     RegimeTransitionMatrix, VolatilityTransitionMatrix, BayesianConfidenceUpdate,
     and WeightPosteriorModel outputs do NOT trigger any execution action.

  2. PERMITTED DATA PATHS:
     - P6 Strategy Layer (via StrategyObject.Weight_Model for WeightPosteriorModel)
     - P8 Confidence Engine (BayesianConfidenceUpdate.posterior_confidence -> Q)
     - P9 Visual Output (all probability displays)

  3. FORBIDDEN DATA PATHS:
     - Execution layer (does not exist)
     - Broker API (does not exist)
     - Direct state mutation (all updates via ctrl.update())

  4. DETERMINISM REQUIREMENT:
     All probability computations are deterministic for identical inputs.
     Same RegimeTransitionMatrix + same input sequence = same output.
     No random seeds, no Monte Carlo paths in production pipeline.
```

## PHASE 3 — REGIME DURATION MODEL (BLOCK E)

**Insertion point:** After PHASE 2 — PROBABILISTIC FORMALIZATION (BLOCK A), end of file.
**Governed by:** P0 — ANALYSIS AND STRATEGY RESEARCH TOOL. No execution, no broker integration.

### REGIME DURATION MODEL

```python
# jarvis/intelligence/regime_duration_model.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
# Phase 3 addition — Decision Quality Maximization
# GOVERNANCE: Output feeds ONLY DecisionQualityEngine.
# May NOT directly alter Risk Engine thresholds.
# Deterministic. No stochastic transition simulation.

from dataclasses import dataclass


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class RegimeDurationResult:
    """
    Frozen output of RegimeDurationModel.
    All fields are deterministically computed from snapshot inputs.
    No randomness. No time-dependent non-deterministic logic.
    """
    regime_age_ratio: float
    # Current regime age / historical_avg_duration.
    # 1.0 = regime has lived exactly its historical average lifespan.
    # > 1.0 = regime is aging beyond its historical norm.
    # Clipped to [0.0, 5.0] for numerical stability.

    duration_z_score: float
    # (current_age - historical_avg_duration) / historical_std_duration
    # Z-score of current regime age relative to its historical distribution.
    # Clipped to [-5.0, 5.0].

    transition_acceleration_flag: bool
    # True when |duration_z_score| >= DURATION_STRESS_Z_LIMIT (2.0).
    # Signals the regime has significantly exceeded or fallen short of
    # its historical mean duration.
    # Does NOT trigger any Risk Engine action directly.


class RegimeDurationModel:
    """
    Computes regime age statistics from snapshot state.

    Governance constraints:
      - DETERMINISTIC: identical inputs produce identical outputs.
      - SNAPSHOT-ONLY: operates on passed-in values; does not read live buffers.
      - NO STATE MUTATION: never calls ctrl.update().
      - NO EXECUTION SEMANTICS: output is purely analytical metadata.
      - OUTPUT ROUTING: RegimeDurationResult is consumed ONLY by
        DecisionQualityEngine. No other layer may read it directly.
      - FORBIDDEN: stochastic transition simulation, Monte Carlo,
        random seeds, live feed access, broker concepts.
    """

    # Phase 3 constant — registered in 99_REFERENCE.md
    DURATION_STRESS_Z_LIMIT: float = 2.0   # mirrors DURATION_STRESS_Z_LIMIT

    def compute(
        self,
        regime_start_timestamp: float,       # Unix epoch seconds (snapshot value)
        current_timestamp: float,            # Unix epoch seconds (snapshot value)
        historical_avg_duration: float,      # seconds; from rolling regime statistics
        historical_std_duration: float,      # seconds; from rolling regime statistics
    ) -> RegimeDurationResult:
        """
        Deterministically compute regime duration stress metrics.

        Args:
            regime_start_timestamp: Timestamp when current regime began.
                                    Must be <= current_timestamp.
            current_timestamp:      Snapshot timestamp at evaluation time.
            historical_avg_duration: Rolling mean of past regime durations
                                     for this regime type. Must be > 0.
            historical_std_duration: Rolling std of past regime durations.
                                     Clipped to min 1.0 to avoid division by zero.

        Returns:
            RegimeDurationResult (frozen, deterministic).

        Raises:
            ValueError: if current_timestamp < regime_start_timestamp,
                        or historical_avg_duration <= 0.
        """
        if current_timestamp < regime_start_timestamp:
            raise ValueError(
                "current_timestamp must be >= regime_start_timestamp. "
                f"Got current={current_timestamp}, start={regime_start_timestamp}"
            )
        if historical_avg_duration <= 0.0:
            raise ValueError(
                f"historical_avg_duration must be > 0. Got {historical_avg_duration}"
            )

        current_age: float = current_timestamp - regime_start_timestamp
        std_safe: float = max(historical_std_duration, 1.0)

        # Regime age ratio: how old is the regime relative to its historical mean
        age_ratio = float(
            max(0.0, min(5.0, current_age / historical_avg_duration))
        )

        # Z-score of current regime age
        z_score = float(
            max(-5.0, min(5.0, (current_age - historical_avg_duration) / std_safe))
        )

        # Acceleration flag: regime is statistically long-lived or unusually short
        acceleration_flag: bool = abs(z_score) >= self.DURATION_STRESS_Z_LIMIT

        return RegimeDurationResult(
            regime_age_ratio=age_ratio,
            duration_z_score=z_score,
            transition_acceleration_flag=acceleration_flag,
        )
```

**GOVERNANCE:**
```
RegimeDurationModel output (RegimeDurationResult) may ONLY:
  1. Feed DecisionQualityEngine.regime_duration_stress_score computation.

RegimeDurationModel may NOT:
  - Directly alter RegimeState fields via ctrl.update()
  - Directly modify Risk Engine thresholds or FM activation conditions
  - Emit analytical events
  - Access live market data buffers
  - Call any broker or execution abstraction

DETERMINISM GUARANTEE:
  Given identical (regime_start_timestamp, current_timestamp,
  historical_avg_duration, historical_std_duration), the output
  RegimeDurationResult is bit-for-bit identical across invocations,
  operating modes, and platform restarts.

ROLLING STATISTICS SOURCE:
  historical_avg_duration and historical_std_duration are derived from
  RegimeMemoryLayer (jarvis/systems/regime_memory.py) snapshot state.
  They are passed as plain float arguments — RegimeDurationModel does not
  hold a reference to any stateful object.

BUDGET: Execution of RegimeDurationModel.compute() is part of the
  DecisionQualityEngine budget (max 20 ms total per cycle — see
  40_RISK_ENGINE_SPECS.md Phase 3 Performance and Safety Constraints).
```

# SESSIONS 26-30: ADAPTIVE STRATEGY & SIMULATION LAB

## SESSION 26: ADAPTIVE STRATEGY ABSTRACTION

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S05, S16, S17, S21-S25
**Zeit:** 70-90 min

### Prinzip

KEINE fixen Strategien.
Stattdessen: Regime aktiviert Strategie-Modus.

    TRENDING  -> Momentum-Modus
    RANGING   -> Mean-Reversion-Modus
    HIGH_VOL  -> Risk-Reduction-Modus
    SHOCK     -> Defensive-Modus
    UNKNOWN   -> Minimal-Exposure-Modus

Strategien sind das RESULTAT der Marktstruktur, NICHT manuell gewaehlt.
Benutzer sieht den aktiven Modus, kann ihn NICHT manuell ueberschreiben.

```python
# jarvis/strategy/adaptive_strategy.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import numpy as np
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, Optional
from enum import Enum

from jarvis.core.regime import GlobalRegimeState, NewsRegimeState

class StrategyMode(Enum):
    MOMENTUM         = "MOMENTUM"
    MEAN_REVERSION   = "MEAN_REVERSION"
    RISK_REDUCTION   = "RISK_REDUCTION"
    DEFENSIVE        = "DEFENSIVE"
    MINIMAL_EXPOSURE = "MINIMAL_EXPOSURE"

@dataclass
class StrategyModeConfig:
    """Parameter-Set pro Strategie-Modus."""
    label:                  str
    confidence_box_scale:   float   # Multiplikator auf Entry/Exit-Boxen
    max_exposure_pct:       float   # Maximale Exposure in %
    position_size_cap:      float   # Max Position-Size-Faktor [0,1]
    recalibration_priority: str     # LOW, MEDIUM, HIGH, CRITICAL

STRATEGY_CONFIGS: Dict[StrategyMode, StrategyModeConfig] = {
    StrategyMode.MOMENTUM: StrategyModeConfig(
        label="MOMENTUM",
        confidence_box_scale=1.0,
        max_exposure_pct=0.80,
        position_size_cap=0.9,
        recalibration_priority="LOW",
    ),
    StrategyMode.MEAN_REVERSION: StrategyModeConfig(
        label="MEAN_REVERSION",
        confidence_box_scale=0.7,
        max_exposure_pct=0.65,
        position_size_cap=0.7,
        recalibration_priority="MEDIUM",
    ),
    StrategyMode.RISK_REDUCTION: StrategyModeConfig(
        label="RISK_REDUCTION",
        confidence_box_scale=1.4,
        max_exposure_pct=0.40,
        position_size_cap=0.45,
        recalibration_priority="HIGH",
    ),
    StrategyMode.DEFENSIVE: StrategyModeConfig(
        label="DEFENSIVE",
        confidence_box_scale=2.0,
        max_exposure_pct=0.20,
        position_size_cap=0.2,
        recalibration_priority="CRITICAL",
    ),
    StrategyMode.MINIMAL_EXPOSURE: StrategyModeConfig(
        label="MINIMAL_EXPOSURE",
        confidence_box_scale=2.5,
        max_exposure_pct=0.10,
        position_size_cap=0.1,
        recalibration_priority="CRITICAL",
    ),
}

@dataclass
class StrategySelection:
    mode:              StrategyMode
    config:            StrategyModeConfig
    activation_reason: str
    override_locked:   bool = True  # IMMER True: kein manuelles Override


class AdaptiveStrategySelector:
    """
    Waehlt Strategie-Modus basierend auf Regime und Risk-Output.
    Kein manuelles Ueberschreiben moeglich.
    """

    REGIME_TO_STRATEGY: Dict[str, StrategyMode] = {
        "TRENDING":  StrategyMode.MOMENTUM,
        "RANGING":   StrategyMode.MEAN_REVERSION,
        "HIGH_VOL":  StrategyMode.RISK_REDUCTION,
        "SHOCK":     StrategyMode.DEFENSIVE,
        "UNKNOWN":   StrategyMode.MINIMAL_EXPOSURE,
    }

    def select(
        self,
        regime:               str,
        risk_compression:     bool,
        volatility_forecast:  float,
        news_regime:          str = "QUIET",
        liquidity_score:      float = 0.8,
    ) -> StrategySelection:
        """
        Automatische Strategie-Selektion. Kein manueller Override.
        """
        # Shock-Bedingungen zuerst pruefen (haben hoechste Prioritaet)
        if risk_compression or news_regime == NewsRegimeState.SHOCK:
            mode = StrategyMode.DEFENSIVE
            reason = (
                f"Risk compression active={risk_compression}, "
                f"news_regime={news_regime}"
            )
        elif liquidity_score < 0.2:
            mode = StrategyMode.DEFENSIVE
            reason = f"Critical liquidity: {liquidity_score:.3f}"
        elif regime == GlobalRegimeState.UNKNOWN:
            mode = StrategyMode.MINIMAL_EXPOSURE
            reason = "Regime unbekannt: minimale Exposure"
        else:
            mode   = self.REGIME_TO_STRATEGY.get(regime, StrategyMode.MINIMAL_EXPOSURE)
            reason = f"Regime={regime}"

        return StrategySelection(
            mode=mode,
            config=STRATEGY_CONFIGS[mode],
            activation_reason=reason,
            override_locked=True,  # Unveraenderlich
        )
```

### Kritische Anforderungen

- R1: override_locked ist IMMER True, keine Ausnahme
- R2: Alle Strategie-Aktivierungen in BUILD_LOG geloggt
- R3: Strategie-Modus ist SICHTBAR im Chart-Interface (Session 31)
- R4: STRATEGY_CONFIGS sind Hash-gesichert (THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json)

### STRATEGY OBJECT SCHEMA (KANONISCH — SYSTEM-WEITER STANDARD)

Alle Strategien im System werden durch exakt dieses Schema repräsentiert.
Keine Strategie darf instanziiert, gewichtet, selektiert oder evaluiert werden
außerhalb dieser Struktur. `AdaptiveStrategySelector` gibt `StrategySelection`
zurück; jede `StrategySelection` muss auf ein registriertes `StrategyObject` auflösen.

**Datei:** `jarvis/core/strategy_schema.py`

```python
# jarvis/core/strategy_schema.py
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, List
from enum import Enum


class StrategyType(Enum):
    MOMENTUM          = "momentum"
    MEAN_REVERSION    = "mean_reversion"
    BREAKOUT          = "breakout"
    CARRY             = "carry"
    VOLATILITY_SELL   = "volatility_sell"
    DEFENSIVE         = "defensive"
    MINIMAL_EXPOSURE  = "minimal_exposure"


class RegimeSensitivity(Enum):
    HIGH    = "high"    # Only active in specific regime
    MEDIUM  = "medium"  # Reduced weight outside target regime
    LOW     = "low"     # Active across all regimes


class VolatilitySensitivity(Enum):
    EXPANDS   = "expands"    # Increases allocation in high vol
    CONTRACTS = "contracts"  # Reduces allocation in high vol
    NEUTRAL   = "neutral"    # Unaffected by vol level


class SessionSensitivity(Enum):
    LIQUID_ONLY  = "liquid_only"   # Disabled during illiquid sessions
    ADAPTIVE     = "adaptive"      # Reduces size during illiquid sessions
    SESSION_FREE = "session_free"  # Asset is 24/7 (crypto)


@dataclass
class EntryModel:
    signal_type:           str    # "momentum_cross", "mean_rev_zscore", etc.
    signal_threshold:      float  # Minimum signal strength to trigger
    confirmation_bars:     int    # Bars signal must persist before entry
    max_entry_spread_bps:  float  # Max spread at entry (bps); 0 = no limit


@dataclass
class ExitModel:
    stop_loss_atr_multiple:   float  # Stop = N * ATR from entry
    take_profit_atr_multiple: float  # TP = N * ATR from entry; 0 = no TP
    time_exit_bars:           int    # Force exit after N bars; 0 = disabled
    trailing_stop:            bool   # Enable trailing stop
    regime_exit:              bool   # Exit immediately on regime change


@dataclass
class RiskModel:
    base_risk_per_trade:   float  # Fraction of capital at risk; max 0.02
    max_position_size:     float  # Hard cap on position as fraction of capital
    kelly_fraction:        float  # Kelly multiplier ∈ [0, 1]
    confidence_floor:      float  # Minimum confidence to allow any sizing
    var_contribution_cap:  float  # Max contribution to portfolio VaR


@dataclass
class WeightModel:
    base_weight:          float            # Default portfolio weight ∈ [0, 1]
    regime_weight_map:    Dict[str, float] # Per-regime weight override
    volatility_scalar_fn: str              # Name of registered scalar function
    min_weight:           float            # Floor; never go below this
    max_weight:           float            # Ceiling; never exceed this


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class StrategyObject:
    """
    Kanonische Repräsentation aller Strategien in JARVIS.
    Immutable nach Konstruktion.
    Adaptive Weighting darf NUR über dieses Schema operieren.
    """
    # Identity
    Strategy_ID:               str
    Strategy_Type:             StrategyType

    # Models
    Entry_Model:               EntryModel
    Exit_Model:                ExitModel
    Risk_Model:                RiskModel
    Weight_Model:              WeightModel

    # Regime and Environment Sensitivity
    Regime_Sensitivity:        RegimeSensitivity
    Volatility_Sensitivity:    VolatilitySensitivity
    Session_Sensitivity:       SessionSensitivity

    # Temporal Profile
    Timeframe_Profile:         str   # "M5", "H1", "H4", "D1", or "MULTI"
    Expected_Holding_Duration: int   # Expected bars held; informs exit model

    # Metadata
    target_regime:             str   # Primary regime this strategy targets
    asset_class_scope:         list  # ["crypto"], ["forex"], ["all"], etc.
    version:                   str   # Schema version; must match STRATEGY_SCHEMA_VERSION

    def validate(self) -> bool:
        """
        Strukturelle Validierung. Wirft ValueError bei Verletzung.
        Wird bei Konstruktion aufgerufen. Kein silent pass.
        """
        assert 0 < self.Risk_Model.base_risk_per_trade <= 0.02, \
            f"base_risk_per_trade {self.Risk_Model.base_risk_per_trade} out of (0, 0.02]"
        assert 0.0 <= self.Risk_Model.confidence_floor <= 1.0, \
            f"confidence_floor out of [0, 1]"
        assert 0.0 <= self.Weight_Model.base_weight <= 1.0, \
            f"base_weight out of [0, 1]"
        assert self.Weight_Model.min_weight <= self.Weight_Model.base_weight \
                                             <= self.Weight_Model.max_weight, \
            f"weight bounds inconsistent"
        assert self.Expected_Holding_Duration > 0, \
            f"Expected_Holding_Duration must be positive"
        return True
```

**ADAPTIVE WEIGHTING CONSTRAINT (nicht verletzbar):**

```python
# KORREKT — Adaptive Weighting NUR über Weight_Model
def apply_adaptive_weight(obj: StrategyObject, current_regime: str) -> float:
    w = obj.Weight_Model.regime_weight_map.get(
            current_regime,
            obj.Weight_Model.base_weight
        )
    return float(np.clip(w, obj.Weight_Model.min_weight, obj.Weight_Model.max_weight))

# VERBOTEN
strategy.weight = 0.3                                # VERLETZUNG
AdaptiveSelector._internal_weight["MOMENTUM"] = 0.5 # VERLETZUNG
```

**STRATEGY REGISTRY:**

```python
# jarvis/core/strategy_registry.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
_REGISTRY: Dict[str, StrategyObject] = {}

def register(obj: StrategyObject) -> None:
    """Registriert StrategyObject. Wirft bei Duplikat oder Validierungsfehler."""
    obj.validate()
    if obj.Strategy_ID in _REGISTRY:
        raise ValueError(f"Duplicate Strategy_ID: {obj.Strategy_ID}")
    if obj.version != STRATEGY_SCHEMA_VERSION:
        raise ValueError(
            f"Schema version mismatch: {obj.version} != {STRATEGY_SCHEMA_VERSION}"
        )
    _REGISTRY[obj.Strategy_ID] = obj

def get(strategy_id: str) -> StrategyObject:
    if strategy_id not in _REGISTRY:
        raise KeyError(f"Unregistered strategy: {strategy_id}")
    return _REGISTRY[strategy_id]
```

**Schema-Version ist in `99_REFERENCE.md` unter `STRATEGY_SCHEMA_VERSION` gepflegt.**
Migration erfordert Version-Bump und vollständigen Registry-Rebuild. Kein silent migration.

**Backwards Compatibility (Crypto-Only):**
- `asset_class_scope = ["crypto"]` auf allen StrategyObjects
- `Session_Sensitivity = SESSION_FREE` (FM-05 wird nie getriggert)
- PortfolioState.positions enthält einen einzigen Asset-Eintrag

## SESSION 27: DETERMINISTISCHE LERNARCHITEKTUR

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S12 (Learning Engine), S09 (Calibration), S15 (Validation)
**Zeit:** 80-100 min

### Prinzip

KEIN unkontrolliertes Live-Selbstlernen.
Stattdessen: Kontrollierter, deterministischer Lernzyklus.

    Schritt 1: Training in Chunks (kontrolliert)
    Schritt 2: Validierung (ECE-Gate)
    Schritt 3: Stress-Test (historische Krisen)
    Schritt 4: Vergleich mit aktiver Version
    Schritt 5: Deployment NUR bei klarer Verbesserung
    Schritt 6: Drift-Ueberwachung (kontinuierlich)
    Schritt 7: Rollback jederzeit moeglich

```python
# jarvis/learning/deterministic_learning.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import hashlib
import json
import numpy as np
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
from datetime import datetime
from pathlib import Path
from typing import List, Optional, Dict, Any

@dataclass
class LearningCycleResult:
    cycle_id:           str
    timestamp:          str
    ece_before:         float
    ece_after:          float
    stress_pass:        bool
    improvement:        float     # ece_before - ece_after (positiv = besser)
    deployed:           bool
    rollback_available: bool
    model_hash:         str
    notes:              str

class DeterministicLearningOrchestrator:
    """
    Kontrollierter Lernzyklus. Kein unkontrolliertes Live-Lernen.
    Jedes Deployment ist auditierbar und rollback-faehig.
    """

    # Unveraenderliche Gates
    MIN_IMPROVEMENT_THRESHOLD = 0.005  # ECE muss um mind. 0.005 besser werden
    MAX_ECE_AFTER_TRAINING    = 0.05   # Absolute Schranke (Systemvertrag)
    REQUIRED_STRESS_PASS      = True   # Stress-Test MUSS bestanden werden

    def __init__(self, model_registry_path: Path, log_layer):
        self.registry_path = model_registry_path
        self.log           = log_layer
        self._active_model_hash: Optional[str] = None

    def run_cycle(
        self,
        new_model_params: Dict[str, Any],
        validation_data: Dict[str, Any],
        stress_test_fn,
        calibration_eval_fn,
        chunk_id: str,
    ) -> LearningCycleResult:
        """
        Vollstaendiger Lernzyklus. Wirft bei jedem Gate-Fail.
        Deployment nur wenn alle Gates bestanden.
        """
        cycle_id  = hashlib.sha256(
            f"{chunk_id}{datetime.utcnow().isoformat()}".encode()
        ).hexdigest()[:12]
        timestamp = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()

        # Schritt 2: Validierung
        ece_before = calibration_eval_fn(model="active",  data=validation_data)
        ece_after  = calibration_eval_fn(model="candidate", data=validation_data)

        # ECE-Gate: absoluter Schwellenwert
        if ece_after > self.MAX_ECE_AFTER_TRAINING:
            self.log.log_event(type="LEARNING_GATE_FAIL",
                               data={"reason": "ECE_ABOVE_HARD_LIMIT",
                                     "ece_after": ece_after, "cycle_id": cycle_id})
            raise RuntimeError(
                f"LEARNING_GATE_FAIL: ECE nach Training = {ece_after:.4f} > "
                f"{self.MAX_ECE_AFTER_TRAINING} (Hard Limit)"
            )

        # Schritt 3: Stress-Test
        stress_pass = stress_test_fn(model="candidate", data=validation_data)
        if not stress_pass and self.REQUIRED_STRESS_PASS:
            self.log.log_event(type="LEARNING_GATE_FAIL",
                               data={"reason": "STRESS_TEST_FAILED", "cycle_id": cycle_id})
            raise RuntimeError("LEARNING_GATE_FAIL: Stress-Test nicht bestanden")

        # Schritt 4: Verbesserungs-Check
        improvement = ece_before - ece_after
        if improvement < self.MIN_IMPROVEMENT_THRESHOLD:
            self.log.log_event(type="LEARNING_NO_DEPLOY",
                               data={"reason": "INSUFFICIENT_IMPROVEMENT",
                                     "improvement": improvement, "cycle_id": cycle_id})
            return LearningCycleResult(
                cycle_id=cycle_id, timestamp=timestamp,
                ece_before=ece_before, ece_after=ece_after,
                stress_pass=stress_pass, improvement=improvement,
                deployed=False, rollback_available=True,
                model_hash="CANDIDATE_NOT_DEPLOYED",
                notes=f"Nicht deployt: Verbesserung {improvement:.4f} < "
                      f"{self.MIN_IMPROVEMENT_THRESHOLD}",
            )

        # Schritt 5: Deployment (Rollback-faehig)
        new_model_hash = hashlib.sha256(
            json.dumps(new_model_params, sort_keys=True).encode()
        ).hexdigest()[:16]

        self._save_rollback_snapshot()
        self._deploy(new_model_params, new_model_hash)
        self._active_model_hash = new_model_hash

        self.log.log_event(type="LEARNING_DEPLOYED",
                           data={"model_hash": new_model_hash,
                                 "ece_improvement": improvement,
                                 "cycle_id": cycle_id})

        return LearningCycleResult(
            cycle_id=cycle_id, timestamp=timestamp,
            ece_before=ece_before, ece_after=ece_after,
            stress_pass=stress_pass, improvement=improvement,
            deployed=True, rollback_available=True,
            model_hash=new_model_hash,
            notes=f"Deployt mit ECE-Verbesserung {improvement:.4f}",
        )

    def rollback(self) -> bool:
        """Rollt auf letzte stabile Version zurueck."""
        snapshot = self._load_rollback_snapshot()
        if snapshot is None:
            self.log.log_event(type="ROLLBACK_FAILED",
                               data={"reason": "NO_SNAPSHOT_AVAILABLE"})
            return False
        self._deploy(snapshot["params"], snapshot["hash"])
        self.log.log_event(type="ROLLBACK_SUCCESS",
                           data={"restored_hash": snapshot["hash"]})
        return True

    def _save_rollback_snapshot(self):
        pass  # Implementierung: aktuellen Modell-State serialisieren

    def _load_rollback_snapshot(self) -> Optional[Dict]:
        return None  # Implementierung: Snapshot deserialisieren

    def _deploy(self, params: Dict, model_hash: str):
        pass  # Implementierung: Modell-Parameter austauschen
```

## SESSION 28: SIMULATION & STRATEGY LAB

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S17, S26, S27
**Zeit:** 90-110 min

### Scope

Weltklasse-Systeme haben ein vollstaendiges Simulations-Labor.
Ohne Simulation = keine institutionelle Reife.

    1. Monte Carlo Simulation
    2. Slippage Modeling
    3. Liquidity Impact Modeling
    4. Walk-Forward Validation
    5. Stress Test Engine

```python
# jarvis/simulation/strategy_lab.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import numpy as np
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import List, Dict, Callable, Optional

@dataclass
class MonteCarloResult:
    n_paths:             int
    mean_final_pnl:      float
    std_final_pnl:       float
    var_95:              float    # Value at Risk (95%)
    cvar_95:             float    # Conditional VaR (95%)
    max_drawdown_mean:   float
    max_drawdown_p95:    float
    win_rate:            float    # Anteil positiver Endwerte

@dataclass
class SlippageModel:
    base_slippage_pct:  float    # Basislevel in % (liquidem Markt)
    vol_multiplier:     float    # Vol-Abhaengigkeit
    size_impact:        float    # Groessen-Impact (Market-Impact-Modell)

@dataclass
class WalkForwardResult:
    n_windows:           int
    oos_sharpe_mean:     float    # Out-of-Sample Sharpe (Mittelwert)
    oos_sharpe_std:      float    # Stabilitaet
    oos_win_rate:        float    # Anteil positiver OOS-Fenster
    degradation_score:   float    # Wie stark verschlechtert sich OOS?

@dataclass
class StressTestResult:
    scenario:           str
    pnl_impact:         float    # PnL-Impact in %
    max_drawdown:       float
    recovery_periods:   int      # Bars bis zur Erholung
    survived:           bool     # True wenn Drawdown < Hard Limit


class StrategyLab:
    """
    Vollstaendiges Simulations-Labor. Pflicht vor jedem Deployment.
    """

    def monte_carlo(
        self,
        strategy_returns: List[float],
        n_paths:          int = 10_000,
        n_periods:        int = 252,
        seed:             int = 42,
    ) -> MonteCarloResult:
        """
        Monte Carlo Simulation via Bootstrap.
        Seed fix fuer Reproduzierbarkeit (Systemvertrag: deterministisch).
        """
        rng = np.random.RandomState(seed)
        arr = np.array(strategy_returns, dtype=float)
        if not np.all(np.isfinite(arr)):
            raise ValueError("Returns enthalten NaN/Inf")

        # Bootstrap: ziehe n_periods aus historischen Returns (mit Zuruecklegen)
        paths = rng.choice(arr, size=(n_paths, n_periods), replace=True)
        cum_returns = np.cumprod(1.0 + paths, axis=1)
        final_pnl   = cum_returns[:, -1] - 1.0

        # Drawdown pro Pfad
        running_max = np.maximum.accumulate(cum_returns, axis=1)
        drawdowns   = (running_max - cum_returns) / np.maximum(running_max, 1e-10)
        max_dd_per_path = drawdowns.max(axis=1)

        var_95  = float(np.percentile(final_pnl, 5))
        cvar_95 = float(np.mean(final_pnl[final_pnl <= var_95]))

        return MonteCarloResult(
            n_paths=n_paths,
            mean_final_pnl=float(np.mean(final_pnl)),
            std_final_pnl=float(np.std(final_pnl)),
            var_95=var_95,
            cvar_95=cvar_95,
            max_drawdown_mean=float(np.mean(max_dd_per_path)),
            max_drawdown_p95=float(np.percentile(max_dd_per_path, 95)),
            win_rate=float(np.mean(final_pnl > 0)),
        )

    def compute_slippage(
        self,
        model: SlippageModel,
        position_size_pct: float,
        current_volatility: float,
    ) -> float:
        """
        Slippage-Schaetzung: base + vol-Anteil + Size-Impact.
        Gibt Slippage in % zurueck.
        """
        if not np.isfinite(position_size_pct) or position_size_pct < 0:
            raise ValueError(f"Ungaeltige position_size_pct: {position_size_pct}")
        if not np.isfinite(current_volatility) or current_volatility < 0:
            raise ValueError(f"Ungaeltige Volatilitaet: {current_volatility}")

        vol_component  = model.vol_multiplier * current_volatility
        size_component = model.size_impact * position_size_pct
        total_slippage = model.base_slippage_pct + vol_component + size_component
        return float(max(total_slippage, 0.0))

    def walk_forward(
        self,
        returns: List[float],
        strategy_fn: Callable[[List[float]], List[float]],
        n_windows:   int = 10,
        train_pct:   float = 0.7,
        seed:        int = 42,
    ) -> WalkForwardResult:
        """
        Walk-Forward Validation: rollierendes Trainingsfenster.
        Misst OOS-Performance (Out-of-Sample).
        """
        arr = np.array(returns, dtype=float)
        if not np.all(np.isfinite(arr)):
            raise ValueError("Returns enthalten NaN/Inf")

        n_total    = len(arr)
        window_sz  = n_total // n_windows
        oos_sharpes: List[float] = []

        for i in range(n_windows):
            start   = i * window_sz
            split   = start + int(window_sz * train_pct)
            end     = start + window_sz

            if end > n_total:
                break

            train_r = arr[start:split].tolist()
            oos_r   = arr[split:end].tolist()

            try:
                strat_oos = strategy_fn(train_r)
                # Sharpe (annualisiert, vereinfacht)
                if len(strat_oos) > 1:
                    oos_arr = np.array(strat_oos)
                    sharpe  = (np.mean(oos_arr) / max(np.std(oos_arr), 1e-10)) * np.sqrt(252)
                else:
                    sharpe = 0.0
            except Exception:
                sharpe = -999.0  # Strategie-Fehler = schlechtester Sharpe

            oos_sharpes.append(float(sharpe))

        if not oos_sharpes:
            raise RuntimeError("Walk-Forward: keine gueltigen Fenster")

        oos_arr = np.array(oos_sharpes)
        degrad  = float(max(0.0, -np.mean(oos_arr)))

        return WalkForwardResult(
            n_windows=len(oos_sharpes),
            oos_sharpe_mean=float(np.mean(oos_arr)),
            oos_sharpe_std=float(np.std(oos_arr)),
            oos_win_rate=float(np.mean(oos_arr > 0)),
            degradation_score=degrad,
        )

    def stress_test(
        self,
        scenario_name:     str,
        scenario_returns:  List[float],
        strategy_fn:       Callable[[List[float]], List[float]],
        drawdown_limit:    float = 0.15,
    ) -> StressTestResult:
        """
        Stress-Test mit historischen oder synthetischen Krisen-Szenarien.
        """
        try:
            strat_returns = strategy_fn(scenario_returns)
        except Exception as e:
            return StressTestResult(
                scenario=scenario_name,
                pnl_impact=-1.0,
                max_drawdown=1.0,
                recovery_periods=-1,
                survived=False,
            )

        arr = np.array(strat_returns, dtype=float)
        if not np.all(np.isfinite(arr)):
            arr = np.zeros_like(arr)

        cum      = np.cumprod(1.0 + arr)
        run_max  = np.maximum.accumulate(cum)
        dd       = (run_max - cum) / np.maximum(run_max, 1e-10)
        max_dd   = float(np.max(dd))
        pnl      = float(cum[-1] - 1.0) if len(cum) > 0 else -1.0

        # Recovery-Perioden: wann ist cum wieder ueber letztem Peak?
        recovery = -1
        peak_val = float(run_max[-1])
        for idx in range(len(cum)):
            if float(cum[idx]) >= peak_val:
                recovery = idx
                break

        return StressTestResult(
            scenario=scenario_name,
            pnl_impact=pnl,
            max_drawdown=max_dd,
            recovery_periods=recovery,
            survived=max_dd < drawdown_limit,
        )
```

    "2008_FINANCIAL_CRISIS",      # Sep-Okt 2008
    "2020_COVID_CRASH",           # Maerz 2020
    "2010_FLASH_CRASH",           # Mai 2010
    "SYNTHETIC_VOL_SHOCK_3X",     # 3x normale Volatilitaet
    "SYNTHETIC_LIQUIDITY_CRISIS", # Spread 10x normal

## RESEARCH EXTENSIONS (STRATEGIE-FORSCHUNGSBEREICH — KEIN NEUER LAYER)

Diese Erweiterungen operieren innerhalb des bestehenden Strategy-Research-Domains (S26–S28).
Sie fuegen KEINEN neuen Architektur-Layer hinzu. Sie sind modulare Research-Werkzeuge.
Alle Outputs sind analytisch. Keine Execution. Keine Broker-Interaktion.

### SCENARIO SANDBOX ENGINE

**Datei:** `jarvis/research/scenario_sandbox.py`
**Attached to:** Strategy Research Domain (S26-S28)
**P0 Classification:** Pure Research. No order flow. No execution.

```python
# jarvis/research/scenario_sandbox.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, List, Optional
import numpy as np


@dataclass
class ScenarioConfig:
    # Konfiguration fuer ein Forschungs-Szenario.
    # Alle Parameter sind hypothetische Eingangsgroessen - keine echten Markt-Orders.
    scenario_id:        str
    scenario_type:      str   # "regime_shift", "vol_spike", "corr_shock",
                              # "confidence_shift", "ev_shift"
    magnitude:          float # Intensitaet des Szenarios [0, 1]
    duration_bars:      int   # Simulierte Dauer in Bars
    asset_scope:        List[str]  # Betroffene Assets


@dataclass
class ScenarioResult:
    # Ergebnis einer Szenario-Simulation.
    # Rein analytisch - kein echtes Portfolio betroffen.
    scenario_id:            str
    regime_impact:          str   # Erwartetes Regime unter Szenario
    confidence_delta:       float # Delta auf ConfidenceBundle.Q
    strategy_mode_shift:    str   # Erwarteter StrategyMode-Wechsel
    expected_vol_change:    float # Hypothetische Vol-Aenderung (%)
    portfolio_heat_change:  float # Simulated exposure change [-1, 1]
    ev_shift:               float # Expected Value Shift in Basispoints
    recovery_bars_estimate: int   # Geschaetzte Recovery-Zeit in Bars
    notes:                  str   # Analytische Erklaerung


class ScenarioSandboxEngine:
    """
    Scenario Sandbox: Simuliert Marktszenarien fuer Strategy-Research.
    ISOLIERT: Kein Zugriff auf echte Positionen. Kein Broker-Kontakt.
    Inputs kommen von RegimeState, VolatilityState (read-only snapshots).
    Outputs gehen NUR an Research-Layer und Visual Output.
    """

    SCENARIO_TYPES = [
        "regime_shift",      # Regime-Uebergang simulieren
        "vol_spike",         # Volatilitaets-Spike simulieren
        "corr_shock",        # Korrelations-Schock simulieren
        "confidence_shift",  # Konfidenz-Verschiebung modellieren
        "ev_shift",          # Expected-Value-Shift modellieren
    ]

    def simulate_regime_shift(
        self,
        from_regime: str,
        to_regime: str,
        current_confidence: float,
        magnitude: float = 0.5,
    ) -> ScenarioResult:
        """Simuliert Regime-Wechsel und berechnet analytische Auswirkungen."""
        if not np.isfinite(magnitude) or not (0.0 <= magnitude <= 1.0):
            raise ValueError(f"magnitude muss in [0,1] liegen: {magnitude}")

        confidence_delta = -magnitude * 0.4
        MODE_MAP = {
            "TRENDING": "MOMENTUM", "RANGING": "MEAN_REVERSION",
            "HIGH_VOL": "RISK_REDUCTION", "SHOCK": "DEFENSIVE",
            "UNKNOWN": "MINIMAL_EXPOSURE",
        }
        strategy_shift = MODE_MAP.get(to_regime, "MINIMAL_EXPOSURE")

        return ScenarioResult(
            scenario_id=f"REGIME_SHIFT_{from_regime}_TO_{to_regime}",
            regime_impact=to_regime,
            confidence_delta=float(np.clip(confidence_delta, -1.0, 0.0)),
            strategy_mode_shift=strategy_shift,
            expected_vol_change=magnitude * 0.3,
            portfolio_heat_change=-magnitude * 0.2,
            ev_shift=-magnitude * 50.0,
            recovery_bars_estimate=int(magnitude * 20),
            notes=f"Simulated shift {from_regime}->{to_regime}, magnitude={magnitude:.2f}",
        )

    def simulate_vol_spike(
        self,
        current_nvu: float,
        spike_factor: float = 3.0,
    ) -> ScenarioResult:
        """Simuliert Volatilitaets-Spike (NVU > 3.0 Szenario)."""
        if spike_factor < 1.0:
            raise ValueError("spike_factor muss >= 1.0 sein")

        simulated_nvu = current_nvu * spike_factor
        triggers_fm02 = simulated_nvu > 3.0

        return ScenarioResult(
            scenario_id=f"VOL_SPIKE_NVU_{simulated_nvu:.1f}",
            regime_impact="HIGH_VOL" if triggers_fm02 else "ELEVATED_VOL",
            confidence_delta=-0.3 if triggers_fm02 else -0.1,
            strategy_mode_shift="RISK_REDUCTION" if triggers_fm02 else "MEAN_REVERSION",
            expected_vol_change=(spike_factor - 1.0) * 100.0,
            portfolio_heat_change=-0.5 if triggers_fm02 else -0.15,
            ev_shift=-80.0 if triggers_fm02 else -20.0,
            recovery_bars_estimate=10 if triggers_fm02 else 3,
            notes=f"NVU spike from {current_nvu:.2f} to {simulated_nvu:.2f}. FM-02: {triggers_fm02}",
        )

    def simulate_correlation_shock(
        self,
        n_assets: int,
        shock_correlation: float = 0.90,
    ) -> ScenarioResult:
        """Simuliert Korrelations-Schock (alle Assets konvergieren)."""
        triggers_fm04 = shock_correlation > 0.85
        return ScenarioResult(
            scenario_id=f"CORR_SHOCK_{shock_correlation:.2f}",
            regime_impact="SHOCK",
            confidence_delta=-0.5 if triggers_fm04 else -0.2,
            strategy_mode_shift="DEFENSIVE",
            expected_vol_change=20.0 * shock_correlation,
            portfolio_heat_change=-shock_correlation * 0.6,
            ev_shift=-100.0 * shock_correlation,
            recovery_bars_estimate=int(20 * shock_correlation),
            notes=f"Correlation shock to {shock_correlation:.2f} across {n_assets} assets. FM-04: {triggers_fm04}",
        )
```

**Requirements:**
- R1: ScenarioSandboxEngine liest NUR read-only Snapshots von RegimeState, VolatilityState
- R2: Kein Output geht an echte Execution-Layer
- R3: ScenarioResult enthaelt keine Order-Felder, keine Broker-Referenzen
- R4: Alle Werte sind geclipt und finite

---

### SCENARIO SANDBOX — LIVE MODE ISOLATION CONSTRAINTS

When the system operates in `MODE_LIVE_ANALYTICAL` or `MODE_HYBRID`, the
`ScenarioSandboxEngine` must obey the following isolation rules without exception.

**ISOLATION RULES (ALL MODES, ENFORCED AT P6):**

```
RULE 1 — SNAPSHOT-ONLY STATE ACCESS
  ScenarioSandboxEngine must receive an immutable snapshot via ctrl.get_state().
  It must NEVER hold a live reference to GlobalSystemState.
  All scenario computations operate on the snapshot copy, not the live state.

RULE 2 — NO STATE MUTATION
  Sandbox must NEVER call ctrl.update() under any condition.
  Sandbox must NEVER write to:
    - GlobalState (mode, meta_uncertainty, ood_status, ...)
    - PortfolioState (positions, correlation_matrix, gross_exposure, ...)
    - StrategyState (active_strategy_id, weight_scalar, entry_active, ...)
    - RegimeState (regime, regime_confidence, regime_probs, ...)
    - VolatilityState (vol_spike_flag, nvu_normalized, realized_vol, ...)

RULE 3 — CLONED STRATEGY OBJECTS
  Any StrategyObject used inside a scenario must be a deep copy.
  The registry instance must never be passed directly.
  Sandbox scenarios may inspect StrategyObject fields but must not modify them.

RULE 4 — ScenarioResult RETURN ONLY
  ScenarioSandboxEngine returns only ScenarioResult objects.
  It must never return:
    - State references
    - Controller references
    - Modified StrategyObject instances
    - Live buffer references
    - Anything that could mutate downstream state

RULE 5 — NO LIVE FEED ACCESS
  Sandbox has no access to LiveDataProvider or the live candle buffer.
  Inputs come only from state snapshots and explicitly passed parameters.
  If a scenario needs current NVU, it reads from the VolatilityState snapshot.
```

**SAFE INVOCATION PATTERN:**

```python
# jarvis/research/sandbox_runner.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import copy
from jarvis.research.scenario_sandbox import ScenarioSandboxEngine, ScenarioResult
from jarvis.core.global_state import GlobalSystemStateController


def run_scenario_safely(
    engine: ScenarioSandboxEngine,
    scenario_type: str,
    ctrl: GlobalSystemStateController,
    strategy_registry_entry,   # StrategyObject from registry
    **kwargs,
) -> ScenarioResult:
    """
    Safe sandbox invocation. Enforces all isolation rules.
    - Takes immutable state snapshot
    - Deep copies StrategyObject before passing
    - Returns ScenarioResult only; never mutates state
    """
    # RULE 1: immutable snapshot
    state_snapshot = ctrl.get_state()   # returns immutable copy

    # RULE 3: deep copy of StrategyObject
    strategy_copy = copy.deepcopy(strategy_registry_entry)

    # RULE 2 enforcement: sandbox has no reference to ctrl
    if scenario_type == "regime_shift":
        return engine.simulate_regime_shift(
            from_regime=state_snapshot.regime,
            to_regime=kwargs["to_regime"],
            current_confidence=1.0 - state_snapshot.meta_uncertainty,
            magnitude=kwargs.get("magnitude", 0.5),
        )
    elif scenario_type == "vol_spike":
        return engine.simulate_vol_spike(
            current_nvu=kwargs["current_nvu"],
            spike_factor=kwargs.get("spike_factor", 3.0),
        )
    elif scenario_type == "corr_shock":
        return engine.simulate_correlation_shock(
            n_assets=kwargs.get("n_assets", 4),
            shock_correlation=kwargs.get("shock_correlation", 0.90),
        )
    else:
        raise ValueError(f"Unknown scenario_type: {scenario_type}")
    # ScenarioResult returned — never written to state (RULE 4)
```

**HARD VERIFICATION (CI CHECK):**

```python
# tests/governance/test_sandbox_isolation.py
import copy
from unittest.mock import MagicMock, patch
from jarvis.research.scenario_sandbox import ScenarioSandboxEngine
from jarvis.research.sandbox_runner import run_scenario_safely


def test_sandbox_does_not_call_ctrl_update():
    ctrl = MagicMock()
    engine = ScenarioSandboxEngine()
    # ctrl.get_state() returns frozen snapshot
    ctrl.get_state.return_value = MagicMock(
        regime="TRENDING", meta_uncertainty=0.2
    )
    strategy = MagicMock()

    result = run_scenario_safely(engine, "regime_shift", ctrl, strategy,
                                 to_regime="SHOCK", magnitude=0.7)

    ctrl.update.assert_not_called()   # MUST NOT mutate state
    assert result is not None         # Must return ScenarioResult


def test_sandbox_result_contains_no_state_reference():
    engine = ScenarioSandboxEngine()
    result = engine.simulate_vol_spike(current_nvu=1.5, spike_factor=2.5)
    # Result is a plain dataclass — no ctrl, no state reference
    assert not hasattr(result, "ctrl")
    assert not hasattr(result, "state")
    assert not hasattr(result, "strategy_registry")
```
