### STRATEGY BENCHMARK ENGINE

**Datei:** `jarvis/research/strategy_benchmark.py`
**Attached to:** Strategy Research Domain (S26-S28)
**P0 Classification:** Pure Research. Backtested comparison only. No execution.

```python
# jarvis/research/strategy_benchmark.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import List
import numpy as np


@dataclass
class BenchmarkResult:
    # Ergebnis eines Strategy-Benchmarks.
    # Alle Werte basieren auf historischen Simulationen - keine echten Trades.
    strategy_id:        str
    benchmark_name:     str
    sharpe_ratio:       float
    benchmark_sharpe:   float
    sharpe_delta:       float
    max_drawdown:       float
    benchmark_drawdown: float
    win_rate:           float
    calmar_ratio:       float
    outperformance_pct: float
    notes:              str


class StrategyBenchmarkEngine:
    """
    Strategy Benchmark Engine: Vergleicht Strategy-Outputs mit Baselines.
    NUR fuer Research und historische Analyse.
    Kein Live-Trading. Kein Execution. Rein analytisch.
    """

    BASELINES = [
        "buy_and_hold",   # Passives Buy-and-Hold
        "ma_crossover",   # Simple MA-Crossover Baseline
        "random_entry",   # Random Entry/Exit Baseline
        "vol_filter",     # Volatility-Filter Baseline
    ]

    def compute_sharpe(self, returns: np.ndarray, risk_free: float = 0.0) -> float:
        """Annualisierter Sharpe Ratio."""
        if len(returns) < 2:
            return 0.0
        excess = returns - risk_free / 252
        std = float(np.std(excess))
        if std < 1e-10:
            return 0.0
        return float(np.mean(excess) / std * np.sqrt(252))

    def compute_max_drawdown(self, returns: np.ndarray) -> float:
        """Maximum Drawdown aus Return-Serie."""
        cumulative = np.cumprod(1 + returns)
        rolling_max = np.maximum.accumulate(cumulative)
        drawdowns = (cumulative - rolling_max) / np.maximum(rolling_max, 1e-10)
        return float(np.min(drawdowns))

    def benchmark_vs_buy_and_hold(
        self,
        strategy_returns: np.ndarray,
        market_returns: np.ndarray,
        strategy_id: str,
    ) -> BenchmarkResult:
        """Vergleich mit Buy-and-Hold."""
        for name, arr in [("strategy_returns", strategy_returns), ("market_returns", market_returns)]:
            if not np.all(np.isfinite(arr)):
                raise ValueError(f"{name} enthalten NaN/Inf")

        s_sharpe  = self.compute_sharpe(strategy_returns)
        bh_sharpe = self.compute_sharpe(market_returns)
        s_dd      = self.compute_max_drawdown(strategy_returns)
        bh_dd     = self.compute_max_drawdown(market_returns)
        calmar    = float(abs(np.mean(strategy_returns) * 252) / max(abs(s_dd), 1e-6))

        return BenchmarkResult(
            strategy_id=strategy_id,
            benchmark_name="buy_and_hold",
            sharpe_ratio=s_sharpe,
            benchmark_sharpe=bh_sharpe,
            sharpe_delta=s_sharpe - bh_sharpe,
            max_drawdown=s_dd,
            benchmark_drawdown=bh_dd,
            win_rate=float(np.mean(strategy_returns > market_returns)),
            calmar_ratio=calmar,
            outperformance_pct=float(np.mean(strategy_returns > market_returns)) * 100.0,
            notes=f"Strategy {strategy_id} vs Buy-and-Hold. Sharpe delta: {s_sharpe - bh_sharpe:.3f}",
        )

    def benchmark_vs_ma_crossover(
        self,
        strategy_returns: np.ndarray,
        prices: np.ndarray,
        fast_period: int = 10,
        slow_period: int = 50,
        strategy_id: str = "STRATEGY",
    ) -> BenchmarkResult:
        """Vergleich mit MA-Crossover Baseline."""
        if len(prices) < slow_period:
            raise ValueError(f"Nicht genug Preisdaten fuer slow_period={slow_period}")

        fast_ma  = np.convolve(prices, np.ones(fast_period) / fast_period, mode='valid')
        slow_ma  = np.convolve(prices, np.ones(slow_period) / slow_period, mode='valid')
        min_len  = min(len(fast_ma), len(slow_ma))
        signals  = np.where(fast_ma[-min_len:] > slow_ma[-min_len:], 1.0, 0.0)
        p_rets   = np.diff(prices[-min_len-1:]) / np.maximum(prices[-min_len:-1], 1e-10)
        ma_rets  = signals[:len(p_rets)] * p_rets

        s_aligned = strategy_returns[-(len(ma_rets)):]
        s_sharpe  = self.compute_sharpe(s_aligned)
        ma_sharpe = self.compute_sharpe(ma_rets)
        s_dd      = self.compute_max_drawdown(s_aligned)
        ma_dd     = self.compute_max_drawdown(ma_rets)
        calmar    = float(abs(np.mean(s_aligned) * 252) / max(abs(s_dd), 1e-6))

        return BenchmarkResult(
            strategy_id=strategy_id,
            benchmark_name=f"ma_crossover_{fast_period}_{slow_period}",
            sharpe_ratio=s_sharpe,
            benchmark_sharpe=ma_sharpe,
            sharpe_delta=s_sharpe - ma_sharpe,
            max_drawdown=s_dd,
            benchmark_drawdown=ma_dd,
            win_rate=float(np.mean(s_aligned > ma_rets)),
            calmar_ratio=calmar,
            outperformance_pct=float(np.mean(s_aligned > ma_rets)) * 100.0,
            notes=f"Strategy vs MA({fast_period}/{slow_period}) crossover",
        )
```

**Requirements:**
- R1: Alle Inputs sind historische Return-Arrays — keine Live-Daten fuer Order-Generierung
- R2: BenchmarkResult enthaelt keine Order-Felder
- R3: Engine operiert vollstaendig auf gecachten historischen Daten
- R4: Outputs gehen NUR an Research-Layer und Visual Output (P9)
- R5: Kein Zugriff auf GlobalSystemStateController — rein statistische Berechnung

## PHASE 2 — META-VALIDATION AND OVERFITTING CONTROL (BLOCK B)

**Datei:** `jarvis/research/walk_forward_validation.py`
**Classification:** Research and backtesting only. Results may not override live state.
No execution semantics.

---

### WALK-FORWARD VALIDATION ENGINE

```python
# jarvis/research/walk_forward_validation.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import List, Dict, Optional
import numpy as np


# Governance constant — registered in 99_REFERENCE.md
WFV_MIN_OOS_RATIO = 0.30   # Minimum out-of-sample fraction (30%)
WFV_MIN_SEGMENTS  = 3      # Minimum number of walk-forward segments
WFV_MIN_IS_BARS   = 100    # Minimum in-sample bars per segment


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class WalkForwardSegment:
    """Single in-sample / out-of-sample segment."""
    segment_id:    int
    is_start:      int    # In-sample bar index start
    is_end:        int    # In-sample bar index end (exclusive)
    oos_start:     int    # Out-of-sample bar index start
    oos_end:       int    # Out-of-sample bar index end (exclusive)
    is_sharpe:     float  # In-sample Sharpe ratio
    oos_sharpe:    float  # Out-of-sample Sharpe ratio
    oos_ratio:     float  # OOS bars / Total bars — must >= WFV_MIN_OOS_RATIO


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class WalkForwardResult:
    """
    Aggregated walk-forward validation result for a strategy.
    Frozen — sandbox results cannot override StabilityScore.

    HARD FAILURE CONDITION:
      If any segment has oos_ratio < WFV_MIN_OOS_RATIO: wfv_passed = False
      Strategy may not be registered if wfv_passed = False.
    """
    strategy_id:    str
    n_segments:     int
    segments:       tuple                # Tuple[WalkForwardSegment]
    mean_oos_sharpe: float
    std_oos_sharpe:  float
    stability_score: float               # See StabilityScore definition
    wfv_passed:     bool                 # False = hard failure
    failure_reason: Optional[str]        # Non-None if wfv_passed = False


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class StabilityScore:
    """
    Measures performance variance across walk-forward segments.
    High variance = lower score. Penalizes strategies with inconsistent OOS performance.

    FORMULA:
      stability_score = max(0, 1 - (std_oos_sharpe / max(abs(mean_oos_sharpe), 0.01)))
      Clipped to [0, 1].

    GOVERNANCE: Sandbox results cannot override this score.
    StrategyRegistry stores stability_score per strategy.
    """
    strategy_id:     str
    mean_oos_sharpe: float
    std_oos_sharpe:  float
    stability_score: float   # [0, 1] — 1 = perfectly stable, 0 = completely inconsistent
    penalty_applied: bool    # True if std_oos_sharpe > mean_oos_sharpe


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class CrossAssetRobustnessScore:
    """
    Measures strategy performance across asset classes.
    Strategy must demonstrate positive OOS Sharpe in >= 2 asset classes.
    Otherwise: penalty_multiplier < 1.0 applied to weight posterior.

    GOVERNANCE: penalty_multiplier only reduces Weight_Model input.
    It does NOT liquidate or modify any simulated position.
    """
    strategy_id:         str
    asset_classes_tested: tuple          # Tuple[str] — e.g. ("crypto", "forex")
    oos_sharpe_by_class:  tuple          # Tuple[Tuple[str, float]]
    classes_positive:     int            # Count with OOS Sharpe > 0
    robustness_passed:   bool           # classes_positive >= 2
    penalty_multiplier:  float          # 1.0 if passed; < 1.0 if failed


class WalkForwardValidationEngine:
    """
    Walk-forward validation with OOS enforcement and stability scoring.
    All computation is deterministic. No random segment generation.
    """

    def validate(
        self,
        strategy_id: str,
        returns: np.ndarray,     # Full return series (historical)
        n_segments: int = 5,
    ) -> WalkForwardResult:
        """
        Segment returns into IS/OOS windows. Validate OOS ratio. Compute stability.
        Raises ValueError if n_segments < WFV_MIN_SEGMENTS.
        """
        if n_segments < WFV_MIN_SEGMENTS:
            raise ValueError(f"n_segments ({n_segments}) < WFV_MIN_SEGMENTS ({WFV_MIN_SEGMENTS})")
        if len(returns) < n_segments * WFV_MIN_IS_BARS * 2:
            raise ValueError(
                f"Insufficient data: {len(returns)} bars for {n_segments} segments. "
                f"Need >= {n_segments * WFV_MIN_IS_BARS * 2} bars."
            )

        n = len(returns)
        seg_size = n // n_segments
        oos_size = max(1, int(seg_size * WFV_MIN_OOS_RATIO))
        is_size  = seg_size - oos_size

        segments = []
        for k in range(n_segments):
            start = k * seg_size
            is_e  = start + is_size
            oos_s = is_e
            oos_e = min(start + seg_size, n)

            is_ret  = returns[start:is_e]
            oos_ret = returns[oos_s:oos_e]
            oos_ratio = len(oos_ret) / max(len(is_ret) + len(oos_ret), 1)

            is_sharpe  = self._sharpe(is_ret)
            oos_sharpe = self._sharpe(oos_ret)

            segments.append(WalkForwardSegment(
                segment_id=k, is_start=start, is_end=is_e,
                oos_start=oos_s, oos_end=oos_e,
                is_sharpe=is_sharpe, oos_sharpe=oos_sharpe,
                oos_ratio=oos_ratio,
            ))

        # Hard failure check
        failed_segs = [s for s in segments if s.oos_ratio < WFV_MIN_OOS_RATIO]
        wfv_passed = len(failed_segs) == 0
        failure_reason = None
        if not wfv_passed:
            failure_reason = (
                f"{len(failed_segs)} segment(s) with OOS ratio < {WFV_MIN_OOS_RATIO}. "
                f"Strategy may not be registered."
            )

        oos_sharpes = [s.oos_sharpe for s in segments]
        mean_s = float(np.mean(oos_sharpes))
        std_s  = float(np.std(oos_sharpes))
        stab   = float(np.clip(1.0 - std_s / max(abs(mean_s), 0.01), 0.0, 1.0))

        return WalkForwardResult(
            strategy_id=strategy_id,
            n_segments=n_segments,
            segments=tuple(segments),
            mean_oos_sharpe=mean_s,
            std_oos_sharpe=std_s,
            stability_score=stab,
            wfv_passed=wfv_passed,
            failure_reason=failure_reason,
        )

    def cross_asset_robustness(
        self,
        strategy_id: str,
        returns_by_class: Dict[str, np.ndarray],
    ) -> CrossAssetRobustnessScore:
        """
        Compute OOS Sharpe per asset class. Count classes with positive Sharpe.
        Penalty multiplier: 1.0 if >= 2 classes positive, else 0.5.
        """
        sharpes = []
        for cls, ret in returns_by_class.items():
            s = self._sharpe(ret)
            sharpes.append((cls, s))

        classes_positive = sum(1 for _, s in sharpes if s > 0.0)
        robustness_passed = classes_positive >= 2
        penalty = 1.0 if robustness_passed else 0.5

        return CrossAssetRobustnessScore(
            strategy_id=strategy_id,
            asset_classes_tested=tuple(cls for cls, _ in sharpes),
            oos_sharpe_by_class=tuple(sharpes),
            classes_positive=classes_positive,
            robustness_passed=robustness_passed,
            penalty_multiplier=penalty,
        )

    def _sharpe(self, returns: np.ndarray, risk_free: float = 0.0) -> float:
        if len(returns) < 2:
            return 0.0
        excess = returns - risk_free / 252
        std = float(np.std(excess))
        if std < 1e-10:
            return 0.0
        return float(np.mean(excess) / std * np.sqrt(252))
```

### OVERFITTING DETECTION RULES

```python
# jarvis/research/overfitting_detector.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
from dataclasses import dataclass
import numpy as np


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class OverfittingReport:
    """
    Overfitting detection result for a strategy.
    Frozen. Stored in StrategyRegistry as metadata.
    """
    strategy_id:        str
    performance_spike:  bool     # IS Sharpe > 3x OOS Sharpe
    param_sensitivity:  bool     # See parameter sensitivity check
    overfitting_flag:   bool     # True if either check triggers
    is_to_oos_ratio:    float    # IS Sharpe / OOS Sharpe (< 3 preferred)
    sensitivity_score:  float    # Lower = less sensitive to parameter changes


PERFORMANCE_SPIKE_THRESHOLD = 3.0   # IS/OOS Sharpe ratio threshold


def detect_overfitting(
    strategy_id: str,
    is_sharpe: float,
    oos_sharpe: float,
    param_sensitivity_score: float,
) -> OverfittingReport:
    """
    Check 1 — Performance Spike: IS Sharpe > 3x OOS Sharpe
    Check 2 — Parameter Sensitivity: sensitivity_score > 0.5
    """
    oos_safe = oos_sharpe if abs(oos_sharpe) > 1e-6 else 1e-6
    is_oos_ratio = abs(is_sharpe) / abs(oos_safe)

    performance_spike = is_oos_ratio > PERFORMANCE_SPIKE_THRESHOLD
    param_sensitive   = param_sensitivity_score > 0.5

    return OverfittingReport(
        strategy_id=strategy_id,
        performance_spike=performance_spike,
        param_sensitivity=param_sensitive,
        overfitting_flag=performance_spike or param_sensitive,
        is_to_oos_ratio=float(is_oos_ratio),
        sensitivity_score=float(np.clip(param_sensitivity_score, 0.0, 1.0)),
    )
```

**REGISTRY GOVERNANCE — ROBUSTNESS METADATA:**
```
StrategyRegistry must store the following metadata per registered strategy:
  - WalkForwardResult (or None if not validated)
  - StabilityScore
  - CrossAssetRobustnessScore
  - OverfittingReport

Registration BLOCKED if:
  - WalkForwardResult.wfv_passed = False
  - OverfittingReport.overfitting_flag = True
  - CrossAssetRobustnessScore.classes_positive < 1

Sandbox results (ScenarioSandboxEngine) CANNOT override StabilityScore.
Stability and robustness scores are computed by WalkForwardValidationEngine only.
```

## PHASE 3 — SIGNAL FRAGILITY ANALYZER (BLOCK F)

**Insertion point:** After PHASE 2 — META-VALIDATION AND OVERFITTING CONTROL (BLOCK B), end of file.
**Governed by:** P0 — ANALYSIS AND STRATEGY RESEARCH TOOL. No execution, no broker integration.

### SIGNAL FRAGILITY ANALYZER

```python
# jarvis/strategy/signal_fragility_analyzer.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
# Phase 3 addition — Decision Quality Maximization
# GOVERNANCE: Output feeds ONLY DecisionQualityEngine (read-only).
# May NOT modify StrategyObject. No live feed access.
# Deterministic local perturbation analysis only.

from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Callable, Dict, Any
import numpy as np


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class SignalFragilityResult:
    """
    Frozen output of SignalFragilityAnalyzer.
    All scores are deterministically derived from snapshot inputs
    using small, fixed delta perturbation analysis.

    No Monte Carlo. No random sampling. No stochastic components.
    """
    parameter_sensitivity_score: float
    # [0.0, 1.0] — normalized gradient magnitude of signal output
    # with respect to key strategy parameters (e.g., lookback window,
    # threshold values). High value = signal is highly sensitive to
    # parameter choices; small parameter changes produce large signal shifts.

    volatility_sensitivity_score: float
    # [0.0, 1.0] — normalized signal change when NVU-normalized volatility
    # is perturbed by ±FRAGILITY_VOL_DELTA (5% of current value, min 0.01).
    # High value = signal is fragile under volatility regime shift.

    spread_sensitivity_score: float
    # [0.0, 1.0] — normalized signal change when bid-ask spread proxy
    # is perturbed by ±FRAGILITY_SPREAD_DELTA (5% of current value, min 0.0001).
    # High value = signal degrades significantly under spread widening.

    correlation_sensitivity_score: float
    # [0.0, 1.0] — normalized signal change when cross-asset correlation
    # coefficient is perturbed by ±FRAGILITY_CORR_DELTA (0.05 absolute).
    # High value = signal assumption breaks under mild correlation shifts.

    fragility_index: float
    # Composite fragility score in [0.0, 1.0].
    # Weighted average of the four sensitivity scores.
    # >= FRAGILITY_HIGH_THRESHOLD (0.65) → classified HIGH FRAGILITY.
    # This classification propagates to DecisionQualityBundle.signal_fragility_score.


class SignalFragilityAnalyzer:
    """
    Deterministic local perturbation analysis of a strategy signal.

    Evaluates how sensitive the strategy's signal output is to small,
    fixed-delta perturbations of key input dimensions:
      - Strategy parameters
      - Realized volatility
      - Bid-ask spread proxy
      - Cross-asset correlation

    GOVERNANCE CONSTRAINTS:
      - DETERMINISTIC: no random seeds, no Monte Carlo, no stochastic sampling.
      - SNAPSHOT-ONLY: all inputs are passed as frozen values; no live buffer reads.
      - NO STATE MUTATION: never calls ctrl.update().
      - NO StrategyObject MODIFICATION: analyzer is purely read-side.
      - OUTPUT ROUTING: SignalFragilityResult is consumed ONLY by
        DecisionQualityEngine. No other layer may route this output.
      - PERTURBATION DELTAS: fixed, small, deterministic. Listed in constants below.
      - FORBIDDEN: Monte Carlo, random sampling, live feed access,
        execution semantics, broker concepts, StrategyObject writes.

    BUDGET: max 30 ms per evaluation (see 40_RISK_ENGINE_SPECS.md
      Phase 3 Performance and Safety Constraints).
    """

    # Perturbation magnitudes — deterministic, fixed
    FRAGILITY_VOL_DELTA: float      = 0.05    # 5% relative of current vol, min 0.01
    FRAGILITY_SPREAD_DELTA: float   = 0.05    # 5% relative of current spread, min 0.0001
    FRAGILITY_CORR_DELTA: float     = 0.05    # 0.05 absolute on correlation coefficient
    FRAGILITY_PARAM_DELTA: float    = 0.01    # 1% relative of each parameter value

    # Composite weights (must sum to 1.0)
    W_PARAM:  float = 0.30
    W_VOL:    float = 0.30
    W_SPREAD: float = 0.20
    W_CORR:   float = 0.20

    # Phase 3 constant — registered in 99_REFERENCE.md
    FRAGILITY_HIGH_THRESHOLD: float = 0.65    # mirrors FRAGILITY_HIGH_THRESHOLD

    def _safe_delta(self, base: float, relative: float, minimum: float) -> float:
        """Compute safe perturbation delta — deterministic, no randomness."""
        return max(abs(base) * relative, minimum)

    def _normalized_sensitivity(
        self,
        signal_fn: Callable[..., float],
        base_kwargs: Dict[str, Any],
        perturb_key: str,
        delta: float,
    ) -> float:
        """
        Compute normalized finite-difference sensitivity for one input dimension.

        s = |f(x + delta) - f(x - delta)| / (2 * delta)
        Normalized to [0.0, 1.0] by clipping to [0.0, 1.0].
        """
        base_val = base_kwargs[perturb_key]

        kwargs_plus  = {**base_kwargs, perturb_key: base_val + delta}
        kwargs_minus = {**base_kwargs, perturb_key: base_val - delta}

        f_plus  = float(signal_fn(**kwargs_plus))
        f_minus = float(signal_fn(**kwargs_minus))

        raw_sensitivity = abs(f_plus - f_minus) / (2.0 * max(delta, 1e-12))
        return float(np.clip(raw_sensitivity, 0.0, 1.0))

    def compute(
        self,
        signal_fn: Callable[..., float],
        # Callable representing the strategy signal computation.
        # Must accept keyword arguments matching base_kwargs keys.
        # Must return a single float in [0.0, 1.0] (signal strength).
        # Passed from snapshot — not a live reference.

        base_volatility: float,
        # Current NVU-normalized volatility (snapshot value). Must be > 0.

        base_spread: float,
        # Current bid-ask spread proxy (snapshot value). Must be >= 0.

        base_correlation: float,
        # Current cross-asset correlation coefficient (snapshot value).
        # Expected range: [-1.0, 1.0].

        strategy_params: Dict[str, float],
        # Snapshot of key strategy parameters (e.g., {"lookback": 20.0,
        # "threshold": 0.015}). Values must be finite floats.
    ) -> SignalFragilityResult:
        """
        Perform deterministic local perturbation analysis across four dimensions.

        Each sensitivity score is computed via central finite differences.
        fragility_index is the weighted average of the four scores.

        Returns:
            SignalFragilityResult (frozen, deterministic).

        Raises:
            ValueError: if base_volatility <= 0, or strategy_params is empty.
        """
        if base_volatility <= 0.0:
            raise ValueError(
                f"base_volatility must be > 0. Got {base_volatility}"
            )
        if not strategy_params:
            raise ValueError("strategy_params must contain at least one parameter.")

        # ── Volatility sensitivity ────────────────────────────────────────
        vol_delta = self._safe_delta(base_volatility, self.FRAGILITY_VOL_DELTA, 0.01)
        base_vol_kwargs = {"volatility": base_volatility}
        vol_score = self._normalized_sensitivity(
            signal_fn=lambda volatility, **_: signal_fn(
                volatility=volatility,
                spread=base_spread,
                correlation=base_correlation,
                **strategy_params,
            ),
            base_kwargs={"volatility": base_volatility},
            perturb_key="volatility",
            delta=vol_delta,
        )

        # ── Spread sensitivity ────────────────────────────────────────────
        spread_delta = self._safe_delta(base_spread, self.FRAGILITY_SPREAD_DELTA, 0.0001)
        spread_score = self._normalized_sensitivity(
            signal_fn=lambda spread, **_: signal_fn(
                volatility=base_volatility,
                spread=spread,
                correlation=base_correlation,
                **strategy_params,
            ),
            base_kwargs={"spread": base_spread},
            perturb_key="spread",
            delta=spread_delta,
        )

        # ── Correlation sensitivity ───────────────────────────────────────
        corr_score = self._normalized_sensitivity(
            signal_fn=lambda correlation, **_: signal_fn(
                volatility=base_volatility,
                spread=base_spread,
                correlation=correlation,
                **strategy_params,
            ),
            base_kwargs={"correlation": base_correlation},
            perturb_key="correlation",
            delta=self.FRAGILITY_CORR_DELTA,
        )

        # ── Parameter sensitivity (mean over all params) ──────────────────
        param_scores = []
        for param_name, param_value in strategy_params.items():
            p_delta = self._safe_delta(param_value, self.FRAGILITY_PARAM_DELTA, 1e-6)
            merged_params_plus  = {**strategy_params, param_name: param_value + p_delta}
            merged_params_minus = {**strategy_params, param_name: param_value - p_delta}

            f_plus  = float(np.clip(signal_fn(
                volatility=base_volatility,
                spread=base_spread,
                correlation=base_correlation,
                **merged_params_plus,
            ), 0.0, 1.0))
            f_minus = float(np.clip(signal_fn(
                volatility=base_volatility,
                spread=base_spread,
                correlation=base_correlation,
                **merged_params_minus,
            ), 0.0, 1.0))

            raw = abs(f_plus - f_minus) / (2.0 * max(p_delta, 1e-12))
            param_scores.append(float(np.clip(raw, 0.0, 1.0)))

        param_score = float(np.mean(param_scores)) if param_scores else 0.0

        # ── Composite fragility index ─────────────────────────────────────
        fragility = float(np.clip(
            self.W_PARAM  * param_score  +
            self.W_VOL    * vol_score    +
            self.W_SPREAD * spread_score +
            self.W_CORR   * corr_score,
            0.0, 1.0
        ))

        return SignalFragilityResult(
            parameter_sensitivity_score=param_score,
            volatility_sensitivity_score=vol_score,
            spread_sensitivity_score=spread_score,
            correlation_sensitivity_score=corr_score,
            fragility_index=fragility,
        )
```

**GOVERNANCE:**
```
SignalFragilityAnalyzer output (SignalFragilityResult) may ONLY:
  1. Feed DecisionQualityEngine.signal_fragility_score computation (read-only).

SignalFragilityAnalyzer may NOT:
  - Modify StrategyObject in any way
  - Call ctrl.update()
  - Access live market data buffers
  - Use random number generation or Monte Carlo simulation
  - Call broker or execution abstractions

PERTURBATION ANALYSIS CONSTRAINTS:
  All deltas are deterministic and fixed per evaluation.
  Central finite differences only (no forward-difference, no adaptive stepping).
  signal_fn is treated as a pure function: same inputs → same output.
  No caching of intermediate results across calls.

COMPUTATIONAL BUDGET:
  FragilityAnalyzer budget max 30 ms per evaluation.
  No recursive recalculation.
  No cascading re-scoring.
  See 40_RISK_ENGINE_SPECS.md Phase 3 Performance and Safety Constraints.

DETERMINISM GUARANTEE:
  Given identical (signal_fn, base_volatility, base_spread,
  base_correlation, strategy_params), SignalFragilityResult is
  bit-for-bit identical across invocations and operating modes.
```

## SESSION 29: CAPITAL ALLOCATION ENGINE

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S17 (Risk Engine), S26 (Adaptive Strategy), S28 (Simulation Lab)
**Zeit:** 80-100 min
**Datei:** jarvis/risk/capital_allocation.py

### Prinzip

System optimiert KAPITAL, nicht Trades.
Kein Kelly-Einsatz ohne Risk-Engine-Freigabe.
Portfolio-Ebene: Volatility Targeting + Cross-Strategy Korrelation.

### CAPITAL ALLOCATION ENGINE FORMALISIERUNG

#### Portfolio Volatility Targeting Formula

```python
# Volatility Targeting mathematische Definition:
#
# Ziel: Konstantes Portfolio-Risiko unabhaengig von Marktvolatilitaet
#
# position_size = (target_vol / realized_vol) * base_position
#
# wobei:
#   target_vol = Ziel-Portfolio-Volatilitaet (z.B. 15% annualisiert)
#   realized_vol = Aktuelle realisierte Volatilitaet (z.B. aus EWMA)
#   base_position = Basispositionsgroesse (z.B. 100% Kapital)
#
# Risk Parity Erweiterung fuer Multi-Strategy:
#   weight_i = (1 / vol_i) / sum_j(1 / vol_j)
#
# wobei vol_i = Volatilitaet von Strategie i

class VolatilityTargeting:
    """
    Volatility Targeting Engine fuer konstantes Portfolio-Risiko.
    """
    
    TARGET_VOL_ANNUAL = 0.15  # 15% annualisiert
    MIN_VOL_FLOOR = 0.05      # Minimum 5% (verhindert Over-Leverage)
    MAX_VOL_CAP = 0.50        # Maximum 50% (verhindert Under-Leverage)
    
    def compute_vol_scaled_position(
        self,
        target_vol: float,
        realized_vol: float,
        base_position: float = 1.0
    ) -> float:
        """
        Berechnet volatilitaets-skalierte Positionsgroesse.
        
        Formula: position = (target_vol / realized_vol) * base_position
        
        Args:
            target_vol: Ziel-Volatilitaet (annualisiert)
            realized_vol: Realisierte Volatilitaet (annualisiert)
            base_position: Basispositionsgroesse
        
        Returns:
            Skalierte Positionsgroesse in [0, max_leverage]
        """
        # Clip realized_vol to reasonable range
        realized_vol = np.clip(realized_vol, self.MIN_VOL_FLOOR, self.MAX_VOL_CAP)
        
        # Vol scaling factor
        vol_scalar = target_vol / realized_vol
        
        # Apply to base position
        scaled_position = base_position * vol_scalar
        
        # Clip to reasonable leverage (max 3x)
        scaled_position = np.clip(scaled_position, 0.0, 3.0)
        
        return float(scaled_position)
```

#### Risk Budget Allocation Mathematics

```python
class RiskBudgetAllocator:
    """
    Risk Budgeting: Allokiert Kapital basierend auf Risikobeitraegen.
    
    Mathematik:
      RC_i = w_i * Cov(R_i, R_p) / sigma_p
      
      wobei:
        RC_i = Risk Contribution von Asset i
        w_i = Gewicht von Asset i
        Cov(R_i, R_p) = Covariance zwischen Asset i und Portfolio
        sigma_p = Portfolio-Volatilitaet
      
    Ziel: RC_i = budget_i fuer alle i (Equal Risk Contribution oder gewichtet)
    """
    
    def compute_risk_contributions(
        self,
        weights: np.ndarray,
        cov_matrix: np.ndarray
    ) -> np.ndarray:
        """
        Berechnet Risk Contributions jedes Assets.
        
        Args:
            weights: (N,) Portfolio-Gewichte
            cov_matrix: (N, N) Kovarianzmatrix
        
        Returns:
            (N,) Risk Contributions
        """
        # Portfolio variance
        portfolio_var = weights @ cov_matrix @ weights
        portfolio_vol = np.sqrt(max(portfolio_var, 1e-10))
        
        # Marginal Risk Contributions
        marginal_rc = cov_matrix @ weights / max(portfolio_vol, 1e-10)
        
        # Risk Contributions
        risk_contributions = weights * marginal_rc
        
        return risk_contributions
    
    def optimize_equal_risk_contribution(
        self,
        cov_matrix: np.ndarray,
        initial_weights: Optional[np.ndarray] = None
    ) -> np.ndarray:
        """
        Optimiert Gewichte fuer Equal Risk Contribution.
        
        Loest:
          minimize sum((RC_i - RC_target)^2)
          subject to: sum(w_i) = 1, w_i >= 0
        
        Returns:
            Optimale Gewichte
        """
        from scipy.optimize import minimize
        
        n_assets = cov_matrix.shape[0]
        
        if initial_weights is None:
            # Start with equal weights
            initial_weights = np.ones(n_assets) / n_assets
        
        def objective(weights):
            rc = self.compute_risk_contributions(weights, cov_matrix)
            target_rc = np.mean(rc)
            return np.sum((rc - target_rc) ** 2)
        
        # Constraints
        constraints = [
            {'type': 'eq', 'fun': lambda w: np.sum(w) - 1.0}  # Sum to 1
        ]
        
        # Bounds
        bounds = [(0.0, 1.0) for _ in range(n_assets)]
        
        # Optimize
        result = minimize(
            objective,
            initial_weights,
            method='SLSQP',
            bounds=bounds,
            constraints=constraints
        )
        
        return result.x
```

#### Kelly-Adjusted Cap

```python
class KellyCriterion:
    """
    Kelly Criterion mit Adjustments fuer praktische Anwendung.
    
    Full Kelly: f* = (p*b - q) / b
      wobei:
        p = Gewinnwahrscheinlichkeit
        q = 1 - p
        b = avg_win / avg_loss (Gewinn-Verlust-Verhaeltnis)
    
    Adjustments:
      - Quarter Kelly: f_adj = f* / 4 (konservativ)
      - Confidence-Scaled: f_adj = f* * confidence
      - Drawdown-Adjusted: f_adj = f* * (1 - current_dd / max_dd)
    """
    
    MAX_KELLY_FRACTION = 0.25  # Quarter Kelly
    
    def compute_kelly_fraction(
        self,
        win_rate: float,
        avg_win: float,
        avg_loss: float,
        confidence: float = 1.0,
        current_drawdown: float = 0.0,
        max_drawdown: float = 0.15
    ) -> float:
        """
        Berechnet Kelly-Fraction mit Adjustments.
        
        Args:
            win_rate: Gewinnwahrscheinlichkeit [0, 1]
            avg_win: Durchschnittlicher Gewinn
            avg_loss: Durchschnittlicher Verlust (positiv)
            confidence: Confidence-Faktor [0, 1]
            current_drawdown: Aktueller Drawdown [0, 1]
            max_drawdown: Maximaler erlaubter Drawdown
        
        Returns:
            Kelly-Fraction [0, MAX_KELLY_FRACTION]
        """
        # Input validation
        if not (0.0 <= win_rate <= 1.0):
            raise ValueError(f"win_rate must be in [0, 1]: {win_rate}")
        if avg_loss <= 0:
            raise ValueError(f"avg_loss must be > 0: {avg_loss}")
        if not (0.0 < confidence <= 1.0):
            raise ValueError(f"confidence must be in (0, 1]: {confidence}")
        
        # Kelly formula
        b = avg_win / avg_loss
        p = win_rate
        q = 1.0 - p
        
        # Full Kelly
        kelly_full = (p * b - q) / max(b, 1e-10)
        
        # Quarter Kelly (conservative)
        kelly_quarter = kelly_full / 4.0
        
        # Confidence adjustment
        kelly_conf = kelly_quarter * confidence
        
        # Drawdown adjustment
        dd_factor = 1.0 - (current_drawdown / max(max_drawdown, 1e-10))
        dd_factor = np.clip(dd_factor, 0.0, 1.0)
        kelly_dd = kelly_conf * dd_factor
        
        # Cap to MAX_KELLY_FRACTION
        kelly_final = np.clip(kelly_dd, 0.0, self.MAX_KELLY_FRACTION)
        
        return float(kelly_final)
```

#### Exposure Limit Definitions

```python
class ExposureLimits:
    """
    Definiert Exposure-Limits auf verschiedenen Ebenen.
    """
    
    # Einzelposition
    MAX_SINGLE_POSITION = 0.20      # 20% des Portfolios
    
    # Strategie-Ebene
    MAX_STRATEGY_EXPOSURE = 0.40    # 40% pro Strategie
    
    # Portfolio-Ebene
    MAX_GROSS_EXPOSURE = 0.80       # 80% Brutto-Exposure
    MAX_NET_EXPOSURE = 0.60         # 60% Netto-Exposure
    MAX_LEVERAGE = 3.0              # 3x Leverage maximum
    
    # Asset-Klasse
    MAX_CRYPTO_EXPOSURE = 0.70      # 70% in Crypto
    MAX_SINGLE_ASSET = 0.30         # 30% in einzelnem Asset
    
    # Korrelation
    MAX_CORRELATION_BUCKET = 0.50   # Max 50% in hochkorrelierten Assets (corr > 0.7)
    
    def check_exposure_limits(
        self,
        positions: Dict[str, float],
        correlations: np.ndarray
    ) -> Dict[str, bool]:
        """
        Prueft alle Exposure-Limits.
        
        Returns:
            Dict mit Limit-Namen und Pass/Fail Status
        """
        checks = {}
        
        # Einzelpositionen
        max_pos = max(positions.values()) if positions else 0.0
        checks['single_position'] = max_pos <= self.MAX_SINGLE_POSITION
        
        # Brutto-Exposure
        gross_exposure = sum(abs(w) for w in positions.values())
        checks['gross_exposure'] = gross_exposure <= self.MAX_GROSS_EXPOSURE
        
        # Netto-Exposure
        net_exposure = abs(sum(positions.values()))
        checks['net_exposure'] = net_exposure <= self.MAX_NET_EXPOSURE
        
        # Korrelation-Buckets
        # (Vereinfachte Implementierung - in Praxis komplexer)
        checks['correlation_bucket'] = True
        
        return checks
```

---

```python
# jarvis/risk/capital_allocation.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import numpy as np
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, List, Optional

@dataclass
class AllocationResult:
    """Capital Allocation Output fuer alle Strategien/Positionen."""
    kelly_fraction:        float   # Kelly-optimale Groesse [0, MAX_KELLY]
    risk_budget_fraction:  float   # Risiko-Budget-Anteil [0, 1]
    vol_target_fraction:   float   # Volatility-targeting Groesse [0, 1]
    final_allocation:      float   # Endgueltige Allokation [0, MAX_ALLOCATION]
    exposure_cap_applied:  bool    # True wenn Exposure Cap aktiv
    reason:                str     # Erklaerung der Allokation


@dataclass
class PortfolioAllocation:
    """Portfolio-weite Allokations-Entscheidung."""
    allocations:           Dict[str, AllocationResult]  # Strategy-ID -> Allokation
    total_gross_exposure:  float   # Gesamt-Brutto-Exposure [0, 1]
    portfolio_vol_est:     float   # Geschaetzte Portfolio-Volatilitaet
    vol_target_met:        bool    # True wenn Volatility-Target erfuellt
    rebalance_required:    bool    # True wenn Rebalancing noetig


class CapitalAllocationEngine:
    """
    Portfolio-Level Capital Allocation.
    Optimiert Kapital-Allokation, nicht einzelne Trades.
    Risk Engine muss immer zuerst konsultiert werden.
    """

    # Immutable Limits (Hash-gesichert)
    MAX_KELLY_FRACTION    = 0.25   # Max Kelly-Anteil (Quartus Kelly)
    MAX_TOTAL_EXPOSURE    = 0.80   # Max Gesamt-Brutto-Exposure
    VOLATILITY_TARGET     = 0.15   # Ziel-Annualisierte Portfolio-Vol (15%)
    REBALANCE_THRESHOLD   = 0.05   # Rebalancing wenn Abweichung > 5%

    def compute_kelly_fraction(
        self,
        win_rate:    float,
        avg_win:     float,
        avg_loss:    float,
        confidence:  float = 1.0,
    ) -> float:
        """
        Kelly-Kriterium: f* = (p*b - q) / b
        p = win_rate, q = 1-p, b = avg_win/avg_loss
        Confidence-adjustiert und gecappt auf MAX_KELLY_FRACTION.
        """
        if avg_loss < 1e-10:
            raise ValueError("avg_loss muss > 0 sein")
        if not (0.0 <= win_rate <= 1.0):
            raise ValueError(f"win_rate muss in [0,1] sein: {win_rate}")
        if not (0.0 < confidence <= 1.0):
            raise ValueError(f"confidence muss in (0,1]: {confidence}")

        b = avg_win / avg_loss
        p = win_rate
        q = 1.0 - p
        kelly = (p * b - q) / max(b, 1e-10)
        # Half-Kelly oder Quarter-Kelly je nach Konfidenz
        adjusted = kelly * confidence * self.MAX_KELLY_FRACTION
        return float(np.clip(adjusted, 0.0, self.MAX_KELLY_FRACTION))

    def compute_risk_budget_fraction(
        self,
        strategy_vol:    float,
        portfolio_vol:   float,
        risk_budget_pct: float = 0.20,
    ) -> float:
        """
        Risiko-Budget-Allokation: Strategie bekommt risk_budget_pct des Gesamt-Budgets.
        Skaliert auf Volatilitaet: mehr Vol = weniger Allokation.
        """
        if strategy_vol < 1e-10:
            return 0.0
        if portfolio_vol < 1e-10:
            raise ValueError("portfolio_vol muss > 0 sein")

        vol_ratio = float(np.clip(strategy_vol / portfolio_vol, 0.1, 10.0))
        fraction  = risk_budget_pct / vol_ratio
        return float(np.clip(fraction, 0.0, 1.0))

    def compute_vol_targeting_fraction(
        self,
        current_vol:   float,
        target_vol:    Optional[float] = None,
        base_fraction: float = 1.0,
    ) -> float:
        """
        Volatility Targeting: Skaliert Position invers zu Volatilitaet.
        Ziel: konstante Risikoeinheit, nicht konstante Kapitaleinheit.
        """
        target = target_vol or self.VOLATILITY_TARGET
        if current_vol < 1e-10:
            return float(np.clip(base_fraction, 0.0, 1.0))

        scaled = base_fraction * (target / current_vol)
        return float(np.clip(scaled, 0.0, 1.0))

    def allocate_single(
        self,
        strategy_id:     str,
        win_rate:        float,
        avg_win:         float,
        avg_loss:        float,
        strategy_vol:    float,
        portfolio_vol:   float,
        confidence:      float,
        risk_compression: bool,
    ) -> AllocationResult:
        """
        Vollstaendige Allokation fuer eine Strategie.
        Risk Compression reduziert auf 25% der normalen Allokation.
        """
        kelly = self.compute_kelly_fraction(win_rate, avg_win, avg_loss, confidence)
        risk_budget = self.compute_risk_budget_fraction(strategy_vol, portfolio_vol)
        vol_target = self.compute_vol_targeting_fraction(strategy_vol)

        # Endgueltige Allokation: Minimum der drei Methoden (konservativste)
        raw_alloc = min(kelly, risk_budget, vol_target)

        # Risk Compression: drastische Reduzierung
        if risk_compression:
            raw_alloc *= 0.25
            reason = f"Risk compression active. Base: {raw_alloc/0.25:.3f} -> {raw_alloc:.3f}"
        else:
            reason = f"Kelly={kelly:.3f} RiskBudget={risk_budget:.3f} VolTarget={vol_target:.3f}"

        final = float(np.clip(raw_alloc, 0.0, self.MAX_KELLY_FRACTION))
        cap_applied = raw_alloc > final

        return AllocationResult(
            kelly_fraction=kelly,
            risk_budget_fraction=risk_budget,
            vol_target_fraction=vol_target,
            final_allocation=final,
            exposure_cap_applied=cap_applied,
            reason=reason,
        )

    def allocate_portfolio(
        self,
        strategies: Dict[str, Dict],
        portfolio_vol: float,
        risk_compression: bool,
    ) -> PortfolioAllocation:
        """
        Portfolio-weite Allokation.
        Prueft Gesamt-Exposure-Cap und Volatility-Target.
        """
        allocations: Dict[str, AllocationResult] = {}
        for sid, params in strategies.items():
            allocations[sid] = self.allocate_single(
                strategy_id=sid,
                win_rate=float(params.get("win_rate", 0.5)),
                avg_win=float(params.get("avg_win", 1.0)),
                avg_loss=float(params.get("avg_loss", 1.0)),
                strategy_vol=float(params.get("vol", 0.2)),
                portfolio_vol=portfolio_vol,
                confidence=float(params.get("confidence", 0.5)),
                risk_compression=risk_compression,
            )

        total_exposure = sum(r.final_allocation for r in allocations.values())
        total_exposure = float(np.clip(total_exposure, 0.0, self.MAX_TOTAL_EXPOSURE))

        # Portfolio Vol schaetzen (vereinfacht: gewichtetes Mittel der Strategy-Vols)
        if allocations:
            weights = np.array([
                allocations[s].final_allocation / max(total_exposure, 1e-10)
                for s in allocations
            ])
            vols = np.array([
                float(strategies[s].get("vol", 0.2)) for s in allocations
            ])
            portfolio_vol_est = float(np.sum(weights * vols))
        else:
            portfolio_vol_est = 0.0

        vol_target_met = abs(portfolio_vol_est - self.VOLATILITY_TARGET) < 0.05
        rebalance = abs(total_exposure - self.MAX_TOTAL_EXPOSURE * 0.8) > self.REBALANCE_THRESHOLD

        return PortfolioAllocation(
            allocations=allocations,
            total_gross_exposure=total_exposure,
            portfolio_vol_est=portfolio_vol_est,
            vol_target_met=vol_target_met,
            rebalance_required=rebalance,
        )
```

```python
# tests/unit/risk/test_capital_allocation.py
import pytest
from jarvis.risk.capital_allocation import CapitalAllocationEngine

def test_kelly_basic():
    eng = CapitalAllocationEngine()
    k = eng.compute_kelly_fraction(win_rate=0.6, avg_win=1.5, avg_loss=1.0, confidence=1.0)
    assert 0.0 <= k <= eng.MAX_KELLY_FRACTION

def test_kelly_capped():
    eng = CapitalAllocationEngine()
    k = eng.compute_kelly_fraction(win_rate=0.99, avg_win=10.0, avg_loss=0.1, confidence=1.0)
    assert k <= eng.MAX_KELLY_FRACTION

def test_kelly_invalid_win_rate():
    eng = CapitalAllocationEngine()
    with pytest.raises(ValueError):
        eng.compute_kelly_fraction(1.5, 1.0, 1.0)

def test_vol_targeting():
    eng = CapitalAllocationEngine()
    # Bei doppelter Ziel-Vol: halbe Position
    f = eng.compute_vol_targeting_fraction(current_vol=0.30, target_vol=0.15)
    assert abs(f - 0.5) < 0.01

def test_risk_compression_reduces():
    eng = CapitalAllocationEngine()
    r_normal = eng.allocate_single("s1", 0.55, 1.0, 1.0, 0.2, 0.2, 0.7, False)
    r_compr  = eng.allocate_single("s1", 0.55, 1.0, 1.0, 0.2, 0.2, 0.7, True)
    assert r_compr.final_allocation < r_normal.final_allocation

def test_portfolio_allocation():
    eng = CapitalAllocationEngine()
    strategies = {
        "s1": {"win_rate": 0.55, "avg_win": 1.2, "avg_loss": 1.0, "vol": 0.2, "confidence": 0.7},
        "s2": {"win_rate": 0.50, "avg_win": 1.0, "avg_loss": 1.0, "vol": 0.3, "confidence": 0.5},
    }
    result = eng.allocate_portfolio(strategies, portfolio_vol=0.2, risk_compression=False)
    assert 0.0 <= result.total_gross_exposure <= eng.MAX_TOTAL_EXPOSURE
```

## SESSION 30: SIMULATED EXECUTION MODELING LAYER

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S17 (Risk Engine), S21 (Liquidity), S29 (Capital Allocation)
**Zeit:** 70-85 min
**Datei:** jarvis/simulation/execution_model.py

### Prinzip

Getrennt vom Signal-Layer.
Modelliert WIE eine hypothetische Position aufgebaut würde — für Simulations- und Forschungszwecke.
Alle Outputs sind Szenarien, keine echten Aufträge.
Kein echter Broker-Kontakt. Kein Real-Capital. Nur Research-Output.

```python
# jarvis/execution/execution_optimizer.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import numpy as np
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Optional

@dataclass
class SimulatedExecutionModel:
    """
    Simuliertes Ausfuehrungs-Modell fuer Research-Zwecke.
    Kein echtes Trading. Kein Broker-Interface. Rein analytisch.
    Alle Outputs sind hypothetische Szenarien fuer Forschung und Backtesting.
    """
    base_size:           float   # Basis-Groesse (in Kapital-Anteil)
    adjusted_size:       float   # Liquiditaets-angepasste Groesse
    estimated_slippage:  float   # Geschaetzter Slippage in %
    max_market_impact:   float   # Maximaler Market Impact in %
    recommended_algo:    str     # "TWAP", "VWAP", "LIMIT", "AGGRESSIVE"
    urgency_score:       float   # [0,1]: 0=kein Eile, 1=sofort
    latency_budget_ms:   float   # Max erlaubte Latenz in ms
    abort_if_spread_pct: float   # Abbruch wenn Spread > X%
    risk_cleared:        bool    # True wenn Risk Engine freigegeben


class SimulatedExecutionOptimizer:
    """
    Simulated Execution Modeling Layer — Research Only.
    SANDBOXED: Kein Broker-Kontakt. Kein echter Order-Flow.
    Alle Outputs sind hypothetische Szenarien fuer Backtesting und Forschung.
    Outputs gehen NUR in Research-Layer und Visual-Output, nicht in Broker-Systeme.
    """

    # Latenz-Budgets in ms
    LATENCY_BUDGET_URGENT  =  50.0
    LATENCY_BUDGET_NORMAL  = 500.0
    LATENCY_BUDGET_PASSIVE = 5000.0

    # Market Impact Schwellen
    MAX_SPREAD_ABORT_PCT  = 0.005   # 0.5%
    MAX_IMPACT_PCT        = 0.002   # 0.2%

    def estimate_slippage(
        self,
        order_size_pct:    float,
        liquidity_score:   float,
        current_vol:       float,
        bid_ask_spread_pct: float,
    ) -> float:
        """
        Slippage-Schaetzung: basierend auf Groesse, Liquiditaet, Vol, Spread.
        Gibt Slippage in % zurueck.
        """
        for name, val in [("order_size_pct", order_size_pct),
                          ("liquidity_score", liquidity_score),
                          ("current_vol", current_vol),
                          ("bid_ask_spread_pct", bid_ask_spread_pct)]:
            if not np.isfinite(val) or val < 0:
                raise ValueError(f"Ungaeltiger Wert: {name}={val}")

        # Basis-Slippage = halber Spread
        base_slippage = bid_ask_spread_pct / 2.0
        # Vol-Komponente: hoehere Vol = mehr Slippage
        vol_component = current_vol * 0.1 * order_size_pct
        # Liquiditaets-Faktor: schlechtere Liquiditaet = mehr Slippage
        liq_factor = 1.0 + (1.0 - float(np.clip(liquidity_score, 0.0, 1.0))) * 2.0

        total = (base_slippage + vol_component) * liq_factor
        return float(np.clip(total, 0.0, 0.05))  # Max 5% Slippage

    def compute_market_impact(
        self,
        order_size_pct:   float,
        avg_daily_vol_pct: float,
    ) -> float:
        """
        Market Impact: Square-Root-Modell.
        Impact ~ sqrt(order_size / avg_daily_vol)
        """
        if avg_daily_vol_pct < 1e-10:
            return self.MAX_IMPACT_PCT

        ratio  = float(np.clip(order_size_pct / avg_daily_vol_pct, 0.0, 1.0))
        impact = 0.1 * float(np.sqrt(ratio))
        return float(np.clip(impact, 0.0, self.MAX_IMPACT_PCT))

    def select_algorithm(
        self,
        urgency_score:   float,
        liquidity_score: float,
        time_horizon_s:  float,
    ) -> str:
        """
        Waehlt optimalen Execution-Algorithmus.
        """
        if urgency_score > 0.8:
            return "AGGRESSIVE"
        elif time_horizon_s > 3600:
            return "TWAP"
        elif liquidity_score > 0.7:
            return "VWAP"
        else:
            return "LIMIT"

    def optimize(
        self,
        base_size_pct:      float,
        liquidity_score:    float,
        bid_ask_spread_pct: float,
        current_vol:        float,
        avg_daily_vol_pct:  float,
        urgency_score:      float,
        time_horizon_s:     float,
        risk_cleared:       bool,
    ) -> ExecutionPlan:
        """
        Vollstaendige Execution-Optimierung.
        Gibt Plan zurueck. Wenn risk_cleared=False: Plan mit size=0.
        """
        if not risk_cleared:
            return ExecutionPlan(
                base_size=base_size_pct,
                adjusted_size=0.0,
                estimated_slippage=0.0,
                max_market_impact=0.0,
                recommended_algo="HOLD",
                urgency_score=urgency_score,
                latency_budget_ms=self.LATENCY_BUDGET_NORMAL,
                abort_if_spread_pct=self.MAX_SPREAD_ABORT_PCT,
                risk_cleared=False,
            )

        # Liquiditaets-angepasste Groesse
        liq_factor    = float(np.clip(liquidity_score, 0.1, 1.0))
        adjusted_size = base_size_pct * liq_factor

        # Slippage und Impact schaetzen
        slippage = self.estimate_slippage(
            adjusted_size, liquidity_score, current_vol, bid_ask_spread_pct
        )
        impact = self.compute_market_impact(adjusted_size, avg_daily_vol_pct)

        # Algo auswaehlen
        algo = self.select_algorithm(urgency_score, liquidity_score, time_horizon_s)

        # Latenz-Budget
        if urgency_score > 0.7:
            latency_budget = self.LATENCY_BUDGET_URGENT
        elif urgency_score > 0.3:
            latency_budget = self.LATENCY_BUDGET_NORMAL
        else:
            latency_budget = self.LATENCY_BUDGET_PASSIVE

        # Spread-Abbruch-Schwelle
        abort_spread = max(self.MAX_SPREAD_ABORT_PCT, bid_ask_spread_pct * 2.0)

        return ExecutionPlan(
            base_size=base_size_pct,
            adjusted_size=float(np.clip(adjusted_size, 0.0, 1.0)),
            estimated_slippage=slippage,
            max_market_impact=impact,
            recommended_algo=algo,
            urgency_score=float(np.clip(urgency_score, 0.0, 1.0)),
            latency_budget_ms=latency_budget,
            abort_if_spread_pct=abort_spread,
            risk_cleared=risk_cleared,
        )
```


### SIMULATION GOVERNANCE CONSTRAINTS (SESSION 30)

```
KRITISCH — Diese Layer ist AUSSCHLIESSLICH für Forschung und Simulation:

  ERLAUBT:
    - Slippage-Modellierung für Backtesting
    - Market-Impact-Schätzung für Strategy-Research
    - Algorithmische Selektion für Szenario-Analyse
    - Latenz-Budget-Schätzung für Simulations-Qualität

  VERBOTEN:
    - Echter Order-Flow zu Brokern
    - Echter Position-Open/Close
    - Margin-Interaktion
    - Account-State-Mutation
    - Broker-Credentials oder API-Keys in diesem Layer

  ENFORCEMENT: Jeder Output dieses Layers ist vom Typ SimulatedPositionPlan.
  Kein externer System-Aufruf erlaubt. Kein Netzwerk-Zugriff.
```

### Tests

```python
# tests/unit/simulation/test_execution_model.py
import pytest
from jarvis.simulation.execution_model import SimulatedExecutionOptimizer

def test_no_execution_without_risk_clearance():
    opt = SimulatedExecutionOptimizer()
    plan = opt.optimize(0.1, 0.8, 0.001, 0.2, 0.02, 0.5, 3600, risk_cleared=False)
    assert plan.adjusted_size == 0.0
    assert plan.recommended_algo == "HOLD"
    assert plan.risk_cleared == False

def test_slippage_increases_with_vol():
    opt = SimulatedExecutionOptimizer()
    low  = opt.estimate_slippage(0.01, 0.8, 0.10, 0.001)
    high = opt.estimate_slippage(0.01, 0.8, 0.50, 0.001)
    assert high > low

def test_slippage_increases_with_low_liquidity():
    opt = SimulatedExecutionOptimizer()
    liq_high = opt.estimate_slippage(0.01, 0.9, 0.2, 0.001)
    liq_low  = opt.estimate_slippage(0.01, 0.1, 0.2, 0.001)
    assert liq_low > liq_high

def test_algo_aggressive_on_urgency():
    opt = SimulatedExecutionOptimizer()
    plan = opt.optimize(0.05, 0.7, 0.001, 0.2, 0.02, 0.9, 60, risk_cleared=True)
    assert plan.recommended_algo == "AGGRESSIVE"

def test_algo_twap_long_horizon():
    opt = SimulatedExecutionOptimizer()
    plan = opt.optimize(0.05, 0.7, 0.001, 0.2, 0.02, 0.1, 7200, risk_cleared=True)
    assert plan.recommended_algo == "TWAP"
```

# SESSIONS 31-32: GOVERNANCE, HARDENING & CHART INTERFACE

## SESSION 31: GOVERNANCE & HARDENING

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S01 (Integrity), S09 (Calibration), S10 (OOD), S15 (Validation)
**Zeit:** 70-85 min

### Prinzip

    Robustheit > Accuracy

Hard Gates sind keine Optionen. Sie sind Systemgrenzen.
Soft Warnings bei Hard-Fehlern sind verboten.

### Immutable Threshold Manifest

Alle kritischen Schwellenwerte sind in THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json
gespeichert und via SHA-256 gehasht. CI blockiert bei Hash-Mismatch.

```json
// THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json (Beispiel - Hash wird aus Inhalt berechnet)
{
    "version": "5.0-final",
    "hash_algorithm": "SHA-256",
    "thresholds": {
        "ece_hard_gate":           0.05,
        "ece_per_regime_drift":    0.02,
        "ood_consensus_minimum":   3,
        "ood_recall_historical":   0.90,
        "ood_recall_synthetic":    0.90,
        "max_drawdown_threshold":  0.15,
        "vol_compression_trigger": 0.30,
        "shock_exposure_cap":      0.25,
        "min_improvement_deploy":  0.005,
        "max_quote_age_seconds":   10.0,
        "crisis_correlation":      0.85
    },
    "joint_risk_multiplier_table": {
        "description": "Deterministic Joint Macro x Correlation Risk Multiplier. Phase 6A.",
        "governance":  "Hash-protected. Change requires version bump and migration doc.",
        "values": {
            "BENIGN":    {"DECOUPLED": 1.00, "COUPLED": 1.15, "CRISIS_COUPLING": 1.40},
            "UNCERTAIN": {"DECOUPLED": 1.15, "COUPLED": 1.35, "CRISIS_COUPLING": 1.65},
            "ADVERSE":   {"DECOUPLED": 1.40, "COUPLED": 1.65, "CRISIS_COUPLING": 2.00}
        },
        "table_hash": "SHA256_PLACEHOLDER_COMPUTED_AT_BUILD_TIME"
    },
    "manifest_hash": "SHA256_PLACEHOLDER_COMPUTED_AT_BUILD_TIME"
}
```

```python
# jarvis/governance/threshold_guardian.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import hashlib
import json
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, Any

class ThresholdGuardian:
    """
    Veririfiziert THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json bei jedem System-Start.
    Wirft bei Hash-Mismatch: KEIN Soft-Warning, KEIN Silent Pass.
    """

    def __init__(self, manifest_path: Path):
        self.manifest_path = manifest_path

    def load_and_verify(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Laedt Manifest und verifiziert Integritaet.
        Wirft RuntimeError bei Hash-Mismatch.
        """
        if not self.manifest_path.exists():
            raise FileNotFoundError(
                f"THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json nicht gefunden: {self.manifest_path}. "
                "System-Start verweigert."
            )

        with open(self.manifest_path, "r") as f:
            raw = f.read()
            data = json.loads(raw)

        stored_hash = data.get("manifest_hash", "")

        # Hash-Berechnung: alles ausser manifest_hash-Feld
        data_for_hash = {k: v for k, v in data.items() if k != "manifest_hash"}
        computed_hash = hashlib.sha256(
            json.dumps(data_for_hash, sort_keys=True).encode("utf-8")
        ).hexdigest()

        if stored_hash != "SHA256_PLACEHOLDER_COMPUTED_AT_BUILD_TIME":
            if computed_hash != stored_hash:
                raise RuntimeError(
                    f"THRESHOLD_MANIFEST Hash-Mismatch. "
                    f"Erwartet: {stored_hash[:12]}... "
                    f"Berechnet: {computed_hash[:12]}... "
                    "System-Start verweigert. Moegliche Manipulation."
                )

        return data["thresholds"]


class HardCalibrationGate:
    """
    Deployment-Gate: Wirft bei ECE-Verletzung. KEIN Soft-Warning.
    """

    def __init__(self, thresholds: Dict[str, Any]):
        self.ECE_HARD_GATE         = float(thresholds["ece_hard_gate"])
        self.ECE_PER_REGIME_DRIFT  = float(thresholds["ece_per_regime_drift"])

    def enforce(self, ece: float, regime: str) -> None:
        """
        Wirft RuntimeError wenn ECE ueber Hard Gate.
        NIEMALS nur loggen und weitermachen.
        """
        if ece > self.ECE_HARD_GATE:
            raise RuntimeError(
                f"CALIBRATION_HARD_GATE_VIOLATED: ECE={ece:.4f} > "
                f"{self.ECE_HARD_GATE} (regime={regime}). "
                "Deployment blockiert."
            )


class OODEnforcer:
    """
    OOD-Enforcement: Blockiert Produktion bei OOD-Recall-Verletzung.
    """

    def __init__(self, thresholds: Dict[str, Any]):
        self.OOD_CONSENSUS_MIN        = int(thresholds["ood_consensus_minimum"])
        self.OOD_RECALL_HISTORICAL    = float(thresholds["ood_recall_historical"])
        self.OOD_RECALL_SYNTHETIC     = float(thresholds["ood_recall_synthetic"])

    def enforce_recall(
        self,
        historical_recall: float,
        synthetic_recall:  float,
    ) -> None:
        """
        Wirft bei OOD-Recall-Verletzung. KEIN Soft-Warning.
        """
        if historical_recall < self.OOD_RECALL_HISTORICAL:
            raise RuntimeError(
                f"OOD_RECALL_GATE_VIOLATED: historical_recall="
                f"{historical_recall:.3f} < {self.OOD_RECALL_HISTORICAL}. "
                "Deployment blockiert."
            )
        if synthetic_recall < self.OOD_RECALL_SYNTHETIC:
            raise RuntimeError(
                f"OOD_RECALL_GATE_VIOLATED: synthetic_recall="
                f"{synthetic_recall:.3f} < {self.OOD_RECALL_SYNTHETIC}. "
                "Deployment blockiert."
            )


class CIGovernanceGuard:
    """
    CI/CD Guard: Blockiert Merge bei Governance-Verletzung.
    Laeut in GitHub Actions / GitLab CI.
    """

    def run_full_governance_check(
        self,
        manifest_path: Path,
        ece_results:   Dict[str, float],  # regime -> ECE
        ood_recall:    Dict[str, float],  # historical/synthetic -> recall
    ) -> None:
        """
        Vollstaendige Governance-Pruefung.
        Wenn IRGENDETWAS fehlschlaegt: Exit Code 1 -> CI blockiert.
        """
        guardian  = ThresholdGuardian(manifest_path)
        thresholds = guardian.load_and_verify()

        gate     = HardCalibrationGate(thresholds)
        enforcer = OODEnforcer(thresholds)

        # ECE pro Regime pruefen
        for regime, ece in ece_results.items():
            gate.enforce(ece=ece, regime=regime)

        # OOD Recall pruefen
        enforcer.enforce_recall(
            historical_recall=ood_recall.get("historical", 0.0),
            synthetic_recall=ood_recall.get("synthetic", 0.0),
        )

        # Alles bestanden
        print("[OK] Governance Check: ALLE GATES BESTANDEN")
```

### CI/CD Integration

```yaml
# .github/workflows/governance_check.yml
# Fuegt man in GitHub Actions Pipeline ein

name: JARVIS Governance Gate
on: [push, pull_request]

jobs:
  governance:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      - name: Run Governance Check
        run: |
          python scripts/ci_governance_check.py \
            --manifest config/THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json \
            --ece-results results/ece_per_regime.json \
            --ood-results results/ood_recall.json
        # Exit Code 1 = Merge blockiert (kein Soft-Warning)
```

### Governance-Anforderungen (PFLICHT, unveraenderlich)

    R1:  Hard Calibration Gates     -> RuntimeError, kein Warning
    R2:  OOD Enforcement            -> RuntimeError, kein Warning
    R3:  Immutable Thresholds       -> Hash-gesichert, CI-blockiert bei Mismatch
    R4:  CI Blockade bei Fehler     -> Exit Code 1, kein Soft-Pass
    R5:  Deterministisch            -> Gleiche Inputs -> Gleiche Outputs, immer
    R6:  Reproduzierbarkeit         -> Seeds gesetzt, Timestamps geloggt
    R7:  Kein Soft-Warning          -> Hard Error bei Hard-Fehler, keine Ausnahme
    R8:  Audit-Trail                -> Alle Gate-Ergebnisse in BUILD_LOG.json

---

## SESSION 32: PROFESSIONELLES CHART-INTERFACE

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S16 (Confidence Zone), S17 (Risk Engine), S26 (Adaptive Strategy)
**Zeit:** 60-80 min

### Prinzip

Im Chart erscheinen KEINE "BUY" / "SELL" Labels.
Stattdessen wird Markstruktur visualisiert:

    Entry Confidence Box      (Wahrscheinlichkeitsraum fuer Einstieg)
    Exit Risk Corridor        (Risikobereich fuer Ausstieg)
    Expected Move %           (Erwartete Bewegung mit Konfidenz)
    Volatility Adjusted Stop  (Dynamischer Stop)
    Regime Label              (Aktuelles Marktregime)
    Strategy Mode Label       (Aktiver Strategie-Modus)
    Meta-Uncertainty Level    (Systemweite Unsicherheit)

Das ist institutionelle Visualisierung.

### UI GOVERNANCE — PERMITTED AND FORBIDDEN DISPLAY ELEMENTS

```
╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗
║  UI CLASSIFICATION: RESEARCH AND ANALYSIS DISPLAY ONLY              ║
║  Kein Ausführungs-Interface. Keine Order-Buttons. Keine Broker-UI.  ║
╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝

PERMITTED — UI darf anzeigen:
  - Entry zones (probability bands, not signals)
  - Exit zones (confidence-based ranges, not instructions)
  - Probability bands and confidence intervals
  - Expected value estimates (research output)
  - Strategy weighting display (regime-mapped weights)
  - Regime timeline and transition history
  - Portfolio heatmap (simulated exposure visualization)
  - Outcome analytics (historical scenario performance)
  - Volatility state and NVU indicator
  - Failure mode banners (FM-01..FM-06 status)
  - Uncertainty metric display (mu, Q, S, U, R from D(t))
  - Simulated P&L curves (backtested, not live)
  - Scenario comparison panels

FORBIDDEN — UI darf NICHT enthalten:
  - "Buy" or "Sell" buttons or labels
  - "Execute" controls of any kind
  - "Close position" buttons
  - "Broker connect" or API link UI
  - Order routing interfaces
  - Account balance display (real)
  - Margin level or margin call UI
  - Any control that triggers external system calls
  - One-click trading elements

ENFORCEMENT:
  Any UI element that could be interpreted as an order instruction
  is a P0 violation and must be removed.
  ChartDataBuilder output contains NO order-type fields.
```

### Chart Data Contract

```python
# jarvis/chart/chart_contract.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Optional

@dataclass
class ChartOverlay:
    """
    Alle Daten die das Chart-Interface benoetigt.
    Wird von ChartDataBuilder aus System-Outputs zusammengestellt.
    """

    # Entry Confidence Box
    entry_box_lower:      float  # Untere Grenze in Preis-Einheiten
    entry_box_upper:      float  # Obere Grenze in Preis-Einheiten
    entry_confidence_pct: float  # Konfidenz in % (0-100)

    # Exit Risk Corridor
    exit_corridor_soft:   float  # Soft-Exit-Level
    exit_corridor_hard:   float  # Hard-Exit-Level (Risikogrenze)
    exit_confidence_pct:  float  # Konfidenz des Exits in %

    # Expected Move
    expected_move_pct:    float  # Erwartete Bewegung in %

    # Volatility Adjusted Stop
    vol_stop_price:       float  # Stop-Preis (vol-adjustiert)
    vol_stop_distance_pct: float # Stop-Abstand in % vom aktuellen Preis

    # Regime Label (ASCII)
    regime_label:         str    # z.B. "TRENDING", "RANGING", "HIGH_VOL", "SHOCK"

    # Strategy Mode Label (ASCII)
    strategy_mode_label:  str    # z.B. "MOMENTUM", "DEFENSIVE", "RISK_REDUCTION"

    # Meta-Uncertainty Level
    meta_uncertainty_pct: float  # Meta-Unsicherheit in % (0=sicher, 100=maximal unsicher)
    uncertainty_band:     str    # "LOW", "MODERATE", "HIGH", "EXTREME"

    # Timeframe Label
    timeframe_label:      str    # z.B. "5m", "15m", "1h"

    # Risk Compression Indicator
    risk_compression_active: bool


class ChartDataBuilder:
    """
    Baut ChartOverlay aus System-Outputs zusammen.
    Einziger Weg, Daten ins Chart-Interface zu bekommen.
    """

    UNCERTAINTY_BANDS = [
        (0.20, "LOW"),
        (0.50, "MODERATE"),
        (0.75, "HIGH"),
        (1.00, "EXTREME"),
    ]

    def build(
        self,
        confidence_zone,    # ConfidenceZone
        risk_output,        # RiskOutput
        strategy_selection, # StrategySelection
        current_price:      float,
        timeframe_label:    str,
    ) -> ChartOverlay:
        """
        Transformiert System-Outputs in Chart-Interface-Daten.
        Keine Berechnungs-Logik hier: nur Datentransformation.
        """
        # Entry Box
        entry_box_lower = confidence_zone.entry_lower
        entry_box_upper = confidence_zone.entry_upper
        entry_conf_pct  = round(confidence_zone.entry_confidence * 100.0, 1)

        # Exit Corridor
        exit_soft       = confidence_zone.exit_soft
        exit_hard       = confidence_zone.exit_hard
        exit_conf_pct   = round(confidence_zone.exit_confidence * 100.0, 1)

        # Expected Move
        exp_move_pct    = round(confidence_zone.expected_move_pct, 2)

        # Volatility Stop
        vol_stop        = confidence_zone.vol_adjusted_stop
        stop_dist_pct   = round(
            abs(current_price - vol_stop) / max(current_price, 1e-10) * 100.0, 2
        )

        # Meta-Uncertainty
        unc_pct  = round(confidence_zone.meta_uncertainty * 100.0, 1)
        unc_band = "EXTREME"
        for threshold, label in self.UNCERTAINTY_BANDS:
            if confidence_zone.meta_uncertainty <= threshold:
                unc_band = label
                break

        return ChartOverlay(
            entry_box_lower=entry_box_lower,
            entry_box_upper=entry_box_upper,
            entry_confidence_pct=entry_conf_pct,
            exit_corridor_soft=exit_soft,
            exit_corridor_hard=exit_hard,
            exit_confidence_pct=exit_conf_pct,
            expected_move_pct=exp_move_pct,
            vol_stop_price=vol_stop,
            vol_stop_distance_pct=stop_dist_pct,
            regime_label=strategy_selection.config.label,
            strategy_mode_label=strategy_selection.mode.value,
            meta_uncertainty_pct=unc_pct,
            uncertainty_band=unc_band,
            timeframe_label=timeframe_label,
            risk_compression_active=risk_output.risk_compression_active,
        )
```

### Chart-Rendering Spezifikation (ASCII-Schema)

```
+------------------------------------------------------------------+
| JARVIS Risk Intelligence Platform                  [5m | 1H | 1D]|
+------------------------------------------------------------------+
|                                                                  |
|  REGIME:   [TRENDING]        STRATEGY: [MOMENTUM]               |
|  META-UNCERTAINTY: 23.4%     BAND: [LOW]                        |
|  RISK COMPRESSION: [OFF]                                         |
|                                                                  |
+------------------------------------------------------------------+
|                                                                  |
|  ---- ENTRY CONFIDENCE BOX ----                                  |
|  Upper:  $48,320    Confidence: 71.2%                           |
|  Lower:  $47,890                                                 |
|                                                                  |
|  ---- EXIT RISK CORRIDOR -----                                   |
|  Soft Exit:  $47,200    Exit Conf: 28.8%                        |
|  Hard Exit:  $46,500                                             |
|                                                                  |
|  ---- EXPECTED MOVE ----------                                   |
|  +/- 2.14%                                                       |
|                                                                  |
|  ---- VOLATILITY ADJ. STOP ---                                   |
|  Stop Price: $46,812    Distance: 2.48% from current            |
|                                                                  |
+------------------------------------------------------------------+
| WARNUNG: Alle Werte sind Wahrscheinlichkeitsbereiche.           |
| Kein Signal. Kein Handelsbefehl. Eigenverantwortung beachten.   |
+------------------------------------------------------------------+
```

### Verbotene Chart-Elemente

```
VERBOTEN im Chart-Interface (P0 ENFORCEMENT):
  - "BUY" oder "SELL" Labels — keine Kauf-/Verkaufsaufforderungen
  - "LONG" oder "SHORT" Empfehlungen — keine Positionsrichtung
  - "TAKE PROFIT" Level (nur Exit-Konfidenz ohne Richtungsangabe)
  - "Execute", "Close", "Open Position" Controls
  - Broker-Connect-UI oder API-Key-Eingaben
  - Order-Routing-Buttons oder -Links
  - Account-Balance (echtes Konto) — nur simuliertes Portfolio
  - Margin-Level oder Margin-Call-Anzeige
  - Pfeil-Symbole die Richtung suggerieren
  - Farben die eindeutig "gut" oder "schlecht" signalisieren
    (AUSNAHME: Uncertainty Band kann Rot/Gelb/Gruen nutzen)
  - Prozentualer Gewinn-Forecast (nur Konfidenz-Schätzung)
  - Trefferquoten-Anzeige ("Accuracy: 75%")
  - Jedes Element das als Order-Instruction interpretierbar ist
```

### Kritische Anforderungen

- R1: ChartDataBuilder ist die EINZIGE Quelle fuer Chart-Daten
- R2: Keine Direktzugriffe auf Berechnungsmodule vom UI
- R3: meta_uncertainty_pct IMMER sichtbar (keine Versteckung)
- R4: risk_compression_active IMMER im Header sichtbar
- R5: Timeframe-Label IMMER sichtbar (verhindert Verwechslung)
- R6: Alle angezeigten Werte muessen aus versioniertem Output stammen

# SESSIONS 33-34, 36: FEATURE RESEARCH, MODEL GOVERNANCE, PERFORMANCE CERTIFICATION
# Version: 5.0-elite | Dependencies: S01-S35

---

## SESSION 33: FEATURE RESEARCH PIPELINE

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S03 (Data), S04 (Features), S05 (Regime)
**Zeit:** 70-90 min
**Datei:** jarvis/research/feature_pipeline.py

### Prinzip

Kein unkontrolliertes Feature-Creep.
Features sind versioniert, dekadierende Features werden automatisch entfernt.
Jedes Feature hat einen Registry-Eintrag.

```python
# jarvis/research/feature_pipeline.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import numpy as np
import json
import hashlib
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, List, Optional
from pathlib import Path

@dataclass
class FeatureEntry:
    """Registry-Eintrag fuer ein Feature."""
    feature_id:       str
    name:             str
    version:          str
    created_at:       str
    last_validated:   str
    importance_score: float   # [0,1]: 0=unwichtig, 1=sehr wichtig
    decay_rate:       float   # Taeglich: wie schnell verliert Feature an Relevanz
    is_active:        bool
    regime_valid:     List[str]  # In welchen Regimen valide
    hash:             str        # SHA-256 der Feature-Definition

@dataclass
class FeatureImportanceResult:
    feature_id:       str
    current_score:    float
    decayed_score:    float
    days_since_valid: int
    should_prune:     bool
    reason:           str


class FeatureRegistry:
    """
    Formale Feature-Verwaltung.
    Alle Features muessen registriert sein.
    Automatisches Pruning bei Decay.
    """

    PRUNE_THRESHOLD      = 0.10   # Features unter 10% werden gepruned
    MAX_DECAY_PER_DAY    = 0.02   # Max 2% Decay pro Tag

    def __init__(self, registry_path: Optional[Path] = None):
        self._registry: Dict[str, FeatureEntry] = {}
        self._path = registry_path

    def register(
        self,
        feature_id:   str,
        name:         str,
        version:      str,
        regime_valid: List[str],
        importance:   float = 0.5,
        decay_rate:   float = 0.005,
    ) -> FeatureEntry:
        """
        Registriert ein neues Feature.
        Wirft wenn feature_id bereits existiert (keine stillen Duplikate).
        """
        if feature_id in self._registry:
            raise ValueError(
                f"Feature '{feature_id}' bereits registriert. "
                "Verwende update_importance() fuer Updates."
            )
        if not (0.0 <= importance <= 1.0):
            raise ValueError(f"importance muss in [0,1]: {importance}")
        if not (0.0 <= decay_rate <= self.MAX_DECAY_PER_DAY):
            raise ValueError(f"decay_rate muss in [0, {self.MAX_DECAY_PER_DAY}]: {decay_rate}")

        feature_def = f"{feature_id}{name}{version}{regime_valid}"
        feat_hash   = hashlib.sha256(feature_def.encode()).hexdigest()[:16]
        now         = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()

        entry = FeatureEntry(
            feature_id=feature_id,
            name=name,
            version=version,
            created_at=now,
            last_validated=now,
            importance_score=float(np.clip(importance, 0.0, 1.0)),
            decay_rate=decay_rate,
            is_active=True,
            regime_valid=regime_valid,
            hash=feat_hash,
        )
        self._registry[feature_id] = entry
        return entry

    def update_importance(
        self,
        feature_id:    str,
        new_importance: float,
    ) -> FeatureEntry:
        """Aktualisiert Importance-Score nach erneutem Backtesting."""
        if feature_id not in self._registry:
            raise KeyError(f"Feature '{feature_id}' nicht in Registry")
        entry = self._registry[feature_id]
        entry.importance_score = float(np.clip(new_importance, 0.0, 1.0))
        entry.last_validated   = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
        return entry

    def compute_decayed_importance(
        self,
        feature_id:   str,
        days_elapsed: int,
    ) -> FeatureImportanceResult:
        """
        Berechnet abgenutzten Importance-Score.
        Exponentieller Decay: score * (1 - decay_rate)^days
        """
        if feature_id not in self._registry:
            raise KeyError(f"Feature '{feature_id}' nicht in Registry")

        entry = self._registry[feature_id]
        decayed = entry.importance_score * ((1.0 - entry.decay_rate) ** days_elapsed)
        decayed = float(max(decayed, 0.0))

        should_prune = decayed < self.PRUNE_THRESHOLD
        reason = ""
        if should_prune:
            reason = (
                f"Decayed score {decayed:.3f} < threshold {self.PRUNE_THRESHOLD}. "
                f"Days elapsed: {days_elapsed}"
            )

        return FeatureImportanceResult(
            feature_id=feature_id,
            current_score=entry.importance_score,
            decayed_score=decayed,
            days_since_valid=days_elapsed,
            should_prune=should_prune,
            reason=reason,
        )

    def prune_stale_features(
        self,
        days_threshold: int = 30,
    ) -> List[str]:
        """
        Deaktiviert Features deren decayed_importance unter Schwellenwert.
        Gibt Liste der geprunten Feature-IDs zurueck.
        """
        pruned = []
        for fid, entry in self._registry.items():
            result = self.compute_decayed_importance(fid, days_threshold)
            if result.should_prune and entry.is_active:
                entry.is_active = False
                pruned.append(fid)
        return pruned

    def get_active_features(
        self,
        regime: Optional[str] = None,
    ) -> List[FeatureEntry]:
        """Gibt alle aktiven Features (optional gefiltert nach Regime) zurueck."""
        features = [e for e in self._registry.values() if e.is_active]
        if regime:
            features = [
                e for e in features
                if not e.regime_valid or regime in e.regime_valid
            ]
        return sorted(features, key=lambda e: -e.importance_score)

    def save(self, path: Optional[Path] = None) -> None:
        """Speichert Registry als JSON."""
        target = path or self._path
        if not target:
            raise ValueError("Kein Registry-Pfad angegeben")
        data = {fid: asdict(entry) for fid, entry in self._registry.items()}
        with open(target, "w") as f:
            json.dump(data, f, indent=2)

    def load(self, path: Optional[Path] = None) -> None:
        """Laedt Registry aus JSON."""
        target = path or self._path
        if not target or not target.exists():
            return
        with open(target) as f:
            data = json.load(f)
        for fid, d in data.items():
            self._registry[fid] = FeatureEntry(**d)
```

### Tests

```python
# tests/unit/research/test_feature_pipeline.py
import pytest
from jarvis.research.feature_pipeline import FeatureRegistry

def test_register_and_retrieve():
    reg = FeatureRegistry()
    entry = reg.register("rsi_14", "RSI-14", "1.0", ["TRENDING", "RANGING"])
    assert entry.feature_id == "rsi_14"
    assert entry.is_active == True

def test_duplicate_register_raises():
    reg = FeatureRegistry()
    reg.register("rsi_14", "RSI-14", "1.0", [])
    with pytest.raises(ValueError):
        reg.register("rsi_14", "RSI-14", "1.0", [])

def test_decay_reduces_score():
    reg = FeatureRegistry()
    reg.register("feat1", "Test", "1.0", [], importance=0.8)
    result = reg.compute_decayed_importance("feat1", days_elapsed=60)
    assert result.decayed_score < 0.8

def test_prune_threshold():
    reg = FeatureRegistry()
    reg.register("feat_bad", "Bad Feature", "1.0", [],
                 importance=0.12, decay_rate=0.015)
    result = reg.compute_decayed_importance("feat_bad", days_elapsed=100)
    assert result.should_prune == True

def test_active_features_filter():
    reg = FeatureRegistry()
    reg.register("rsi", "RSI", "1.0", ["TRENDING"])
    reg.register("bb", "BB", "1.0", ["RANGING"])
    active = reg.get_active_features(regime="TRENDING")
    assert any(f.feature_id == "rsi" for f in active)
    assert not any(f.feature_id == "bb" for f in active)
```
