## SESSION 34: MODEL GOVERNANCE FRAMEWORK

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S01, S09 (Calibration), S10 (OOD), S27 (Det. Learning)
**Zeit:** 75-90 min
**Datei:** jarvis/governance/model_registry.py

### Prinzip

Vollstaendige Model Risk Governance nach SR 11-7 (Federal Reserve Guidance).
Deployment ohne Governance-Genehmigung ist VERBOTEN.

### Model Registry

```python
# jarvis/governance/model_registry.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
from dataclasses import dataclass
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, List, Optional
from enum import Enum
import json
import hashlib

class ModelStatus(Enum):
    DEVELOPMENT = "development"
    VALIDATION = "validation"
    APPROVED = "approved"
    DEPLOYED = "deployed"
    DEPRECATED = "deprecated"
    SUSPENDED = "suspended"

class ModelRiskTier(Enum):
    """SR 11-7 Risk Tiers"""
    TIER_1_HIGH = "tier_1_high"        # High risk, requires full validation
    TIER_2_MODERATE = "tier_2_moderate"  # Moderate risk
    TIER_3_LOW = "tier_3_low"          # Low risk, simplified validation

@dataclass
class ModelVersion:
    """Einzelne Modell-Version mit vollstaendiger Traceability."""
    model_id: str
    version: str
    created_at: datetime
    created_by: str
    status: ModelStatus
    risk_tier: ModelRiskTier
    
    # Code und Konfiguration
    code_hash: str            # SHA-256 des Model-Codes
    config_hash: str          # SHA-256 der Konfiguration
    dependency_hash: str      # Hash aller Dependencies
    
    # Performance Metrics
    validation_metrics: Dict[str, float]
    backtest_metrics: Dict[str, float]
    oos_metrics: Dict[str, float]  # Out-of-sample
    
    # Governance
    validator_name: Optional[str] = None
    validation_date: Optional[datetime] = None
    approval_date: Optional[datetime] = None
    approved_by: Optional[str] = None
    
    # Dokumentation
    change_log: List[str] = None
    assumptions: List[str] = None
    limitations: List[str] = None
    
    def __post_init__(self):
        if self.change_log is None:
            self.change_log = []
        if self.assumptions is None:
            self.assumptions = []
        if self.limitations is None:
            self.limitations = []

@dataclass
class ValidationReport:
    """Unabhaengiger Validierungsbericht."""
    model_id: str
    version: str
    validator_name: str
    validation_date: datetime
    
    # Validierungsergebnisse
    conceptual_soundness: bool
    data_quality_verified: bool
    implementation_correct: bool
    performance_adequate: bool
    sensitivity_analyzed: bool
    
    # Metriken
    ece_score: float
    ood_recall: float
    backtest_sharpe: float
    max_drawdown: float
    
    # Governance Gates
    all_gates_passed: bool
    failed_gates: List[str]
    
    # Empfehlung
    recommendation: str  # "APPROVE", "REJECT", "CONDITIONAL_APPROVE"
    conditions: List[str]
    
    notes: str

class ModelRegistry:
    """
    Zentrale Model Registry mit vollstaendiger Governance.
    SR 11-7 compliant.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, registry_path: str):
        self.registry_path = registry_path
        self.models: Dict[str, List[ModelVersion]] = {}
        self.validations: Dict[str, List[ValidationReport]] = {}
        self.load()
    
    def register_model(
        self,
        model_id: str,
        version: str,
        code_hash: str,
        config_hash: str,
        created_by: str,
        risk_tier: ModelRiskTier
    ) -> ModelVersion:
        """
        Registriert neue Modell-Version.
        PFLICHT: Alle Hashes muessen unique sein (keine Duplikate).
        """
        # Pruefe auf Duplikat-Hashes
        if model_id in self.models:
            for existing_version in self.models[model_id]:
                if existing_version.code_hash == code_hash:
                    raise ValueError(
                        f"Model mit identischem Code-Hash bereits registriert: "
                        f"{model_id} v{existing_version.version}"
                    )
        
        # Dependency-Hash berechnen
        dependency_hash = self._compute_dependency_hash()
        
        model_version = ModelVersion(
            model_id=model_id,
            version=version,
            created_at=datetime.utcnow(),
            created_by=created_by,
            status=ModelStatus.DEVELOPMENT,
            risk_tier=risk_tier,
            code_hash=code_hash,
            config_hash=config_hash,
            dependency_hash=dependency_hash,
            validation_metrics={},
            backtest_metrics={},
            oos_metrics={}
        )
        
        if model_id not in self.models:
            self.models[model_id] = []
        self.models[model_id].append(model_version)
        
        self.save()
        return model_version
    
    def submit_for_validation(
        self,
        model_id: str,
        version: str,
        validation_metrics: Dict[str, float],
        backtest_metrics: Dict[str, float],
        oos_metrics: Dict[str, float]
    ) -> None:
        """
        Submitted Modell zur unabhaengigen Validation.
        PFLICHT: Alle erforderlichen Metriken muessen vorhanden sein.
        """
        model_version = self._get_version(model_id, version)
        
        # Validate required metrics
        required_metrics = {
            'validation': ['ece', 'ood_recall', 'calibration_error'],
            'backtest': ['sharpe_ratio', 'max_drawdown', 'win_rate'],
            'oos': ['oos_sharpe', 'oos_return', 'oos_volatility']
        }
        
        for metric in required_metrics['validation']:
            if metric not in validation_metrics:
                raise ValueError(f"Missing validation metric: {metric}")
        
        model_version.validation_metrics = validation_metrics
        model_version.backtest_metrics = backtest_metrics
        model_version.oos_metrics = oos_metrics
        model_version.status = ModelStatus.VALIDATION
        
        self.save()
    
    def add_validation_report(
        self,
        model_id: str,
        version: str,
        validator_name: str,
        report: ValidationReport
    ) -> None:
        """
        Fuegt unabhaengigen Validierungsbericht hinzu.
        PFLICHT: Validator darf nicht Model-Entwickler sein.
        """
        model_version = self._get_version(model_id, version)
        
        if model_version.created_by == validator_name:
            raise ValueError(
                "Validator darf nicht identisch mit Model-Entwickler sein. "
                "Unabhaengige Validation erforderlich."
            )
        
        model_version.validator_name = validator_name
        model_version.validation_date = datetime.utcnow()
        
        if model_id not in self.validations:
            self.validations[model_id] = []
        self.validations[model_id].append(report)
        
        self.save()
    
    def approve_model(
        self,
        model_id: str,
        version: str,
        approved_by: str,
        conditions: Optional[List[str]] = None
    ) -> None:
        """
        Genehmigt Modell fuer Deployment.
        PFLICHT: Validation Report muss existieren und positiv sein.
        PFLICHT: Alle Governance Gates muessen bestanden sein.
        """
        model_version = self._get_version(model_id, version)
        
        # Check validation exists
        if model_version.validator_name is None:
            raise ValueError(
                f"Model {model_id} v{version} hat keine Validation. "
                "Validation erforderlich vor Approval."
            )
        
        # Check validation report
        validation_reports = self.validations.get(model_id, [])
        relevant_reports = [r for r in validation_reports if r.version == version]
        
        if not relevant_reports:
            raise ValueError(f"Kein Validierungsbericht fuer {model_id} v{version}")
        
        latest_report = relevant_reports[-1]
        
        if latest_report.recommendation == "REJECT":
            raise ValueError(
                f"Validation empfiehlt REJECT fuer {model_id} v{version}. "
                f"Deployment blockiert."
            )
        
        if not latest_report.all_gates_passed:
            raise ValueError(
                f"Nicht alle Governance Gates bestanden: {latest_report.failed_gates}"
            )
        
        # Approve
        model_version.status = ModelStatus.APPROVED
        model_version.approved_by = approved_by
        model_version.approval_date = datetime.utcnow()
        
        if conditions:
            model_version.change_log.append(
                f"Approved with conditions: {', '.join(conditions)}"
            )
        
        self.save()
    
    def deploy_model(
        self,
        model_id: str,
        version: str
    ) -> None:
        """
        Markiert Modell als deployed.
        PFLICHT: Model muss APPROVED status haben.
        """
        model_version = self._get_version(model_id, version)
        
        if model_version.status != ModelStatus.APPROVED:
            raise ValueError(
                f"Model {model_id} v{version} ist nicht approved. "
                f"Aktueller Status: {model_version.status.value}. "
                "Deployment VERBOTEN."
            )
        
        # Deprecate alte deployed versions
        if model_id in self.models:
            for v in self.models[model_id]:
                if v.version != version and v.status == ModelStatus.DEPLOYED:
                    v.status = ModelStatus.DEPRECATED
                    v.change_log.append(
                        f"Deprecated by deployment of v{version} at {datetime.utcnow()}"
                    )
        
        model_version.status = ModelStatus.DEPLOYED
        model_version.change_log.append(
            f"Deployed at {datetime.utcnow()}"
        )
        
        self.save()
    
    def rollback_model(
        self,
        model_id: str,
        from_version: str,
        to_version: str,
        reason: str
    ) -> None:
        """
        Rollback zu vorheriger Version.
        PFLICHT: to_version muss DEPLOYED oder APPROVED sein.
        """
        current_version = self._get_version(model_id, from_version)
        target_version = self._get_version(model_id, to_version)
        
        if target_version.status not in [ModelStatus.DEPLOYED, ModelStatus.APPROVED]:
            raise ValueError(
                f"Rollback-Target {to_version} muss DEPLOYED oder APPROVED sein. "
                f"Aktueller Status: {target_version.status.value}"
            )
        
        # Suspend current version
        current_version.status = ModelStatus.SUSPENDED
        current_version.change_log.append(
            f"Suspended and rolled back from at {datetime.utcnow()}. Reason: {reason}"
        )
        
        # Re-deploy target version
        target_version.status = ModelStatus.DEPLOYED
        target_version.change_log.append(
            f"Rolled back to from v{from_version} at {datetime.utcnow()}. Reason: {reason}"
        )
        
        self.save()
    
    def get_deployed_version(self, model_id: str) -> Optional[ModelVersion]:
        """Gibt aktuell deployed Version zurueck."""
        if model_id not in self.models:
            return None
        
        deployed = [v for v in self.models[model_id] if v.status == ModelStatus.DEPLOYED]
        return deployed[0] if deployed else None
    
    def _get_version(self, model_id: str, version: str) -> ModelVersion:
        """Helper: Holt spezifische Version oder wirft KeyError."""
        if model_id not in self.models:
            raise KeyError(f"Model {model_id} nicht in Registry")
        
        versions = [v for v in self.models[model_id] if v.version == version]
        if not versions:
            raise KeyError(f"Version {version} von Model {model_id} nicht gefunden")
        
        return versions[0]
    
    def _compute_dependency_hash(self) -> str:
        """Berechnet Hash aller Dependencies."""
        # In Praxis: requirements.txt + Python version hashen
        return hashlib.sha256(b"dependencies").hexdigest()[:16]
    
    def save(self) -> None:
        """Speichert Registry."""
        data = {
            'models': {
                mid: [self._serialize_version(v) for v in versions]
                for mid, versions in self.models.items()
            },
            'validations': {
                mid: [self._serialize_report(r) for r in reports]
                for mid, reports in self.validations.items()
            }
        }
        with open(self.registry_path, 'w') as f:
            json.dump(data, f, indent=2, default=str)
    
    def load(self) -> None:
        """Laedt Registry."""
        try:
            with open(self.registry_path) as f:
                data = json.load(f)
            # Deserialisierung hier implementieren
        except FileNotFoundError:
            pass
    
    def _serialize_version(self, v: ModelVersion) -> dict:
        """Serialisiert ModelVersion."""
        return {
            'model_id': v.model_id,
            'version': v.version,
            'created_at': v.created_at.isoformat(),
            'created_by': v.created_by,
            'status': v.status.value,
            'risk_tier': v.risk_tier.value,
            'code_hash': v.code_hash,
            'config_hash': v.config_hash,
            'dependency_hash': v.dependency_hash,
            'validation_metrics': v.validation_metrics,
            'backtest_metrics': v.backtest_metrics,
            'oos_metrics': v.oos_metrics,
            'validator_name': v.validator_name,
            'validation_date': v.validation_date.isoformat() if v.validation_date else None,
            'approval_date': v.approval_date.isoformat() if v.approval_date else None,
            'approved_by': v.approved_by,
            'change_log': v.change_log,
            'assumptions': v.assumptions,
            'limitations': v.limitations
        }
    
    def _serialize_report(self, r: ValidationReport) -> dict:
        """Serialisiert ValidationReport."""
        return {
            'model_id': r.model_id,
            'version': r.version,
            'validator_name': r.validator_name,
            'validation_date': r.validation_date.isoformat(),
            'conceptual_soundness': r.conceptual_soundness,
            'data_quality_verified': r.data_quality_verified,
            'implementation_correct': r.implementation_correct,
            'performance_adequate': r.performance_adequate,
            'sensitivity_analyzed': r.sensitivity_analyzed,
            'ece_score': r.ece_score,
            'ood_recall': r.ood_recall,
            'backtest_sharpe': r.backtest_sharpe,
            'max_drawdown': r.max_drawdown,
            'all_gates_passed': r.all_gates_passed,
            'failed_gates': r.failed_gates,
            'recommendation': r.recommendation,
            'conditions': r.conditions,
            'notes': r.notes
        }
```

### Backtest Governance

```python
# jarvis/governance/backtest_governance.py

@dataclass
class BacktestConfig:
    """Backtest-Konfiguration mit Reproducibility-Guarantee."""
    start_date: datetime
    end_date: datetime
    initial_capital: float
    transaction_costs: float
    slippage_model: str
    random_seed: int
    
    # Governance
    config_hash: str
    approved_by: Optional[str] = None

class BacktestGovernance:
    """
    Governance fuer Backtests.
    Verhindert Look-Ahead Bias, Data Snooping, Overfitting.
    """
    
    # Walk-Forward Parameters
    TRAIN_WINDOW_MIN = 365  # Tage
    TEST_WINDOW = 90        # Tage
    MIN_TRADES = 30         # Minimum Trades in Test Period
    
    def validate_backtest_config(
        self,
        config: BacktestConfig
    ) -> bool:
        """
        Validiert Backtest-Konfiguration.
        PFLICHT: Keine Data Leakage.
        """
        # Train Period >= 365 Tage
        train_days = (config.end_date - config.start_date).days
        if train_days < self.TRAIN_WINDOW_MIN:
            raise ValueError(
                f"Train window {train_days} Tage < minimum {self.TRAIN_WINDOW_MIN}"
            )
        
        # Transaction Costs realistisch
        if config.transaction_costs < 0.0001:  # 1 bps minimum
            raise ValueError(
                "Transaction costs zu niedrig. Minimum 1 bps erforderlich."
            )
        
        return True
    
    def enforce_walk_forward(
        self,
        total_data_days: int
    ) -> List[tuple]:
        """
        Erzwingt Walk-Forward Validation.
        Returns: Liste von (train_start, train_end, test_start, test_end) Tuples
        """
        splits = []
        current_day = 0
        
        while current_day + self.TRAIN_WINDOW_MIN + self.TEST_WINDOW <= total_data_days:
            train_start = current_day
            train_end = current_day + self.TRAIN_WINDOW_MIN
            test_start = train_end
            test_end = test_start + self.TEST_WINDOW
            
            splits.append((train_start, train_end, test_start, test_end))
            
            # Slide forward
            current_day += self.TEST_WINDOW
        
        return splits
```

### SR 11-7 Alignment Checklist

```python
class SR11_7_Compliance:
    """
    Federal Reserve SR 11-7 Model Risk Management Checklist.
    """
    
    REQUIRED_COMPONENTS = [
        "model_development_documentation",
        "model_validation",
        "governance_and_controls",
        "policies_and_procedures",
        "model_inventory",
        "three_lines_of_defense",
        "model_risk_rating",
        "ongoing_monitoring",
        "issue_management",
        "board_reporting"
    ]
    
    def check_compliance(
        self,
        model_id: str,
        registry: ModelRegistry
    ) -> Dict[str, bool]:
        """
        Prueft SR 11-7 Compliance fuer Modell.
        """
        model_version = registry.get_deployed_version(model_id)
        if not model_version:
            return {comp: False for comp in self.REQUIRED_COMPONENTS}
        
        compliance = {}
        
        # Development Documentation
        compliance['model_development_documentation'] = (
            len(model_version.assumptions) > 0 and
            len(model_version.limitations) > 0 and
            len(model_version.change_log) > 0
        )
        
        # Validation
        compliance['model_validation'] = (
            model_version.validator_name is not None and
            model_version.validator_name != model_version.created_by
        )
        
        # Governance
        compliance['governance_and_controls'] = (
            model_version.status == ModelStatus.DEPLOYED and
            model_version.approved_by is not None
        )
        
        # Model Inventory
        compliance['model_inventory'] = True  # Registry exists
        
        # Risk Rating
        compliance['model_risk_rating'] = (
            model_version.risk_tier is not None
        )
        
        # Ongoing Monitoring
        compliance['ongoing_monitoring'] = True  # Via continuous validation
        
        # Default others
        for comp in self.REQUIRED_COMPONENTS:
            if comp not in compliance:
                compliance[comp] = False
        
        return compliance
```

---

```python
# jarvis/governance/model_registry.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import hashlib
import json
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
from datetime import datetime
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any
import numpy as np

@dataclass
class ModelEntry:
    """Registry-Eintrag fuer ein Modell."""
    model_id:          str
    version:           str
    created_at:        str
    deployed_at:       Optional[str]
    status:            str   # CANDIDATE, SHADOW, ACTIVE, ARCHIVED, FAILED
    ece:               float
    ood_recall:        float
    stress_passed:     bool
    monte_carlo_var95: float
    model_hash:        str
    is_active:         bool
    notes:             str


class ModelRegistry:
    """
    Model Governance: Versionierung, A/B-Vergleich, Shadow-Deployment.
    Kein Deployment ohne vollstaendige Zertifizierung.
    """

    REQUIRED_ECE         = 0.05
    REQUIRED_OOD_RECALL  = 0.90
    REQUIRED_STRESS_PASS = True

    def __init__(self, registry_path: Optional[Path] = None):
        self._models: Dict[str, ModelEntry] = {}
        self._path = registry_path
        self._active_model_id: Optional[str] = None

    def register_candidate(
        self,
        model_id:  str,
        version:   str,
        params:    Dict[str, Any],
    ) -> ModelEntry:
        """Registriert ein Kandidaten-Modell. Startet als CANDIDATE."""
        model_hash = hashlib.sha256(
            json.dumps(params, sort_keys=True).encode()
        ).hexdigest()[:16]

        entry = ModelEntry(
            model_id=model_id,
            version=version,
            created_at=datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            deployed_at=None,
            status="CANDIDATE",
            ece=1.0,
            ood_recall=0.0,
            stress_passed=False,
            monte_carlo_var95=-1.0,
            model_hash=model_hash,
            is_active=False,
            notes="",
        )
        self._models[model_id] = entry
        return entry

    def certify(
        self,
        model_id:          str,
        ece:               float,
        ood_recall:        float,
        stress_passed:     bool,
        monte_carlo_var95: float,
        notes:             str = "",
    ) -> ModelEntry:
        """
        Zertifiziert Modell. Prueft alle Gates.
        Setzt status=SHADOW wenn bestanden.
        Wirft RuntimeError wenn Gates nicht bestanden.
        """
        if model_id not in self._models:
            raise KeyError(f"Modell '{model_id}' nicht in Registry")

        entry = self._models[model_id]

        # Alle Gates pruefen
        failures = []
        if ece > self.REQUIRED_ECE:
            failures.append(f"ECE={ece:.4f} > {self.REQUIRED_ECE}")
        if ood_recall < self.REQUIRED_OOD_RECALL:
            failures.append(f"OOD_Recall={ood_recall:.3f} < {self.REQUIRED_OOD_RECALL}")
        if not stress_passed and self.REQUIRED_STRESS_PASS:
            failures.append("Stress-Test nicht bestanden")

        if failures:
            entry.status = "FAILED"
            entry.notes  = f"Zertifizierung fehlgeschlagen: {'; '.join(failures)}"
            raise RuntimeError(
                f"MODEL_CERTIFICATION_FAILED fuer '{model_id}': {'; '.join(failures)}"
            )

        entry.ece               = float(ece)
        entry.ood_recall        = float(ood_recall)
        entry.stress_passed     = stress_passed
        entry.monte_carlo_var95 = float(monte_carlo_var95)
        entry.status            = "SHADOW"  # Zuerst Shadow, dann Active
        entry.notes             = notes
        return entry

    def promote_to_active(self, model_id: str) -> ModelEntry:
        """
        Befoerdert SHADOW-Modell zu ACTIVE.
        Archiviert vorheriges ACTIVE-Modell.
        """
        if model_id not in self._models:
            raise KeyError(f"Modell '{model_id}' nicht in Registry")

        entry = self._models[model_id]
        if entry.status != "SHADOW":
            raise RuntimeError(
                f"Nur SHADOW-Modelle koennen promoted werden. Status: {entry.status}"
            )

        # Altes ACTIVE archivieren
        if self._active_model_id and self._active_model_id in self._models:
            old = self._models[self._active_model_id]
            old.status    = "ARCHIVED"
            old.is_active = False

        entry.status      = "ACTIVE"
        entry.is_active   = True
        entry.deployed_at = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
        self._active_model_id = model_id
        return entry

    def rollback(self) -> Optional[ModelEntry]:
        """
        Rollt auf letztes ARCHIVED Modell zurueck.
        """
        archived = [
            m for m in self._models.values()
            if m.status == "ARCHIVED" and m.stress_passed
        ]
        if not archived:
            return None

        # Neuestes Archived-Modell finden
        latest = sorted(archived, key=lambda m: m.deployed_at or "", reverse=True)[0]

        # Aktuelles ACTIVE deaktivieren
        if self._active_model_id and self._active_model_id in self._models:
            current = self._models[self._active_model_id]
            current.status    = "ARCHIVED"
            current.is_active = False

        latest.status    = "ACTIVE"
        latest.is_active = True
        self._active_model_id = latest.model_id
        return latest

    def ab_compare(
        self,
        model_id_a: str,
        model_id_b: str,
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """A/B-Vergleich zweier Modelle."""
        if model_id_a not in self._models or model_id_b not in self._models:
            raise KeyError("Eines der Modelle nicht in Registry")

        a = self._models[model_id_a]
        b = self._models[model_id_b]

        winner = model_id_a if a.ece < b.ece else model_id_b
        return {
            "model_a": {"id": model_id_a, "ece": a.ece, "ood_recall": a.ood_recall},
            "model_b": {"id": model_id_b, "ece": b.ece, "ood_recall": b.ood_recall},
            "winner":  winner,
            "ece_diff": abs(a.ece - b.ece),
        }
```

## SESSION 36: PERFORMANCE CERTIFICATION ENGINE

**Abhaengigkeiten:** S09, S10, S15, S28, S29, S34
**Zeit:** 70-85 min
**Datei:** jarvis/governance/performance_certification.py

### Prinzip

Deployment NIEMALS ohne vollstaendige Zertifizierung.
Alle 8 Zertifizierungs-Kriterien muessen bestanden werden.

```python
# jarvis/governance/performance_certification.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
import json
from dataclasses import dataclass
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, List, Optional

@dataclass
class CertificationResult:
    """Vollstaendiges Zertifizierungs-Ergebnis."""
    model_id:          str
    timestamp:         str
    calibration_ok:    bool   # ECE < 0.05
    ood_ok:            bool   # Recall >= 0.90
    stress_ok:         bool   # Alle Szenarien bestanden
    monte_carlo_ok:    bool   # VaR95 innerhalb Limit
    slippage_ok:       bool   # Slippage innerhalb Budget
    capital_alloc_ok:  bool   # Allocation Engine zertifiziert
    reproducibility_ok: bool  # Deterministisch + reproduzierbar
    integrity_ok:      bool   # Hash-Chain + Manifest verified
    all_passed:        bool   # True wenn ALLE 8 bestanden
    deployment_cleared: bool  # Equivalent zu all_passed
    failures:          List[str]
    certification_hash: str


class PerformanceCertificationEngine:
    """
    Deployment-Zertifizierung: 8 Pflicht-Kriterien.
    Kein Deployment ohne all_passed == True.
    Kein Soft-Warning. Nur Hard-Block.
    """

    # Certification Thresholds (hash-gesichert in THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json)
    ECE_LIMIT          = 0.05
    OOD_RECALL_LIMIT   = 0.90
    MONTE_CARLO_VAR_LIMIT = -0.20   # Max -20% VaR95
    MAX_SLIPPAGE_PCT   = 0.01       # Max 1% Slippage

    def certify(
        self,
        model_id:              str,
        ece:                   float,
        ood_recall_historical: float,
        ood_recall_synthetic:  float,
        stress_scenarios_passed: List[str],
        stress_scenarios_required: List[str],
        monte_carlo_var95:     float,
        avg_slippage_pct:      float,
        capital_alloc_validated: bool,
        reproducibility_hash:  str,
        integrity_hash:        str,
        expected_integrity_hash: str,
    ) -> CertificationResult:
        """
        Prueft alle 8 Zertifizierungs-Kriterien.
        Gibt CertificationResult zurueck.
        Wirft RuntimeError wenn deployment_cleared == False (Hard-Block).
        """
        failures = []

        # 1. Calibration
        calibration_ok = ece < self.ECE_LIMIT
        if not calibration_ok:
            failures.append(f"CALIBRATION: ECE={ece:.4f} >= {self.ECE_LIMIT}")

        # 2. OOD
        ood_ok = (
            ood_recall_historical >= self.OOD_RECALL_LIMIT and
            ood_recall_synthetic >= self.OOD_RECALL_LIMIT
        )
        if not ood_ok:
            failures.append(
                f"OOD: hist={ood_recall_historical:.3f}, "
                f"synth={ood_recall_synthetic:.3f} (limit={self.OOD_RECALL_LIMIT})"
            )

        # 3. Stress Tests
        missing_scenarios = set(stress_scenarios_required) - set(stress_scenarios_passed)
        stress_ok = len(missing_scenarios) == 0
        if not stress_ok:
            failures.append(f"STRESS: Fehlende Szenarien: {missing_scenarios}")

        # 4. Monte Carlo
        monte_carlo_ok = monte_carlo_var95 >= self.MONTE_CARLO_VAR_LIMIT
        if not monte_carlo_ok:
            failures.append(
                f"MONTE_CARLO: VaR95={monte_carlo_var95:.3f} < {self.MONTE_CARLO_VAR_LIMIT}"
            )

        # 5. Slippage
        slippage_ok = avg_slippage_pct <= self.MAX_SLIPPAGE_PCT
        if not slippage_ok:
            failures.append(
                f"SLIPPAGE: {avg_slippage_pct:.4f} > {self.MAX_SLIPPAGE_PCT}"
            )

        # 6. Capital Allocation
        capital_alloc_ok = capital_alloc_validated
        if not capital_alloc_ok:
            failures.append("CAPITAL_ALLOCATION: Nicht validiert")

        # 7. Reproducibility
        reproducibility_ok = bool(reproducibility_hash)
        if not reproducibility_ok:
            failures.append("REPRODUCIBILITY: Kein Reproduzierbarkeits-Hash")

        # 8. Integrity
        integrity_ok = (integrity_hash == expected_integrity_hash)
        if not integrity_ok:
            failures.append(
                f"INTEGRITY: Hash-Mismatch. "
                f"Erwartet={expected_integrity_hash[:8]}..., "
                f"Berechnet={integrity_hash[:8]}..."
            )

        all_passed = len(failures) == 0

        import hashlib
        cert_data = {
            "model_id": model_id,
            "ece": ece,
            "ood_hist": ood_recall_historical,
            "ood_synth": ood_recall_synthetic,
            "stress_ok": stress_ok,
            "var95": monte_carlo_var95,
            "all_passed": all_passed,
        }
        cert_hash = hashlib.sha256(
            json.dumps(cert_data, sort_keys=True).encode()
        ).hexdigest()[:16]

        result = CertificationResult(
            model_id=model_id,
            timestamp=datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            calibration_ok=calibration_ok,
            ood_ok=ood_ok,
            stress_ok=stress_ok,
            monte_carlo_ok=monte_carlo_ok,
            slippage_ok=slippage_ok,
            capital_alloc_ok=capital_alloc_ok,
            reproducibility_ok=reproducibility_ok,
            integrity_ok=integrity_ok,
            all_passed=all_passed,
            deployment_cleared=all_passed,
            failures=failures,
            certification_hash=cert_hash,
        )

        # Hard Block: KEIN Deployment ohne Zertifizierung
        if not all_passed:
            raise RuntimeError(
                f"DEPLOYMENT_BLOCKED fuer '{model_id}'. "
                f"Fehlgeschlagene Gates ({len(failures)}): "
                + "; ".join(failures)
            )

        return result
```

### Tests

```python
# tests/unit/governance/test_certification.py
import pytest
from jarvis.governance.performance_certification import PerformanceCertificationEngine

REQUIRED = ["2008_CRASH", "COVID", "FLASH_CRASH", "SYNTHETIC_VOL"]

def certify_ok(engine):
    return engine.certify(
        model_id="m1",
        ece=0.03, ood_recall_historical=0.92, ood_recall_synthetic=0.91,
        stress_scenarios_passed=REQUIRED, stress_scenarios_required=REQUIRED,
        monte_carlo_var95=-0.12, avg_slippage_pct=0.005,
        capital_alloc_validated=True,
        reproducibility_hash="abc123", integrity_hash="hash_ok",
        expected_integrity_hash="hash_ok",
    )

def test_full_pass():
    eng = PerformanceCertificationEngine()
    result = certify_ok(eng)
    assert result.all_passed == True
    assert result.deployment_cleared == True
    assert result.failures == []

def test_ece_failure_blocks():
    eng = PerformanceCertificationEngine()
    with pytest.raises(RuntimeError, match="DEPLOYMENT_BLOCKED"):
        eng.certify(
            model_id="m2",
            ece=0.08,  # TOO HIGH
            ood_recall_historical=0.92, ood_recall_synthetic=0.91,
            stress_scenarios_passed=REQUIRED, stress_scenarios_required=REQUIRED,
            monte_carlo_var95=-0.12, avg_slippage_pct=0.005,
            capital_alloc_validated=True,
            reproducibility_hash="abc", integrity_hash="ok", expected_integrity_hash="ok",
        )

def test_missing_stress_scenario_blocks():
    eng = PerformanceCertificationEngine()
    with pytest.raises(RuntimeError, match="DEPLOYMENT_BLOCKED"):
        eng.certify(
            model_id="m3",
            ece=0.03, ood_recall_historical=0.92, ood_recall_synthetic=0.91,
            stress_scenarios_passed=["2008_CRASH"],  # MISSING 3 SCENARIOS
            stress_scenarios_required=REQUIRED,
            monte_carlo_var95=-0.12, avg_slippage_pct=0.005,
            capital_alloc_validated=True,
            reproducibility_hash="abc", integrity_hash="ok", expected_integrity_hash="ok",
        )

def test_integrity_mismatch_blocks():
    eng = PerformanceCertificationEngine()
    with pytest.raises(RuntimeError, match="DEPLOYMENT_BLOCKED"):
        eng.certify(
            model_id="m4",
            ece=0.03, ood_recall_historical=0.92, ood_recall_synthetic=0.91,
            stress_scenarios_passed=REQUIRED, stress_scenarios_required=REQUIRED,
            monte_carlo_var95=-0.12, avg_slippage_pct=0.005,
            capital_alloc_validated=True,
            reproducibility_hash="abc",
            integrity_hash="WRONG_HASH",          # MISMATCH
            expected_integrity_hash="CORRECT_HASH",
        )
```

# SESSION 37: SYSTEM ADDENDUM - ARCHITECTURE & METRICS
# Version: 5.0-elite | Comprehensive System Documentation

---

## SYSTEM INTERACTION ARCHITECTURE

### END-TO-END MASTER DATA FLOW PIPELINE (AUTORITATIV)

Dies ist die einzige autoritative Datenfluß-Definition. Alle Module referenzieren diese Pipeline.
Keine impliziten Datenpfade erlaubt. Jeder Datentransfer muss in dieser Definition erscheinen.

```
LAYER HIERARCHY (Enforcement Priority):
  P0  Integrity / Hash Chain          (S01)       — blocks ALL if violated
  P1  Global State Controller         (S35)       — singleton, no bypass permitted
  P2  OOD Ensemble Gate               (S10)       — blocks P3–P9 if OOD=True
  P3  Regime Engine                   (S05)       — required before P4–P9
  P4  Volatility Layer                (S16–S17)   — required before P5–P9
  P5  Risk Engine                     (S17)       — required before P6–P9
  P6  Strategy Layer                  (S26)       — required before P7–P9
  P7  Portfolio Context               (S29–S30)   — required before P8–P9
  P8  Confidence Engine               (S08, S11)  — required before P9
  P9  Visual Output                   (S13)       — terminal, ZERO write permissions
```

```
```
LIVE DATA INTEGRITY GATE — STAGE 0 (MODE_LIVE_ANALYTICAL and MODE_HYBRID only)

In MODE_HISTORICAL: gate is bypassed (data pre-validated in store).
In MODE_LIVE_ANALYTICAL and MODE_HYBRID (live window):
  All incoming ticks and candles must pass ALL of the following checks
  before being admitted to the pipeline as StandardizedMarketDataObject:

  CHECK 1 — MISSING DATA:
    No required OHLCV field may be None, NaN, or Inf.
    volume must be > 0.
    Failure → FM-03 (DATA_GAP) triggered for affected asset.

  CHECK 2 — TIMESTAMP CONTINUITY:
    sequence_id must be monotonically increasing per symbol/timeframe.
    Gap between current and previous timestamp must not exceed:
      Crypto:      2 * timeframe_seconds (24/7)
      Forex:       5 * timeframe_seconds (during session)
      Indices:     1 * timeframe_seconds (during session hours)
      Commodities: 3 * timeframe_seconds (during session)
    Failure → FM-03 triggered; is_stale = True on object.

  CHECK 3 — SPREAD ANOMALY DETECTION:
    spread_bps must be < max_entry_spread_bps * 2.0 (from StrategyObject.EntryModel).
    If spread_bps >= threshold: FM-06 (SPREAD_ANOMALY) triggered.
    Object is passed through but flagged; no new entries permitted for asset.

  CHECK 4 — OUTLIER FILTER (Robust Z-Score):
    close price must satisfy: |z_score| < 5.0
    where z_score = (close - rolling_median) / rolling_MAD
    rolling window: 20 candles (rolling_median and rolling_MAD from buffer)
    Failure → quality_score reduced by 0.30; object passed as SUSPECT.
    If quality_score < 0.5 after reduction → FM-03 triggered.

  CHECK 5 — ASSET CLASS VALIDATION:
    asset_class must resolve in VOLATILITY_SCALING (38_MULTI_ASSET_UPGRADE.md).
    session_tag must be valid for declared asset_class.
    Failure → FM-03 triggered; object rejected.

  ON INTEGRITY FAILURE:
    - Trigger appropriate Failure Mode (FM-03 or FM-06) via failure_handler.py
    - meta_uncertainty increases per IMPACT_TABLE
    - Confidence decreases per Failure Mode rules
    - System does NOT halt unless FM rules mandate it
    - All failures logged to structured audit log

  ENFORCEMENT:
    This gate is implemented in: jarvis/core/live_data_integrity_gate.py
    LiveDataProvider.ingest_tick() calls this gate before buffering.
    No StandardizedMarketDataObject from live source may bypass this gate.
```

[0. LIVE DATA INTEGRITY GATE — applies before Stage 1 in live/hybrid modes]
     INPUT:   Raw tick/candle from LiveDataProvider
     OUTPUT:  StandardizedMarketDataObject (validated) or FM trigger
     READ:    VolatilityState rolling buffer, StrategyObject spread thresholds
     WRITE:   meta_uncertainty (via ctrl) if integrity fails
     GATE:    All 5 checks must pass → else FM-03 or FM-06
     DEPS:    S03 (market_data_provider.py), failure_handler.py
              │
              ▼
[1. MARKET DATA]
     INPUT:   Raw OHLCV, order book snapshots, tick data per asset_id
     OUTPUT:  EnhancedMarketData (validated, gap-flagged, session-tagged,
              spread_bps, liquidity_regime)
     READ:    External feeds, config/assets.yaml
     WRITE:   EnhancedMarketData object — data_layer.py ONLY
     GATE:    quality_score >= 0.5 → else STOP, log FM-03
     DEPS:    S03, S19 (microstructure advisory)
              │
              ▼
[2. NVU NORMALIZATION]
     INPUT:   EnhancedMarketData.volatility, asset_class
     OUTPUT:  nvu_score (float ≥ 0, normalized relative to asset baseline)
     READ:    VOLATILITY_SCALING constants (38_MULTI_ASSET_UPGRADE.md §3) — IMMUTABLE
     WRITE:   FeatureVector.nvu_score — feature_registry.py ONLY
     GATE:    asset_class must resolve in VOLATILITY_SCALING → else STOP
     RULE:    VOLATILITY_SCALING values are FROZEN. No runtime override permitted.
     DEPS:    S04, 38_MULTI_ASSET_UPGRADE.md
              │
              ▼
[3. REGIME ENGINE]
     INPUT:   FeatureVector (including nvu_score), RegimeState (read-only)
     OUTPUT:  RegimeResult {regime: str, confidence: float, probs: Dict[str,float]}
     READ:    FeatureVector, GlobalSystemState.regime (snapshot)
     WRITE:   RegimeState — via GlobalSystemStateController.update() ONLY
     GATE:    drift_severity < 0.8 (Drift Gate); OOD Gate (P2)
     RULE:    Cannot write StrategyState or PortfolioState directly
     FAILURE: confidence < 0.40 → triggers FM-01 (UNDEFINED_REGIME)
     DEPS:    S05, S10
              │
              ▼
[4. VOLATILITY LAYER]
     INPUT:   RegimeResult, nvu_score, microstructure_vol_idx
     OUTPUT:  VolatilityResult {realized_vol, forecast_vol, vol_regime,
              vol_percentile, vol_spike_flag}
     READ:    RegimeState (snapshot), NVU output from FeatureVector
     WRITE:   VolatilityState — via GlobalSystemStateController.update() ONLY
     GATE:    vol_regime must align with RegimeResult.regime or emit WARNING
     FAILURE: nvu_normalized > 3.0 or vol_percentile > 0.95 → FM-02
     DEPS:    S16, S17
              │
              ▼
[5. STRATEGY LAYER]
     INPUT:   RegimeResult, VolatilityResult, GlobalSystemState snapshot
     OUTPUT:  StrategyObject (canonical schema — see S26)
     READ:    RegimeState, VolatilityState, GlobalSystemState (all read-only)
     WRITE:   StrategyState — via GlobalSystemStateController.update() ONLY
     GATE:    Regime must not be UNKNOWN; vol_spike_flag must be False for new entries
     RULE:    Adaptive Weighting ONLY operates through StrategyObject.Weight_Model
     FAILURE: UNKNOWN regime → FM-01; vol spike → FM-02 size scalar applied
     DEPS:    S26, S05
              │
              ▼
[6. RISK ENGINE]
     INPUT:   StrategyObject, VolatilityResult, PortfolioState snapshot
     OUTPUT:  RiskDecision {position_size, var_estimate, risk_mode, compression_flag}
     READ:    StrategyState, VolatilityState, PortfolioState (all read-only snapshots)
     WRITE:   risk_mode, risk_compression fields only — via GlobalSystemStateController
     GATE:    VaR >= -0.20 (Monte Carlo); drawdown < 0.15; slippage < 0.01
     RULE:    Cannot reduce confidence floors. Cannot bypass VaR gate. No exceptions.
     FAILURE: Extreme correlation → FM-04; vol spike → FM-02 size scalar
     DEPS:    S17, S40
              │
              ▼
[7. PORTFOLIO CONTEXT]
     INPUT:   RiskDecision, current_positions (read-only PortfolioState snapshot)
     OUTPUT:  PortfolioDecision {allocation, cross_asset_exposure, correlation_matrix,
              diversification_ratio}
     READ:    PortfolioState snapshot, RiskDecision
     WRITE:   PortfolioState — via GlobalSystemStateController.update() ONLY
     GATE:    All correlation matrix values must be finite → else FM-04
     FAILURE: mean pairwise correlation > 0.85 → FM-04; illiquid session → FM-05
     DEPS:    S29, S30
              │
              ▼
[8. CONFIDENCE ENGINE]
     INPUT:   All prior layer outputs, GlobalSystemState snapshot
     OUTPUT:  ConfidenceBundle {mu, sigma2, Q, S, U, R} — Systemvertrag D(t)
     READ:    ALL states (read-only snapshots only)
     WRITE:   GlobalSystemState.meta_uncertainty ONLY
     GATE:    None — Confidence Engine always runs, even in degraded mode
     RULE:    Can ONLY reduce confidence. Never fabricates certainty.
              Failure mode impacts applied via IMPACT_TABLE (see FM section below).
     DEPS:    S08, S11
              │
              ▼
[9. VISUAL OUTPUT]
     INPUT:   ConfidenceBundle, StrategyObject, PortfolioDecision
     OUTPUT:  DisplayPayload (human-readable decision support — manual use ONLY)
     READ:    ALL states (read-only snapshots)
     WRITE:   NONE — zero write permissions at this layer under any condition
     GATE:    None — always renders; failure modes shown as banners
     RULE:    This system is purely analytical. No order execution. No broker API.
     DEPS:    S13
```

## EVENT BUS FORMALIZATION (ANALYTICAL EVENT LAYER)

**Datei:** `jarvis/core/event_bus.py`
**Classification:** Analytical and research only. No execution triggers. No order events.
**Governance:** All events are immutable. All state mutation routes through `ctrl.update()`.
The event system is the sole mechanism for communicating state changes between layers.

---

### EVENT OBJECT DEFINITIONS (IMMUTABLE)

```python
# jarvis/core/event_bus.py
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional
from enum import Enum


class EventType(Enum):
    MARKET_DATA          = "market_data"
    REGIME_CHANGE        = "regime_change"
    FAILURE_MODE         = "failure_mode"
    EXPOSURE             = "exposure"
    STRATEGY_WEIGHT      = "strategy_weight_change"
    CONFIDENCE_UPDATE    = "confidence_update"


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class BaseEvent:
    # Base for all analytical events. Immutable after creation.
    event_id:    str       # UUID — unique per event
    event_type:  EventType
    timestamp:   datetime
    sequence_id: int       # Global monotonic sequence — for replay ordering
    asset_id:    Optional[str] = None   # None means system-wide event


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class MarketDataEvent(BaseEvent):
    # Emitted when a new StandardizedMarketDataObject is admitted through
    # the Live Data Integrity Gate or loaded from historical store.
    symbol:        str = ""
    timeframe:     str = ""
    close:         float = 0.0
    quality_score: float = 1.0
    gap_detected:  bool = False
    is_stale:      bool = False
    data_source:   str = "historical"   # "historical", "live", "hybrid_backfill", "hybrid_live"


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class RegimeChangeEvent(BaseEvent):
    # Emitted when RegimeState.regime changes value.
    from_regime:   str = ""
    to_regime:     str = ""
    confidence:    float = 0.0
    transition_flag: bool = True


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class FailureModeEvent(BaseEvent):
    # Emitted when a Failure Mode (FM-01..FM-06) is activated or resolved.
    failure_mode_code:   str = ""   # "FM-01", "FM-02", ..., "FM-06"
    activated:           bool = True  # True=activated, False=resolved
    trigger_condition:   str = ""   # Human-readable trigger description
    confidence_impact:   Dict[str, float] = field(default_factory=dict)
    # e.g. {"R": -0.40, "Q": -0.40} from IMPACT_TABLE


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ExposureEvent(BaseEvent):
    # Emitted when PortfolioState.gross_exposure or net_exposure changes
    # beyond the EXPOSURE_DELTA_THRESHOLD.
    prior_gross_exposure:   float = 0.0
    current_gross_exposure: float = 0.0
    prior_net_exposure:     float = 0.0
    current_net_exposure:   float = 0.0
    trigger_source:         str = ""   # "risk_engine", "portfolio_context"


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class StrategyWeightChangeEvent(BaseEvent):
    # Emitted when StrategyState.weight_scalar changes.
    # Weight may ONLY change via StrategyObject.Weight_Model (see 26-30_STRATEGY_SIM.md).
    strategy_id:     str = ""
    prior_weight:    float = 0.0
    new_weight:      float = 0.0
    regime_trigger:  str = ""   # Regime that caused the weight change


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ConfidenceUpdateEvent(BaseEvent):
    # Emitted when ConfidenceBundle values change.
    # Only emitted on permitted refresh triggers (see CONFIDENCE REFRESH LOGIC).
    prior_mu:    float = 0.0
    new_mu:      float = 0.0
    prior_Q:     float = 0.0
    new_Q:       float = 0.0
    prior_U:     float = 0.0
    new_U:       float = 0.0
    trigger:     str = ""   # One of the permitted refresh triggers
```

---

### EVENT QUEUE — DETERMINISTIC SPECIFICATION

```python
# jarvis/core/event_queue.py
from collections import deque
from typing import Iterator, List
import threading


class DeterministicEventQueue:
    """
    Deterministic FIFO event queue for the analytical event system.

    INVARIANTS (non-negotiable):
      1. FIFO ordering — events are processed in emission order
      2. No parallel mutation — single-threaded event processing
      3. All state mutation routes through ctrl.update() — never inside queue
      4. No execution events permitted — queue is analytical only
      5. Queue is not a broker interface — no order objects may enter the queue
      6. Events are immutable (frozen dataclasses) — never modified in transit
    """

    def __init__(self, max_size: int = 10_000):
        self._queue: deque = deque(maxlen=max_size)
        self._lock = threading.Lock()
        self._sequence_counter: int = 0
        self._processed_count: int = 0

    def emit(self, event: BaseEvent) -> int:
        """
        Add an event to the queue. Returns assigned sequence_id.
        Thread-safe. Raises if max_size exceeded (no silent drop).
        """
        with self._lock:
            if len(self._queue) >= self._queue.maxlen:
                raise OverflowError(
                    f"EventQueue full ({self._queue.maxlen} events). "
                    "System backpressure — reduce event rate or increase max_size."
                )
            self._sequence_counter += 1
            # Events are frozen; we trust the caller set sequence_id correctly
            self._queue.append(event)
            return self._sequence_counter

    def drain(self) -> Iterator[BaseEvent]:
        """
        Yields all pending events in FIFO order, removing them from the queue.
        Must be called from single processing thread only.
        """
        with self._lock:
            pending = list(self._queue)
            self._queue.clear()
        for event in pending:
            self._processed_count += 1
            yield event

    def peek(self) -> List[BaseEvent]:
        """Read-only view of current queue — does not consume events."""
        with self._lock:
            return list(self._queue)

    @property
    def depth(self) -> int:
        return len(self._queue)

    @property
    def processed_count(self) -> int:
        return self._processed_count
```

---

### EVENT PROPAGATION RULES (SYSTEM-WIDE)

```
EVENT PROPAGATION FLOW:
  Source Layer emits Event → EventQueue (FIFO) → EventDispatcher reads queue
  → Handler calls ctrl.update() → State updated → Next event processed

  ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
  │ Layer                   │ Emits                                 │
  ├─────────────────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Live/Historical Provider│ MarketDataEvent                       │
  │ Integrity Gate          │ FailureModeEvent (FM-03, FM-06)       │
  │ Regime Engine (P3)      │ RegimeChangeEvent                     │
  │ Failure Handler         │ FailureModeEvent (all FM types)       │
  │ Portfolio Context (P7)  │ ExposureEvent                         │
  │ Strategy Layer (P6)     │ StrategyWeightChangeEvent             │
  │ Confidence Engine (P8)  │ ConfidenceUpdateEvent                 │
  └─────────────────────────┴───────────────────────────────────────┘

PROPAGATION CONSTRAINTS:
  1. Events do NOT trigger other events inside the same dispatch cycle
     (no cascading emission — prevents infinite loops)
  2. State reads inside event handlers use snapshot from BEFORE the cycle
  3. All ctrl.update() calls happen AFTER the full event is processed
  4. Visual Output (P9) reads state AFTER all events in cycle are processed
  5. Sandbox/Research layers may read the event log but may not emit events
     during live operation (only in replay mode)

HYBRID MODE — SAME EVENT SYSTEM:
  In all three operating modes, the same DeterministicEventQueue is used.
  Historical mode: events are replayed from EventLog (see Replay Engine).
  Live mode: events emitted in real-time from LiveDataProvider and layers.
  Hybrid mode: historical events replayed until sync_point, then live events.
  The event system has no mode-specific branches — mode affects only source.
```

---

### FORBIDDEN EVENT PATTERNS

```
FORBIDDEN — Events that must never enter the queue:
  - OrderEvent (no order objects permitted)
  - BrokerConnectEvent (no broker connectivity)
  - ExecutionEvent (no execution triggers)
  - CapitalMutationEvent (no real capital changes)
  - AccountStateEvent (no broker account state)

Any event type not listed in EventType enum is rejected at emission time.
```

```
+----------------+     +-----------------+     +------------------+

   q_score>=0.5                               P2 blocks if OOD

+------------------+     +----------------+     +----------------+
                                                        |

                                                 is_ood=False

+-------------------+     +----------------+     +----------------+

 [Health Gate P7]

```

### PROBABILISTIC MODULES — PIPELINE INTEGRATION (BLOCK A)

```
Probabilistic modules (Block A) integrate into the pipeline as follows:

  Stage 3 (REGIME ENGINE):
    → RegimeTransitionEstimator.estimate() runs on observed regime history
    → RegimeTransitionMatrix stored in StrategyState (read-only for downstream)
    → most_likely_next() informs ConfidenceUpdateEvent.trigger field

  Stage 4 (VOLATILITY LAYER):
    → VolatilityTransitionMatrix updated from NVU history
    → prob_fm02_trigger() informs Confidence Engine pre-update weighting

  Stage 8 (CONFIDENCE ENGINE):
    → BayesianConfidenceEngine.update() computes posterior Q
    → Spike-up constraint enforced (regime_stable AND NOT fm_active AND quality >= 0.70)
    → Decay applied via apply_confidence_decay() if no confirmation signal

  Strategy Layer (P6):
    → WeightPosteriorEstimator.estimate() computes posterior mean per strategy
    → posterior_mean passed as input to StrategyObject.Weight_Model (read-only)

  PERMITTED OUTPUTS:
    - P6 Strategy Layer: WeightPosteriorModel.posterior_mean
    - P8 Confidence Engine: BayesianConfidenceUpdate.posterior_confidence
    - P9 Visual Output: all probability matrices and uncertainty displays

  FORBIDDEN: None of these modules trigger execution or broker connectivity.
```

## CONFIDENCE SCORE GOVERNANCE (RESEARCH STRENGTH INDICATOR)

Der Confidence Score ist ein **Research Strength Indicator** — kein Handels-Trigger.

```
DEFINITION:
  ConfidenceBundle {mu, sigma2, Q, S, U, R} ist ein Maß für die
  epistemische Qualität der aktuellen Analyse.
  Es quantifiziert, wie verlässlich die aktuelle Markteinschätzung ist.
  Es ist KEIN Handels-Signal und KEIN Auslöser für irgendeine Aktion.

ERLAUBT — Confidence Score darf:
  - Im UI als Qualitätsindikator angezeigt werden
  - Strategy-Gewichtungsmodelle informieren (via Weight_Model)
  - Research-Layer als Input dienen
  - In Scenario-Sandbox-Simulationen verwendet werden
  - In Benchmark-Analysen einbezogen werden

VERBOTEN — Confidence Score darf NICHT:
  - Execution triggern
  - Automatisch Positionen öffnen
  - Portfolio-State direkt überschreiben
  - Broker-API aufrufen
  - Irgendeine externe System-Aktion auslösen

ENFORCEMENT:
  Confidence-Output geht NUR an:
    1. Visual Output Layer (P9) — zur Anzeige
    2. Strategy Layer (P6) — via Weight_Model (read-only)
    3. Research Extensions — Scenario Sandbox, Benchmark Engine
  Jeder andere Datenpfad vom Confidence Engine ist eine Architektur-Verletzung.
```

---


### CONFIDENCE REFRESH LOGIC (MODE-AWARE)

In MODE_LIVE_ANALYTICAL and MODE_HYBRID (live window), the following rules
govern ConfidenceBundle recalculation.

**CONFIDENCE MAY ONLY UPDATE WHEN (live/hybrid):**
```
PERMITTED REFRESH TRIGGERS:
  - regime_change:             RegimeState.regime value changed
  - volatility_state_change:   VolatilityState.vol_regime or vol_spike_flag changed
  - strategy_weight_change:    StrategyState.weight_scalar changed
  - portfolio_exposure_change: PortfolioState.gross_exposure delta > threshold
  - failure_mode_trigger:      Any FM-01..FM-06 activated or deactivated

NOT PERMITTED — Confidence must NOT recalculate when:
  - A tick arrives but no state has changed
  - Regime and volatility state are identical to prior snapshot
  - No failure mode status changed
  - Only sequence_id incremented (pure data flow, no analytical change)
```

```python
# jarvis/confidence/confidence_refresh.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
def should_refresh_confidence(
    prev_state,
    curr_state,
    operating_mode: str,
) -> bool:
    """
    Returns True if confidence engine should recompute.
    HISTORICAL mode: always True (batch recompute).
    LIVE / HYBRID: only on defined state changes.
    """
    if operating_mode == "historical":
        return True

    # Live / Hybrid: only on genuine state changes
    return any([
        prev_state.regime          != curr_state.regime,
        prev_state.risk_mode       != curr_state.risk_mode,
        prev_state.strategy_mode   != curr_state.strategy_mode,
        prev_state.ood_status      != curr_state.ood_status,
        prev_state.meta_uncertainty != curr_state.meta_uncertainty,
    ])
```

**FORBIDDEN — Confidence violations:**
```python
# FORBIDDEN: Recalculate on every tick without state change
for tick in live_ticks:
    confidence = engine.compute(state)  # VIOLATION

# FORBIDDEN: Spike confidence upward without state trigger
bundle.R = 0.95                         # VIOLATION — no direct write

# FORBIDDEN: Override Risk Engine output
bundle.S = 1.0                          # VIOLATION
```

**CORRECT PATTERN:**
```python
prev_snapshot = ctrl.get_state()
provider.ingest_tick(...)               # Data update
curr_snapshot = ctrl.get_state()

if should_refresh_confidence(prev_snapshot, curr_snapshot, mode):
    new_bundle = confidence_engine.compute(curr_snapshot)
    ctrl.update(meta_uncertainty=new_bundle.U)
    # Bundle goes ONLY to Visual Output (P9)
```

**SPIKE-UP PREVENTION:**
Confidence score increases are only permitted when:
- A Failure Mode has been resolved (FM deactivated)
- Regime transitions from SHOCK/UNKNOWN to a stable regime
- Recovery criteria met (per FM-01..FM-06 recovery rules)
Even then, recovery is incremental — not instantaneous.


### PHASE 3 — ADAPTIVE SELECTIVITY THRESHOLD (BLOCK G)

**Insertion point:** Inside CONFIDENCE SCORE GOVERNANCE section.
**Governed by:** P0 — ANALYSIS AND STRATEGY RESEARCH TOOL. No execution, no broker integration.

```python
# jarvis/confidence/adaptive_selectivity_model.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
# Phase 3 addition — Decision Quality Maximization
# GOVERNANCE: Threshold may only increase selectivity.
#   Cannot decrease below BASE_SELECTIVITY_THRESHOLD.
#   Cannot override Failure Modes. Cannot override Risk Engine.
#   Deterministic mapping only.

from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import FrozenSet

from jarvis.core.regime import CorrelationRegimeState


# Phase 3 constants — registered in 99_REFERENCE.md
BASE_SELECTIVITY_THRESHOLD: float = 0.55
# FRAGILITY_HIGH_THRESHOLD: float = 0.65  (imported from constants)
# DURATION_STRESS_Z_LIMIT: float = 2.0    (imported from constants)


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class AdaptiveSelectivityResult:
    """
    Frozen result of AdaptiveSelectivityModel.
    Contains the resolved selectivity threshold for this evaluation cycle.
    Threshold is always >= BASE_SELECTIVITY_THRESHOLD.
    """
    resolved_threshold: float
    # Selectivity threshold for the current cycle: [BASE_SELECTIVITY_THRESHOLD, 1.0).
    # Higher = more selective; fewer signals pass.

    adjustment_reason: str
    # Human-readable description of which factors increased the threshold.
    # For Visual Output and audit trail only.

    base_used: float
    # BASE_SELECTIVITY_THRESHOLD used in this computation.
    # Must always equal the registered constant (0.55).


class AdaptiveSelectivityModel:
    """
    Dynamically adjusts the analytical selectivity threshold based on:
      1. Regime stability (from DecisionQualityBundle.regime_stability_score)
      2. Uncertainty total score (from UncertaintyBundle.total_uncertainty)
      3. Correlation regime flag (from CorrelationRiskScore or equivalent snapshot)
      4. Active failure modes (from GlobalSystemState failure mode flags)

    GOVERNANCE CONSTRAINTS:
      - THRESHOLD MONOTONICITY: resolved_threshold >= BASE_SELECTIVITY_THRESHOLD always.
      - DETERMINISTIC MAPPING: identical inputs → identical threshold.
      - CANNOT OVERRIDE FAILURE MODES: FM-01..FM-06 activation rules are unchanged.
      - CANNOT OVERRIDE RISK ENGINE: threshold adjustments are advisory to
        DecisionQualityEngine only.
      - NO STATE MUTATION: never calls ctrl.update().
      - SNAPSHOT-ONLY: all inputs are passed as frozen values.
    """

    BASE: float = BASE_SELECTIVITY_THRESHOLD

    # Additive penalties applied to base threshold
    PENALTY_LOW_REGIME_STABILITY: float   = 0.10  # regime_stability_score < 0.40
    PENALTY_HIGH_UNCERTAINTY: float       = 0.08  # total_uncertainty > 0.50
    PENALTY_CORRELATION_STRESS: float     = 0.07  # correlation_regime == "HIGH"
    PENALTY_PER_ACTIVE_FM: float          = 0.05  # per active failure mode (capped at 3)
    PENALTY_DURATION_STRESS: float        = 0.05  # transition_acceleration_flag = True

    # Threshold ceiling (never reach 1.0 — would block all signals)
    THRESHOLD_CEILING: float = 0.92

    def compute_threshold(
        self,
        regime_stability_score: float,
        # DecisionQualityBundle.regime_stability_score; range [0.0, 1.0].
        total_uncertainty: float,
        # UncertaintyBundle.total_uncertainty; range [0.0, 1.0].
        correlation_regime: str,
        # "LOW", "MEDIUM", "HIGH" — from cross-asset correlation snapshot.
        active_failure_modes: FrozenSet[str],
        # Set of currently active FM identifiers, e.g. frozenset({"FM-01", "FM-04"}).
        transition_acceleration_flag: bool,
        # RegimeDurationResult.transition_acceleration_flag.
    ) -> AdaptiveSelectivityResult:
        """
        Compute resolved selectivity threshold from current analytical state.

        All adjustments are additive penalties on top of BASE_SELECTIVITY_THRESHOLD.
        Threshold is clipped to [BASE_SELECTIVITY_THRESHOLD, THRESHOLD_CEILING].

        Returns:
            AdaptiveSelectivityResult (frozen, deterministic).
        """
        penalty: float = 0.0
        reasons = []

        if regime_stability_score < 0.40:
            penalty += self.PENALTY_LOW_REGIME_STABILITY
            reasons.append(
                f"LOW_REGIME_STABILITY({regime_stability_score:.3f})"
            )

        if total_uncertainty > 0.50:
            penalty += self.PENALTY_HIGH_UNCERTAINTY
            reasons.append(
                f"HIGH_UNCERTAINTY({total_uncertainty:.3f})"
            )

        if correlation_regime == CorrelationRegimeState.CRISIS_COUPLING:
            penalty += self.PENALTY_CORRELATION_STRESS
            reasons.append("CORRELATION_STRESS(HIGH)")

        fm_count = min(len(active_failure_modes), 3)
        if fm_count > 0:
            fm_penalty = fm_count * self.PENALTY_PER_ACTIVE_FM
            penalty += fm_penalty
            reasons.append(
                f"ACTIVE_FM_COUNT({fm_count},penalty={fm_penalty:.3f})"
            )

        if transition_acceleration_flag:
            penalty += self.PENALTY_DURATION_STRESS
            reasons.append("DURATION_STRESS_FLAG(True)")

        raw_threshold = self.BASE + penalty
        resolved = float(max(
            self.BASE,
            min(raw_threshold, self.THRESHOLD_CEILING)
        ))

        return AdaptiveSelectivityResult(
            resolved_threshold=resolved,
            adjustment_reason="; ".join(reasons) if reasons else "NO_ADJUSTMENT",
            base_used=self.BASE,
        )
```

**GOVERNANCE:**
```
AdaptiveSelectivityModel output (AdaptiveSelectivityResult) may ONLY:
  1. Inform DecisionQualityEngine threshold evaluation.
  2. Be displayed in Visual Output (P9) as analytical selectivity indicator.

AdaptiveSelectivityModel may NOT:
  - Override FM-01..FM-06 activation or deactivation
  - Override Risk Engine thresholds
  - Reduce resolved_threshold below BASE_SELECTIVITY_THRESHOLD
  - Call ctrl.update()
  - Access live data buffers

INVARIANT:
  resolved_threshold >= BASE_SELECTIVITY_THRESHOLD = 0.55 at all times.
  This is enforced inside compute_threshold() via max(self.BASE, ...).
```

---

## PHASE 3 — DECISION QUALITY ENGINE (NEW CORE ANALYTICAL LAYER)

**Insertion point:** After Confidence Governance, before Control Flow.
**Governed by:** P0 — ANALYSIS AND STRATEGY RESEARCH TOOL. No execution, no broker integration.

```python
# jarvis/intelligence/decision_quality_engine.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0
# Phase 3 addition — Decision Quality Maximization
# This is a NEW CORE ANALYTICAL LAYER — defined exactly once in this file.
# P-layer assignment: runs at the same pipeline position as Confidence Engine (P8),
# AFTER all analytical layers and BEFORE Visual Output (P9).
# NO new P-layer is created; DecisionQualityEngine runs as a sub-component of P8.

from __future__ import annotations
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import FrozenSet, Optional
import numpy as np

# Phase 3 imports — all from snapshot state
from jarvis.intelligence.regime_duration_model import RegimeDurationResult
from jarvis.strategy.signal_fragility_analyzer import SignalFragilityResult
from jarvis.core.decision_context_state import DecisionContextSnapshot
from jarvis.confidence.adaptive_selectivity_model import (
    AdaptiveSelectivityModel,
    AdaptiveSelectivityResult,
)

# Phase 3 constants — registered in 99_REFERENCE.md
QUALITY_SCORE_CAP_UNDER_UNCERTAINTY: float = 0.60
QUALITY_SCORE_MIN_FLOOR: float             = 0.05


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class DecisionQualityBundle:
    """
    Frozen output of DecisionQualityEngine.

    Defined exactly once here.
    All fields are deterministically computed from snapshot inputs.
    No randomness. No time-dependent non-deterministic logic.

    OUTPUT ROUTING — DecisionQualityBundle may ONLY affect:
      1. ConfidenceBundle (read-only modifier — informs sigma^2 weighting)
      2. Strategy Weight Posterior (cap only — never direct write to StrategyObject)
      3. Visual Output (P9) — full display of all quality sub-scores

    DecisionQualityBundle may NOT:
      - Trigger execution
      - Override Risk Engine thresholds
      - Override Failure Mode activation
      - Call ctrl.update()
      - Emit events
    """

    regime_stability_score: float
    # [0.0, 1.0] — how stable is the current regime across recent history.
    # Derived from RegimeTransitionMatrix stability (posterior diagonal mean)
    # and regime_duration model. High = stable.

    regime_duration_stress_score: float
    # [0.0, 1.0] — stress score derived from RegimeDurationResult.
    # 0.0 = regime age is within normal historical range.
    # 1.0 = regime is dramatically outside its historical duration distribution.

    signal_fragility_score: float
    # [0.0, 1.0] — SignalFragilityResult.fragility_index.
    # High value = signal is highly sensitive to small input perturbations.

    correlation_risk_modifier: float
    # [0.0, 1.0] — modifier derived from active correlation regime.
    # 0.0 = LOW correlation risk. 1.0 = HIGH concentration correlation risk.

    overfit_risk_modifier: float
    # [0.0, 1.0] — derived from OverfittingReport.overfitting_risk_score
    # (StrategyRegistry snapshot). High = elevated overfit risk.

    uncertainty_modifier: float
    # [0.0, 1.0] — UncertaintyBundle.total_uncertainty at evaluation time.

    composite_quality_score: float
    # [QUALITY_SCORE_MIN_FLOOR, QUALITY_SCORE_CAP_UNDER_UNCERTAINTY or 1.0]
    # Weighted aggregate of all sub-scores.
    # Capped at QUALITY_SCORE_CAP_UNDER_UNCERTAINTY (0.60) when
    # uncertainty_modifier > 0.5.
    # Always >= QUALITY_SCORE_MIN_FLOOR (0.05).

    selectivity_threshold: float
    # Resolved AdaptiveSelectivityResult.resolved_threshold for this cycle.
    # >= BASE_SELECTIVITY_THRESHOLD (0.55).

    signal_passes_selectivity: bool
    # True if composite_quality_score >= selectivity_threshold.
    # Informs Visual Output and ConfidenceBundle modifier.
    # Does NOT trigger any execution action.

    streak_instability: float
    # [0.0, 1.0] — from DecisionContextSnapshot streak analysis.

    regime_misalignment: float
    # [0.0, 1.0] — from DecisionContextSnapshot regime misalignment analysis.

    repeated_failure_penalty: float
    # [0.0, 1.0] — from DecisionContextSnapshot repeated failure analysis.


class DecisionQualityEngine:
    """
    Core analytical layer for decision quality maximization.

    Computes DecisionQualityBundle from snapshot state.
    Runs as a sub-component of P8 (Confidence Engine pipeline stage).
    Budget: max 20 ms per cycle.

    GOVERNANCE CONSTRAINTS:
      - DETERMINISTIC: identical snapshot inputs → identical output.
      - SNAPSHOT-ONLY: never accesses live buffers.
      - NO STATE MUTATION: never calls ctrl.update().
      - NO EVENT EMISSION: never emits analytical events.
      - NO EXECUTION SEMANTICS: output is purely analytical.
      - OUTPUT ROUTING: DecisionQualityBundle → ConfidenceBundle modifier,
        Strategy Weight Posterior cap, Visual Output only.
      - FORBIDDEN: broker concepts, execution triggers, direct FM overrides,
        Risk Engine threshold overrides, random number generation.
    """

    # Sub-score weights for composite_quality_score (must sum to 1.0)
    W_REGIME_STABILITY:          float = 0.20
    W_DURATION_STRESS:           float = 0.15
    W_SIGNAL_FRAGILITY:          float = 0.20
    W_CORRELATION_RISK:          float = 0.15
    W_OVERFIT_RISK:              float = 0.10
    W_UNCERTAINTY:               float = 0.10
    W_STREAK_INSTABILITY:        float = 0.05
    W_REGIME_MISALIGNMENT:       float = 0.03
    W_REPEATED_FAILURE_PENALTY:  float = 0.02

    def __init__(self) -> None:
        self._selectivity_model = AdaptiveSelectivityModel()

    def compute(
        self,
        # ── Regime inputs ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
        regime_transition_diagonal_mean: float,
        # Mean of diagonal of RegimeTransitionMatrix (stability proxy).
        # Range [0.0, 1.0]. Higher = more stable regime transitions.
        duration_result: RegimeDurationResult,
        # Output of RegimeDurationModel for current cycle.

        # ── Signal fragility ───────────────────────────────────────────────
        fragility_result: SignalFragilityResult,
        # Output of SignalFragilityAnalyzer for current strategy.

        # ── Correlation risk ───────────────────────────────────────────────
        correlation_regime: str,
        # "LOW", "MEDIUM", or "HIGH" from cross-asset correlation snapshot.

        # ── Overfit risk ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
        overfitting_risk_score: float,
        # OverfittingReport.overfitting_risk_score from StrategyRegistry snapshot.
        # Range [0.0, 1.0].

        # ── Uncertainty ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
        total_uncertainty: float,
        # UncertaintyBundle.total_uncertainty at this cycle. Range [0.0, 1.0].

        # ── Decision context ───────────────────────────────────────────────
        decision_snapshot: DecisionContextSnapshot,
        # Frozen snapshot of DecisionContextState.

        # ── Failure modes ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
        active_failure_modes: FrozenSet[str],
        # Set of active FM identifiers, e.g. frozenset({"FM-01"}).

    ) -> DecisionQualityBundle:
        """
        Compute DecisionQualityBundle from all snapshot inputs.
        Fully deterministic. No side effects.

        Returns:
            DecisionQualityBundle (frozen).
        """
        # ── Regime stability score ─────────────────────────────────────────
        regime_stability = float(np.clip(regime_transition_diagonal_mean, 0.0, 1.0))

        # ── Duration stress score ──────────────────────────────────────────
        # Map |z_score| to [0, 1]; flag adds 0.3 bonus stress
        z_abs = abs(duration_result.duration_z_score)
        duration_stress = float(np.clip(z_abs / 5.0, 0.0, 1.0))
        if duration_result.transition_acceleration_flag:
            duration_stress = float(np.clip(duration_stress + 0.30, 0.0, 1.0))

        # ── Signal fragility score ─────────────────────────────────────────
        signal_fragility = float(np.clip(fragility_result.fragility_index, 0.0, 1.0))

        # ── Correlation risk modifier ──────────────────────────────────────
        corr_map = {"LOW": 0.0, "MEDIUM": 0.40, "HIGH": 0.85}
        correlation_risk = corr_map.get(correlation_regime, 0.40)

        # ── Overfit risk modifier ──────────────────────────────────────────
        overfit_risk = float(np.clip(overfitting_risk_score, 0.0, 1.0))

        # ── Uncertainty modifier ───────────────────────────────────────────
        uncertainty = float(np.clip(total_uncertainty, 0.0, 1.0))

        # ── Decision context patterns ──────────────────────────────────────
        streak_instability = self._streak_instability(decision_snapshot)
        regime_misalignment = self._regime_misalignment(
            decision_snapshot,
            # Use "UNKNOWN" as fallback if regime context is unavailable here;
            # actual regime string is available via the snapshot regime field
            # on the most recent record.
            current_regime=self._infer_current_regime(decision_snapshot),
        )
        repeated_failure = self._repeated_failure_penalty(decision_snapshot)

        # ── Composite quality score ────────────────────────────────────────
        # Note: quality_score uses INVERTED sub-scores where higher = worse.
        # We invert so that high fragility → low quality.
        raw_quality = (
            self.W_REGIME_STABILITY          * regime_stability          +   # HIGH = good
            self.W_DURATION_STRESS           * (1.0 - duration_stress)   +   # LOW stress = good
            self.W_SIGNAL_FRAGILITY          * (1.0 - signal_fragility)  +   # LOW fragility = good
            self.W_CORRELATION_RISK          * (1.0 - correlation_risk)  +   # LOW risk = good
            self.W_OVERFIT_RISK              * (1.0 - overfit_risk)      +   # LOW overfit = good
            self.W_UNCERTAINTY               * (1.0 - uncertainty)       +   # LOW uncertainty = good
            self.W_STREAK_INSTABILITY        * (1.0 - streak_instability) +  # LOW = good
            self.W_REGIME_MISALIGNMENT       * (1.0 - regime_misalignment) + # LOW = good
            self.W_REPEATED_FAILURE_PENALTY  * (1.0 - repeated_failure),     # LOW = good
        )

        composite = float(np.clip(raw_quality, 0.0, 1.0))

        # Apply uncertainty cap
        if uncertainty > 0.50:
            composite = float(min(composite, QUALITY_SCORE_CAP_UNDER_UNCERTAINTY))

        # Apply floor
        composite = float(max(composite, QUALITY_SCORE_MIN_FLOOR))

        # ── Adaptive selectivity threshold ─────────────────────────────────
        selectivity_result: AdaptiveSelectivityResult = (
            self._selectivity_model.compute_threshold(
                regime_stability_score=regime_stability,
                total_uncertainty=uncertainty,
                correlation_regime=correlation_regime,
                active_failure_modes=active_failure_modes,
                transition_acceleration_flag=duration_result.transition_acceleration_flag,
            )
        )

        passes_selectivity = composite >= selectivity_result.resolved_threshold

        return DecisionQualityBundle(
            regime_stability_score=regime_stability,
            regime_duration_stress_score=duration_stress,
            signal_fragility_score=signal_fragility,
            correlation_risk_modifier=correlation_risk,
            overfit_risk_modifier=overfit_risk,
            uncertainty_modifier=uncertainty,
            composite_quality_score=composite,
            selectivity_threshold=selectivity_result.resolved_threshold,
            signal_passes_selectivity=passes_selectivity,
            streak_instability=streak_instability,
            regime_misalignment=regime_misalignment,
            repeated_failure_penalty=repeated_failure,
        )

    # ── Private deterministic helper methods ──────────────────────────────

    def _streak_instability(
        self,
        snapshot: DecisionContextSnapshot,
        window: int = 10,
    ) -> float:
        """Outcome transition rate in recent window. Pure function."""
        recent = list(snapshot.records)[-window:]
        if len(recent) < 2:
            return 0.0
        outcomes = [r.outcome for r in recent]
        transitions = sum(1 for a, b in zip(outcomes, outcomes[1:]) if a != b)
        return float(transitions / max(len(recent) - 1, 1))

    def _infer_current_regime(self, snapshot: DecisionContextSnapshot) -> str:
        """Infer most recent regime from snapshot. Deterministic."""
        if not snapshot.records:
            return "UNKNOWN"
        return snapshot.records[-1].regime_at_decision

    def _regime_misalignment(
        self,
        snapshot: DecisionContextSnapshot,
        current_regime: str,
        window: int = 20,
    ) -> float:
        """Fraction of recent decisions in a different regime. Pure function."""
        recent = list(snapshot.records)[-window:]
        if not recent:
            return 0.0
        misaligned = sum(1 for r in recent if r.regime_at_decision != current_regime)
        return float(misaligned / len(recent))

    def _repeated_failure_penalty(
        self,
        snapshot: DecisionContextSnapshot,
        window: int = 10,
        loss_threshold: float = 0.60,
    ) -> float:
        """Penalty when recent LOSS rate exceeds threshold. Pure function."""
        recent = list(snapshot.records)[-window:]
        if not recent:
            return 0.0
        losses = sum(1 for r in recent if r.outcome == "LOSS")
        loss_rate = float(losses / len(recent))
        if loss_rate <= loss_threshold:
            return 0.0
        return float(min(1.0, (loss_rate - loss_threshold) / max(1.0 - loss_threshold, 1e-9)))
```

**DECISIONQUALITYENGINE — DOWNSTREAM EFFECTS:**
```
DecisionQualityBundle outputs are consumed as follows:

  1. ConfidenceBundle (read-only modifier):
     If signal_passes_selectivity = False:
       - ConfidenceBundle.Q is informatively marked as LOW_QUALITY_SIGNAL
         in the Visual Output display.
       - ConfidenceBundle.sigma2 receives a read-only informational tag.
       - No direct write to ConfidenceBundle fields.
     If composite_quality_score < 0.30:
       - Visual Output renders QUALITY_ALERT banner.

  2. Strategy Weight Posterior (cap only):
     If composite_quality_score < 0.40:
       - WeightPosteriorModel.posterior_mean is capped at
         prior_weight * (composite_quality_score / 0.40)
       - This cap is applied read-side, not by modifying StrategyObject.
       - Consistent with existing UncertaintyBundle weight cap pattern
         (UncertaintyBundle: if total_uncertainty > 0.5 → cap at 0.3).

  3. Visual Output (P9):
     Full DecisionQualityBundle displayed:
       - regime_stability_score gauge
       - signal_fragility_score gauge
       - composite_quality_score prominently displayed
       - selectivity_threshold with pass/fail indicator
       - streak_instability, regime_misalignment, repeated_failure_penalty
       - all sub-scores in expandable detail panel

  4. AdaptiveSelectivityResult embedded in bundle:
     selectivity_threshold and signal_passes_selectivity exposed to Visual Output.
```

**GOVERNANCE:**
```
DecisionQualityEngine:
  - Defined EXACTLY ONCE: jarvis/intelligence/decision_quality_engine.py
  - NEVER emits events
  - NEVER calls ctrl.update()
  - NEVER accesses live buffers
  - Operates on snapshot state only
  - Budget: max 20 ms per cycle (see 40_RISK_ENGINE_SPECS.md)
  - No recursive recalculation
  - No cascading re-scoring
  - No re-triggering of event loop

DecisionQualityBundle:
  - Defined EXACTLY ONCE (this file, frozen dataclass above)
  - All fields frozen and deterministic
  - Read-only to all downstream consumers

P-LAYER COMPLIANCE:
  DecisionQualityEngine runs as sub-component of P8 (Confidence Engine).
  NO NEW P-LAYER is introduced. P0–P9 hierarchy is unchanged.
```
