```python
# jarvis/systems/control_flow.py

from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Optional, Dict
from enum import Enum

class ControlSignal(Enum):
    CONTINUE = "continue"
    DEGRADE = "degrade"
    STOP = "stop"
    EMERGENCY = "emergency"

@dataclass
class FlowState:
    """Repraesentiert aktuellen Zustand im Control Flow."""
    layer: int
    signal: ControlSignal
    gate_passed: bool
    reason: str
    data: Dict

class SystemControlFlow:
    """
    Definiert Control Flow durch alle 11 Layer.
    Hard Stop Nodes erzwingen Abbruch bei Gate-Verletzungen.
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.current_layer = 0
        self.flow_state = None
    
    def execute_flow(self, input_data: Dict) -> FlowState:
        """
        Fuehrt vollstaendigen System-Flow aus.
        Stoppt bei jedem Hard Stop Node.
        """
        flow_state = FlowState(
            layer=0,
            signal=ControlSignal.CONTINUE,
            gate_passed=True,
            reason="Start",
            data=input_data
        )
        
        # Layer 1: Data Ingestion
        flow_state = self._layer_1_data_ingestion(flow_state)
        if flow_state.signal != ControlSignal.CONTINUE:
            return flow_state
        
        # Layer 2: Feature Preprocessing
        flow_state = self._layer_2_features(flow_state)
        if flow_state.signal != ControlSignal.CONTINUE:
            return flow_state
        
        # Layer 3: State Estimation
        flow_state = self._layer_3_state(flow_state)
        if flow_state.signal != ControlSignal.CONTINUE:
            return flow_state
        
        # Layer 4: Regime Detection
        flow_state = self._layer_4_regime(flow_state)
        if flow_state.signal != ControlSignal.CONTINUE:
            return flow_state
        
        # Layer 5: Calibration
        flow_state = self._layer_5_calibration(flow_state)
        if flow_state.signal != ControlSignal.CONTINUE:
            return flow_state
        
        # Layer 6: Uncertainty Aggregation
        flow_state = self._layer_6_uncertainty(flow_state)
        if flow_state.signal != ControlSignal.CONTINUE:
            return flow_state
        
        # Layer 7: OOD Ensemble
        flow_state = self._layer_7_ood(flow_state)
        if flow_state.signal != ControlSignal.CONTINUE:
            return flow_state
        
        # Layer 8: Risk Engine
        flow_state = self._layer_8_risk(flow_state)
        if flow_state.signal != ControlSignal.CONTINUE:
            return flow_state
        
        # Layer 9: Strategy Abstraction
        flow_state = self._layer_9_strategy(flow_state)
        if flow_state.signal != ControlSignal.CONTINUE:
            return flow_state
        
        # Layer 10: Degradation Controller
        flow_state = self._layer_10_degradation(flow_state)
        if flow_state.signal != ControlSignal.CONTINUE:
            return flow_state
        
        # Layer 11: Output Interface
        flow_state = self._layer_11_output(flow_state)
        
        return flow_state
    
    def _layer_1_data_ingestion(self, state: FlowState) -> FlowState:
        """Layer 1 mit Quality Gate."""
        state.layer = 1
        
        # Simulate data fetch
        quality_score = state.data.get('quality_score', 1.0)
        
        # HARD STOP: Quality Gate
        if quality_score < 0.5:
            state.signal = ControlSignal.STOP
            state.gate_passed = False
            state.reason = f"Quality Gate failed: {quality_score} < 0.5"
            return state
        
        state.reason = "Data ingestion passed"
        return state
    
    def _layer_7_ood(self, state: FlowState) -> FlowState:
        """Layer 7 mit OOD Gate."""
        state.layer = 7
        
        is_ood = state.data.get('is_ood', False)
        
        # HARD STOP: OOD Gate
        if is_ood:
            state.signal = ControlSignal.DEGRADE
            state.gate_passed = False
            state.reason = "OOD detected - switching to defensive mode"
            return state
        
        state.reason = "OOD check passed"
        return state
    
    def _layer_8_risk(self, state: FlowState) -> FlowState:
        """Layer 8 mit Risk Gate."""
        state.layer = 8
        
        drawdown = state.data.get('drawdown', 0.0)
        
        # HARD STOP: Drawdown Gate
        if drawdown > 0.15:
            state.signal = ControlSignal.EMERGENCY
            state.gate_passed = False
            state.reason = f"Drawdown exceeded: {drawdown} > 0.15"
            return state
        
        state.reason = "Risk check passed"
        return state
    
    # Weitere Layer-Methoden...
    def _layer_2_features(self, state: FlowState) -> FlowState:
        state.layer = 2
        state.reason = "Feature preprocessing"
        return state
    
    def _layer_3_state(self, state: FlowState) -> FlowState:
        state.layer = 3
        state.reason = "State estimation"
        return state
    
    def _layer_4_regime(self, state: FlowState) -> FlowState:
        state.layer = 4
        state.reason = "Regime detection"
        return state
    
    def _layer_5_calibration(self, state: FlowState) -> FlowState:
        state.layer = 5
        state.reason = "Calibration"
        return state
    
    def _layer_6_uncertainty(self, state: FlowState) -> FlowState:
        state.layer = 6
        state.reason = "Uncertainty aggregation"
        return state
    
    def _layer_9_strategy(self, state: FlowState) -> FlowState:
        state.layer = 9
        state.reason = "Strategy selection"
        return state
    
    def _layer_10_degradation(self, state: FlowState) -> FlowState:
        state.layer = 10
        state.reason = "Degradation control"
        return state
    
    def _layer_11_output(self, state: FlowState) -> FlowState:
        state.layer = 11
        state.reason = "Output generation"
        return state

### Validation Gates

```python
# jarvis/systems/validation_gates.py

class ValidationGate:
    """Base class fuer alle Validation Gates."""
    
    def __init__(self, name: str, threshold: float):
        self.name = name
        self.threshold = threshold
    
    def check(self, value: float) -> tuple[bool, str]:
        """
        Prueft Gate-Bedingung.
        Returns: (passed, reason)
        """
        raise NotImplementedError

class QualityGate(ValidationGate):
    """Layer 1: Data Quality Gate."""
    
    def check(self, quality_score: float) -> tuple[bool, str]:
        passed = quality_score >= self.threshold
        reason = f"Quality score {quality_score:.3f} {'>=':'<'[not passed]} {self.threshold}"
        return passed, reason

class DriftGate(ValidationGate):
    """Layer 2: Feature Drift Gate."""
    
    def check(self, drift_severity: float) -> tuple[bool, str]:
        passed = drift_severity < self.threshold
        reason = f"Drift severity {drift_severity:.3f} {'<':'>='[not passed]} {self.threshold}"
        return passed, reason

class KalmanGate(ValidationGate):
    """Layer 3: Kalman Stability Gate."""
    
    def check(self, condition_number: float) -> tuple[bool, str]:
        passed = condition_number < self.threshold
        reason = f"Condition number {condition_number:.2e} {'<':'>='[not passed]} {self.threshold}"
        return passed, reason

class ECEGate(ValidationGate):
    """Layer 5: Calibration Gate (ECE)."""
    
    def check(self, ece: float) -> tuple[bool, str]:
        passed = ece < self.threshold
        reason = f"ECE {ece:.4f} {'<':'>='[not passed]} {self.threshold}"
        return passed, reason

class OODGate(ValidationGate):
    """Layer 7: OOD Detection Gate."""
    
    def check(self, is_ood: bool) -> tuple[bool, str]:
        passed = not is_ood
        reason = f"OOD {'not ' if passed else ''}detected"
        return passed, reason

class RiskGate(ValidationGate):
    """Layer 8: Risk Limit Gate."""
    
    def check(self, var: float) -> tuple[bool, str]:
        passed = var >= self.threshold  # VaR is negative
        reason = f"VaR {var:.3f} {'>=':<'[not passed]} {self.threshold}"
        return passed, reason
```

### Mode Transitions

```python
# jarvis/systems/mode_controller.py

from enum import Enum

class SystemMode(Enum):
    NORMAL = "normal"
    DEFENSIVE = "defensive"
    HOLD = "hold"
    EMERGENCY = "emergency"

class ModeTransition:
    """
    Definiert Zustandsuebergaenge zwischen Modi.
    """
    
    TRANSITIONS = {
        (SystemMode.NORMAL, 'ood_detected'): SystemMode.DEFENSIVE,
        (SystemMode.NORMAL, 'high_uncertainty'): SystemMode.DEFENSIVE,
        (SystemMode.NORMAL, 'drawdown_warning'): SystemMode.DEFENSIVE,
        (SystemMode.NORMAL, 'critical_failure'): SystemMode.EMERGENCY,
        
        (SystemMode.DEFENSIVE, 'ood_cleared'): SystemMode.NORMAL,
        (SystemMode.DEFENSIVE, 'uncertainty_spike'): SystemMode.HOLD,
        (SystemMode.DEFENSIVE, 'drawdown_exceeded'): SystemMode.EMERGENCY,
        
        (SystemMode.HOLD, 'stability_restored'): SystemMode.DEFENSIVE,
        (SystemMode.HOLD, 'critical_failure'): SystemMode.EMERGENCY,
        
        (SystemMode.EMERGENCY, 'manual_recovery'): SystemMode.HOLD,
    }
    
    def transition(
        self,
        current_mode: SystemMode,
        trigger: str
    ) -> Optional[SystemMode]:
        """
        Gibt neuen Mode basierend auf Trigger zurueck.
        None = kein Uebergang moeglich.
        """
        return self.TRANSITIONS.get((current_mode, trigger))
```

## FAILURE SIMULATION: FLASH CRASH TIMELINE

### Scenario: Bitcoin Flash Crash (Mai 2021 Simulation)

```python
# jarvis/testing/flash_crash_simulation.py

from dataclasses import dataclass
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import List

@dataclass
class TimelineEvent:
    """Einzelnes Event in Flash Crash Timeline."""
    time_offset: float  # Sekunden seit Crash-Start
    event_type: str
    description: str
    system_response: str
    metrics: Dict[str, float]

class FlashCrashSimulation:
    """
    Simuliert Flash Crash und tracked System-Response.
    
    Timeline:
      T+0s:   Preis-Drop -15% in 5 Sekunden
      T+5s:   OOD Detection getriggert
      T+6s:   Meta-Uncertainty Spike U=0.9
      T+7s:   Risk Compression aktiviert
      T+8s:   Strategy auf HOLD geswitched
      T+10s:  Mode Transition zu DEFENSIVE
      T+30s:  Stabilitaet teilweise restored
      T+60s:  Mode Transition zu NORMAL (conditional)
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.timeline: List[TimelineEvent] = []
        self.start_time = datetime.utcnow()
    
    def simulate(self) -> List[TimelineEvent]:
        """
        Fuehrt Flash Crash Simulation aus.
        Returns: Vollstaendige Timeline mit System-Responses.
        """
        timeline = []
        
        # T+0: Crash Event
        timeline.append(TimelineEvent(
            time_offset=0.0,
            event_type="CRASH_START",
            description="Price drop -15% in 5 seconds",
            system_response="Data ingestion registers anomaly",
            metrics={
                'price_change': -0.15,
                'volatility': 0.50,
                'quality_score': 0.8
            }
        ))
        
        # T+5: OOD Detection
        timeline.append(TimelineEvent(
            time_offset=5.0,
            event_type="OOD_TRIGGER",
            description="OOD Ensemble detects anomaly (5/5 sensors)",
            system_response="OOD flag set, is_ood=True",
            metrics={
                'ood_score': 0.95,
                'consensus_count': 5,
                'mahalanobis_dist': 8.5
            }
        ))
        
        # T+6: Meta-Uncertainty Spike
        timeline.append(TimelineEvent(
            time_offset=6.0,
            event_type="META_UNCERTAINTY_SPIKE",
            description="Meta-Uncertainty U spikes to 0.9",
            system_response="GlobalSystemState updated, U=0.9",
            metrics={
                'U': 0.9,
                'sigma_squared': 0.45,
                'Q': 0.2
            }
        ))
        
        # T+7: Risk Compression
        timeline.append(TimelineEvent(
            time_offset=7.0,
            event_type="RISK_COMPRESSION",
            description="Risk Engine activates compression",
            system_response="Position sizes reduced to 25%",
            metrics={
                'risk_compression': True,
                'position_scalar': 0.25,
                'max_exposure': 0.20
            }
        ))
        
        # T+8: Strategy Suppression
        timeline.append(TimelineEvent(
            time_offset=8.0,
            event_type="STRATEGY_SUPPRESSION",
            description="Strategy switched to HOLD",
            system_response="All active strategies suppressed",
            metrics={
                'strategy': 'HOLD',
                'signal_strength': 0.0,
                'confidence': 0.1
            }
        ))
        
        # T+10: Mode Switch
        timeline.append(TimelineEvent(
            time_offset=10.0,
            event_type="MODE_TRANSITION",
            description="System mode switched to DEFENSIVE",
            system_response="Mode transition: NORMAL -> DEFENSIVE",
            metrics={
                'mode': 'DEFENSIVE',
                'stability': 0.3,
                'degradation_level': 2
            }
        ))
        
        # T+30: Partial Recovery
        timeline.append(TimelineEvent(
            time_offset=30.0,
            event_type="PARTIAL_RECOVERY",
            description="Volatility decreases, OOD score drops",
            system_response="System begins recovery process",
            metrics={
                'ood_score': 0.65,
                'volatility': 0.25,
                'U': 0.6
            }
        ))
        
        # T+60: Full Recovery (Conditional)
        timeline.append(TimelineEvent(
            time_offset=60.0,
            event_type="RECOVERY_CHECK",
            description="System evaluates return to NORMAL",
            system_response="Mode transition: DEFENSIVE -> NORMAL (if conditions met)",
            metrics={
                'ood_score': 0.35,
                'volatility': 0.15,
                'U': 0.3,
                'mode': 'NORMAL'
            }
        ))
        
        self.timeline = timeline
        return timeline
    
    def verify_correct_behavior(self) -> Dict[str, bool]:
        """
        Verifiziert dass System korrekt auf Flash Crash reagiert hat.
        """
        checks = {
            'ood_detected_within_10s': False,
            'risk_compression_activated': False,
            'strategy_suppressed': False,
            'mode_switched_to_defensive': False,
            'no_trades_during_crash': False,
            'recovery_procedure_followed': False
        }
        
        for event in self.timeline:
            if event.event_type == 'OOD_TRIGGER' and event.time_offset <= 10.0:
                checks['ood_detected_within_10s'] = True
            
            if event.event_type == 'RISK_COMPRESSION':
                checks['risk_compression_activated'] = True
            
            if event.event_type == 'STRATEGY_SUPPRESSION':
                checks['strategy_suppressed'] = True
            
            if event.event_type == 'MODE_TRANSITION':
                if event.metrics.get('mode') == 'DEFENSIVE':
                    checks['mode_switched_to_defensive'] = True
            
            if event.event_type == 'RECOVERY_CHECK':
                checks['recovery_procedure_followed'] = True
        
        # No trades check
        trades_during_crash = [
            e for e in self.timeline
            if e.event_type == 'TRADE_EXECUTED' and e.time_offset < 30.0
        ]
        checks['no_trades_during_crash'] = len(trades_during_crash) == 0
        
        return checks
```

## ADDITIONAL SYSTEM METRICS

### Structural Fragility Index

```python
# jarvis/metrics/fragility_index.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0

class StructuralFragilityIndex:
    """
    Misst System-Fragilitaet: Wie nah ist System an kritischem Versagen?
    
    Komponenten:
      - Layer Coupling: Wie stark sind Layer gekoppelt?
      - Error Propagation: Wie schnell propagieren Fehler?
      - Recovery Time: Wie lange dauert Recovery?
      - Cascade Risk: Risiko fuer Cascade Failures
    """
    
    def compute(
        self,
        layer_metrics: Dict[int, Dict[str, float]],
        recent_failures: List[Dict]
    ) -> float:
        """
        Berechnet Fragility Index in [0, 1].
        0 = robust, 1 = fragil
        """
        # Layer Coupling Score
        coupling = self._compute_coupling(layer_metrics)
        
        # Error Propagation Score
        propagation = self._compute_error_propagation(recent_failures)
        
        # Recovery Time Score
        recovery = self._compute_recovery_time(recent_failures)
        
        # Cascade Risk Score
        cascade = self._compute_cascade_risk(layer_metrics, recent_failures)
        
        # Weighted combination
        fragility = (
            0.3 * coupling +
            0.3 * propagation +
            0.2 * recovery +
            0.2 * cascade
        )
        
        return float(np.clip(fragility, 0.0, 1.0))
    
    def _compute_coupling(self, layer_metrics: Dict) -> float:
        """Misst Inter-Layer Coupling."""
        # Vereinfachte Implementierung
        # In Praxis: Mutual Information zwischen Layern
        return 0.3
    
    def _compute_error_propagation(self, failures: List) -> float:
        """Misst wie schnell Fehler propagieren."""
        if not failures:
            return 0.0
        
        # Durchschnittliche Propagation-Zeit
        prop_times = [f.get('propagation_time', 0) for f in failures]
        avg_time = np.mean(prop_times) if prop_times else 0
        
        # Normalisiert auf [0, 1]: schnelle Propagation = hoch
        return float(np.clip(avg_time / 10.0, 0.0, 1.0))
    
    def _compute_recovery_time(self, failures: List) -> float:
        """Misst Recovery-Zeit."""
        if not failures:
            return 0.0
        
        recovery_times = [f.get('recovery_time', 0) for f in failures]
        avg_recovery = np.mean(recovery_times) if recovery_times else 0
        
        # Lange Recovery = hohe Fragility
        return float(np.clip(avg_recovery / 60.0, 0.0, 1.0))
    
    def _compute_cascade_risk(
        self,
        layer_metrics: Dict,
        failures: List
    ) -> float:
        """Misst Risiko fuer Cascade Failures."""
        # Anzahl simultaner Layer-Failures
        recent_simultaneous = sum(
            1 for f in failures
            if f.get('simultaneous_layers', 0) > 1
        )
        
        return float(np.clip(recent_simultaneous / 10.0, 0.0, 1.0))
```

### Trust Score (System Health Composite)

```python
# jarvis/metrics/trust_score.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0

class TrustScore:
    """
    Composite Score fuer System Health / Trustworthiness.
    
    Komponenten:
      - Calibration Quality (ECE)
      - OOD Detection Accuracy
      - Prediction Stability
      - Risk Control Effectiveness
      - Operational Reliability
    """
    
    def compute(
        self,
        ece: float,
        ood_recall: float,
        prediction_variance: float,
        drawdown: float,
        uptime: float
    ) -> float:
        """
        Berechnet Trust Score in [0, 1].
        1 = vollstaendig vertrauenswuerdig
        0 = nicht vertrauenswuerdig
        """
        # Calibration component
        cal_score = 1.0 - min(ece / 0.05, 1.0)
        
        # OOD component
        ood_score = ood_recall
        
        # Stability component
        stab_score = 1.0 - min(prediction_variance / 0.1, 1.0)
        
        # Risk component
        risk_score = 1.0 - min(drawdown / 0.15, 1.0)
        
        # Operational component
        ops_score = uptime
        
        # Weighted combination
        trust = (
            0.30 * cal_score +
            0.25 * ood_score +
            0.20 * stab_score +
            0.15 * risk_score +
            0.10 * ops_score
        )
        
        return float(np.clip(trust, 0.0, 1.0))
```

### Regime Memory Layer

```python
# jarvis/systems/regime_memory.py

from collections import deque
from datetime import datetime

class RegimeMemoryLayer:
    """
    Speichert Regime-Historie fuer Context-Aware Decisions.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, memory_size: int = 1000):
        self.memory_size = memory_size
        self.regime_history: deque = deque(maxlen=memory_size)
        self.transition_history: deque = deque(maxlen=memory_size)
    
    def add_regime(
        self,
        regime: str,
        confidence: float,
        timestamp: datetime
    ):
        """Fuegt Regime-Observation zur Historie hinzu."""
        self.regime_history.append({
            'regime': regime,
            'confidence': confidence,
            'timestamp': timestamp
        })
    
    def add_transition(
        self,
        from_regime: str,
        to_regime: str,
        timestamp: datetime
    ):
        """Tracked Regime-Transition."""
        self.transition_history.append({
            'from': from_regime,
            'to': to_regime,
            'timestamp': timestamp
        })
    
    def get_regime_persistence(self, regime: str) -> float:
        """
        Berechnet durchschnittliche Persistenz eines Regimes.
        Returns: Durchschnittliche Dauer in Sekunden
        """
        transitions = [
            t for t in self.transition_history
            if t['from'] == regime
        ]
        
        if not transitions:
            return 0.0
        
        durations = []
        for i in range(len(transitions) - 1):
            duration = (
                transitions[i+1]['timestamp'] - transitions[i]['timestamp']
            ).total_seconds()
            durations.append(duration)
        
        return np.mean(durations) if durations else 0.0
    
    def get_transition_probability(
        self,
        from_regime: str,
        to_regime: str
    ) -> float:
        """
        Berechnet empirische Uebergangswahrscheinlichkeit.
        """
        transitions_from = [
            t for t in self.transition_history
            if t['from'] == from_regime
        ]
        
        if not transitions_from:
            return 0.0
        
        transitions_to = [
            t for t in transitions_from
            if t['to'] == to_regime
        ]
        
        return len(transitions_to) / len(transitions_from)
```

## SYSTEM COMPUTATIONAL GOVERNANCE

**Purpose:** Formalize all computational safety constraints to prevent analytical
instability, non-determinism, and resource exhaustion across all operating modes.

---

### COMPUTATIONAL SAFETY CONSTRAINTS (ALL MODES)

```
CONSTRAINT 1 — NO RECURSIVE EVENT LOOPS
  Events must NOT emit new events during the same dispatch cycle.
  DeterministicEventQueue.emit() may not be called from within
  an event handler. New events generated as a consequence of a
  state change are queued for the NEXT dispatch cycle only.

  Violation detection: EventDispatcher tracks call stack depth.
  If emit() is called while drain() is active: RuntimeError raised.

CONSTRAINT 2 — NO CASCADING RE-SCORING WITHOUT STATE CHANGE
  Confidence Engine must not recompute unless should_refresh_confidence()
  returns True. Re-scoring without a permitted trigger is a correctness
  violation. See CONFIDENCE REFRESH LOGIC in 37_SYSTEM_ADDENDUM.md.

CONSTRAINT 3 — NO CONFIDENCE REFRESH WITHOUT TRIGGER
  ConfidenceUpdateEvent must not be emitted unless:
    a. One of the five defined refresh triggers is present, AND
    b. should_refresh_confidence(prev, curr, mode) returns True.
  Tick-level recalculation is explicitly forbidden.

CONSTRAINT 4 — NO FULL PORTFOLIO RECOMPUTE ON SINGLE TICK
  PortfolioState recompute (correlation matrix, VaR, exposure) must only
  trigger on EXPOSURE_DELTA_THRESHOLD or CORRELATION_REGIME_SHIFT events.
  Single tick ingestion does not trigger full portfolio recompute.

CONSTRAINT 5 — NO SANDBOX MUTATION OF LIVE STATE
  ScenarioSandboxEngine operates on immutable state snapshots.
  ctrl.update() may not be called from within ScenarioSandboxEngine
  or any research/benchmark extension module.
  See sandbox isolation rules in 26-30_STRATEGY_SIM.md.

CONSTRAINT 6 — NO CROSS-MODE STATE LEAKAGE
  In MODE_HYBRID:
    - Backtest-window state must not overwrite live-window state after sync_point.
    - Live-window state must not contaminate backtest-window results.
    - sync_point is session-immutable. No code may modify it after setting.
    - State from historical phase is READ-ONLY reference after sync_point.
  Cross-mode leakage is verified by comparing state_hash at sync_point
  to the expected checkpoint hash.

CONSTRAINT 7 — SINGLE MUTATION PATH
  All state mutations route through GlobalSystemStateController.update().
  No module may directly assign fields on SystemState, RegimeState,
  VolatilityState, StrategyState, or PortfolioState.
  Direct field assignment is a P1-level violation detectable by static analysis.

CONSTRAINT 8 — NO UNBOUNDED BACKFILL LOOPS
  Historical backfill in MODE_HYBRID must terminate at sync_point.
  Maximum backfill duration: 10 minutes (see Performance Envelope).
  If duration exceeded: checkpoint exported; backfill paused; operator notified.
```

---

### VIOLATION DETECTION MECHANISMS

```python
# jarvis/core/governance_monitor.py
# Governance monitor runs alongside the event dispatcher.
# It detects violations and raises errors before state corruption occurs.

GOVERNANCE_CHECKS = {
    "no_recursive_emit": (
        "EventDispatcher tracks active dispatch flag. "
        "emit() during active drain() raises RuntimeError immediately."
    ),
    "single_ctrl_update": (
        "ctrl.update() logs caller module and line. "
        "If called from outside permitted modules: WARNING logged + violation count incremented."
    ),
    "no_sandbox_ctrl_access": (
        "ScenarioSandboxEngine constructor does not accept ctrl reference. "
        "Any attempt to inject ctrl raises TypeError at construction."
    ),
    "confidence_trigger_required": (
        "ConfidenceUpdateEvent is only emitted by confidence_engine.py. "
        "Any other module emitting ConfidenceUpdateEvent raises EventAuthorizationError."
    ),
    "sync_point_immutability": (
        "hybrid_sync_point in GlobalSystemState is set once. "
        "Any subsequent ctrl.update(hybrid_sync_point=...) raises ImmutabilityViolationError."
    ),
}
```

---

## ARCHITECTURE CLARITY IMPROVEMENTS

**Purpose:** Remove all remaining ambiguities in the blueprint regarding mode
transitions, state mutation exclusivity, data integrity escalation, failure mode
propagation, and confidence update paths.

---

### HYBRID SYNC_POINT LOGIC (UNAMBIGUOUS)

```
sync_point LIFECYCLE:

  1. INITIALIZATION:
     At MODE_HYBRID startup: GlobalSystemState.hybrid_sync_point = None
     HistoricalDataProvider is active. Backfill begins from start_time.

  2. SYNC_POINT DETECTION:
     sync_point is set when:
       a. LiveDataProvider confirms first valid candle ingested (all 5 integrity
          checks pass), AND
       b. The candle timestamp > backfill_end_time (configurable)
     Detection happens in: jarvis/core/hybrid_coordinator.py

  3. SYNC_POINT SETTING (ATOMIC):
     ctrl.update(hybrid_sync_point=detected_timestamp)
     This is the ONLY call that sets hybrid_sync_point.
     After this call: hybrid_sync_point is immutable for the session.
     Any subsequent attempt to modify it raises ImmutabilityViolationError.

  4. POST SYNC_POINT BEHAVIOR:
     - HistoricalDataProvider is stopped (no more backfill events emitted)
     - LiveDataProvider becomes sole data source
     - RefreshPolicy switches to LIVE_ANALYTICAL rules:
         full_recompute_allowed = False
         incremental_only = True
     - All state updates: incremental only, rolling window, deterministic cycle
     - EventLog continues uninterrupted — no session break at sync_point
```

---

### MODE TRANSITION ATOMICITY

```
MODE TRANSITIONS are atomic operations:

  Permitted transitions:
    HISTORICAL     -> LIVE_ANALYTICAL  (not recommended; requires full restart)
    HISTORICAL     -> HYBRID           (normal for hybrid session startup)
    HYBRID         -> LIVE_ANALYTICAL  (after sync_point stabilizes, if configured)
    LIVE_ANALYTICAL -> (none; terminal mode for session)

  Transition execution:
    1. ctrl.update(operating_mode=new_mode) — single atomic call
    2. RefreshPolicy updated immediately: REFRESH_POLICIES[new_mode]
    3. Data provider swapped: HistoricalDataProvider -> LiveDataProvider
    4. No intermediate state permitted between modes
    5. In-flight events at transition time: completed in old mode, then new mode applies
    6. EventLog records mode_transition event (internal, non-analytical)

  FORBIDDEN:
    - Running two modes simultaneously
    - Partial mode switch (some layers in old mode, some in new mode)
    - Mode transition triggered by external API call (only by HybridCoordinator)
```

---

### STATE MUTATION EXCLUSIVITY

```
ctrl.update() IS THE ONLY PERMITTED STATE MUTATION PATH.

AUDIT TRAIL:
  Every ctrl.update() call is logged with:
    - calling module and line number
    - event_id that triggered the update (if applicable)
    - fields being modified
    - state_hash before and after
  Log destination: structured JSON append-only audit log

PERMITTED CALLERS:
  Module                   | Fields it may update
  ─────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────
  regime_engine.py         | regime_*, regime_confidence, regime_probs
  volatility_layer.py      | vol_regime, vol_percentile, vol_spike_flag, nvu_normalized
  strategy_selector.py     | strategy_mode, weight_scalar, active_strategy_id
  risk_engine.py           | risk_mode, risk_compression
  portfolio_context.py     | positions, gross_exposure, net_exposure, correlation_matrix
  confidence_engine.py     | meta_uncertainty
  failure_handler.py       | meta_uncertainty (via IMPACT_TABLE deltas)
  hybrid_coordinator.py    | hybrid_sync_point (once only), operating_mode
  replay_engine.py         | all fields (during replay from checkpoint only)
  ─────────────────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────
  ALL OTHER MODULES:       FORBIDDEN from calling ctrl.update()
```

---

### DATA INTEGRITY ESCALATION FLOW

```
ESCALATION PATH when data integrity issue detected:

  Level 1 — WARNING (quality_score reduced, asset flagged as SUSPECT):
    Trigger: Outlier filter (CHECK 4 in Integrity Gate)
    Action: quality_score -= 0.30; is_stale = True on StandardizedMarketDataObject
    No FM triggered if quality_score >= 0.5 after reduction

  Level 2 — FM-03 (DATA_GAP) or FM-06 (SPREAD_ANOMALY):
    Trigger: Any integrity gate check fails; quality_score < 0.5
    Action: FM emitted via FailureModeEvent; IMPACT_TABLE applied to confidence;
            asset excluded from new allocations
    System continues operating — no halt

  Level 3 — FM-01 (UNDEFINED_REGIME) cascading from data gap:
    Trigger: FM-03 causes FeatureVector STALE; Regime Engine cannot update
    Action: regime = UNKNOWN; MINIMAL_EXPOSURE mode; meta_uncertainty + 0.30

  Level 4 — Emergency Shutdown:
    Trigger: meta_uncertainty > 0.90 OR integrity_status = COMPROMISED
    Action: ctrl.emergency_shutdown(reason); mode = EMERGENCY
    All state writes frozen; system readable for diagnostics only

  ESCALATION IS UNIDIRECTIONAL:
    Once meta_uncertainty > 0.90: only emergency_shutdown() can proceed.
    No module may manually reduce meta_uncertainty to avoid shutdown.
    Recovery from EMERGENCY requires explicit operator restart.
```

---

### FAILURE MODE PROPAGATION PATH

```
FM PROPAGATION (system-wide, authoritative):

  Detection Layer → failure_handler.py → FailureModeEvent emitted →
  EventQueue → EventDispatcher → ctrl.update() → IMPACT_TABLE applied →
  ConfidenceBundle updated → ConfidenceUpdateEvent emitted (if trigger met) →
  Visual Output renders FM banners

  DETECTION LAYERS:
    FM-01: Regime Engine — regime_confidence < 0.40
    FM-02: Volatility Layer — nvu_normalized > 3.0 or vol_percentile > 0.95
    FM-03: Data Layer / Integrity Gate — gap detected or quality_score < 0.5
    FM-04: Portfolio Context — mean pairwise correlation > 0.85
    FM-05: Strategy Layer — session classified as illiquid + LIQUID_ONLY sensitivity
    FM-06: Risk Engine / Integrity Gate — spread_bps > max_entry_spread_bps * 2.0

  PROPAGATION RULES:
    1. Only failure_handler.py emits FailureModeEvent — no other module
    2. Detection layers call failure_handler.handle(fm_code, context)
    3. failure_handler applies IMPACT_TABLE via ctrl.update()
    4. Multiple simultaneous FMs: most-restrictive behavior applied (no averaging)
    5. FM resolution: failure_handler.resolve(fm_code) emits deactivation event
```

---

### CONFIDENCE UPDATE PATH

```
CONFIDENCE UPDATE PATH (complete, unambiguous):

  1. STATE CHANGE OCCURS (any of five permitted triggers)
  2. should_refresh_confidence(prev, curr, mode) → True
  3. confidence_engine.compute(curr_snapshot) → new ConfidenceBundle
  4. IMPACT_TABLE applied if any FM active (confidence can only decrease)
  5. ctrl.update(meta_uncertainty=new_bundle.U) — ONLY field written to state
  6. ConfidenceUpdateEvent emitted with delta values
  7. EventQueue → EventDispatcher routes to Visual Output (P9)
  8. Visual Output renders updated confidence display

  WHAT DOES NOT HAPPEN:
    - confidence_engine does NOT write mu, Q, S, R to GlobalSystemState
      (only meta_uncertainty is written — other bundle fields are display-only)
    - Confidence does NOT trigger execution of any kind
    - Confidence does NOT override Risk Engine outputs
    - Confidence does NOT auto-adjust StrategyObject weights directly
      (strategy weight changes are a separate event: StrategyWeightChangeEvent)
```

---

---

## PHASE 2 — EPISTEMIC UNCERTAINTY LAYER (BLOCK D)

**Datei:** `jarvis/intelligence/epistemic_uncertainty.py`
**Classification:** Analytical only. UncertaintyBundle is read-only for downstream.
No execution triggers. Deterministic decay — no time-based randomness.

---

### UNCERTAINTY BUNDLE (CANONICAL DEFINITION)

```python
# jarvis/intelligence/epistemic_uncertainty.py
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict
import numpy as np


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class UncertaintyBundle:
    """
    Aggregated uncertainty quantification for the current analytical state.
    Frozen — downstream layers receive this as a read-only input.

    COMPONENTS:
      epistemic_model:  Uncertainty from model limitations (regime instability,
                        feature sparsity, OOD detection)
      epistemic_data:   Uncertainty from data quality (gaps, staleness, outliers)
      aleatoric:        Irreducible market randomness (from realized volatility)
      total_uncertainty: Weighted combination [0, 1]

    PERMITTED DATA PATHS (read-only):
      - ConfidenceBundle: total_uncertainty contributes to sigma^2 (system contract)
      - Strategy Weight posterior: reduces weight if total_uncertainty > 0.5
      - Visual Output (P9): full display

    FORBIDDEN:
      - Direct state mutation
      - Execution triggers
      - Overriding Risk Engine outputs
    """
    epistemic_model:   float   # [0, 1] — model uncertainty
    epistemic_data:    float   # [0, 1] — data uncertainty
    aleatoric:         float   # [0, 1] — irreducible volatility component
    total_uncertainty: float   # [0, 1] — weighted composite
    model_uncertainty_score: float   # Specific model uncertainty score (below)
    data_sparsity_penalty:   float   # [0, 1] — below-threshold sample penalty
    confidence_decay_applied: float  # [0, 0.30] — decay applied this cycle

    def __post_init__(self):
        for name, val in [
            ("epistemic_model", self.epistemic_model),
            ("epistemic_data", self.epistemic_data),
            ("aleatoric", self.aleatoric),
            ("total_uncertainty", self.total_uncertainty),
        ]:
            if not (0.0 <= val <= 1.0):
                raise ValueError(f"UncertaintyBundle.{name} must be in [0,1]: {val}")
```

---

### MODEL UNCERTAINTY SCORE

```python
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ModelUncertaintyScore:
    """
    Quantifies epistemic uncertainty from model and system quality.
    Three components: regime instability, data sparsity, failure mode frequency.
    Deterministic computation — no stochastic elements.
    """
    regime_instability_score: float   # High = frequent regime changes
    data_sparsity_score:      float   # High = few valid samples
    fm_frequency_score:       float   # High = many recent Failure Mode activations
    model_uncertainty_score:  float   # Weighted sum [0, 1]


# Weights for model uncertainty components — registered in 99_REFERENCE.md
MUS_WEIGHT_REGIME    = 0.40
MUS_WEIGHT_SPARSITY  = 0.35
MUS_WEIGHT_FM_FREQ   = 0.25


def compute_model_uncertainty(
    n_regime_changes_last_20: int,    # Regime changes in last 20 bars
    n_valid_samples: int,             # Valid samples in rolling window
    n_fm_activations_last_20: int,    # FM activations in last 20 bars
    rolling_window_size: int = 20,
) -> ModelUncertaintyScore:
    """
    Deterministic model uncertainty scoring.
    All inputs are counts/integers — no randomness.
    """
    # Regime instability: normalized to [0,1] against max 10 changes in 20 bars
    regime_score = float(np.clip(n_regime_changes_last_20 / 10.0, 0.0, 1.0))

    # Data sparsity: inverse of fill rate
    fill_rate = float(np.clip(n_valid_samples / max(rolling_window_size, 1), 0.0, 1.0))
    sparsity_score = 1.0 - fill_rate

    # FM frequency: normalized to [0,1] against max 6 activations in 20 bars
    fm_score = float(np.clip(n_fm_activations_last_20 / 6.0, 0.0, 1.0))

    total = (MUS_WEIGHT_REGIME * regime_score +
             MUS_WEIGHT_SPARSITY * sparsity_score +
             MUS_WEIGHT_FM_FREQ * fm_score)

    return ModelUncertaintyScore(
        regime_instability_score=regime_score,
        data_sparsity_score=sparsity_score,
        fm_frequency_score=fm_score,
        model_uncertainty_score=float(np.clip(total, 0.0, 1.0)),
    )
```

---

### DATA SPARSITY PENALTY

```python
# Governance constant — registered in 99_REFERENCE.md
DATA_SPARSITY_THRESHOLD = 0.60   # Minimum valid sample fraction (60%)
DATA_SPARSITY_MAX_PENALTY = 0.40 # Maximum confidence multiplier reduction


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class DataSparsityPenalty:
    """
    Applied when valid sample fraction drops below DATA_SPARSITY_THRESHOLD.
    Confidence multiplier is reduced proportionally.
    Deterministic.
    """
    valid_fraction:       float   # Valid samples / window size
    below_threshold:      bool    # valid_fraction < DATA_SPARSITY_THRESHOLD
    confidence_multiplier: float  # [1 - max_penalty, 1.0] applied to Q
    sparsity_penalty:     float   # Absolute reduction amount


def compute_sparsity_penalty(
    n_valid: int,
    window_size: int,
) -> DataSparsityPenalty:
    """
    If valid fraction < threshold: apply linear confidence penalty.
    """
    valid_frac = float(np.clip(n_valid / max(window_size, 1), 0.0, 1.0))
    below = valid_frac < DATA_SPARSITY_THRESHOLD

    if below:
        deficit = DATA_SPARSITY_THRESHOLD - valid_frac
        penalty = float(np.clip(deficit * DATA_SPARSITY_MAX_PENALTY / DATA_SPARSITY_THRESHOLD,
                                0.0, DATA_SPARSITY_MAX_PENALTY))
        multiplier = 1.0 - penalty
    else:
        penalty = 0.0
        multiplier = 1.0

    return DataSparsityPenalty(
        valid_fraction=valid_frac,
        below_threshold=below,
        confidence_multiplier=float(np.clip(multiplier, 1.0 - DATA_SPARSITY_MAX_PENALTY, 1.0)),
        sparsity_penalty=penalty,
    )
```

---

### CONFIDENCE DECAY RULE

```python
# Governance constants — registered in 99_REFERENCE.md
CONFIDENCE_DECAY_FACTOR      = 0.02   # Per-bar decay rate when no confirmation signal
CONFIDENCE_DECAY_MAX         = 0.10   # Maximum total decay per update cycle
CONFIDENCE_DECAY_MIN_VALUE   = 0.30   # Minimum confidence Q after decay


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ConfidenceDecayResult:
    """
    Deterministic confidence decay applied when no confirmation signal is present.
    Confidence decreases over time without fresh evidence.
    No time-based randomness — decay is per-bar, deterministic.

    CONFIRMATION SIGNALS (decay is NOT applied when these are present):
      - Fresh MarketDataEvent admitted (quality_score >= 0.70)
      - RegimeChangeEvent in current cycle
      - StrategyWeightChangeEvent in current cycle

    DECAY DOES NOT:
      - Fall below CONFIDENCE_DECAY_MIN_VALUE
      - Exceed CONFIDENCE_DECAY_MAX per cycle
      - Use random rate variation
    """
    prior_Q:          float
    bars_since_signal: int    # Bars elapsed since last confirmation signal
    decay_applied:    float   # Actual decay magnitude applied
    new_Q:            float   # Q after decay
    decay_was_active: bool    # True if decay was applied (no confirmation signal)


def apply_confidence_decay(
    prior_Q: float,
    bars_since_signal: int,
    has_confirmation_signal: bool,
) -> ConfidenceDecayResult:
    """
    Apply deterministic per-bar confidence decay.
    """
    if has_confirmation_signal or bars_since_signal == 0:
        return ConfidenceDecayResult(
            prior_Q=prior_Q,
            bars_since_signal=bars_since_signal,
            decay_applied=0.0,
            new_Q=prior_Q,
            decay_was_active=False,
        )

    raw_decay = CONFIDENCE_DECAY_FACTOR * bars_since_signal
    decay = float(np.clip(raw_decay, 0.0, CONFIDENCE_DECAY_MAX))
    new_Q = float(np.clip(prior_Q - decay, CONFIDENCE_DECAY_MIN_VALUE, 1.0))

    return ConfidenceDecayResult(
        prior_Q=prior_Q,
        bars_since_signal=bars_since_signal,
        decay_applied=prior_Q - new_Q,
        new_Q=new_Q,
        decay_was_active=True,
    )
```

---

### UNCERTAINTY BUNDLE ASSEMBLY

```python
class EpistemicUncertaintyEngine:
    """
    Assembles the full UncertaintyBundle from all epistemic components.
    Deterministic. Frozen output.
    GOVERNANCE: Output is read-only for all downstream layers.
    """

    def compute(
        self,
        model_uncertainty: ModelUncertaintyScore,
        sparsity_penalty: DataSparsityPenalty,
        decay_result: ConfidenceDecayResult,
        realized_vol_nvu: float,    # Current NVU-normalized volatility [0+]
    ) -> UncertaintyBundle:
        """
        Assemble UncertaintyBundle from all components.
        Total uncertainty = weighted sum of epistemic and aleatoric components.
        """
        ep_model = model_uncertainty.model_uncertainty_score
        ep_data  = sparsity_penalty.sparsity_penalty + decay_result.decay_applied
        ep_data  = float(np.clip(ep_data, 0.0, 1.0))

        # Aleatoric = irreducible market noise; mapped from NVU
        aleatoric = float(np.clip(realized_vol_nvu / 5.0, 0.0, 1.0))

        total = float(np.clip(
            0.45 * ep_model + 0.35 * ep_data + 0.20 * aleatoric, 0.0, 1.0
        ))

        return UncertaintyBundle(
            epistemic_model=ep_model,
            epistemic_data=ep_data,
            aleatoric=aleatoric,
            total_uncertainty=total,
            model_uncertainty_score=ep_model,
            data_sparsity_penalty=sparsity_penalty.sparsity_penalty,
            confidence_decay_applied=decay_result.decay_applied,
        )
```

**GOVERNANCE:**
```
UncertaintyBundle may ONLY influence:
  1. ConfidenceBundle: total_uncertainty -> contributes to sigma^2 in system contract
     D(t) = {mu, sigma^2, Q, S, U, R}; U = meta_uncertainty informed by total_uncertainty
  2. Strategy Weight posterior: if total_uncertainty > 0.5, weight posterior capped at 0.3
  3. Visual Output (P9): full uncertainty breakdown displayed

UncertaintyBundle may NOT:
  - Directly modify any state via ctrl.update()
  - Trigger execution
  - Override Risk Engine thresholds
  - Cause FM activation by itself (FMs have their own trigger conditions)
```

# MULTI-ASSET SYSTEM UPGRADE: CRYPTO + FOREX + INDICES + COMMODITIES

## EXECUTIVE SUMMARY

**Zielsetzung:** Erweiterung von einem Crypto-only System zu einem vollständigen Multi-Asset Trading System (Crypto, Forex, Indices, Commodities, Rates).

**Kernbotschaft:** Die bestehende 11-Layer Architektur ist **bereits multi-asset fähig**. Keine Neuarchitektur notwendig. Nur **gezielte Module-Upgrades** und **Asset-Class-Awareness** in kritischen Layern.

**Status:** CRITICAL PATH für Production-Ready System

---

## SECTION 1: ARCHITEKTUR-BEWERTUNG

### 1.1 Bestehende Architektur bleibt gültig ✅

Die 11-Layer Struktur funktioniert universal:
- Layer 1-11 bleiben strukturell identisch
- Flow: Data → Features → State → Regime → OOD → Risk → Capital → Execution
- Keine neuen Layer notwendig

### 1.2 Was sich ZWINGEND ändern muss ⚠️

| Layer | Status | Upgrade-Typ | Kritikalität |
|-------|--------|-------------|--------------|
| Layer 1 (Data) | ⚠️ UPGRADE | Market Microstructure | CRITICAL |
| Layer 2 (Features) | ⚠️ UPGRADE | Asset-Class Registry | CRITICAL |
| Layer 4 (Regime) | ⚠️ UPGRADE | Multi-Regime Engine | HIGH |
| Layer 5 (OOD) | ⚠️ UPGRADE | Asset-Conditional Thresholds | HIGH |
| Layer 8 (Risk) | ⚠️ UPGRADE | Cross-Asset Risk | CRITICAL |
| Layer 9 (Capital) | ✅ IMPROVE | Diversification Gain | MEDIUM |
| Layer 10 (Execution) | ⚠️ UPGRADE | Session Awareness | MEDIUM |

**Alle anderen Layer:** Minimal oder keine Änderungen

---

## SECTION 2: LAYER-BY-LAYER UPGRADE SPEZIFIKATION

### LAYER 1: DATA INGESTION - CRITICAL UPGRADE

#### Problem
Crypto, Forex und Indices haben fundamental unterschiedliche Marktmechanik:

| Merkmal | Crypto | Forex | Indices | Commodities |
|---------|--------|-------|---------|-------------|
| Handelszeiten | 24/7 | 24/5 | Session-basiert | Session-basiert |
| Liquidität | Fragmentiert | Zentral/Hoch | Zentralisiert | Variabel |
| Gaps | Selten | Selten | Häufig (Open) | Häufig |
| Volatilität | Hoch | Mittel | Regime-abhängig | Mittel-Hoch |
| Spreads | Variabel | Eng | Mittel | Variabel |

#### Upgrade-Anforderungen

**Neu hinzufügen zu `jarvis/core/data_layer.py`:**

```python
class MarketMicrostructure(BaseModel):
    """Asset-class specific market characteristics"""
    asset_class: Literal["crypto", "forex", "indices", "commodities", "rates"]
    trading_hours: TradingHours  # 24/7, 24/5, session-based
    gap_detection: bool  # Enable gap analysis
    spread_model: SpreadModel  # Fixed, variable, session-dependent
    liquidity_regime: LiquidityRegime
    session_structure: Optional[SessionStructure]
    holiday_calendar: Optional[str]

class SessionStructure(BaseModel):
    """For session-based markets (indices, some commodities)"""
    sessions: List[Session]  # Asia, Europe, US
    pre_market: Optional[TimeWindow]
    post_market: Optional[TimeWindow]
    auction_times: List[datetime]
    
class EnhancedMarketData(MarketData):
    """Extended with multi-asset awareness"""
    microstructure: MarketMicrostructure
    gap_detected: bool
    gap_size: Optional[float]
    current_session: Optional[str]  # "asia", "europe", "us"
    liquidity_regime: LiquidityRegime
    spread_estimate: float
    execution_cost_estimate: float
```

**Neue Validierung:**

```python
def validate_market_data(data: EnhancedMarketData) -> ValidationResult:
    """Asset-class specific validation"""
    
    if data.microstructure.asset_class == "indices":
        # Check for gaps at market open
        if data.gap_detected and data.gap_size > 0.02:  # 2%
            return ValidationResult(
                valid=True,  # Gaps are normal for indices
                warnings=["Large gap detected at market open"],
                gap_adjusted=True
            )
    
    if data.microstructure.asset_class == "forex":
        # Different validation for FX
        if data.current_session == "asia" and data.liquidity_regime == "low":
            return ValidationResult(
                valid=True,
                warnings=["Low liquidity in Asian session"],
                liquidity_adjusted=True
            )
    
    # ... asset-specific checks
```

**Migration von bestehendem Code:**

1. Alle `MarketData` Instanzen werden zu `EnhancedMarketData`
2. Crypto behält bisheriges Verhalten (24/7, no gaps)
3. Neue Assets erhalten ihre spezifischen Microstructure-Configs

**Quality Metrics Update:**

# Alt (Crypto-only):
quality_score = base_score * (1 - nan_ratio)

# Neu (Multi-Asset):
quality_score = base_score * (1 - nan_ratio) * session_factor * liquidity_factor

session_factor = get_session_quality(asset_class, current_time)

```python
class FeatureRegistry:
    """Asset-class aware feature system"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.universal_features = UniversalFeatures()  # Work for all assets
        self.crypto_features = CryptoFeatures()
        self.fx_features = ForexFeatures()
        self.indices_features = IndicesFeatures()
        self.commodities_features = CommoditiesFeatures()
    
    def get_features(self, asset_class: str, market_data: EnhancedMarketData) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Returns asset-appropriate feature set"""
        
        # Always compute universal features
        features = self.universal_features.compute(market_data)
        
        # Add asset-specific features
        if asset_class == "crypto":
            features.update(self.crypto_features.compute(market_data))
        elif asset_class == "forex":
            features.update(self.fx_features.compute(market_data))
        elif asset_class == "indices":
            features.update(self.indices_features.compute(market_data))
        # ...
        
        return features

class UniversalFeatures:
    """Features that work across all asset classes"""
    
    def compute(self, data: EnhancedMarketData) -> Dict[str, float]:
        return {
            # Price-based
            "returns_1h": calculate_returns(data, "1h"),
            "returns_4h": calculate_returns(data, "4h"),
            "returns_24h": calculate_returns(data, "24h"),
            "volatility_realized": calculate_volatility(data),
            "volatility_parkinson": parkinson_volatility(data),
            
            # Volume-based
            "volume_ratio": volume_ratio(data),
            "volume_trend": volume_trend(data),
            
            # Technical
            "rsi_14": calculate_rsi(data, 14),
            "macd": calculate_macd(data),
            "bollinger_position": bollinger_position(data),
            
            # Microstructure (adjusted per asset)
            "spread_bps": data.spread_estimate * 10000,
            "liquidity_score": data.liquidity_regime.score,
            
            # ... ~40 universal features
        }

class ForexFeatures:
    """FX-specific features"""
    
    def compute(self, data: EnhancedMarketData) -> Dict[str, float]:
        return {
            # Macro
            "rate_differential": get_rate_differential(data.symbol),
            "dxy_correlation": calculate_dxy_correlation(data),
            "carry_signal": calculate_carry_signal(data),
            
            # FX-specific
            "bid_ask_spread": calculate_fx_spread(data),
            "forward_points": get_forward_points(data),
            "option_skew": get_fx_option_skew(data.symbol),
            
            # Central bank
            "cb_meeting_proximity": days_to_cb_meeting(data.symbol),
            "policy_rate_trend": get_policy_rate_trend(data.symbol),
            
            # ... ~20 FX features
        }

class IndicesFeatures:
    """Index-specific features"""
    
    def compute(self, data: EnhancedMarketData) -> Dict[str, float]:
        return {
            # Risk sentiment
            "vix_level": get_vix_level(),
            "vix_term_structure": get_vix_term_structure(),
            "put_call_ratio": get_put_call_ratio(data.symbol),
            "credit_spread": get_credit_spread(),
            
            # Market regime
            "risk_on_off_score": calculate_risk_sentiment(),
            "sector_rotation": calculate_sector_rotation(),
            "breadth_indicator": calculate_market_breadth(data.symbol),
            
            # Index-specific
            "futures_basis": get_futures_basis(data.symbol),
            "dividend_yield": get_dividend_yield(data.symbol),
            
            # ... ~15 index features
        }

**Feature Dimension Management:**

```python
# CRITICAL: Models expect fixed dimension input
# Solution: Feature padding/masking

class FeatureEncoder:
    """Ensures consistent feature dimensions across assets"""
    
    def __init__(self, target_dim: int = 99):
        self.target_dim = target_dim
        self.feature_mask = {}  # Tracks which features are active
    
    def encode(self, features: Dict[str, float], asset_class: str) -> np.ndarray:
        """Converts variable-length features to fixed dimension"""
        
        # Create base array
        encoded = np.zeros(self.target_dim)
        
        # Fill with universal features (indices 0-39)
        for i, key in enumerate(UNIVERSAL_FEATURE_ORDER):
            if key in features:
                encoded[i] = features[key]
        
        # Fill asset-specific features (indices 40-98)
        if asset_class == "crypto":
            for i, key in enumerate(CRYPTO_FEATURE_ORDER, start=40):
                if key in features:
                    encoded[i] = features[key]
        elif asset_class == "forex":
            for i, key in enumerate(FX_FEATURE_ORDER, start=40):
                if key in features:
                    encoded[i] = features[key]
        # ...
        
        # Store mask (for gradient computation)
        self.feature_mask[asset_class] = (encoded != 0).astype(float)
        
        return encoded
```

### LAYER 4: REGIME DETECTION - HIGH PRIORITY UPGRADE

#### Problem
Ein einzelnes Regime-Modell für alle Asset-Classes ist instabil:
- Crypto-Regimes (high vol, funding-driven) ≠ FX-Regimes (macro-driven)
- FX-Regimes ≠ Index-Regimes (risk sentiment-driven)

#### Upgrade: Hierarchical Multi-Regime System

**Neue Architektur:**

```
Global Macro Regime (Top-Level)
├── Monetary Policy Regime (Fed, ECB, BoJ)
├── Risk Sentiment Regime (Risk-On / Risk-Off)
└── Liquidity Regime (Tight / Normal / Abundant)
    │
    ├── Asset-Class Regimes
    │   ├── Crypto Regime (Leverage / Retail / Institutional)
    │   ├── FX Regime (Carry / Trend / Range)
    │   ├── Indices Regime (Bull / Bear / Rotation)
    │   └── Commodities Regime (Contango / Backwardation / Squeeze)
    │
    └── Cross-Asset Correlation Regime
        ├── Normal Correlation
        ├── Correlation Breakdown (Crisis)
        └── Divergence Regime
```

**Implementation in `jarvis/intelligence/regime_detector.py`:**

```python
class HierarchicalRegimeDetector:
    """Multi-level regime detection"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.global_regime = GlobalMacroRegime()
        self.asset_regimes = {
            "crypto": CryptoRegimeDetector(),
            "forex": ForexRegimeDetector(),
            "indices": IndicesRegimeDetector(),
            "commodities": CommoditiesRegimeDetector()
        }
        self.correlation_regime = CorrelationRegimeDetector()
    
    def detect(self, 
               market_data: Dict[str, EnhancedMarketData],
               features: Dict[str, np.ndarray]) -> HierarchicalRegime:
        """Detects regimes at all levels"""
        
        # Level 1: Global macro regime
        global_regime = self.global_regime.detect(
            fed_rates=get_fed_rates(),
            vix=get_vix(),
            credit_spreads=get_credit_spreads()
        )
        
        # Level 2: Asset-specific regimes (conditioned on global)
        asset_regimes = {}
        for asset_class, detector in self.asset_regimes.items():
            if asset_class in features:
                asset_regimes[asset_class] = detector.detect(
                    features=features[asset_class],
                    global_regime=global_regime  # Conditioning
                )
        
        # Level 3: Cross-asset correlation
        correlation_regime = self.correlation_regime.detect(
            market_data=market_data,
            asset_regimes=asset_regimes
        )
        
        return HierarchicalRegime(
            global_regime=global_regime,
            asset_regimes=asset_regimes,
            correlation_regime=correlation_regime,
            timestamp=datetime.now()
        )

class CryptoRegimeDetector:
    """Crypto-specific regime detection"""
    
    REGIMES = ["leverage_mania", "retail_fomo", "institutional", "deleveraging", "capitulation"]
    
    def detect(self, features: np.ndarray, global_regime: GlobalRegime) -> RegimeResult:
        # Use crypto-specific features
        funding_rate = features[40]  # Crypto-specific feature index
        open_interest = features[41]
        liquidations = features[42]
        
        # HMM tuned for crypto
        regime_probs = self.hmm.predict_proba(features)
        
        # Condition on global regime
        if global_regime.state == "risk_off" and regime_probs["leverage_mania"] > 0.5:
            # Override: leverage in risk-off = high danger
            regime_probs["deleveraging"] = 0.8
        
        return RegimeResult(
            state=self._select_regime(regime_probs),
            probabilities=regime_probs,
            confidence=calculate_confidence(regime_probs)
        )

class ForexRegimeDetector:
    """FX-specific regime detection"""
    
    REGIMES = ["carry_trade", "trend_following", "range_bound", "risk_off_flight"]
    
    def detect(self, features: np.ndarray, global_regime: GlobalRegime) -> RegimeResult:
        # Use FX-specific features
        rate_differential = features[40]  # FX feature index
        dxy_correlation = features[41]
        carry_signal = features[42]
        
        # Different HMM for FX
        regime_probs = self.fx_hmm.predict_proba(features)
        
        return RegimeResult(...)
```

**Regime Memory Extension:**

```python
class RegimeMemory:
    """Extended for multi-asset"""
    
    def update(self, regime: HierarchicalRegime):
        # Store global regime history (longer cycles)
        self.global_history.append(regime.global_regime)
        
        # Store asset-specific histories (shorter cycles)
        for asset_class, asset_regime in regime.asset_regimes.items():
            self.asset_histories[asset_class].append(asset_regime)
        
        # Detect regime transitions
        transitions = self._detect_transitions()
        
        # Multi-asset: track correlation regime changes
        if regime.correlation_regime.state == "breakdown":
            # CRITICAL: All correlations → 1 in crisis
            self._set_high_alert()
```

### LAYER 5: OOD DETECTION - HIGH PRIORITY UPGRADE

#### Problem
OOD-Definitionen unterscheiden sich massiv zwischen Asset-Classes:

| Event | Crypto | Forex | Indices |
|-------|--------|-------|---------|
| Flash Crash 10% | Normal | EXTREME | Medium |
| Central Bank Shock | Low impact | EXTREME | High |
| Gap Open 2% | Rare | Rare | NORMAL |
| 50% Vol Spike | Medium | EXTREME | Medium |

#### Upgrade: Asset-Conditional OOD Thresholds

**Implementation in `jarvis/intelligence/ood_engine.py`:**

```python
class AssetConditionalOOD:
    """Asset-class aware OOD detection"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.thresholds = {
            "crypto": CryptoOODThresholds(),
            "forex": ForexOODThresholds(),
            "indices": IndicesOODThresholds(),
            "commodities": CommoditiesOODThresholds()
        }
        self.macro_ood = MacroEventDetector()
    
    def detect(self, 
               asset_class: str,
               features: np.ndarray,
               market_data: EnhancedMarketData) -> OODResult:
        """Asset-aware OOD detection"""
        
        # Get asset-specific thresholds
        thresholds = self.thresholds[asset_class]
        
        # Compute OOD scores
        distribution_ood = self._distribution_ood(features, thresholds)
        event_ood = self._event_ood(market_data, thresholds)
        macro_ood = self.macro_ood.detect(asset_class)
        
        # Combine with asset-specific weighting
        total_ood = (
            thresholds.distribution_weight * distribution_ood +
            thresholds.event_weight * event_ood +
            thresholds.macro_weight * macro_ood
        )
        
        return OODResult(
            is_ood=total_ood > thresholds.ood_threshold,
            score=total_ood,
            severity=self._calculate_severity(total_ood, thresholds),
            components={
                "distribution": distribution_ood,
                "event": event_ood,
                "macro": macro_ood
            }
        )

class CryptoOODThresholds:
    """Crypto-specific thresholds (more tolerant to vol)"""
    ood_threshold = 0.7  # Higher than FX
    
    # Event thresholds
    flash_crash_threshold = 0.15  # 15% move = normal for crypto
    volatility_spike_threshold = 2.0  # 200% vol increase
    liquidity_drain_threshold = 0.3  # 70% liquidity drop
    
    # Weights
    distribution_weight = 0.4
    event_weight = 0.4
    macro_weight = 0.2  # Crypto less macro-sensitive

class ForexOODThresholds:
    """FX-specific thresholds (very strict)"""
    ood_threshold = 0.5  # Lower = more sensitive
    
    # Event thresholds
    flash_crash_threshold = 0.03  # 3% move = extreme for FX
    central_bank_shock_threshold = 0.02  # 2% on CB announcement
    volatility_spike_threshold = 0.8  # 80% vol increase
    
    # Weights
    distribution_weight = 0.3
    event_weight = 0.3
    macro_weight = 0.4  # FX very macro-sensitive

class MacroEventDetector:
    """Detects macro events affecting multiple assets"""
    
    MACRO_EVENTS = [
        "fed_meeting",
        "ecb_meeting",
        "nonfarm_payrolls",
        "cpi_release",
        "geopolitical_shock",
        "credit_event"
    ]
    
    def detect(self, asset_class: str) -> float:
        """Returns macro OOD score [0, 1]"""
        
        # Check economic calendar
        upcoming_events = self._get_upcoming_events(hours=24)
        
        score = 0.0
        for event in upcoming_events:
            if event.type in self.MACRO_EVENTS:
                # Weight by event importance and asset sensitivity
                sensitivity = ASSET_MACRO_SENSITIVITY[asset_class][event.type]
                score = max(score, event.importance * sensitivity)
        
        return score

# Asset-macro sensitivity matrix
ASSET_MACRO_SENSITIVITY = {
    "crypto": {
        "fed_meeting": 0.5,
        "ecb_meeting": 0.2,
        "nonfarm_payrolls": 0.3,
        "cpi_release": 0.4,
        "geopolitical_shock": 0.6,
        "credit_event": 0.7
    },
    "forex": {
        "fed_meeting": 0.9,  # Very sensitive
        "ecb_meeting": 0.9,
        "nonfarm_payrolls": 0.8,
        "cpi_release": 0.8,
        "geopolitical_shock": 0.7,
        "credit_event": 0.6
    },
    "indices": {
        "fed_meeting": 0.8,
        "ecb_meeting": 0.6,
        "nonfarm_payrolls": 0.7,
        "cpi_release": 0.7,
        "geopolitical_shock": 0.9,
        "credit_event": 0.9  # Very sensitive
    }
}
```

---

### LAYER 8: RISK ENGINE - CRITICAL UPGRADE

#### Problem
Aktuelles Risk-System versteht nur Single-Asset Crypto:
- Keine Cross-Asset Correlation
- Keine FX Exposure Netting
- Keine Tail Risk Diversification
- Keine Overnight Gap Risk (für Indices)

#### Upgrade: Portfolio Cross-Asset Risk Management

**New `jarvis/risk/portfolio_risk.py`:**

```python
class PortfolioRiskEngine:
    """Cross-asset portfolio risk management"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.correlation_model = DynamicCorrelationModel()
        self.tail_model = MultivariateTailModel()
        self.fx_exposure = FXExposureManager()
        self.gap_risk = GapRiskModel()
    
    def calculate_portfolio_risk(self, 
                                  positions: Dict[str, Position],
                                  market_data: Dict[str, EnhancedMarketData]) -> PortfolioRisk:
        """Comprehensive multi-asset risk calculation"""
        
        # 1. Individual asset risks
        asset_risks = {
            symbol: self._calculate_asset_risk(pos, market_data[symbol])
            for symbol, pos in positions.items()
        }
        
        # 2. Correlation matrix (dynamic)
        correlation_matrix = self.correlation_model.estimate(
            positions=positions,
            market_data=market_data,
            regime=current_regime
        )
        
        # 3. Portfolio variance (with correlations)
        portfolio_var = self._calculate_portfolio_variance(
            asset_risks=asset_risks,
            correlation_matrix=correlation_matrix,
            positions=positions
        )
        
        # 4. Tail risk (multivariate)
        tail_risk = self.tail_model.estimate_tail_risk(
            positions=positions,
            market_data=market_data,
            correlation_matrix=correlation_matrix
        )
        
        # 5. FX exposure (if multi-currency)
        fx_exposure = self.fx_exposure.calculate_exposure(positions)
        
        # 6. Gap risk (for session-based assets)
        gap_risk = self.gap_risk.estimate_gap_risk(
            positions=positions,
            market_data=market_data
        )
        
        return PortfolioRisk(
            total_var=portfolio_var,
            asset_risks=asset_risks,
            correlation_matrix=correlation_matrix,
            tail_var_95=tail_risk.var_95,
            tail_cvar_95=tail_risk.cvar_95,
            fx_exposure=fx_exposure,
            gap_risk=gap_risk,
            diversification_benefit=self._calculate_diversification_benefit(
                asset_risks, portfolio_var
            )
        )

class DynamicCorrelationModel:
    """Estimates time-varying correlations"""
    
    def estimate(self, 
                 positions: Dict[str, Position],
                 market_data: Dict[str, EnhancedMarketData],
                 regime: HierarchicalRegime) -> np.ndarray:
        """Correlation matrix that updates with regime"""
        
        # Base correlation (from historical data)
        base_corr = self._estimate_base_correlation(positions, market_data)
        
        # Regime adjustment
        if regime.correlation_regime.state == "breakdown":
            # CRITICAL: In crisis, all correlations → 1
            crisis_corr = np.ones_like(base_corr) * 0.8
            np.fill_diagonal(crisis_corr, 1.0)
            return crisis_corr
        
        elif regime.correlation_regime.state == "divergence":
            # Correlations lower than normal (good for diversification)
            return base_corr * 0.7
        
        else:
            # Normal regime
            return base_corr

class MultivariateTailModel:
    """Multi-asset tail risk estimation"""
    
    def estimate_tail_risk(self, 
                           positions: Dict[str, Position],
                           market_data: Dict[str, EnhancedMarketData],
                           correlation_matrix: np.ndarray) -> TailRisk:
        """Copula-based tail risk"""
        
        # 1. Fit marginal distributions (per asset)
        marginals = {}
        for symbol, pos in positions.items():
            asset_class = market_data[symbol].microstructure.asset_class
            
            # Use asset-specific tail distribution
            if asset_class == "crypto":
                marginals[symbol] = self._fit_crypto_tail(market_data[symbol])
            elif asset_class == "forex":
                marginals[symbol] = self._fit_fx_tail(market_data[symbol])
            # ...
        
        # 2. Fit copula (captures joint tail behavior)
        copula = self._fit_copula(marginals, correlation_matrix)
        
        # 3. Simulate joint tail scenarios
        tail_scenarios = copula.sample(n_scenarios=10000, tail_only=True)
        
        # 4. Calculate portfolio returns in tail scenarios
        portfolio_returns = self._calculate_portfolio_returns(
            scenarios=tail_scenarios,
            positions=positions
        )
        
        # 5. Compute VaR and CVaR
        var_95 = np.percentile(portfolio_returns, 5)
        cvar_95 = portfolio_returns[portfolio_returns <= var_95].mean()
        
        return TailRisk(
            var_95=var_95,
            cvar_95=cvar_95,
            worst_scenario=portfolio_returns.min(),
            tail_scenarios=tail_scenarios
        )

class GapRiskModel:
    """Overnight gap risk for session-based markets"""
    
    def estimate_gap_risk(self, 
                          positions: Dict[str, Position],
                          market_data: Dict[str, EnhancedMarketData]) -> GapRisk:
        """Estimates risk from overnight gaps"""
        
        total_gap_risk = 0.0
        asset_gap_risks = {}
        
        for symbol, pos in positions.items():
            asset_class = market_data[symbol].microstructure.asset_class
            
            # Only session-based markets have gap risk
            if asset_class in ["indices", "commodities"]:
                # Historical gap distribution
                gap_dist = self._estimate_gap_distribution(symbol, market_data[symbol])
                
                # Position size * expected gap
                asset_gap_risk = pos.notional * gap_dist.std() * GAP_MULTIPLIER
                asset_gap_risks[symbol] = asset_gap_risk
                total_gap_risk += asset_gap_risk
        
        return GapRisk(
            total=total_gap_risk,
            by_asset=asset_gap_risks,
            recommendation="Consider reducing size before market close"
            if total_gap_risk > GAP_RISK_THRESHOLD else None
        )
```

**Risk Budget Allocation Update:**

```python
class PortfolioRiskBudget:
    """Multi-asset risk budgeting"""
    
    def allocate(self, 
                 total_capital: float,
                 asset_classes: List[str],
                 regime: HierarchicalRegime) -> Dict[str, RiskBudget]:
        """Allocates risk budget across asset classes"""
        
        # 1. Base allocation (equal risk contribution)
        base_allocation = self._equal_risk_contribution(asset_classes)
        
        # 2. Regime adjustment
        regime_adjustment = self._regime_adjusted_allocation(
            base_allocation,
            regime
        )
        
        # 3. Correlation adjustment (increase when correlations low)
        correlation_adjustment = self._correlation_adjusted_allocation(
            regime_adjustment,
            regime.correlation_regime
        )
        
        # 4. Apply constraints
        final_allocation = self._apply_constraints(correlation_adjustment)
        
        return final_allocation
    
    def _regime_adjusted_allocation(self, 
                                     base: Dict[str, float],
                                     regime: HierarchicalRegime) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Adjust allocation based on regime"""
        
        adjusted = base.copy()
        
        # In risk-off regime, reduce risk assets
        if regime.global_regime.risk_sentiment == "risk_off":
            adjusted["crypto"] *= 0.5  # Reduce crypto exposure
            adjusted["indices"] *= 0.7  # Reduce equity exposure
            adjusted["forex"] *= 1.2   # Increase FX (safe haven)
        
        # In high correlation regime, reduce overall exposure
        if regime.correlation_regime.state == "breakdown":
            # All assets moving together = less diversification
            adjusted = {k: v * 0.6 for k, v in adjusted.items()}
        
        return adjusted
```

### LAYER 9: CAPITAL ALLOCATION - IMPROVEMENT (NICHT KRITISCH)

Gute Nachricht: Multi-Asset **verbessert** Capital Allocation automatisch!

#### Neue Vorteile:

```python
class MultiAssetCapitalAllocator:
    """Enhanced with diversification benefits"""
    
    def allocate(self, 
                 strategies: List[Strategy],
                 portfolio_risk: PortfolioRisk) -> Dict[Strategy, float]:
        """Capital allocation with diversification bonus"""
        
        # 1. Base Kelly allocation (per strategy)
        base_allocation = self._kelly_allocation(strategies)
        
        # 2. Diversification bonus
        diversification_benefit = portfolio_risk.diversification_benefit
        
        # Can increase total leverage due to diversification
        if diversification_benefit > 0.2:  # 20% risk reduction from diversification
            leverage_multiplier = 1.0 + (diversification_benefit * 0.5)
            base_allocation = {
                s: alloc * leverage_multiplier 
                for s, alloc in base_allocation.items()
            }
        
        # 3. Cross-asset rebalancing
        rebalanced = self._cross_asset_rebalancing(
            base_allocation,
            portfolio_risk.correlation_matrix
        )
        
        return rebalanced
    
    def _cross_asset_rebalancing(self, 
                                  allocation: Dict[Strategy, float],
                                  correlation_matrix: np.ndarray) -> Dict[Strategy, float]:
        """Rebalance to minimize correlation"""
        
        # Identify correlated strategies
        high_corr_pairs = self._find_high_correlation_pairs(correlation_matrix)
        
        # Reduce allocation to one of each correlated pair
        for strategy_a, strategy_b in high_corr_pairs:
            # Keep the better performer
            if allocation[strategy_a] < allocation[strategy_b]:
                allocation[strategy_a] *= 0.7
            else:
                allocation[strategy_b] *= 0.7
        
        return allocation
```

### LAYER 10: EXECUTION - MEDIUM PRIORITY UPGRADE

#### Problem
Execution muss session-aware werden für Indices und einige Commodities.

**Upgrade in `jarvis/execution/execution_engine.py`:**

```python
class SessionAwareExecutor:
    """Asset-class aware execution"""
    
    def execute(self, 
                order: Order,
                market_data: EnhancedMarketData) -> ExecutionResult:
        """Execution with session awareness"""
        
        asset_class = market_data.microstructure.asset_class
        
        if asset_class == "crypto":
            # 24/7 execution (existing logic)
            return self._execute_crypto(order, market_data)
        
        elif asset_class == "forex":
            # Check FX session
            current_session = market_data.current_session
            
            if current_session == "asia" and market_data.liquidity_regime == "low":
                # Wider spreads in Asian session
                return self._execute_with_wider_spreads(order, market_data)
            else:
                return self._execute_fx(order, market_data)
        
        elif asset_class == "indices":
            # Check if near market open/close
            if self._near_market_open(market_data):
                # Wait for opening auction
                return self._execute_at_auction(order, market_data)
            elif self._near_market_close(market_data):
                # Avoid execution near close (gap risk)
                return ExecutionResult(
                    status="deferred",
                    reason="Near market close, defer to next session"
                )
            else:
                return self._execute_indices(order, market_data)
```

Multi-asset correlation governance for VOLATILITY_SCALING-defined asset classes:

    computed by Dynamic Correlation Model (Section 2, correlation.py)
  - CORR_FM04_THRESHOLD = 0.85 is UNCHANGED (existing FM-04 rule)
  - CORR_LOW_THRESHOLD = 0.40, CORR_MEDIUM_THRESHOLD = 0.65 are additive
    classification layers — they do not modify FM-04 trigger behavior

  Asset classes covered:
    crypto, forex, indices, commodities (as defined in VOLATILITY_SCALING)

  ConcentrationRiskScore uses simulated weights_by_class — keyed by the
  same asset class labels as VOLATILITY_SCALING (never raw prices).

  No changes to VOLATILITY_SCALING constants.
  No changes to NVU normalization logic.

## SECTION 3: ENTSTEHENDE FEHLER & LÖSUNGEN

### Fehler 1: False Regime Mixing ⚠️

**Problem:** Wenn alle Assets dieselbe Regime-Engine teilen:
```python
# FALSCH:
regime = single_hmm.detect(features)  # Mischt Crypto + FX + Indices
```

**Lösung:** Hierarchisches Regime-System (siehe Layer 4)

---

### Fehler 2: Correlation Collapse in Crisis ⚠️

**Problem:** In Stress korrelieren ALLE Assets → 1:
- Diversifikation verschwindet
- Risk-Engine unterschätzt Risiko

**Lösung:**
```python
if regime.correlation_regime.state == "breakdown":
    # Force correlation adjustment
    correlation_matrix = np.ones_like(correlation_matrix) * 0.8
    
    # Reduce overall exposure
    risk_budget *= 0.5  # Cut risk in half
```

---

### Fehler 3: OOD Misclassification ⚠️

**Problem:**
- 10% Crypto move = normal
- 10% FX move = EXTREME

**Lösung:** Asset-conditional thresholds (siehe Layer 5)

---

### Fehler 4: Feature Leakage ⚠️

**Problem:** Crypto Features in FX Model:
```python
# FALSCH:
fx_prediction = model.predict(features_with_funding_rate)
```

**Lösung:** Asset-aware Feature Registry (siehe Layer 2)

---

### Fehler 5: Volatility Mismatch ⚠️

**Problem:**
- Crypto 5% daily vol = normal
- FX 5% daily vol = crisis

**Lösung:**
```python
def normalize_volatility(vol: float, asset_class: str) -> float:
    """Normalize to comparable scale"""
    return vol / VOLATILITY_SCALING[asset_class]

VOLATILITY_SCALING = {
    "crypto": 1.0,
    "forex": 0.3,  # FX 3x less volatile
    "indices": 0.6,
    "commodities": 0.8
}
```

# tests/test_multi_asset.py

def test_feature_registry_asset_separation():
    """Ensures crypto features don't leak into FX"""
    registry = FeatureRegistry()
    
    # Crypto data
    crypto_features = registry.get_features("crypto", crypto_data)
    assert "funding_rate" in crypto_features
    
    # FX data
    fx_features = registry.get_features("forex", fx_data)
    assert "funding_rate" not in fx_features  # Must NOT appear
    assert "rate_differential" in fx_features

def test_ood_asset_conditional():
    """Ensures OOD thresholds are asset-appropriate"""
    ood_engine = AssetConditionalOOD()
    
    # 10% move
    crypto_ood = ood_engine.detect("crypto", features, crypto_data_10pct_move)
    fx_ood = ood_engine.detect("forex", features, fx_data_10pct_move)
    
    assert not crypto_ood.is_ood  # Normal for crypto
    assert fx_ood.is_ood  # Extreme for FX
    assert fx_ood.severity == "critical"

def test_correlation_breakdown_risk():
    """Tests risk engine response to correlation collapse"""
    risk_engine = PortfolioRiskEngine()
    
    # Normal regime
    normal_risk = risk_engine.calculate_portfolio_risk(positions, normal_regime)
    
    # Crisis regime (correlations → 1)
    crisis_regime = create_crisis_regime()
    crisis_risk = risk_engine.calculate_portfolio_risk(positions, crisis_regime)
    
    assert crisis_risk.total_var > normal_risk.total_var * 2.0  # Risk doubles
    assert crisis_risk.diversification_benefit < 0.1  # Diversification lost
```
