```python
def test_full_multi_asset_flow():
    """End-to-end test with multiple assets"""
    
    # Portfolio: BTC (crypto) + EURUSD (forex) + SPX (index)
    symbols = ["BTC/USDT", "EUR/USD", "SPX"]
    
    # Ingest data
    market_data = {}
    for symbol in symbols:
        market_data[symbol] = data_layer.ingest(symbol)
        assert market_data[symbol].microstructure.asset_class in VALID_CLASSES
    
    # Compute features
    features = {}
    for symbol, data in market_data.items():
        features[symbol] = feature_layer.compute(data)
        # Check dimension consistency
        assert len(features[symbol]) == 99
    
    # Detect regimes
    regime = regime_detector.detect(market_data, features)
    assert hasattr(regime, "global_regime")
    assert hasattr(regime, "asset_regimes")
    assert "crypto" in regime.asset_regimes
    
    # Calculate risk
    portfolio_risk = risk_engine.calculate_portfolio_risk(positions, market_data)
    assert portfolio_risk.diversification_benefit > 0  # Should benefit from multi-asset
    
    # Generate signals
    signals = strategy_engine.generate_signals(features, regime, portfolio_risk)
    
    # Execute
    for signal in signals:
        result = execution_engine.execute(signal, market_data[signal.symbol])
        assert result.status in ["filled", "deferred", "rejected"]
```

def test_crisis_scenario():
    """Simulates 2008-style crisis"""
    
    # Setup: Multi-asset portfolio
    # Trigger: Credit event → correlation breakdown
    crisis_regime = create_2008_crisis_regime()
    
    # All correlations → 0.95
    crisis_data = generate_crisis_market_data()
    
    # System should:
    # 1. Detect correlation breakdown
    regime = regime_detector.detect(crisis_data, features)
    assert regime.correlation_regime.state == "breakdown"
    
    # 2. Reduce exposure dramatically
    risk = risk_engine.calculate_portfolio_risk(positions, crisis_data)
    assert risk.total_var > normal_var * 3.0  # Risk triples
    
    # 3. Cut positions
    new_allocation = capital_allocator.allocate(strategies, risk)
    assert sum(new_allocation.values()) < sum(normal_allocation.values()) * 0.5

## SECTION 7: MIGRATION GUIDE

### Migrating Existing Crypto Code

**Schritt 1:** Update Data Layer
```python
# Alt:
market_data = data_layer.ingest(symbol)

# Neu:
market_data = data_layer.ingest(
    symbol=symbol,
    asset_class="crypto"  # Explizit angeben
)
```

**Schritt 2:** Update Feature Computation
```python
# Alt:
features = compute_features(market_data)

# Neu:
feature_registry = FeatureRegistry()
features = feature_registry.get_features(
    asset_class="crypto",
    market_data=market_data
)
```

**Schritt 3:** Update Regime Detection
```python
# Alt:
regime = hmm.detect(features)

# Neu:
regime_detector = HierarchicalRegimeDetector()
regime = regime_detector.detect(
    market_data={"BTC/USDT": market_data},
    features={"crypto": features}
)
crypto_regime = regime.asset_regimes["crypto"]
```

**Schritt 4:** Update Risk Calculation
```python
# Alt:
risk = risk_engine.calculate_risk(position)

# Neu:
portfolio_risk = risk_engine.calculate_portfolio_risk(
    positions={symbol: position},
    market_data={symbol: market_data}
)
asset_risk = portfolio_risk.asset_risks[symbol]
```

# MULTI-ASSET UPGRADE: REGIME DETECTION & RISK ENGINE

## CRITICAL LAYER UPGRADES - DETAILSPEZIFIKATION

---

## LAYER 4: REGIME DETECTION - HIERARCHICAL SYSTEM

### Problem Statement

**Single-Regime Ansatz versagt bei Multi-Asset:**
- Crypto Regime: Funding-driven, High Volatility, 24/7
- FX Regime: Macro-driven, Policy-sensitive, Session-based
- Indices Regime: Risk-sentiment-driven, Correlation-dependent
- Commodities Regime: Supply-driven, Weather-sensitive

**Lösung:** 3-Level Hierarchical Regime System

---

### Architecture: 3-Tier Regime Hierarchy

```
TIER 1: GLOBAL MACRO REGIME
├── Monetary Policy Regime
│   ├── States: Easing, Neutral, Tightening, Emergency
│   ├── Drivers: Fed rates, ECB policy, BoJ intervention
│   └── Cycle: Years
│
├── Risk Sentiment Regime  
│   ├── States: Risk-On, Risk-Off, Transition, Panic
│   ├── Drivers: VIX, credit spreads, equity flows
│   └── Cycle: Weeks to Months
│
└── Liquidity Regime
    ├── States: Abundant, Normal, Tight, Crisis
    ├── Drivers: Central bank balance sheets, repo rates
    └── Cycle: Months

TIER 2: ASSET-CLASS REGIMES (Conditioned on Tier 1)
├── Crypto Regime
│   ├── States: Leverage_Mania, Retail_FOMO, Institutional, Deleveraging, Capitulation
│   ├── Drivers: Funding rates, OI, liquidations, retail sentiment
│   └── Model: HMM with 5 states, crypto-specific features
│
├── Forex Regime
│   ├── States: Carry_Trade, Trend_Following, Range_Bound, Risk_Off_Flight
│   ├── Drivers: Rate differentials, carry signals, CB meetings
│   └── Model: HMM with 4 states, macro features
│
├── Indices Regime
│   ├── States: Bull_Market, Bear_Market, Sector_Rotation, Defensive, Panic
│   ├── Drivers: VIX, breadth, credit spreads, earnings
│   └── Model: HMM with 5 states, risk sentiment features
│
└── Commodities Regime
    ├── States: Contango, Backwardation, Supply_Shock, Demand_Shock
    ├── Drivers: Inventory levels, seasonality, geopolitics
    └── Model: Asset-specific (oil ≠ gold ≠ wheat)

TIER 3: CORRELATION REGIME (Critical for Risk)
├── States: Normal, Divergence, Convergence, Breakdown
├── Drivers: Cross-asset correlation matrix, stress indicators
└── Alert: Breakdown triggers immediate portfolio risk reduction
```

---

### Implementation Specifications

#### Tier 1: Global Macro Regime

**Module:** `jarvis/intelligence/global_regime.py`

```python
class GlobalMacroRegime(BaseModel):
    """Top-level regime affecting all assets"""
    monetary_policy: MonetaryRegime
    risk_sentiment: RiskSentimentRegime
    liquidity: LiquidityRegime
    timestamp: datetime
    confidence: float

class MonetaryRegime(BaseModel):
    """Central bank policy regime"""
    state: Literal["easing", "neutral", "tightening", "emergency"]
    fed_rate: float
    fed_direction: Literal["cutting", "holding", "hiking"]
    ecb_rate: float
    boj_policy: str
    next_meeting_days: int
    probability: Dict[str, float]  # State probabilities

class RiskSentimentRegime(BaseModel):
    """Market-wide risk appetite"""
    state: Literal["risk_on", "risk_off", "transition", "panic"]
    vix_level: float
    vix_term_structure: float  # Positive = contango (calm), Negative = backwardation (fear)
    credit_spread_bps: float
    equity_flows_7d: float
    probability: Dict[str, float]

class LiquidityRegime(BaseModel):
    """System-wide liquidity"""
    state: Literal["abundant", "normal", "tight", "crisis"]
    fed_balance_sheet: float
    repo_rate_spread: float
    ted_spread: float  # LIBOR-OIS spread
    probability: Dict[str, float]
```

**Detection Logic:**

```python
class GlobalMacroDetector:
    """Detects global macro regime"""
    
    def detect(self) -> GlobalMacroRegime:
        """Runs every 1 hour (slow-moving)"""
        
        # 1. Monetary Policy
        monetary = self._detect_monetary_policy()
        
        # 2. Risk Sentiment
        risk_sentiment = self._detect_risk_sentiment()
        
        # 3. Liquidity
        liquidity = self._detect_liquidity()
        
        return GlobalMacroRegime(
            monetary_policy=monetary,
            risk_sentiment=risk_sentiment,
            liquidity=liquidity,
            timestamp=datetime.now(),
            confidence=self._calculate_confidence([monetary, risk_sentiment, liquidity])
        )
    
    def _detect_risk_sentiment(self) -> RiskSentimentRegime:
        """VIX-based risk sentiment"""
        
        vix = get_vix_level()
        vix_term = get_vix_term_structure()
        credit_spread = get_credit_spread()
        
        # State classification
        if vix > 40 and vix_term < -0.1:
            state = "panic"
        elif vix > 30:
            state = "risk_off"
        elif vix < 15 and vix_term > 0.05:
            state = "risk_on"
        else:
            state = "transition"
        
        return RiskSentimentRegime(
            state=state,
            vix_level=vix,
            vix_term_structure=vix_term,
            credit_spread_bps=credit_spread,
            equity_flows_7d=get_equity_flows(),
            probability=self._calculate_state_probs(vix, vix_term, credit_spread)
        )
```

#### Tier 2: Asset-Class Specific Regimes

**Module:** `jarvis/intelligence/asset_regimes.py`

**Crypto Regime Example:**

```python
class CryptoRegimeDetector:
    """Crypto-specific regime using funding + OI + liquidations"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.hmm = HiddenMarkovModel(n_states=5)
        self.states = [
            "leverage_mania",      # High funding, rising OI, low liquidations
            "retail_fomo",         # Rising prices, social media activity
            "institutional",       # Low funding, stable OI, organized flows
            "deleveraging",        # Falling OI, high liquidations, negative funding
            "capitulation"         # Extreme liquidations, despair
        ]
        
        # Load trained HMM
        self.hmm.load_weights("models/crypto_regime_hmm.pkl")
    
    def detect(self, 
               features: np.ndarray, 
               global_regime: GlobalMacroRegime) -> CryptoRegime:
        """Detect crypto regime conditioned on global regime"""
        
        # Extract crypto-specific features
        funding_rate = features[40]
        open_interest = features[41]
        liquidations_24h = features[42]
        social_sentiment = features[43]
        
        # Base HMM prediction
        regime_probs = self.hmm.predict_proba(features)
        
        # CRITICAL: Condition on global regime
        if global_regime.risk_sentiment.state == "risk_off":
            # In risk-off, suppress "leverage_mania" probability
            regime_probs["leverage_mania"] *= 0.2
            
            # Boost "deleveraging" probability
            if funding_rate < 0 and open_interest.decreasing():
                regime_probs["deleveraging"] *= 2.0
        
        if global_regime.risk_sentiment.state == "panic":
            # In panic, force capitulation if liquidations extreme
            if liquidations_24h > EXTREME_LIQUIDATION_THRESHOLD:
                regime_probs["capitulation"] = 0.8
        
        # Normalize probabilities
        regime_probs = self._normalize_probs(regime_probs)
        
        # Select regime
        current_state = max(regime_probs, key=regime_probs.get)
        
        return CryptoRegime(
            state=current_state,
            probabilities=regime_probs,
            confidence=regime_probs[current_state],
            features={
                "funding_rate": funding_rate,
                "open_interest": open_interest,
                "liquidations_24h": liquidations_24h
            },
            conditioned_on=global_regime
        )
```

**Forex Regime Example:**

```python
class ForexRegimeDetector:
    """FX-specific regime using rates + carry + CB policy"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.hmm = HiddenMarkovModel(n_states=4)
        self.states = [
            "carry_trade",        # High rate differential, low vol
            "trend_following",    # Strong directional move
            "range_bound",        # Low vol, mean-reverting
            "risk_off_flight"     # Flight to safety (USD, JPY, CHF)
        ]
        
        self.hmm.load_weights("models/fx_regime_hmm.pkl")
    
    def detect(self, 
               features: np.ndarray, 
               global_regime: GlobalMacroRegime) -> ForexRegime:
        """Detect FX regime"""
        
        # Extract FX-specific features
        rate_differential = features[40]
        dxy_correlation = features[41]
        carry_signal = features[42]
        cb_meeting_days = features[43]
        
        # Base HMM prediction
        regime_probs = self.hmm.predict_proba(features)
        
        # CRITICAL: Condition on global regime
        if global_regime.risk_sentiment.state in ["risk_off", "panic"]:
            # Force risk-off flight
            regime_probs["risk_off_flight"] = 0.7
            regime_probs["carry_trade"] = 0.05  # Carry unwinding
        
        if global_regime.monetary_policy.state == "tightening":
            # Boost trend-following (strong USD)
            regime_probs["trend_following"] *= 1.5
        
        # CB meeting proximity
        if cb_meeting_days < 3:
            # Suppress carry trades near CB meetings
            regime_probs["carry_trade"] *= 0.5
            regime_probs["range_bound"] *= 1.5
        
        regime_probs = self._normalize_probs(regime_probs)
        
        return ForexRegime(
            state=max(regime_probs, key=regime_probs.get),
            probabilities=regime_probs,
            confidence=max(regime_probs.values()),
            conditioned_on=global_regime
        )
```

#### Tier 3: Correlation Regime (CRITICAL FOR RISK)

**Module:** `jarvis/intelligence/correlation_regime.py`

```python
class CorrelationRegimeDetector:
    """Detects correlation breakdown (most critical for risk)"""
    
    STATES = [
        "normal",       # Correlations within historical range
        "divergence",   # Correlations lower than usual (good for diversification)
        "convergence",  # Correlations rising
        "breakdown"     # ALL correlations → 1 (CRISIS)
    ]
    
    def detect(self, 
               market_data: Dict[str, EnhancedMarketData],
               asset_regimes: Dict[str, AssetRegime]) -> CorrelationRegime:
        """Detects correlation regime"""
        
        # 1. Compute current correlation matrix
        current_corr = self._compute_correlation_matrix(market_data)
        
        # 2. Compare to historical distribution
        historical_corr = self._get_historical_correlation()
        
        # 3. Detect breakdown
        avg_corr = self._average_correlation(current_corr)
        hist_avg = self._average_correlation(historical_corr)
        
        if avg_corr > 0.8:
            state = "breakdown"  # CRITICAL: All assets moving together
            alert_level = "CRITICAL"
        elif avg_corr > hist_avg + 0.2:
            state = "convergence"
            alert_level = "HIGH"
        elif avg_corr < hist_avg - 0.2:
            state = "divergence"  # Good for diversification
            alert_level = "LOW"
        else:
            state = "normal"
            alert_level = "NORMAL"
        
        return CorrelationRegime(
            state=state,
            correlation_matrix=current_corr,
            average_correlation=avg_corr,
            historical_average=hist_avg,
            alert_level=alert_level,
            timestamp=datetime.now()
        )
    
    def _compute_correlation_matrix(self, 
                                     market_data: Dict[str, EnhancedMarketData]) -> np.ndarray:
        """Rolling 30-day correlation"""
        
        returns = {}
        for symbol, data in market_data.items():
            returns[symbol] = data.returns[-30:]  # Last 30 days
        
        # Convert to matrix
        returns_matrix = np.column_stack(list(returns.values()))
        
        # Compute correlation
        corr_matrix = np.corrcoef(returns_matrix, rowvar=False)
        
        return corr_matrix
```

### Regime Memory Extension

**Module:** `jarvis/intelligence/regime_memory.py`

```python
class MultiAssetRegimeMemory:
    """Extended regime memory for multi-asset"""
    
    def __init__(self, lookback_days: int = 365):
        self.lookback_days = lookback_days
        
        # Separate histories
        self.global_history = deque(maxlen=lookback_days * 24)  # Hourly
        self.crypto_history = deque(maxlen=lookback_days * 24)
        self.fx_history = deque(maxlen=lookback_days * 24)
        self.indices_history = deque(maxlen=lookback_days * 24)
        self.correlation_history = deque(maxlen=lookback_days * 24)
        
        # Transition tracking
        self.last_transition = {}
        self.transition_counts = defaultdict(int)
    
    def update(self, regime: HierarchicalRegime):
        """Update all regime histories"""
        
        # Global
        self.global_history.append(regime.global_regime)
        
        # Asset-specific
        for asset_class, asset_regime in regime.asset_regimes.items():
            getattr(self, f"{asset_class}_history").append(asset_regime)
        
        # Correlation
        self.correlation_history.append(regime.correlation_regime)
        
        # Detect transitions
        self._detect_transitions(regime)
    
    def _detect_transitions(self, regime: HierarchicalRegime):
        """Detects regime state changes"""
        
        # Check global regime transitions
        if len(self.global_history) > 1:
            prev_global = self.global_history[-2]
            curr_global = regime.global_regime
            
            if prev_global.risk_sentiment.state != curr_global.risk_sentiment.state:
                transition = f"risk_{prev_global.risk_sentiment.state}_to_{curr_global.risk_sentiment.state}"
                self.transition_counts[transition] += 1
                self.last_transition["risk_sentiment"] = {
                    "from": prev_global.risk_sentiment.state,
                    "to": curr_global.risk_sentiment.state,
                    "timestamp": datetime.now()
                }
        
        # Check correlation regime transitions
        if len(self.correlation_history) > 1:
            prev_corr = self.correlation_history[-2]
            curr_corr = regime.correlation_regime
            
            if prev_corr.state != curr_corr.state:
                if curr_corr.state == "breakdown":
                    # CRITICAL ALERT
                    self._trigger_correlation_breakdown_alert()
    
    def _trigger_correlation_breakdown_alert(self):
        """Emergency alert when correlation breaks down"""
        logger.critical("CORRELATION BREAKDOWN DETECTED - ALL ASSETS MOVING TOGETHER")
        logger.critical("RECOMMENDATION: Reduce overall exposure by 50%")
        
        # Could trigger automatic position reduction here
```

class AssetOODConfig(BaseModel):
    """OOD configuration per asset class"""
    asset_class: str
    
    # Thresholds
    ood_threshold: float
    flash_crash_threshold: float
    volatility_spike_threshold: float
    liquidity_drain_threshold: float
    
    # Weights
    distribution_weight: float
    event_weight: float
    macro_weight: float
    
    # Event sensitivities
    macro_sensitivity: Dict[str, float]

# Crypto Config
CRYPTO_OOD = AssetOODConfig(
    asset_class="crypto",
    ood_threshold=0.7,              # More tolerant
    flash_crash_threshold=0.15,     # 15% move normal
    volatility_spike_threshold=2.0, # 200% vol increase
    liquidity_drain_threshold=0.3,  # 70% liquidity drop
    distribution_weight=0.4,
    event_weight=0.4,
    macro_weight=0.2,               # Less macro-sensitive
    macro_sensitivity={
        "fed_meeting": 0.5,
        "credit_event": 0.7,
        "geopolitical": 0.6
    }
)

# Forex Config
FOREX_OOD = AssetOODConfig(
    asset_class="forex",
    ood_threshold=0.5,              # Very sensitive
    flash_crash_threshold=0.03,     # 3% move extreme
    volatility_spike_threshold=0.8, # 80% vol increase
    liquidity_drain_threshold=0.5,  # 50% liquidity drop
    distribution_weight=0.3,
    event_weight=0.3,
    macro_weight=0.4,               # Very macro-sensitive
    macro_sensitivity={
        "fed_meeting": 0.9,
        "ecb_meeting": 0.9,
        "nonfarm_payrolls": 0.8,
        "cpi_release": 0.8
    }
)

# Indices Config
INDICES_OOD = AssetOODConfig(
    asset_class="indices",
    ood_threshold=0.6,
    flash_crash_threshold=0.05,     # 5% move significant
    volatility_spike_threshold=1.2,
    liquidity_drain_threshold=0.4,
    distribution_weight=0.35,
    event_weight=0.35,
    macro_weight=0.3,
    macro_sensitivity={
        "fed_meeting": 0.8,
        "credit_event": 0.9,
        "earnings_season": 0.6
    }
)

### OOD Detection with Asset Awareness

```python
class AssetConditionalOOD:
    """Main OOD detector with asset awareness"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.configs = {
            "crypto": CRYPTO_OOD,
            "forex": FOREX_OOD,
            "indices": INDICES_OOD,
            "commodities": COMMODITIES_OOD
        }
        self.macro_detector = MacroEventDetector()
    
    def detect(self, 
               asset_class: str,
               features: np.ndarray,
               market_data: EnhancedMarketData,
               regime: HierarchicalRegime) -> OODResult:
        """Full OOD detection"""
        
        config = self.configs[asset_class]
        
        # 1. Distribution OOD (feature space)
        dist_ood = self._distribution_ood(features, config)
        
        # 2. Event OOD (price action)
        event_ood = self._event_ood(market_data, config)
        
        # 3. Macro OOD (calendar events)
        macro_ood = self.macro_detector.detect(asset_class, regime)
        
        # 4. Regime OOD (regime transition)
        regime_ood = self._regime_ood(regime)
        
        # Combine
        total_ood = (
            config.distribution_weight * dist_ood +
            config.event_weight * event_ood +
            config.macro_weight * macro_ood +
            0.1 * regime_ood  # Small weight to regime transitions
        )
        
        is_ood = total_ood > config.ood_threshold
        severity = self._calculate_severity(total_ood, config)
        
        return OODResult(
            is_ood=is_ood,
            score=total_ood,
            severity=severity,
            components={
                "distribution": dist_ood,
                "event": event_ood,
                "macro": macro_ood,
                "regime": regime_ood
            },
            recommendation=self._generate_recommendation(is_ood, severity, components)
        )
```

# MULTI-ASSET RISK ENGINE - COMPLETE SPECIFICATION

## LAYER 8: RISK ENGINE - PORTFOLIO CROSS-ASSET RISK

### Architecture Overview

```
RISK ENGINE COMPONENTS:

1. Individual Asset Risk Calculator
   ├── Volatility Estimation (asset-specific)
   ├── Tail Risk Model (asset-specific distribution)
   └── Execution Cost Modeling

2. Correlation Model (Dynamic, Regime-Dependent)
   ├── Base Correlation (historical)
   ├── Regime Adjustment
   └── Crisis Correlation Override

3. Portfolio Risk Aggregator
   ├── Portfolio Variance (with correlations)
   ├── Multivariate Tail Risk (copula-based)
   └── Diversification Benefit Calculation

4. FX Exposure Manager
   ├── Multi-currency P&L tracking
   ├── FX hedging recommendations
   └── Currency risk contribution

5. Gap Risk Model (Session-based assets)
   ├── Overnight gap distribution
   ├── Weekend gap risk
   └── Holiday gap risk

6. Structural Fragility Monitor
   ├── Cross-asset stress indicators
   ├── Liquidity breakdown detection
   └── Systemic risk signals
```

## 1. INDIVIDUAL ASSET RISK

### Module: `jarvis/risk/asset_risk.py`

```python
class AssetRiskCalculator:
    """Calculates risk for individual positions"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.vol_models = {
            "crypto": CryptoVolatilityModel(),
            "forex": ForexVolatilityModel(),
            "indices": IndicesVolatilityModel(),
            "commodities": CommoditiesVolatilityModel()
        }
        self.tail_models = {
            "crypto": CryptoTailModel(),  # Fat tails
            "forex": ForexTailModel(),     # Thinner tails
            "indices": IndicesTailModel(), # Medium tails
            "commodities": CommoditiesTailModel()
        }
    
    def calculate_risk(self, 
                       position: Position,
                       market_data: EnhancedMarketData,
                       regime: AssetRegime) -> AssetRisk:
        """Complete asset-level risk calculation"""
        
        asset_class = market_data.microstructure.asset_class
        
        # 1. Volatility (regime-dependent)
        volatility = self.vol_models[asset_class].estimate(
            market_data=market_data,
            regime=regime
        )
        
        # 2. Tail risk
        tail_risk = self.tail_models[asset_class].estimate(
            market_data=market_data,
            lookback_days=90
        )
        
        # 3. Position-level risk
        notional = position.size * market_data.close
        
        # Daily VaR (95%)
        daily_var = notional * volatility.daily * 1.645  # 95% confidence
        
        # Tail VaR (99%)
        tail_var = notional * tail_risk.var_99
        
        # 4. Execution cost estimate
        execution_cost = self._estimate_execution_cost(
            position=position,
            market_data=market_data
        )
        
        return AssetRisk(
            symbol=position.symbol,
            asset_class=asset_class,
            notional=notional,
            volatility=volatility,
            daily_var_95=daily_var,
            tail_var_99=tail_var,
            tail_cvar_99=tail_risk.cvar_99 * notional,
            execution_cost=execution_cost,
            liquidity_score=market_data.liquidity_regime.score
        )

class CryptoVolatilityModel:
    """Crypto-specific volatility with funding rate influence"""
    
    def estimate(self, 
                 market_data: EnhancedMarketData,
                 regime: CryptoRegime) -> VolatilityEstimate:
        """Estimates crypto volatility"""
        
        # Base realized volatility (EWMA)
        realized_vol = self._calculate_realized_vol(market_data.returns)
        
        # Funding rate adjustment
        funding_rate = market_data.features.get("funding_rate", 0)
        if abs(funding_rate) > 0.0005:  # > 0.05% per 8h
            funding_adjustment = 1.0 + abs(funding_rate) * 100
            realized_vol *= funding_adjustment
        
        # Regime adjustment
        regime_multiplier = {
            "leverage_mania": 1.3,      # Higher vol expected
            "retail_fomo": 1.2,
            "institutional": 0.9,       # Lower vol
            "deleveraging": 1.5,        # Very high vol
            "capitulation": 2.0         # Extreme vol
        }
        
        adjusted_vol = realized_vol * regime_multiplier[regime.state]
        
        return VolatilityEstimate(
            daily=adjusted_vol / np.sqrt(365),
            weekly=adjusted_vol / np.sqrt(52),
            monthly=adjusted_vol / np.sqrt(12),
            regime_adjusted=True,
            confidence=regime.confidence
        )

class ForexVolatilityModel:
    """FX-specific volatility with CB meeting adjustments"""
    
    def estimate(self, 
                 market_data: EnhancedMarketData,
                 regime: ForexRegime) -> VolatilityEstimate:
        """Estimates FX volatility"""
        
        # Base realized volatility
        realized_vol = self._calculate_realized_vol(market_data.returns)
        
        # Session adjustment
        if market_data.current_session == "asia":
            realized_vol *= 0.7  # Lower vol in Asian session
        elif market_data.current_session == "us":
            realized_vol *= 1.2  # Higher vol in US session
        
        # CB meeting proximity
        cb_days = market_data.features.get("cb_meeting_proximity", 30)
        if cb_days < 3:
            realized_vol *= 1.5  # Vol spike before CB meetings
        
        # Regime adjustment
        regime_multiplier = {
            "carry_trade": 0.8,        # Low vol environment
            "trend_following": 1.0,    # Normal vol
            "range_bound": 0.7,        # Very low vol
            "risk_off_flight": 1.8     # High vol
        }
        
        adjusted_vol = realized_vol * regime_multiplier[regime.state]
        
        return VolatilityEstimate(
            daily=adjusted_vol / np.sqrt(252),  # Trading days
            weekly=adjusted_vol / np.sqrt(52),
            monthly=adjusted_vol / np.sqrt(12),
            regime_adjusted=True,
            confidence=regime.confidence
        )

class CryptoTailModel:
    """Crypto tail distribution (fat tails)"""
    
    def estimate(self, 
                 market_data: EnhancedMarketData,
                 lookback_days: int = 90) -> TailRiskEstimate:
        """Fits Student-t distribution to crypto returns"""
        
        returns = market_data.returns[-lookback_days:]
        
        # Fit Student-t distribution
        from scipy.stats import t
        params = t.fit(returns)
        df, loc, scale = params  # degrees of freedom, location, scale
        
        # VaR and CVaR at 99%
        var_99 = t.ppf(0.01, df, loc=loc, scale=scale)  # 1% quantile
        cvar_99 = self._calculate_cvar(returns, var_99)
        
        return TailRiskEstimate(
            distribution="student_t",
            degrees_of_freedom=df,
            var_95=t.ppf(0.05, df, loc=loc, scale=scale),
            var_99=var_99,
            cvar_99=cvar_99,
            tail_index=1/df  # Lower = fatter tails
        )

class ForexTailModel:
    """FX tail distribution (thinner tails than crypto)"""
    
    def estimate(self, 
                 market_data: EnhancedMarketData,
                 lookback_days: int = 90) -> TailRiskEstimate:
        """Fits Normal distribution to FX returns"""
        
        returns = market_data.returns[-lookback_days:]
        
        # FX usually more Gaussian (except during CB shocks)
        from scipy.stats import norm
        mu, std = norm.fit(returns)
        
        # VaR and CVaR at 99%
        var_99 = norm.ppf(0.01, loc=mu, scale=std)
        cvar_99 = self._calculate_cvar(returns, var_99)
        
        return TailRiskEstimate(
            distribution="normal",
            var_95=norm.ppf(0.05, loc=mu, scale=std),
            var_99=var_99,
            cvar_99=cvar_99,
            tail_index=0  # Normal distribution
        )
```

## 2. DYNAMIC CORRELATION MODEL

### Module: `jarvis/risk/correlation.py`

```python
class DynamicCorrelationModel:
    """Time-varying, regime-dependent correlation"""
    
    def __init__(self, lookback_days: int = 90):
        self.lookback_days = lookback_days
        self.base_correlations = {}  # Historical correlations
        self.dcc_models = {}  # DCC-GARCH models per pair
    
    def estimate(self, 
                 positions: Dict[str, Position],
                 market_data: Dict[str, EnhancedMarketData],
                 regime: HierarchicalRegime) -> CorrelationMatrix:
        """Estimates current correlation matrix"""
        
        symbols = list(positions.keys())
        n = len(symbols)
        
        # 1. Compute base correlation (rolling window)
        base_corr = self._compute_base_correlation(market_data, symbols)
        
        # 2. Regime adjustments
        if regime.correlation_regime.state == "breakdown":
            # CRITICAL: Force high correlations in crisis
            adjusted_corr = self._apply_crisis_correlation(base_corr)
        
        elif regime.correlation_regime.state == "divergence":
            # Lower correlations (good for diversification)
            adjusted_corr = base_corr * 0.7
            np.fill_diagonal(adjusted_corr, 1.0)
        
        elif regime.global_regime.risk_sentiment.state == "panic":
            # Panic: all correlations increase
            adjusted_corr = self._apply_panic_correlation(base_corr)
        
        else:
            # Normal regime
            adjusted_corr = base_corr
        
        # 3. Ensure positive semi-definite
        adjusted_corr = self._nearest_psd(adjusted_corr)
        
        return CorrelationMatrix(
            matrix=adjusted_corr,
            symbols=symbols,
            regime=regime.correlation_regime.state,
            average_correlation=self._average_correlation(adjusted_corr),
            timestamp=datetime.now()
        )
    
    def _compute_base_correlation(self, 
                                   market_data: Dict[str, EnhancedMarketData],
                                   symbols: List[str]) -> np.ndarray:
        """Computes rolling correlation"""
        
        # Extract returns
        returns_dict = {}
        for symbol in symbols:
            returns_dict[symbol] = market_data[symbol].returns[-self.lookback_days:]
        
        # Align timestamps (important for multi-asset)
        returns_df = pd.DataFrame(returns_dict)
        returns_df = returns_df.fillna(0)  # Handle missing data
        
        # Correlation matrix
        corr_matrix = returns_df.corr().values
        
        return corr_matrix
    
    def _apply_crisis_correlation(self, base_corr: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
        """Forces high correlations during crisis"""
        
        n = base_corr.shape[0]
        crisis_corr = np.ones((n, n)) * 0.8  # All correlations → 0.8
        
        # Keep diagonal = 1
        np.fill_diagonal(crisis_corr, 1.0)
        
        # Blend with base (20% base, 80% crisis)
        adjusted = 0.2 * base_corr + 0.8 * crisis_corr
        
        return adjusted
    
    def _apply_panic_correlation(self, base_corr: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
        """Increases all correlations in panic"""
        
        # Boost all off-diagonal elements by 50%
        mask = ~np.eye(base_corr.shape[0], dtype=bool)
        adjusted = base_corr.copy()
        adjusted[mask] *= 1.5
        
        # Cap at 0.95
        adjusted[mask] = np.minimum(adjusted[mask], 0.95)
        
        return adjusted
    
    def _nearest_psd(self, matrix: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
        """Projects matrix to nearest positive semi-definite"""
        
        # Eigenvalue decomposition
        eigvals, eigvecs = np.linalg.eigh(matrix)
        
        # Clip negative eigenvalues to small positive
        eigvals = np.maximum(eigvals, 1e-8)
        
        # Reconstruct
        psd_matrix = eigvecs @ np.diag(eigvals) @ eigvecs.T
        
        # Rescale to have unit diagonal
        d = np.sqrt(np.diag(psd_matrix))
        psd_matrix = psd_matrix / np.outer(d, d)
        
        return psd_matrix
```

## 3. PORTFOLIO RISK AGGREGATION

### Module: `jarvis/risk/portfolio_risk.py`

```python
class PortfolioRiskEngine:
    """Main portfolio risk calculator"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.asset_calculator = AssetRiskCalculator()
        self.correlation_model = DynamicCorrelationModel()
        self.tail_model = MultivariateTailModel()
        self.fx_exposure = FXExposureManager()
        self.gap_risk = GapRiskModel()
    
    def calculate_portfolio_risk(self, 
                                  positions: Dict[str, Position],
                                  market_data: Dict[str, EnhancedMarketData],
                                  regime: HierarchicalRegime) -> PortfolioRisk:
        """Complete portfolio risk calculation"""
        
        # 1. Individual asset risks
        asset_risks = {}
        for symbol, position in positions.items():
            asset_regime = regime.asset_regimes.get(
                market_data[symbol].microstructure.asset_class
            )
            asset_risks[symbol] = self.asset_calculator.calculate_risk(
                position=position,
                market_data=market_data[symbol],
                regime=asset_regime
            )
        
        # 2. Correlation matrix
        correlation_matrix = self.correlation_model.estimate(
            positions=positions,
            market_data=market_data,
            regime=regime
        )
        
        # 3. Portfolio variance (with correlations)
        portfolio_var = self._calculate_portfolio_variance(
            asset_risks=asset_risks,
            correlation_matrix=correlation_matrix
        )
        
        # 4. Multivariate tail risk
        tail_risk = self.tail_model.estimate_tail_risk(
            positions=positions,
            market_data=market_data,
            correlation_matrix=correlation_matrix,
            asset_risks=asset_risks
        )
        
        # 5. FX exposure
        fx_exposure = self.fx_exposure.calculate_exposure(positions, market_data)
        
        # 6. Gap risk
        gap_risk = self.gap_risk.estimate_gap_risk(positions, market_data)
        
        # 7. Diversification benefit
        diversification = self._calculate_diversification_benefit(
            asset_risks=asset_risks,
            portfolio_var=portfolio_var
        )
        
        return PortfolioRisk(
            total_var=portfolio_var,
            asset_risks=asset_risks,
            correlation_matrix=correlation_matrix,
            tail_var_95=tail_risk.var_95,
            tail_cvar_95=tail_risk.cvar_95,
            tail_var_99=tail_risk.var_99,
            tail_cvar_99=tail_risk.cvar_99,
            fx_exposure=fx_exposure,
            gap_risk=gap_risk,
            diversification_benefit=diversification,
            regime=regime,
            timestamp=datetime.now()
        )
    
    def _calculate_portfolio_variance(self, 
                                       asset_risks: Dict[str, AssetRisk],
                                       correlation_matrix: CorrelationMatrix) -> float:
        """Portfolio variance with correlations"""
        
        # Extract volatilities
        symbols = list(asset_risks.keys())
        vols = np.array([asset_risks[s].volatility.daily for s in symbols])
        notionals = np.array([asset_risks[s].notional for s in symbols])
        
        # Position volatilities
        position_vols = vols * notionals
        
        # Portfolio variance: w' Σ w
        # where Σ = D * Corr * D (D = diag of volatilities)
        corr = correlation_matrix.matrix
        
        # Covariance matrix
        cov = np.outer(position_vols, position_vols) * corr
        
        # Portfolio variance (sum of all covariances)
        portfolio_var = np.sum(cov)
        
        # Portfolio std dev
        portfolio_std = np.sqrt(portfolio_var)
        
        return portfolio_std
    
    def _calculate_diversification_benefit(self, 
                                            asset_risks: Dict[str, AssetRisk],
                                            portfolio_var: float) -> float:
        """Measures diversification benefit"""
        
        # Sum of individual risks (if uncorrelated)
        sum_individual = sum(r.daily_var_95 for r in asset_risks.values())
        
        # Portfolio risk (with correlations)
        portfolio_risk = portfolio_var * 1.645  # 95% VaR
        
        # Diversification benefit
        benefit = (sum_individual - portfolio_risk) / sum_individual
        
        return max(0.0, benefit)  # Between 0 and 1
```

## 4. MULTIVARIATE TAIL RISK

### Module: `jarvis/risk/tail_risk.py`

```python
class MultivariateTailModel:
    """Copula-based multivariate tail risk"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.copula_type = "student_t"  # Student-t copula captures tail dependence
    
    def estimate_tail_risk(self, 
                           positions: Dict[str, Position],
                           market_data: Dict[str, EnhancedMarketData],
                           correlation_matrix: CorrelationMatrix,
                           asset_risks: Dict[str, AssetRisk]) -> MultivariateTailRisk:
        """Estimates joint tail risk using copulas"""
        
        symbols = list(positions.keys())
        
        # 1. Fit marginal distributions (per asset)
        marginals = {}
        for symbol in symbols:
            asset_class = market_data[symbol].microstructure.asset_class
            marginals[symbol] = self._fit_marginal_distribution(
                returns=market_data[symbol].returns,
                asset_class=asset_class
            )
        
        # 2. Fit copula
        copula = self._fit_copula(
            marginals=marginals,
            correlation_matrix=correlation_matrix.matrix
        )
        
        # 3. Simulate tail scenarios (Monte Carlo)
        n_scenarios = 10000
        tail_scenarios = self._simulate_tail_scenarios(
            copula=copula,
            marginals=marginals,
            n_scenarios=n_scenarios
        )
        
        # 4. Calculate portfolio P&L in each scenario
        portfolio_pnl = self._calculate_portfolio_pnl(
            scenarios=tail_scenarios,
            positions=positions,
            market_data=market_data
        )
        
        # 5. Compute VaR and CVaR
        var_95 = np.percentile(portfolio_pnl, 5)
        var_99 = np.percentile(portfolio_pnl, 1)
        
        cvar_95 = portfolio_pnl[portfolio_pnl <= var_95].mean()
        cvar_99 = portfolio_pnl[portfolio_pnl <= var_99].mean()
        
        return MultivariateTailRisk(
            var_95=var_95,
            cvar_95=cvar_95,
            var_99=var_99,
            cvar_99=cvar_99,
            worst_case=portfolio_pnl.min(),
            best_case=portfolio_pnl.max(),
            scenario_distribution=portfolio_pnl
        )
    
    def _fit_copula(self, 
                    marginals: Dict[str, Distribution],
                    correlation_matrix: np.ndarray) -> Copula:
        """Fits Student-t copula"""
        
        from scipy.stats import t as student_t
        
        # Estimate degrees of freedom for copula
        # (lower df = stronger tail dependence)
        df = self._estimate_copula_df(correlation_matrix)
        
        return StudentTCopula(
            correlation=correlation_matrix,
            degrees_of_freedom=df
        )
    
    def _simulate_tail_scenarios(self, 
                                  copula: Copula,
                                  marginals: Dict[str, Distribution],
                                  n_scenarios: int) -> Dict[str, np.ndarray]:
        """Simulates joint tail scenarios"""
        
        # Sample from copula (uniform marginals)
        uniform_samples = copula.sample(n_scenarios)
        
        # Transform to actual return distributions
        scenarios = {}
        for i, (symbol, marginal) in enumerate(marginals.items()):
            # Inverse CDF transform
            scenarios[symbol] = marginal.ppf(uniform_samples[:, i])
        
        return scenarios
```

## 5. GAP RISK MODEL

### Module: `jarvis/risk/gap_risk.py`

```python
class GapRiskModel:
    """Models overnight/weekend gap risk"""
    
    def estimate_gap_risk(self, 
                          positions: Dict[str, Position],
                          market_data: Dict[str, EnhancedMarketData]) -> GapRisk:
        """Estimates gap risk for session-based markets"""
        
        total_gap_risk = 0.0
        asset_gap_risks = {}
        
        for symbol, position in positions.items():
            asset_class = market_data[symbol].microstructure.asset_class
            
            # Only session-based markets have gap risk
            if asset_class in ["indices", "commodities"]:
                gap_risk = self._estimate_asset_gap_risk(
                    symbol=symbol,
                    position=position,
                    market_data=market_data[symbol]
                )
                asset_gap_risks[symbol] = gap_risk
                total_gap_risk += gap_risk
        
        # Recommendations
        recommendation = None
        if total_gap_risk > 0.05 * sum(pos.notional for pos in positions.values()):
            # Gap risk > 5% of notional
            recommendation = "REDUCE positions in indices/commodities before close"
        
        return GapRisk(
            total=total_gap_risk,
            by_asset=asset_gap_risks,
            recommendation=recommendation
        )
    
    def _estimate_asset_gap_risk(self, 
                                  symbol: str,
                                  position: Position,
                                  market_data: EnhancedMarketData) -> float:
        """Estimates gap risk for single asset"""
        
        # Historical gap distribution
        gaps = self._get_historical_gaps(symbol, lookback_days=365)
        
        # Gap statistics
        gap_mean = gaps.mean()
        gap_std = gaps.std()
        gap_max = gaps.max()
        gap_min = gaps.min()
        
        # Position size
        notional = position.size * market_data.close
        
        # Expected gap risk (1-sigma)
        expected_gap_risk = notional * gap_std
        
        # Worst-case gap risk (3-sigma)
        worst_gap_risk = notional * 3 * gap_std
        
        return expected_gap_risk
    
    def _get_historical_gaps(self, symbol: str, lookback_days: int) -> np.ndarray:
        """Fetches historical gap data"""
        
        # Query historical open-to-close gaps
        df = fetch_ohlcv(symbol, lookback_days)
        
        # Calculate gaps: (Open - Prev_Close) / Prev_Close
        gaps = (df['open'] - df['close'].shift(1)) / df['close'].shift(1)
        gaps = gaps.dropna()
        
        return gaps.values
```

## 6. RISK BUDGET ALLOCATION

### Module: `jarvis/risk/risk_budget.py`

```python
class PortfolioRiskBudget:
    """Multi-asset risk budgeting"""
    
    def allocate(self, 
                 total_capital: float,
                 asset_classes: List[str],
                 regime: HierarchicalRegime,
                 portfolio_risk: PortfolioRisk) -> Dict[str, RiskBudget]:
        """Allocates risk budget across asset classes"""
        
        # 1. Base allocation (equal risk contribution)
        base_allocation = self._equal_risk_contribution(
            asset_classes=asset_classes,
            portfolio_risk=portfolio_risk
        )
        
        # 2. Regime adjustment
        regime_adjusted = self._regime_adjusted_allocation(
            base=base_allocation,
            regime=regime
        )
        
        # 3. Correlation adjustment
        correlation_adjusted = self._correlation_adjusted_allocation(
            regime_adjusted=regime_adjusted,
            correlation_regime=regime.correlation_regime
        )
        
        # 4. Apply constraints
        final_allocation = self._apply_constraints(
            allocation=correlation_adjusted,
            total_capital=total_capital
        )
        
        return final_allocation
    
    def _regime_adjusted_allocation(self, 
                                     base: Dict[str, float],
                                     regime: HierarchicalRegime) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Adjusts allocation based on regime"""
        
        adjusted = base.copy()
        
        # Global regime adjustments
        if regime.global_regime.risk_sentiment.state == "risk_off":
            # Reduce risk assets
            adjusted["crypto"] *= 0.5
            adjusted["indices"] *= 0.7
            adjusted["forex"] *= 1.2  # Safe haven currencies
            
        elif regime.global_regime.risk_sentiment.state == "panic":
            # Cut all risk dramatically
            adjusted["crypto"] *= 0.2
            adjusted["indices"] *= 0.4
            adjusted["forex"] *= 0.8
            adjusted["commodities"] *= 0.5
        
        # Correlation regime adjustments
        if regime.correlation_regime.state == "breakdown":
            # All assets correlated → less diversification
            # Reduce overall exposure
            adjusted = {k: v * 0.6 for k, v in adjusted.items()}
        
        return adjusted
```

## PORTFOLIO HEATMAP LIVE UPDATE POLICY

**Applies to:** `MODE_LIVE_ANALYTICAL` and `MODE_HYBRID` (live window)
**Datei:** `jarvis/risk/portfolio_heatmap.py`
**P0 Classification:** Purely analytical visualization layer. No execution. No orders.

### UPDATE TRIGGER RULES (LIVE / HYBRID MODE)

The Portfolio Heatmap must update ONLY on these triggers — no per-tick redraw,
no unnecessary recompute.

```
PERMITTED UPDATE TRIGGERS:
  1. NEW_CONFIRMED_CANDLE
       A new candle has been confirmed closed for any tracked asset.
       Trigger only on candle close, not on tick or mid-candle price change.

  2. CORRELATION_REGIME_SHIFT
       PortfolioState.correlation_matrix has changed sufficiently:
       mean pairwise correlation delta > 0.05 from prior snapshot,
       OR any single correlation delta > 0.10 from prior snapshot.
       Trigger: correlation_engine output differs from cached matrix.

  3. EXPOSURE_DELTA_THRESHOLD
       PortfolioState.gross_exposure has changed by more than:
         EXPOSURE_DELTA_THRESHOLD = 0.05  (5% of simulated capital)
       OR PortfolioState.net_exposure has changed by more than:
         NET_EXPOSURE_DELTA_THRESHOLD = 0.03  (3% of simulated capital)

  4. FAILURE_MODE_STATUS_CHANGE
       Any FM-01..FM-06 has been activated or deactivated since last render.
       Heatmap must reflect current failure mode states visually.

  5. REGIME_TRANSITION
       RegimeState.regime_transition_flag = True
       Heatmap updates to reflect new regime-driven exposure weighting.

NOT PERMITTED — Heatmap must NOT update on:
  - Every tick or price update within a candle
  - Sequence_id increment without state change
  - Confidence score change alone (confidence shown, but no redraw)
  - Operating mode change alone
```

### IMPLEMENTATION

```python
# jarvis/risk/portfolio_heatmap.py
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, Optional, List
import numpy as np


# Update trigger thresholds — hash-protected constants
EXPOSURE_DELTA_THRESHOLD     = 0.05   # 5% gross exposure change
NET_EXPOSURE_DELTA_THRESHOLD = 0.03   # 3% net exposure change
CORRELATION_DELTA_THRESHOLD  = 0.05   # Mean pairwise correlation delta
CORRELATION_SINGLE_THRESHOLD = 0.10   # Single pair correlation delta


@dataclass
class HeatmapCell:
    # Single cell in the portfolio heatmap
    asset_id:         str
    simulated_weight: float          # Simulated portfolio weight [0,1]
    regime_alignment: bool           # Asset regime aligns with strategy
    vol_percentile:   float          # Volatility percentile [0,1]
    correlation_mean: float          # Mean correlation with rest of portfolio
    failure_modes:    List[str]      # Active FM codes for this asset
    heat_score:       float          # Composite heat [0,1]; 1=hottest
    last_updated:     datetime


@dataclass
class PortfolioHeatmapSnapshot:
    # Full portfolio heatmap at a point in time.
    # Rein analytisch — kein Execution-Bezug.
    timestamp:           datetime
    operating_mode:      str
    cells:               Dict[str, HeatmapCell]
    global_heat:         float          # Portfolio-level heat [0,1]
    diversification_ratio: float
    active_failure_modes: List[str]     # All active FM codes
    regime:              str
    trigger_reason:      str            # Why this update was triggered


class PortfolioHeatmapEngine:
    """
    Portfolio Heatmap Engine — Live Update Policy enforced.
    READ-ONLY access to portfolio state.
    No execution. No orders. Pure analytical display output.
    """

    def __init__(self):
        self._last_snapshot:    Optional[PortfolioHeatmapSnapshot] = None
        self._last_corr_matrix: Optional[np.ndarray] = None
        self._last_gross_exp:   float = 0.0
        self._last_net_exp:     float = 0.0
        self._last_regime:      str = ""
        self._last_fm_states:   List[str] = []

    def should_update(
        self,
        new_candle_confirmed:   bool,
        current_corr_matrix:    np.ndarray,
        current_gross_exp:      float,
        current_net_exp:        float,
        current_regime:         str,
        active_failure_modes:   List[str],
        regime_transition_flag: bool,
    ) -> tuple:
        """
        Returns (should_update: bool, reason: str).
        Enforces the live update policy — no spurious redraws.
        """
        if new_candle_confirmed:
            return True, "NEW_CONFIRMED_CANDLE"

        if regime_transition_flag or current_regime != self._last_regime:
            return True, "REGIME_TRANSITION"

        if active_failure_modes != self._last_fm_states:
            return True, "FAILURE_MODE_STATUS_CHANGE"

        if abs(current_gross_exp - self._last_gross_exp) > EXPOSURE_DELTA_THRESHOLD:
            return True, "EXPOSURE_DELTA_THRESHOLD"

        if abs(current_net_exp - self._last_net_exp) > NET_EXPOSURE_DELTA_THRESHOLD:
            return True, "EXPOSURE_DELTA_THRESHOLD"

        if self._last_corr_matrix is not None:
            if current_corr_matrix.shape == self._last_corr_matrix.shape:
                delta = current_corr_matrix - self._last_corr_matrix
                idx = np.triu_indices_from(delta, k=1)
                mean_delta = float(np.mean(np.abs(delta[idx])))
                max_delta  = float(np.max(np.abs(delta[idx])))
                if mean_delta > CORRELATION_DELTA_THRESHOLD:
                    return True, "CORRELATION_REGIME_SHIFT"
                if max_delta > CORRELATION_SINGLE_THRESHOLD:
                    return True, "CORRELATION_REGIME_SHIFT"

        return False, "NO_TRIGGER"

    def build_snapshot(
        self,
        portfolio_state,      # PortfolioState snapshot (read-only)
        regime_state,         # RegimeState snapshot (read-only)
        volatility_states,    # Dict[asset_id, VolatilityState] snapshots
        active_failure_modes: List[str],
        trigger_reason:       str,
        operating_mode:       str,
    ) -> PortfolioHeatmapSnapshot:
        """
        Builds a new heatmap snapshot from current state snapshots.
        All inputs are immutable snapshots — no live state references.
        """
        cells = {}
        for asset_id, weight in portfolio_state.positions.items():
            vol_state = volatility_states.get(asset_id)
            vol_pct = vol_state.vol_percentile if vol_state else 0.5
            fm_for_asset = [fm for fm in active_failure_modes
                            if asset_id in fm or fm in ["FM-02", "FM-04"]]

            # Heat = weighted blend of vol percentile + abs correlation
            corr_matrix = portfolio_state.correlation_matrix
            n = corr_matrix.shape[0] if corr_matrix is not None else 1
            corr_mean = 0.0
            if corr_matrix is not None and n > 1:
                corr_mean = float(np.mean(np.abs(corr_matrix[np.triu_indices(n, k=1)])))

            heat = float(np.clip(0.5 * vol_pct + 0.5 * corr_mean, 0.0, 1.0))

            cells[asset_id] = HeatmapCell(
                asset_id=asset_id,
                simulated_weight=float(np.clip(weight, 0.0, 1.0)),
                regime_alignment=(regime_state.regime != "UNKNOWN"),
                vol_percentile=vol_pct,
                correlation_mean=corr_mean,
                failure_modes=fm_for_asset,
                heat_score=heat,
                last_updated=__import__('datetime').datetime.utcnow(),
            )

        global_heat = float(np.mean([c.heat_score for c in cells.values()])) if cells else 0.0
        snapshot = PortfolioHeatmapSnapshot(
            timestamp=__import__('datetime').datetime.utcnow(),
            operating_mode=operating_mode,
            cells=cells,
            global_heat=global_heat,
            diversification_ratio=portfolio_state.diversification_ratio,
            active_failure_modes=active_failure_modes,
            regime=regime_state.regime,
            trigger_reason=trigger_reason,
        )

        # Cache for next comparison
        self._last_snapshot    = snapshot
        self._last_corr_matrix = portfolio_state.correlation_matrix.copy() \
                                 if portfolio_state.correlation_matrix is not None else None
        self._last_gross_exp   = portfolio_state.gross_exposure
        self._last_net_exp     = portfolio_state.net_exposure
        self._last_regime      = regime_state.regime
        self._last_fm_states   = list(active_failure_modes)
        return snapshot
```

### TESTS

```python
# tests/unit/risk/test_portfolio_heatmap.py
import numpy as np
from jarvis.risk.portfolio_heatmap import PortfolioHeatmapEngine

def test_no_update_on_tick_without_change():
    engine = PortfolioHeatmapEngine()
    corr = np.eye(3)
    should, reason = engine.should_update(
        new_candle_confirmed=False,
        current_corr_matrix=corr,
        current_gross_exp=0.5,
        current_net_exp=0.2,
        current_regime="TRENDING",
        active_failure_modes=[],
        regime_transition_flag=False,
    )
    assert not should
    assert reason == "NO_TRIGGER"

def test_update_on_candle_close():
    engine = PortfolioHeatmapEngine()
    corr = np.eye(3)
    should, reason = engine.should_update(
        new_candle_confirmed=True,
        current_corr_matrix=corr,
        current_gross_exp=0.5,
        current_net_exp=0.2,
        current_regime="TRENDING",
        active_failure_modes=[],
        regime_transition_flag=False,
    )
    assert should
    assert reason == "NEW_CONFIRMED_CANDLE"

def test_update_on_exposure_delta():
    engine = PortfolioHeatmapEngine()
    engine._last_gross_exp = 0.5
    corr = np.eye(3)
    should, reason = engine.should_update(
        new_candle_confirmed=False,
        current_corr_matrix=corr,
        current_gross_exp=0.56,   # delta > 0.05
        current_net_exp=0.2,
        current_regime="TRENDING",
        active_failure_modes=[],
        regime_transition_flag=False,
    )
    assert should
    assert reason == "EXPOSURE_DELTA_THRESHOLD"

def test_update_on_failure_mode_change():
    engine = PortfolioHeatmapEngine()
    engine._last_fm_states = []
    corr = np.eye(3)
    should, reason = engine.should_update(
        new_candle_confirmed=False,
        current_corr_matrix=corr,
        current_gross_exp=0.5,
        current_net_exp=0.2,
        current_regime="TRENDING",
        active_failure_modes=["FM-02"],
        regime_transition_flag=False,
    )
    assert should
    assert reason == "FAILURE_MODE_STATUS_CHANGE"
```

### HARD REQUIREMENTS

- R1: No per-tick redraw under any operating mode
- R2: `PortfolioHeatmapSnapshot` contains zero order-type fields
- R3: All inputs to `build_snapshot` must be immutable state snapshots
- R4: `PortfolioHeatmapEngine` has no reference to `GlobalSystemStateController`
- R5: Output goes ONLY to `Visual Output Layer (P9)` — not to strategy or risk layers
- R6: Heatmap constants are hash-protected in `THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json`

## META-VALIDATION CROSS-REFERENCE (BLOCK B)

```
WalkForwardValidationEngine outputs integrate with Risk Engine as follows:

  StabilityScore -> informs PortfolioFragilityIndex weighting
    (low stability = higher fragility contribution)

  CrossAssetRobustnessScore.penalty_multiplier -> applied to simulated
    position weight in PortfolioContext — reduces, never increases

  OverfittingReport.overfitting_flag -> if True, strategy barred from
    StrategyRegistry; risk engine never sees an overfitted strategy

  Sandbox results (ScenarioSandboxEngine) CANNOT override StabilityScore.
```

## PERFORMANCE ENVELOPE SPECIFICATION

**Classification:** Specification only. No code implementation in this section.
**Purpose:** Define hard computational limits to prevent unbounded resource consumption,
enforce predictable cycle latency, and ensure system stability under all operating modes.

---

### SYSTEM CAPACITY LIMITS

```
SUPPORTED SCALE (HARD LIMITS):

  Max symbols tracked simultaneously:          50
    (per operating mode; applies to live and hybrid modes)
    Rationale: Correlation matrix is O(n^2); 50 assets = 2500 cells = manageable.
    Above 50: raise CapacityError before admission.

  Max timeframes per symbol:                    5
    (e.g. M1, M5, H1, H4, D1 — any 5 of the defined set)
    Above 5: configuration rejected at startup validation.

  Max rolling window size (bars):           2,000
    Applies to: NVU computation, correlation rolling window, vol history
    Above 2000 bars: oldest bar is evicted (strict LRU, no silent growth)

  Max correlation matrix dimension:            50 x 50
    (n_assets x n_assets) — tied to max symbols limit
    Computation per update: O(n^2) — budget defined below

  Max event queue depth:                   10,000 events
    Above 10,000: OverflowError raised (backpressure — no silent drop)

  Max EventLog entries per session:     1,000,000
    Above limit: session must be rotated (new EventLog file, checkpoint exported)
```

---

### COMPUTATIONAL BUDGET PER UPDATE CYCLE

```
UPDATE CYCLE = one full pipeline pass triggered by a single event or candle close.

  Budget limits per cycle (all operating modes):

  Stage 0  (Integrity Gate):            < 5 ms
  Stage 1  (Market Data ingestion):     < 10 ms
  Stage 2  (NVU Normalization):         < 2 ms
  Stage 3  (Regime Engine):             < 50 ms
  Stage 4  (Volatility Layer):          < 20 ms
  Stage 5  (Strategy Layer):            < 15 ms
  Stage 6  (Risk Engine):               < 100 ms  (Monte Carlo VaR included)
  Stage 7  (Portfolio Context):         < 50 ms
  Stage 8  (Confidence Engine):         < 10 ms
  Stage 8b (Decision Quality Engine):   < 20 ms   [PHASE 3 — sub-component of P8]
  Stage 9  (Visual Output):             < 20 ms  (async render permitted)

  TOTAL BUDGET PER CYCLE:              < 320 ms  (increased by 20 ms for Phase 3)

  Exceeding total budget: log WARNING with actual duration.
  Exceeding 3x budget (> 960 ms): log CRITICAL; trigger FM-03 for affected asset.
  No stage may block the queue for unbounded time.
```

---

### PHASE 3 — PERFORMANCE AND SAFETY CONSTRAINTS

```
PHASE 3 COMPONENT BUDGETS (part of Stage 8b — Decision Quality Engine):

  Component                               Budget       Notes
  ─────────────────────────────────────── ──────────── ────────────────────────────────
  DecisionQualityEngine.compute()         < 20 ms      Total per cycle including all
                                                        sub-calls listed below.
  RegimeDurationModel.compute()           < 2 ms       Included in 20 ms total.
  SignalFragilityAnalyzer.compute()       < 30 ms      Per evaluation (may be called
                                                        less frequently than every cycle;
                                                        see FRAGILITY EVALUATION POLICY).
  AdaptiveSelectivityModel.compute()      < 2 ms       Included in 20 ms total.
  DecisionContextSnapshot consumption     < 1 ms       Included in 20 ms total.

FRAGILITY EVALUATION POLICY:
  SignalFragilityAnalyzer.compute() has a budget of 30 ms per evaluation.
  It NEED NOT run every cycle. Permitted trigger conditions:
    - Strategy parameter change (StrategyObject.Weight_Model updated)
    - Regime transition event
    - Volatility state change (vol_regime or vol_spike_flag changed)
    - Manual analysis request (research / sandbox mode)
  Between trigger conditions, the last SignalFragilityResult is reused.
  Stale fragility results must not be held for more than
  FRAGILITY_MAX_STALE_CYCLES = 50 cycles; recompute forced at that boundary.

RECURSIVE RECALCULATION — FORBIDDEN:
  DecisionQualityEngine must NOT re-invoke itself recursively.
  No cascading re-scoring is permitted.
  If DecisionQualityBundle output changes a ConfidenceBundle modifier,
  that modifier change does NOT re-trigger a new DecisionQualityEngine cycle.
  One compute pass per pipeline cycle only.

EVENT LOOP RE-TRIGGERING — FORBIDDEN:
  DecisionQualityEngine must NOT:
    - Emit events into EventQueue
    - Call EventDispatcher
    - Invoke ctrl.update()
    - Modify GlobalSystemState
  These actions are architecturally forbidden regardless of code path.

BUDGET VIOLATION HANDLING:
  If DecisionQualityEngine.compute() exceeds 20 ms:
    - Log WARNING: "DecisionQualityEngine cycle budget exceeded: {actual_ms} ms"
    - Return last valid DecisionQualityBundle (stale, but safe)
    - Do NOT raise exception; do NOT trigger FM activation
  If SignalFragilityAnalyzer.compute() exceeds 30 ms:
    - Log WARNING: "SignalFragilityAnalyzer budget exceeded: {actual_ms} ms"
    - Return last valid SignalFragilityResult with fragility_index = 1.0
      (conservative: assume maximum fragility on timeout)
    - Do NOT raise exception; do NOT trigger FM activation

MONITORING:
  Both DecisionQualityEngine and SignalFragilityAnalyzer must publish
  timing metrics to the existing operational metrics subsystem
  (see 40_RISK_ENGINE_SPECS.md SLA targets):
    - decision_quality_engine_latency_ms  (histogram)
    - fragility_analyzer_latency_ms       (histogram)
  These metrics are visible in the Visual Output (P9) system health panel.
```

---

### HYBRID MODE BUDGET ALLOCATION

```
In MODE_HYBRID:

  Historical backfill phase:
    No per-cycle time budget enforced (batch processing).
    Total backfill duration limit: 10 minutes (configurable at startup).
    If backfill exceeds limit: checkpoint exported; session pauses; resume from checkpoint.

  After sync_point (live phase):
    Same per-cycle budget applies as MODE_LIVE_ANALYTICAL (< 300 ms).
    Correlation matrix recompute: only on CORRELATION_REGIME_SHIFT trigger (not every cycle).
    Full portfolio recompute: only on EXPOSURE_DELTA_THRESHOLD trigger.

  HYBRID BUDGET SEPARATION:
    Backfill and live phases must not share compute threads.
    After sync_point: backfill computation is terminated; resources released.
```

---

### MEMORY CONSTRAINT POLICY

```
MEMORY ALLOCATION CONSTRAINTS:

  Rolling window buffers (per symbol/timeframe):
    Max size: 2,000 bars * 8 fields * 8 bytes = ~128 KB per symbol/timeframe
    With 50 symbols * 5 timeframes: 50 * 5 * 128 KB = ~32 MB for window buffers

  Correlation matrix (50 x 50, float64):
    50 * 50 * 8 bytes = 20 KB — negligible

  EventLog in-memory cache:
    Max 10,000 events cached; older events written to append-only log file.
    Estimated: 10,000 * ~2 KB per event = ~20 MB max in-memory

  Total estimated memory envelope:
    ~100 MB operational budget for analytical layers
    Exceeding 80% utilization: log WARNING
    Exceeding 100%: raise MemoryPressureError; trigger checkpointing; reduce window sizes

PROHIBITION OF UNBOUNDED RECOMPUTE LOOPS:
  - No while True: in any analytical layer without explicit exit condition
  - No recursive event emission (events do not trigger new events in same cycle)
  - No full portfolio recompute on single tick (only on defined triggers)
  - No full correlation matrix recompute on every candle (only on threshold trigger)
  - Historical backfill loops must have explicit termination at sync_point
```

---


---

## PHASE 2 — SYSTEMIC RISK AND CORRELATION HARDENING (BLOCK C)

**Datei:** `jarvis/risk/systemic_risk.py`
**Classification:** Analytical only. Correlation spikes may only reduce Confidence.
No auto-liquidation. No simulated capital modification.

---

### CORRELATION REGIME CLASSIFIER

```python
# jarvis/risk/systemic_risk.py
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, List, Tuple
import numpy as np

from jarvis.core.regime import CorrelationRegimeState

# Deterministic thresholds — registered in 99_REFERENCE.md
CORR_LOW_THRESHOLD    = 0.40   # Mean pairwise correlation < 0.40 -> DECOUPLED
CORR_MEDIUM_THRESHOLD = 0.65   # 0.40-0.65 -> COUPLED
# Above 0.65 -> CRISIS_COUPLING (triggers systemic risk evaluation)
CORR_FM04_THRESHOLD   = 0.85   # Existing FM-04 threshold — UNCHANGED

# Legacy string -> canonical CorrelationRegimeState enum mapping
# "LOW"    -> CorrelationRegimeState.DECOUPLED
# "MEDIUM" -> CorrelationRegimeState.COUPLED
# "HIGH"   -> CorrelationRegimeState.CRISIS_COUPLING


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class CorrelationRegimeResult:
    """
    Full classification result for the current systemic correlation regime.
    Deterministic — threshold-based, no stochastic sampling.
    Carries the canonical CorrelationRegimeState enum from jarvis.core.regime.

    GOVERNANCE:
      - CRISIS_COUPLING state informs Confidence Engine and Visual Output only
      - Cannot auto-liquidate positions
      - Cannot modify simulated capital directly
      - Feeds FM-04 detection in existing Risk Engine (unchanged)
    """
    state:              CorrelationRegimeState  # Canonical enum from jarvis.core.regime
    mean_pairwise_corr: float                   # Mean of upper-triangle correlation values
    max_pairwise_corr:  float                   # Maximum single-pair correlation
    n_pairs:            int                     # Number of asset pairs in matrix
    fm04_triggered:     bool                    # mean_pairwise_corr > CORR_FM04_THRESHOLD


def classify_correlation_regime(corr_matrix: np.ndarray) -> CorrelationRegimeResult:
    """
    Classify correlation regime from current correlation matrix.
    Deterministic threshold-based — no randomness.
    Returns CorrelationRegimeResult carrying canonical CorrelationRegimeState enum.

    Threshold mapping (registered in 99_REFERENCE.md):
      mean_corr < 0.40  -> CorrelationRegimeState.DECOUPLED   (legacy: "LOW")
      mean_corr < 0.65  -> CorrelationRegimeState.COUPLED     (legacy: "MEDIUM")
      mean_corr >= 0.65 -> CorrelationRegimeState.CRISIS_COUPLING (legacy: "HIGH")
    """
    n = corr_matrix.shape[0]
    if n < 2:
        return CorrelationRegimeResult(
            state=CorrelationRegimeState.DECOUPLED,
            mean_pairwise_corr=0.0,
            max_pairwise_corr=0.0,
            n_pairs=0,
            fm04_triggered=False,
        )

    idx = np.triu_indices(n, k=1)
    vals = np.abs(corr_matrix[idx])
    mean_corr = float(np.mean(vals))
    max_corr  = float(np.max(vals))
    n_pairs   = len(vals)

    if mean_corr < CORR_LOW_THRESHOLD:
        state = CorrelationRegimeState.DECOUPLED
    elif mean_corr < CORR_MEDIUM_THRESHOLD:
        state = CorrelationRegimeState.COUPLED
    else:
        state = CorrelationRegimeState.CRISIS_COUPLING

    return CorrelationRegimeResult(
        state=state,
        mean_pairwise_corr=mean_corr,
        max_pairwise_corr=max_corr,
        n_pairs=n_pairs,
        fm04_triggered=(mean_corr > CORR_FM04_THRESHOLD),
    )
```

---

### PORTFOLIO FRAGILITY INDEX

```python
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class PortfolioFragilityIndex:
    """
    Herfindahl-style metric measuring correlation concentration.
    High fragility = portfolio dominated by highly correlated assets = more systemic risk.

    FORMULA:
      HHI_corr = sum_i(mean_corr_i^2) / n_assets
      where mean_corr_i = mean absolute correlation of asset i with all others.
      Normalized to [0, 1].

    GOVERNANCE:
      - Feeds ConfidenceBundle.Q reduction (via Confidence Engine)
      - Feeds Visual Output portfolio heatmap heat_score
      - Does NOT trigger execution or capital mutation
    """
    hhi_correlation:     float   # [0,1] — 0=no concentration, 1=full concentration
    fragility_band:      str     # "LOW", "MEDIUM", "HIGH"
    dominant_asset_id:   str     # Asset with highest mean correlation
    dominant_corr:       float   # Dominant asset's mean correlation
    confidence_penalty:  float   # Confidence Q reduction: fragility * 0.20


def compute_portfolio_fragility(
    corr_matrix: np.ndarray,
    asset_ids: List[str],
) -> PortfolioFragilityIndex:
    """
    Compute Herfindahl-style correlation concentration index.
    """
    n = len(asset_ids)
    if n < 2:
        return PortfolioFragilityIndex(0.0, "LOW", asset_ids[0] if asset_ids else "", 0.0, 0.0)

    mean_corrs = []
    for i in range(n):
        row = np.abs(corr_matrix[i])
        row_vals = np.delete(row, i)
        mean_corrs.append(float(np.mean(row_vals)))

    hhi = float(np.sum(np.array(mean_corrs) ** 2) / n)
    dom_idx = int(np.argmax(mean_corrs))

    if hhi < 0.30:
        band = "LOW"
    elif hhi < 0.60:
        band = "MEDIUM"
    else:
        band = "HIGH"

    confidence_penalty = hhi * 0.20

    return PortfolioFragilityIndex(
        hhi_correlation=float(np.clip(hhi, 0.0, 1.0)),
        fragility_band=band,
        dominant_asset_id=asset_ids[dom_idx],
        dominant_corr=mean_corrs[dom_idx],
        confidence_penalty=float(np.clip(confidence_penalty, 0.0, 0.20)),
    )
```

---

### TAIL DEPENDENCY STRESS MODEL

```python
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class TailDependencyStressResult:
    """
    Deterministic stress simulation of correlation spike scenario.
    No random generator. Uses deterministic stress multiplier.

    GOVERNANCE:
      - Output used for research and Visual Output only
      - May not modify PortfolioState
      - May not trigger liquidation
      - Feeds into ScenarioSandboxEngine as input scenario parameter
    """
    base_mean_corr:      float   # Current mean pairwise correlation
    stressed_mean_corr:  float   # Stressed correlation (base * multiplier)
    stress_multiplier:   float   # Applied multiplier (deterministic)
    fm04_triggered_base: bool    # FM-04 status at base correlation
    fm04_triggered_stress: bool  # FM-04 status at stressed correlation
    confidence_impact:   float   # Expected confidence Q reduction under stress
    recovery_scenario:   str     # "FAST" (< 5 bars), "SLOW" (>= 5 bars), "PERSISTENT"


# Deterministic stress multipliers by scenario type
TAIL_STRESS_MULTIPLIERS: Dict[str, float] = {
    "MILD":       1.30,   # 30% correlation increase
    "MODERATE":   1.60,   # 60% correlation increase
    "SEVERE":     2.00,   # 100% correlation increase (doubling)
    "EXTREME":    2.50,   # 150% correlation increase
}


def simulate_tail_stress(
    current_corr_regime: CorrelationRegimeResult,
    stress_scenario: str = "MODERATE",
) -> TailDependencyStressResult:
    """
    Apply deterministic stress multiplier to current correlation state.
    No Monte Carlo — single deterministic outcome per stress scenario.
    """
    if stress_scenario not in TAIL_STRESS_MULTIPLIERS:
        raise ValueError(f"Unknown stress scenario: {stress_scenario}. "
                         f"Valid: {list(TAIL_STRESS_MULTIPLIERS.keys())}")

    multiplier = TAIL_STRESS_MULTIPLIERS[stress_scenario]
    stressed = float(np.clip(current_corr_regime.mean_pairwise_corr * multiplier, 0.0, 1.0))

    fm04_stress = stressed > CORR_FM04_THRESHOLD
    confidence_impact = stressed * 0.30 if fm04_stress else stressed * 0.10

    if stressed < 0.70:
        recovery = "FAST"
    elif stressed < 0.85:
        recovery = "SLOW"
    else:
        recovery = "PERSISTENT"

    return TailDependencyStressResult(
        base_mean_corr=current_corr_regime.mean_pairwise_corr,
        stressed_mean_corr=stressed,
        stress_multiplier=multiplier,
        fm04_triggered_base=current_corr_regime.fm04_triggered,
        fm04_triggered_stress=fm04_stress,
        confidence_impact=float(np.clip(confidence_impact, 0.0, 0.40)),
        recovery_scenario=recovery,
    )
```

---

### CONCENTRATION RISK SCORE

```python
@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ConcentrationRiskScore:
    """
    Asset class weight concentration measure.
    High concentration = strategy overexposed to one asset class.

    FORMULA:
      HHI_weight = sum_k(w_k^2)
      where w_k = simulated weight fraction of asset class k.
      HHI_weight in [0, 1]. HHI = 1/(n_classes) = perfectly diversified.

    GOVERNANCE:
      - Informs WeightPosteriorModel (penalizes concentrated strategies)
      - Feeds Visual Output only for display
      - Does NOT auto-modify weights or liquidate
    """
    hhi_weight:          float   # [0, 1]
    concentration_band:  str     # "LOW", "MEDIUM", "HIGH"
    dominant_class:      str     # Asset class with largest weight fraction
    dominant_weight:     float
    weight_penalty:      float   # [0, 0.30] — penalty to weight posterior


def compute_concentration_risk(
    weights_by_class: Dict[str, float],
) -> ConcentrationRiskScore:
    """HHI-based concentration measure over simulated asset class weights."""
    if not weights_by_class:
        return ConcentrationRiskScore(0.0, "LOW", "", 0.0, 0.0)

    total = sum(weights_by_class.values())
    if total < 1e-10:
        return ConcentrationRiskScore(0.0, "LOW", "", 0.0, 0.0)

    fracs = {k: v / total for k, v in weights_by_class.items()}
    hhi = float(sum(w ** 2 for w in fracs.values()))
    dom = max(fracs, key=lambda k: fracs[k])

    if hhi < 0.25:
        band = "LOW"
    elif hhi < 0.50:
        band = "MEDIUM"
    else:
        band = "HIGH"

    penalty = hhi * 0.30

    return ConcentrationRiskScore(
        hhi_weight=float(np.clip(hhi, 0.0, 1.0)),
        concentration_band=band,
        dominant_class=dom,
        dominant_weight=float(fracs[dom]),
        weight_penalty=float(np.clip(penalty, 0.0, 0.30)),
    )
```

**SYSTEMIC RISK GOVERNANCE:**
```
CONSTRAINT — CORRELATION SPIKE BEHAVIOR:
  Correlation spikes may only:
    - Reduce ConfidenceBundle.Q via confidence_penalty field
    - Trigger FM-04 if CORR_FM04_THRESHOLD exceeded (existing FM rules unchanged)
    - Reduce WeightPosteriorModel.posterior_mean via weight_penalty
    - Update Visual Output heatmap

  Correlation spikes may NOT:
    - Auto-liquidate simulated positions
    - Directly modify PortfolioState.positions
    - Override StrategyObject.Weight_Model directly
    - Trigger execution of any kind
```

def test_full_multi_asset_pipeline():
    """Tests BTC (crypto) + EURUSD (forex) + SPX (index)"""
    
    # 1. Ingest data
    btc_data = data_layer.ingest("BTC/USDT", "crypto", ...)
    eur_data = data_layer.ingest("EUR/USD", "forex", ...)
    spx_data = data_layer.ingest("SPX", "indices", ...)

        "BTC/USDT": feature_layer.compute(btc_data, "crypto"),
        "EUR/USD": feature_layer.compute(eur_data, "forex"),
        "SPX": feature_layer.compute(spx_data, "indices")

    regime = regime_detector.detect(market_data, features)
    
    # 4. Risk
    portfolio_risk = risk_engine.calculate_portfolio_risk(...)
    
    # 5. Signals
    signals = strategy_engine.generate_signals(...)
    
    # 6. Execute

        result = execution_engine.execute(signal, ...)

### Spezifische Ausnahmen
```python
class NumericalInstabilityError(Exception):
    """Ausgeloest bei NaN/Inf-Erkennung. Niemals still ignorieren."""
    pass

class CalibrationGateViolation(Exception):
    """Ausgeloest wenn ECE >= 0.05. Blockiert Deployment."""
    pass

class ThresholdViolation(Exception):
    """Ausgeloest wenn Schwellenwerte veraendert wurden. Kein Warning."""
    pass

class ContractViolation(Exception):
    """Ausgeloest wenn D(t)-Felder fehlen oder inkonsistent sind."""
    pass

class OODConsensusViolation(Exception):
    """Ausgeloest wenn OOD-Konsens nicht berechenbar ist (< 5 Sensoren aktiv)."""
    pass
```
