## UTILITY-FUNKTIONEN

### Numerische Sicherheits-Utils (PFLICHT ueberall)
```python
# jarvis/utils/numeric_safety.py

import math
import numpy as np
from typing import Union

def clip_probability(prob: float, context: str = "") -> float:
    """
    PFLICHT: Alle Wahrscheinlichkeiten muessen diese Funktion durchlaufen.
    Clippt auf [1e-6, 1 - 1e-6].
    """
    if math.isnan(prob) or math.isinf(prob):
        raise NumericalInstabilityError(
            f"Wahrscheinlichkeit NaN/Inf in '{context}': {prob}"
        )
    return float(np.clip(prob, 1e-6, 1 - 1e-6))

def safe_divide(numerator: float, denominator: float, context: str = "") -> float:
    """
    PFLICHT: Kein Division ohne Epsilon-Floor.
    """
    if abs(denominator) < 1e-10:
        return 0.0 if abs(numerator) < 1e-10 else float(np.sign(numerator)) * 1e10
    return numerator / denominator

def enforce_psd(matrix: np.ndarray) -> np.ndarray:
    """
    PFLICHT: Alle Kovarianzmatrizen vor Verwendung.
    Erzwingt positiv-semidefinite Eigenschaft.
    """
    M = (matrix + matrix.T) / 2
    min_eig = np.min(np.linalg.eigvalsh(M))
    if min_eig < 0:
        M += (-min_eig + 1e-8) * np.eye(M.shape[0])
    return M

def safe_matrix_inverse(M: np.ndarray, lambda_: float = 1e-6) -> np.ndarray:
    """
    PFLICHT: Tikhonov-regularisierte Inverse.
    Niemals np.linalg.inv() direkt verwenden.
    """
    regularized = M + lambda_ * np.eye(M.shape[0])
    return np.linalg.inv(regularized)

def check_nan_inf(value: Union[float, np.ndarray], context: str) -> None:
    """
    PFLICHT: Vor jeder kritischen Berechnung.
    Wirft NumericalInstabilityError bei NaN/Inf.
    """
    if isinstance(value, np.ndarray):
        if np.any(np.isnan(value)) or np.any(np.isinf(value)):
            raise NumericalInstabilityError(
                f"NaN/Inf in Array '{context}'"
            )
    else:
        if math.isnan(value) or math.isinf(value):
            raise NumericalInstabilityError(
                f"NaN/Inf in '{context}': {value}"
            )
```

### Statistische Utils
```python
# jarvis/utils/helpers.py
from typing import List, Tuple
import math

def compute_ece(predictions: List, outcomes: List, bins: int = 10) -> float:
    """Expected Calibration Error via Equal-Width Binning."""
    if not predictions:
        return 0.0
    n = max(len(predictions), 1)
    bin_bounds = [i / bins for i in range(bins + 1)]
    ece = 0.0
    for i in range(bins):
        lo, hi = bin_bounds[i], bin_bounds[i + 1]
        in_bin = [(p, o) for p, o in zip(predictions, outcomes)
                  if lo <= p.confidence < hi]
        if not in_bin:
            continue
        bin_n = len(in_bin)
        avg_conf = sum(p.confidence for p, _ in in_bin) / bin_n
        avg_acc  = sum(o for _, o in in_bin) / bin_n
        ece += (bin_n / n) * abs(avg_conf - avg_acc)
    return ece

def compute_mce(predictions: List, outcomes: List, bins: int = 10) -> float:
    """Maximum Calibration Error."""
    n = max(len(predictions), 1)
    bin_bounds = [i / bins for i in range(bins + 1)]
    mce = 0.0
    for i in range(bins):
        lo, hi = bin_bounds[i], bin_bounds[i + 1]
        in_bin = [(p, o) for p, o in zip(predictions, outcomes)
                  if lo <= p.confidence < hi]
        if not in_bin:
            continue
        avg_conf = sum(p.confidence for p, _ in in_bin) / len(in_bin)
        avg_acc  = sum(o for _, o in in_bin) / len(in_bin)
        mce = max(mce, abs(avg_conf - avg_acc))
    return mce

def compute_brier_score(predictions: List, outcomes: List) -> float:
    """Brier Score: Mittlerer quadratischer Fehler von Wahrscheinlichkeitsvorhersagen."""
    n = max(len(predictions), 1)
    return sum((p.confidence - o)**2 for p, o in zip(predictions, outcomes)) / n

def ks_statistic(sample1: List[float], sample2: List[float]) -> Tuple[float, float]:
    """Kolmogorov-Smirnov Zwei-Stichproben-Statistik. Gibt (ks_stat, p_value) zurueck."""
    n1, n2 = len(sample1), len(sample2)
    combined = sorted(set(sample1 + sample2))
    cdf1 = [sum(x <= v for x in sample1) / max(n1, 1) for v in combined]
    cdf2 = [sum(x <= v for x in sample2) / max(n2, 1) for v in combined]
    ks = max(abs(c1 - c2) for c1, c2 in zip(cdf1, cdf2))
    en = math.sqrt(n1 * n2 / max(n1 + n2, 1))
    p_value = 2 * math.exp(-2 * (en * ks)**2)
    return ks, min(p_value, 1.0)

def wasserstein_distance(dist1: List[float], dist2: List[float]) -> float:
    """Earth Mover's Distance (1D Wasserstein) via sortierte Arrays."""
    s1 = sorted(dist1)
    s2 = sorted(dist2)
    n = min(len(s1), len(s2))
    if n == 0:
        return 0.0
    return sum(abs(a - b) for a, b in zip(s1[:n], s2[:n])) / n
```

- [ ] Backups konfiguriert

### Deployment-Schritte
1. Docker Image bauen
2. `scripts/verify_threshold_hashes.py` ausfuehren ? MUSS PASSEN
3. `scripts/verify_contracts.py` ausfuehren ? MUSS PASSEN
4. Image in Registry pushen
5. Kubernetes Manifests aktualisieren
6. In Staging deployen
7. Smoke Tests ausfuehren
8. Canary Deployment in Production
9. 24h Monitoring
10. Vollstaendiger Rollout

- [ ] Logs zugaenglich
- [ ] Backup verifiziert
- [ ] Performance akzeptabel

- [ ] Nutzer informiert

```python
# ---- BLOCK A: Probabilistic Formalization ----

# Thresholds: LOW < 1.0 NVU, MEDIUM 1.0-2.0, HIGH 2.0-3.0, EXTREME >= 3.0

# Bayesian Confidence Update

# LIKELIHOOD_TABLE defined in jarvis/intelligence/bayesian_confidence.py (source of truth)

# Weight Posterior

# ---- BLOCK B: Meta-Validation ----

WFV_MIN_SEGMENTS            = 3      # Min walk-forward segments
WFV_MIN_IS_BARS             = 100    # Min in-sample bars per segment
PERFORMANCE_SPIKE_THRESHOLD = 3.0    # IS/OOS Sharpe ratio -> overfitting flag

ROBUSTNESS_PENALTY          = 0.5    # Weight posterior penalty if robustness fails

MUS_WEIGHT_SPARSITY         = 0.35   # Model uncertainty: data sparsity weight
MUS_WEIGHT_FM_FREQ          = 0.25   # Model uncertainty: failure mode frequency weight

# ---- BLOCK C: Systemic Risk ----
CORR_LOW_THRESHOLD          = 0.40   # Mean pairwise corr < 0.40 -> LOW regime

# CORR_FM04_THRESHOLD = 0.85 UNCHANGED (existing FM-04 rule in 16-20_RISK_PLATFORM.md)

# ---- BLOCK D: Epistemic Uncertainty ----
```

## PHASE 3 DECISION QUALITY CONSTANTS
# Version-aligned: STRATEGY_SCHEMA_VERSION = "1.0.0"
# All constants below are hash-protected via THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json.
# Changes require signed release + updated THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json.
# CI blocks merge on hash mismatch.

```python
# jarvis/utils/constants.py — Phase 3 Decision Quality Section
# HASH-PROTECTED — NEVER OVERWRITE DIRECTLY AT RUNTIME

from jarvis.core.regime import MacroRegimeState, CorrelationRegimeState

# ── Joint Macro x Correlation Risk Multiplier (Phase 6A) ──────────────────
# Deterministic lookup table. No stochastic behavior.
# Hash-registered in THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json under "joint_risk_multiplier_table".
# Applied in RiskEngine.assess() (exposure scaling) and
# BayesianConfidenceEngine.update() (likelihood scaling).
# Backward compatible: if either input is None, multiplier defaults to 1.0.
JOINT_RISK_MULTIPLIER_TABLE = {
    MacroRegimeState.BENIGN: {
        CorrelationRegimeState.DECOUPLED:       1.00,
        CorrelationRegimeState.COUPLED:         1.15,
        CorrelationRegimeState.CRISIS_COUPLING: 1.40,
    },
    MacroRegimeState.UNCERTAIN: {
        CorrelationRegimeState.DECOUPLED:       1.15,
        CorrelationRegimeState.COUPLED:         1.35,
        CorrelationRegimeState.CRISIS_COUPLING: 1.65,
    },
    MacroRegimeState.ADVERSE: {
        CorrelationRegimeState.DECOUPLED:       1.40,
        CorrelationRegimeState.COUPLED:         1.65,
        CorrelationRegimeState.CRISIS_COUPLING: 2.00,
    },
}

# ── Decision Memory Context ────────────────────────────────────────────────
MAX_DECISION_CONTEXT = 200
# Maximum number of analytical decision records stored in DecisionContextState.
# Rolling window; oldest record evicted when limit exceeded.
# Deterministic cap — no dynamic expansion.

# ── Selectivity Threshold Governance ──────────────────────────────────────
BASE_SELECTIVITY_THRESHOLD = 0.55
# Minimum composite quality score required for a strategy signal to be
# considered analytically valid. AdaptiveSelectivityModel may only increase
# this value; it may never fall below BASE_SELECTIVITY_THRESHOLD.
# Enforcement: all threshold adjustments must pass through
# AdaptiveSelectivityModel.compute_threshold() — never mutated directly.

# ── Regime Duration Stress ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
DURATION_STRESS_Z_LIMIT = 2.0
# Z-score of regime age (relative to historical mean duration) at which
# RegimeDurationModel sets transition_acceleration_flag = True.
# Signals that current regime has exceeded its statistically expected lifespan.
# Does NOT directly modify Risk Engine thresholds.

# ── Signal Fragility Classification ───────────────────────────────────────
FRAGILITY_HIGH_THRESHOLD = 0.65
# fragility_index >= FRAGILITY_HIGH_THRESHOLD → signal classified as
# HIGH FRAGILITY. DecisionQualityBundle.signal_fragility_score weighted
# accordingly. No stochastic process involved; deterministic boundary.

# ── Decision Quality Score Governance ─────────────────────────────────────
QUALITY_SCORE_CAP_UNDER_UNCERTAINTY = 0.60
# When UncertaintyBundle.total_uncertainty > 0.5, composite_quality_score
# is capped at this value regardless of other sub-scores.
# Prevents optimistic quality ratings during high epistemic uncertainty.

QUALITY_SCORE_MIN_FLOOR = 0.05
# composite_quality_score is always >= QUALITY_SCORE_MIN_FLOOR.
# Prevents division-by-zero and degenerate downstream calculations.
# Does not represent a "good" signal — floor exists for numerical stability only.

# ── Cross-Reference: Version Alignment ────────────────────────────────────
# All Phase 3 constants are co-versioned with:
#   STRATEGY_SCHEMA_VERSION   = "1.0.0"  (99_REFERENCE.md line 28)
#   GLOBAL_STATE_VERSION      = "1.0.0"  (19-35_MICROSTRUCTURE_GLOBALSTATE.md)
#   CONFIDENCE_BUNDLE_VERSION = "1.0.0"  (19-35_MICROSTRUCTURE_GLOBALSTATE.md)
# Any change to Phase 3 constants requires version bump in all three tags
# and explicit migration documentation per MIGRATION GOVERNANCE rules.
```

# JARVIS v5.0-elite - ANFAENGER SCHNELLSTART
## Schritt-fuer-Schritt Bauanleitung fuer Einsteiger

**Version:** 5.0-elite | **Datum:** Februar 2026
**Zielgruppe:** Entwickler mit Python-Grundkenntnissen

---

## WAS IST JARVIS?

JARVIS ist ein **probabilistisches Risiko-Intelligence-System** fuer Krypto-Trading.

**Wichtigste Eigenschaften:**
- Berechnet Unsicherheit in jeder Entscheidung
- Stoppt automatisch bei zu hohem Risiko
- Lernt aus Daten, aber mit harten Sicherheitsgates
- Designed fuer institutionelle Qualitaet

**Was JARVIS NICHT ist:**
- Kein "schnell reich werden" Bot
- Keine Gewinn-Garantie
- Kein vollautomatischer Trader

---

## DATEIEN VERSTEHEN

### Start hier:
1. **README.md** - Projekt-Uebersicht
2. **00_INDEX.md** - Navigation und System-Vertrag
3. **BUILDABILITY_GUIDE.md** - Vollstaendige Build-Anleitung
4. **UPGRADE_QUICK_REFERENCE.md** - Was ist neu in v5.0-elite

### Core System (baue in dieser Reihenfolge):
1. **01_INTEGRITY.md** (S01) - Hash-Chain fuer Integritaet
2. **02-05_CORE.md** (S02-S05) - Daten, Features, Zustand
3. **06-10_MODELS.md** (S06-S10) - KI-Modelle und Unsicherheit
4. **11-15_FINAL.md** (S11-S15) - API und Validierung

### Erweitert (nach Core):

## 5-MINUTEN QUICKSTART

### Schritt 1: Projekt verstehen

```bash
# Lies zuerst diese Dateien (in dieser Reihenfolge):
1. README.md                  # Was ist JARVIS?
2. 00_INDEX.md                # Wie ist es organisiert?
3. BUILDABILITY_GUIDE.md      # Wie baue ich es?
```

**Verstehe den Systemvertrag:**
```
J : X(t-k:t) -> D(t)
D(t) = { mu, sigma^2, Q, S, U, R }

Bedeutung:
- mu      = Informationsqualitaet (wie gut sind die Daten?)
- sigma^2 = Unsicherheit (wie unsicher ist die Vorhersage?)
- Q       = Kontext-Kohaerenz (passt der Kontext?)
- S       = System-Stabilitaet (laeuft alles stabil?)
- U       = Meta-Unsicherheit (wie unsicher sind wir ueber die Unsicherheit?)
- R       = Regime-Konfidenz (wie sicher sind wir welches Markt-Regime vorliegt?)
```

### Schritt 2: Ordnerstruktur erstellen

```bash
jarvis/
├── core/              # Kern-Komponenten (S01-S05)
├── models/            # KI-Modelle (S06-S10)
├── systems/           # System-Layer (S11-S15)
├── risk/              # Risk Engine (S16-S20)
├── intelligence/      # Intelligence Stack (S21-S25)
├── strategy/          # Strategien (S26-S30)
├── governance/        # Governance (S31-S36)
├── production/        # Production Engineering (neu v5.0)
├── metrics/           # System Metriken (neu v5.0)
├── testing/           # Tests und Simulationen
└── utils/             # Konstanten und Helpers

tests/
├── unit/              # Unit Tests
├── integration/       # Integration Tests
└── stress/            # Stress Tests

config/
├── THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json
└── constants.py

scripts/
├── verify_threshold_hashes.py

└── ci_governance_check.py
```

### Schritt 4: Ersten Baublock erstellen

Starte mit **SESSION 01** (Integrity Layer):

```python
# jarvis/core/integrity_layer.py  # ✅ IMPLEMENTED v6.2.0

import hashlib
import json
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Dict, List

@dataclass
class IntegrityBlock:
    """
    Speichert Hash eines Config-Blocks.
    Wie eine Blockchain - jeder Block referenziert den vorherigen.
    """
    block_id: str
    prev_hash: str
    data_hash: str
    timestamp: str

class IntegrityChain:
    """
    Hash-Chain fuer Integritaet.
    Verhindert dass Configs heimlich geaendert werden.
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.blocks: List[IntegrityBlock] = []
        self.genesis_hash = "0000000000000000"  # Erster Block
    
    def add_block(self, data: Dict) -> str:
        """
        Fuegt neuen Block hinzu.
        Hash wird aus Daten + vorherigem Hash berechnet.
        """
        # Vorheriger Hash holen
        if not self.blocks:
            prev_hash = self.genesis_hash
        else:
            prev_hash = self.blocks[-1].data_hash
        
        # Daten serialisieren
        data_str = json.dumps(data, sort_keys=True)
        
        # Hash berechnen
        combined = f"{prev_hash}{data_str}"
        data_hash = hashlib.sha256(combined.encode()).hexdigest()
        
        # Block erstellen
        block = IntegrityBlock(
            block_id=f"block_{len(self.blocks)}",
            prev_hash=prev_hash,
            data_hash=data_hash,
            timestamp="2026-02-16T12:00:00"  # In Praxis: datetime.utcnow()
        )
        
        self.blocks.append(block)
        return data_hash
    
    def verify(self) -> bool:
        """
        Prueft ob Chain unveraendert ist.
        Jeder Hash muss zum vorherigen passen.
        """
        for i, block in enumerate(self.blocks):
            if i == 0:
                expected_prev = self.genesis_hash
            else:
                expected_prev = self.blocks[i-1].data_hash
            
            if block.prev_hash != expected_prev:
                return False  # Chain manipuliert!
        
        return True

# VERWENDUNG:
# chain = IntegrityChain()
# hash1 = chain.add_block({"ECE_THRESHOLD": 0.05})
# hash2 = chain.add_block({"OOD_THRESHOLD": 0.90})
# is_valid = chain.verify()  # True wenn nicht manipuliert
```

**Test schreiben:**

```python
# tests/unit/core/test_integrity_layer.py

import pytest
from jarvis.core.integrity_layer import IntegrityChain

def test_integrity_chain_basic():
    """Teste dass Chain funktioniert."""
    chain = IntegrityChain()
    
    # Ersten Block hinzufuegen
    hash1 = chain.add_block({"key": "value1"})
    assert len(chain.blocks) == 1
    
    # Zweiten Block hinzufuegen
    hash2 = chain.add_block({"key": "value2"})
    assert len(chain.blocks) == 2
    
    # Hashes muessen unterschiedlich sein
    assert hash1 != hash2

def test_integrity_verification():
    """Teste dass Verifikation funktioniert."""
    chain = IntegrityChain()
    chain.add_block({"test": 1})
    chain.add_block({"test": 2})
    
    # Chain sollte valide sein
    assert chain.verify() == True
    
    # Manipulation simulieren
    chain.blocks[0].data_hash = "fake_hash"
    
    # Chain sollte jetzt invalide sein
    assert chain.verify() == False
```

**Test ausfuehren:**

```bash
pytest tests/unit/core/test_integrity_layer.py -v
```

---

## WICHTIGSTE KONZEPTE

### 1. Probabilistische Unsicherheit

**Alles** im System hat Unsicherheit:
- Jede Vorhersage hat `sigma` (Unsicherheit)
- Hohe Unsicherheit = System wird vorsichtig
- Niedrige Unsicherheit = System ist konfident

```python
# FALSCH (deterministisch):
if price > 50000:
    trade()

# RICHTIG (probabilistisch):
prediction = model.predict(features)
if prediction.mu > 0.5 and prediction.sigma < 0.15:
    trade()  # Nur wenn Konfident UND Unsicherheit niedrig
```

### 2. Hard Gates (keine Umgehung!)

Gates sind **harte Stops** - kein Bypass moeglich:

```python
# ECE Hard Gate (Kalibrierungs-Qualitaet)
if ece >= 0.05:
    raise RuntimeError("ECE zu hoch! Deployment BLOCKIERT")

# OOD Gate (Out-of-Distribution)
if ood_detector.is_ood():
    strategy = "HOLD"  # Nicht traden wenn Out-of-Distribution
```

### 3. Layer-Architektur

System hat 11 Layer - **keine Abkuerzungen**:

```
Daten -> Features -> Zustand -> Regime -> Kalibration 
  -> Unsicherheit -> OOD -> Risk -> Strategie 
  -> Degradation -> Output
```

Jeder Layer kann sagen "STOP" - dann stoppt das ganze System.

### 4. Numerische Stabilitaet

**Immer** NaN/Inf pruefen:

```python
# FALSCH:
result = a / b

# RICHTIG:
import math
if math.isnan(a) or math.isnan(b):
    raise ValueError("NaN detected!")
result = a / max(b, 1e-10)  # Division durch 0 verhindern
```

---

## HAEUFIGE ANFAENGER-FEHLER

### ❌ FEHLER 1: Unsicherheit ignorieren

```python
# FALSCH:
prediction = model.predict(features)
trade(prediction)  # Unsicherheit ignoriert!

# RICHTIG:
prediction = model.predict(features)
if prediction.sigma > 0.15:
    print("Zu unsicher - nicht traden")
else:
    trade(prediction)
```

### ❌ FEHLER 2: Gates umgehen

```python
# FALSCH:
if ece >= 0.05:
    print("Warning: ECE hoch")  # Nur warnen - weitermachen
    continue

# RICHTIG:
if ece >= 0.05:
    raise RuntimeError("ECE Gate verletzt - STOP!")
```

### ❌ FEHLER 3: Keine Tests schreiben

```python
# FALSCH:
# Code schreiben und "hoffen dass es funktioniert"

# RICHTIG:
# Fuer jede Funktion einen Test schreiben:
def test_my_function():
    result = my_function(input)
    assert result == expected
```

### ❌ FEHLER 4: NaN/Inf nicht pruefen

```python
# FALSCH:
value = compute_something()
return value  # Was wenn NaN?

# RICHTIG:
value = compute_something()
if math.isnan(value) or math.isinf(value):
    raise ValueError(f"Invalid value: {value}")
return float(np.clip(value, 0.0, 1.0))
```

## DEBUGGING TIPPS

### Problem: Tests schlagen fehl

```bash
# 1. Verbose output
pytest -v

# 2. Nur einen Test
pytest tests/unit/core/test_integrity_layer.py::test_integrity_chain_basic -v

# 3. Mit Debugger
pytest --pdb

# 4. Print Statements hinzufuegen
print(f"DEBUG: value = {value}")
```

### Problem: NaN/Inf Fehler

```python
# Debug Helper:
def debug_value(name, value):
    import math
    if math.isnan(value):
        raise ValueError(f"{name} ist NaN!")
    if math.isinf(value):
        raise ValueError(f"{name} ist Inf!")
    print(f"DEBUG {name}: {value}")
    return value

# Verwendung:
value = debug_value("prediction", model.predict())
```

### Problem: Import Fehler

```bash
# Stelle sicher dass PYTHONPATH gesetzt ist:
export PYTHONPATH="${PYTHONPATH}:/path/to/jarvis"

# Oder in Code:
import sys
sys.path.append('/path/to/jarvis')
```

# JARVIS BUILD ASSESSMENT SYSTEM
# Version: 5.0-final

---

## Was ist das?

Ein automatisches System das:
1. Bestehenden JARVIS-Code analysiert
2. Jeden Baustein mit dem Blueprint vergleicht
3. Die Blueprint-MD-Dateien mit Status-Reports aktualisiert
4. Claude sagt was zu tun ist: REUSE, ADAPT, REWRITE oder BUILD NEW

---

## Nutzung

### Schritt 1: ZIP entpacken

```bash
unzip jarvis_existing.zip -d ./jarvis_existing
```

### Schritt 2: Assessment durchfuehren

```bash
python assess_build.py ./jarvis_existing ./blueprints

# Beispiel-Output:
# ============================================================
# Assessment for S01:
# ============================================================
# [BUILD STATUS CHECK] - S01
# Overall Status: PARTIAL
# Test Coverage: 45.0%
# ...
```

### Schritt 3: Blueprint-MDs aktualisieren

```bash
python update_blueprints.py ./jarvis_existing ./blueprints

# Output:
# Starting Blueprint Update Process...
# Processing S01...
# [OK] Updated 01_INTEGRITY.md
# ...
# Update Complete: 15/15 sessions updated
```

### Schritt 4: Governance-Check

```bash
python scripts/ci_governance_check.py \
    --manifest config/THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json \
    --ece-results results/ece_per_regime.json \
    --ood-results results/ood_recall.json
```

---

## Assessment-Kategorien

### [OK] REUSE - Perfekt, nutze ohne Aenderung
Funktion hat Docstring + Type Hints + Tests. Blueprint-konform.
Claude-Aktion: Nutze EXAKT wie vorhanden. Keine Aenderungen.

### [WARN] ADAPT - Fast gut, kleine Aenderungen
Funktion existiert aber fehlt Docstring oder Type Hints oder Tests.
Claude-Aktion: Fuege nur fehlende Teile hinzu.

### [FAIL] REWRITE - Kaputt, neu implementieren
Funktion vorhanden aber Logik-Fehler oder falscher Return-Typ.
Claude-Aktion: Implementiere vollstaendig neu vom Blueprint.

### [FAIL] BUILD NEW - Fehlt komplett
Funktion existiert nicht.
Claude-Aktion: Implementiere vom Blueprint.

---

```
S01 -> 01_INTEGRITY.md       (standalone)
```

## Troubleshooting

### "Module not found"
```bash
ls -la assess_build.py update_blueprints.py
# Beide muessen im gleichen Verzeichnis sein
```

### "No functions found"
```bash
python -m py_compile jarvis/core/*.py
python -c "import ast; ast.parse(open('jarvis/core/integrity_layer.py').read())"
```

### "Governance gate failed"
```bash
# Governance-Fehler sind IMMER kritisch. Keine Umgehung.
# 1. Finde den Fehler in den Logs
# 2. Behebe das zugrunde liegende Problem
# 3. Starte den Check neu
```

```bash
python3 scripts/ci_governance_check.py

# Performance Certification (Trockentest)
python3 scripts/run_performance_certification.py --dry-run
```

---

## 3. KRITISCHE FEHLERQUELLEN (Claude-Tipps)

### Import-Fehler

```
PROBLEM: ModuleNotFoundError: No module named 'jarvis.risk'
URSACHE: __init__.py fehlt in jarvis/risk/
LOESUNG: touch jarvis/risk/__init__.py
         python3 -c "from jarvis.risk.risk_engine import RiskEngine"
```

```
PROBLEM: Import-Reihenfolge falsch
URSACHE: S17 versucht S35 zu importieren bevor S35 gebaut
LOESUNG: IMMER Phase-Reihenfolge einhalten
         GlobalSystemState (S35) vor Risk-Engine (S17)
```

### NaN/Inf-Fehler

```
PROBLEM: ValueError: NaN oder Inf in Input erkannt
URSACHE: Rohe Marktdaten nicht validiert
LOESUNG: Immer data_layer.validate_data() vor Feature-Berechnung
         Alle Numpy-Arrays: np.all(np.isfinite(arr)) pruefen
```

### Governance-Gate-Fehler

```
PROBLEM: RuntimeError: DEPLOYMENT_BLOCKED
URSACHE: ECE zu hoch oder OOD-Recall zu niedrig
LOESUNG: Kalibrierung verbessern (S09)
         NIEMALS Gate-Threshold senken als "Loesung"
```

### Thread-Safety

```
PROBLEM: Race Condition im GlobalSystemStateController
URSACHE: Gleichzeitige Schreibzugriffe
LOESUNG: Immer ctrl.update() verwenden (intern gesperrt)
         Niemals _state direkt schreiben
```

---

## 4. CLAUDE-SESSION-PROMPT-TEMPLATE

Fuer jede neue Session genau diesen Prompt verwenden:

```
JARVIS v5.0-elite Build -- Session [XX]: [NAME]

Lies: blueprints/[DATEI].md, Abschnitt "SESSION [XX]"
Status: blueprints/STATUS.json

Implementiere:
  Datei: jarvis/[pfad]/[modul].py
  Tests: tests/unit/[pfad]/test_[modul].py

Anforderungen:
  1. Alle Code-Snippets aus Blueprint exakt implementieren
  2. Alle Docstrings vorhanden
  3. Alle Type Hints vorhanden
  4. NaN/Inf-Checks in jeder oeffentlichen Methode
  5. Tests komplett (alle test_* Funktionen)
  6. Kein hardcoded Pfad (nur Path-Objekte)
  7. Kein global state (nur GlobalSystemStateController)
  8. Keine print()-Aufrufe (nur log_event)

Nach Implementierung:
  python3 -m pytest tests/unit/[pfad]/test_[modul].py -v
  python3 -c "from jarvis.[pfad].[modul] import [Klasse]; print('OK')"

Wenn Tests gruen:
  Aktualisiere blueprints/STATUS.json: "[session_name]": "COMPLETE"
```

## 6. MINIMALER LAUFFAEHIGER KERN (MVP)

Wenn Zeit begrenzt: Dieser Kern reicht fuer erste Demo.

    MUSS: S01, S02, S03, S05, S08, S09, S10, S11, S16, S17, S26, S35
    KANN FOLGEN: S04, S06, S07, S12-S15, S18-S25, S27-S36

MVP-Test:
```bash
# Minimal-Smoke-Test
python3 - << 'EOF'
import numpy as np
from jarvis.core.global_state import GlobalSystemStateController
from jarvis.risk.risk_engine import RiskEngine
from jarvis.risk.confidence_zone_engine import ConfidenceZoneEngine, ConfidenceZoneRequest

# Global State
ctrl = GlobalSystemStateController()
print("State:", ctrl.get_state().mode)

# Risk Engine
rng = np.random.RandomState(42)
returns = (rng.randn(100) * 0.01).tolist()
risk = RiskEngine()
result = risk.assess(returns, "TRENDING", 0.3)
print("Risk Regime:", result.risk_regime)
print("Vol Forecast:", round(result.volatility_forecast, 4))

# Confidence Zone
engine = ConfidenceZoneEngine()
req = ConfidenceZoneRequest(
    current_price=100.0,
    regime="TRENDING",
    sigma_sq=result.volatility_forecast ** 2,
    mu=0.7,
    regime_confidence=0.8,
)
zone = engine.compute(req)
print("Entry Box:", round(zone.entry_lower, 2), "-", round(zone.entry_upper, 2))
print("Entry Confidence:", round(zone.entry_confidence * 100, 1), "%")
print("Meta-Uncertainty:", round(zone.meta_uncertainty * 100, 1), "%")
print("MVP: OK")
EOF
```

## 7. HAEUFIGE FEHLER BEI CLAUDE-BUILDS

### Fehler 1: Emojis/Unicode vergessen zu entfernen
```
SYMPTOM: ascii codec can't encode character
LOESUNG: Alle Strings im Code pruefen:
         grep -rn "[^\x00-\x7F]" jarvis/
```

### Fehler 2: Fehlende __init__.py
```
SYMPTOM: ImportError: cannot import name 'X' from 'jarvis.Y'
LOESUNG: find jarvis -type d | xargs -I{} touch {}/__init__.py
```

### Fehler 3: Falsche Rueckgabe-Typen
```
SYMPTOM: TypeError: expected float, got numpy.float64
LOESUNG: Immer explizit konvertieren: float(np.result)
         Alle Dataclass-Felder: float(np.clip(...))
```

### Fehler 4: GlobalSystemState nicht initialisiert
```
SYMPTOM: AttributeError: 'NoneType' object has no attribute '_state'
LOESUNG: ctrl = GlobalSystemStateController.get_instance()
         (Singleton, nicht direkt instanziieren)
```

### Fehler 5: Circular Imports
```
SYMPTOM: ImportError: cannot import name 'X' (circular)
URSACHE: z.B. global_state importiert risk_engine, risk_engine importiert global_state
LOESUNG: global_state hat KEINE Imports aus anderen jarvis-Modulen
         Andere Module importieren global_state, nicht umgekehrt
```

### Fehler 6: Test-Isolation fehlt
```
SYMPTOM: Tests beeinflussen sich gegenseitig (GlobalState-Singleton)
LOESUNG: In conftest.py:
         @pytest.fixture(autouse=True)
         def reset_global_state():
             GlobalSystemStateController._instance = None
             yield
             GlobalSystemStateController._instance = None
```

## 8. VERIFIKATIONS-SKRIPT (NACH VOLLSTAENDIGEM BUILD)

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# scripts/verify_full_build.py
"""
Vollstaendige Build-Verifikation.
Prueft alle Module, Imports und kritischen Pfade.
"""
import sys
import subprocess

MODULES = [
    ("jarvis.core.integrity_layer",          "IntegrityLayer"),
    ("jarvis.core.logging_layer",            "EventLogger"),
    ("jarvis.core.data_layer",               "DataLayer"),
    ("jarvis.core.feature_layer",            "FeatureLayer"),
    ("jarvis.core.state_layer",              "StateLayer"),
    ("jarvis.core.global_state",             "GlobalSystemStateController"),
    ("jarvis.models.fast_path",              "FastPathEnsemble"),
    ("jarvis.models.uncertainty",            "UncertaintyDecomposer"),
    ("jarvis.models.calibration",            "CalibrationEngine"),
    ("jarvis.models.ood_detection",          "OODDetector"),
    ("jarvis.systems.quality_scorer",        "QualityScorer"),
    ("jarvis.risk.confidence_zone_engine",   "ConfidenceZoneEngine"),
    ("jarvis.risk.risk_engine",              "RiskEngine"),
    ("jarvis.risk.capital_allocation",       "CapitalAllocationEngine"),
    ("jarvis.intelligence.microstructure_layer", "MarketMicrostructureLayer"),
    ("jarvis.intelligence.liquidity_layer",  "LiquidityLayer"),
    ("jarvis.intelligence.news_layer",       "NewsIntelligenceLayer"),
    ("jarvis.strategy.adaptive_strategy",    "AdaptiveStrategySelector"),
    ("jarvis.simulation.strategy_lab",       "StrategyLab"),
    ("jarvis.execution.execution_optimizer", "ExecutionOptimizer"),
    ("jarvis.research.feature_pipeline",     "FeatureRegistry"),
    ("jarvis.governance.model_registry",     "ModelRegistry"),
    ("jarvis.governance.performance_certification", "PerformanceCertificationEngine"),
    ("jarvis.governance.threshold_guardian", "ThresholdGuardian"),
    ("jarvis.chart.chart_data_builder",      "ChartDataBuilder"),
]

def verify_imports():
    failures = []
    for module, classname in MODULES:
        try:
            mod = __import__(module, fromlist=[classname])
            getattr(mod, classname)
            print(f"[OK]   {module}.{classname}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"[FAIL] {module}.{classname}: {e}")
            failures.append(module)
    return failures

def run_all_tests():
    result = subprocess.run(
        ["python3", "-m", "pytest", "tests/", "-v", "--tb=short", "-q"],
        capture_output=True, text=True
    )
    print(result.stdout[-3000:])
    if result.returncode != 0:
        print(result.stderr[-1000:])
    return result.returncode == 0

if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("=" * 60)
    print("JARVIS v5.0-elite -- Vollstaendige Build-Verifikation")
    print("=" * 60)
    print()

    print("--- Import-Check ---")
    import_failures = verify_imports()

    print()
    print("--- Test-Suite ---")
    tests_ok = run_all_tests()

    print()
    print("=" * 60)
    if import_failures:
        print(f"[FAIL] {len(import_failures)} Import-Fehler")
        for f in import_failures:
            print(f"       - {f}")
        sys.exit(1)
    elif not tests_ok:
        print("[FAIL] Test-Suite nicht bestanden")
        sys.exit(1)
    else:
        print("[OK]   Build vollstaendig und funktionsfaehig")
        sys.exit(0)
```

---

## 9. LAUFZEIT-VERHALTEN SICHERSTELLEN

### Was das System tut (korrekt):
```
1. Beim Start: GlobalSystemStateController initialisiert (deployment_blocked=True)
2. Risk Compression aktiv bis erste Kalibrierung bestanden
3. Confidence Zones werden berechnet (NICHT: BUY/SELL ausgegeben)
4. Strategy wird automatisch gewaehlt (NICHT: manuell konfiguriert)
5. Jede State-Aenderung wird geloggt
6. Deployment erst nach PerformanceCertificationEngine freigegeben
7. Rollback jederzeit moeglich (ModelRegistry.rollback())
```

### Was das System NICHT tut (Fehler):
```
1. Niemals: BUY/SELL als String ausgeben
2. Niemals: Governance-Gate ignorieren (kein try/except um Gates)
3. Niemals: GlobalState direkt schreiben (_state = ...)
4. Niemals: NaN/Inf in Output-Feldern zurueckgeben
5. Niemals: Deployment ohne PerformanceCertificationEngine.certify()
6. Niemals: Execution Layer direkt mit Broker verbinden
7. Niemals: Nicht-whitelisted News-Quellen verarbeiten
```

## INTEGRATION IN MD-DATEIEN

Jede Session-MD erhaelt am Anfang (nach Header):

```
# SESSION XX: [NAME]

---

## [BUILD STATUS CHECK]

[Automatisch generierter Assessment-Report hier]

---

## SCOPE
[Rest des Blueprints...]
```

Claude liest den Assessment-Report und weiss sofort:
1. Was existiert
2. Was funktioniert
3. Was gefixt werden muss
4. Was neu gebaut werden muss

Dadurch:
- Keine doppelte Arbeit
- Bestehender Code wird wiederverwendet
- Nur Fixes/Ergaenzungen wo noetig
- Governance-Fehler werden zuerst behoben

================================================================================
=== ZIP_A FILE: COMPARISON_v4_vs_v5_final.md ===
================================================================================
# JARVIS BUILD SYSTEM: v4.0 vs v5.0-final VERGLEICH

## EXECUTIVE SUMMARY

v5.0-final ist die institutionell-reife, numerisch gehaertete,
probabilistisch korrekte Weiterentwicklung von v4.0.

### Kernmetriken

| Metrik                   | v4.0                | v5.0-final            | Verbesserung |
|--------------------------|---------------------|-----------------------|--------------|
| Sessions                 | 15                  | 28+                   | +87%         |
| Systemidentitaet         | Signal-System       | Risk Intelligence     | Fundamental  |
| Numerische Stabilitaet   | Partiell            | Vollstaendig (Pflicht)| +100%        |
| Governance Gates         | Soft Warnings       | Hard Exceptions       | Kritisch     |
| Risk Engine              | Nicht vorhanden     | Zentraler Kern        | Neu          |
| Multi-Layer Intelligence | Nicht vorhanden     | 7 Layer               | Neu          |
| Chart-Interface          | Buy/Sell (implizit) | Confidence Boxen      | Fundamental  |
| Simulation Lab           | Nicht vorhanden     | Monte Carlo + 5 Tools | Neu          |
| Deterministic Learning   | Nicht vorhanden     | 7-Schritt-Zyklus      | Neu          |
| News Intelligence        | Nicht vorhanden     | Whitelisted + NLP     | Neu          |
| Multi-Timeframe          | Nicht vorhanden     | 5 TF + Rekalibrierung | Neu          |
| Token pro Session        | ~3,000              | ~4,500                | +50% (noetig)|
| Rollback-Faehigkeit      | Nicht vorhanden     | Vollstaendig          | Neu          |
| Hash-gesicherte Gates    | Nicht vorhanden     | THRESHOLD_MANIFEST    | Neu          |
| CI/CD Integration        | Nicht vorhanden     | GitHub Actions Gate   | Neu          |

---

## DETAILLIERTE UNTERSCHIEDE

### 1. SYSTEMIDENTITAET

v4.0:
  - Implizit als Vorhersage-/Signal-System konzipiert
  - Output: Prediction mit Konfidenz
  - Keine explizite Abgrenzung zu "Signal Bot"

v5.0-final:
  - Explizit: Probabilistic Risk Intelligence Platform
  - Output: Confidence Boxen + Risiko-Korridore
  - Strikte Abgrenzung: KEINE Buy/Sell Signale
  - Chart-Interface zeigt institutionelle Metadaten

### 2. NUMERISCHE STABILITAET

v4.0:
  - Clip-Regeln dokumentiert aber nicht erzwungen
  - NaN/Inf Handling partiell
  - Keine systematische PSD-Erzwingung

v5.0-final:
  - Numerische Stabilitaetsdoktrin = Systemvertrag
  - Alle Wahrscheinlichkeiten: clip([1e-6, 1-1e-6]) PFLICHT
  - NaN/Inf: immer Exception, nie Silent-Fail
  - PSD-Erzwingung fuer alle Kovarianzmatrizen
  - Regularisierung aller Matrixinversionen (Tikhonov, lambda >= 1e-6)

### 3. GOVERNANCE & GATES

v4.0:
  - ECE-Schwellenwerte als Konfiguration
  - Warnungen moeglich bei Grenzwert-Verletzungen
  - Keine CI-Integration

v5.0-final:
  - THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json: SHA-256 Hash-gesichert
  - Jede Gate-Verletzung = RuntimeError (kein Warning)
  - CI-Pipeline: Exit Code 1 bei Governance-Fail
  - Kein Deployment ohne Bestehen ALLER Gates

### 4. RISK ENGINE

v4.0:
  - Kein dedizierter Risk Engine
  - Risiko-Gedanken im Uncertainty-Modul (S08)
  - Kein Drawdown-Forecast

v5.0-final:
  - RiskEngine als eigenstaendiger Kern (S17)
  - Expected Drawdown Forecast (mean + p95)
  - EWMA Volatilitaets-Forecast
  - Adaptive Position Sizing (multi-faktoriell)
  - Confidence-Weighted Exposure
  - Risk Compression Mode
  - Defensive Mode bei Schock

### 5. MULTI-LAYER INTELLIGENCE

v4.0:
  - Nur Preis + Volatilitaet + Regime
  - Keine Liquidity-Analyse
  - Keine Cross-Asset Korrelation
  - Keine Makro-Sensitivitaet
  - Kein News-Impact

v5.0-final:
  - Layer 1: Price & Volatility (S06+S08+S17)
  - Layer 2: Regime Detection (S05)
  - Layer 3: Liquidity Layer (S21)
  - Layer 4: Cross-Asset Correlation (S22)
  - Layer 5: Macro Sensitivity (S23)
  - Layer 6: News Intelligence (S24)
  - Layer 7: Risk Forecasting (S17 kombiniert)

### 6. DETERMINISTISCHES LERNEN

v4.0:
  - Learning Engine (S12) ohne kontrollierten Zyklus
  - Kein Rollback-Konzept
  - Keine Deployment-Gates fuer Updates

v5.0-final:
  - 7-Schritt-Lernzyklus (kontrolliert und auditierbar)
  - Kein Deployment ohne ECE-Gate + Stress-Test
  - Rollback jederzeit moeglich (Snapshot-basiert)
  - Drift-Ueberwachung (kontinuierlich)
  - Alle Lernschritte in BUILD_LOG.json

### 7. SIMULATION LAB

v4.0:
  - Keine dedizierte Simulation
  - Walk-Forward nur in S15 (Validation)

v5.0-final:
  - Monte Carlo (Bootstrap, deterministischer Seed)
  - Slippage Modeling (vol-abhaengig + groessen-abhaengig)
  - Liquidity Impact Modeling
  - Walk-Forward Validation (rollierende Fenster)
  - Stress Test Engine (historisch + synthetisch)
  - Pflicht-Szenarien: 2008, COVID, Flash Crash, synthetisch

### 8. MULTI-TIMEFRAME

v4.0:
  - Kein Timeframe-Konzept
  - Einheitliche Kalibrierung

v5.0-final:
  - 5 Timeframes: 5m, 15m, 1h, 4h, 1D
  - Vollstaendige Rekalibrierung bei Wechsel (Pflicht)
  - Zeitrahmen-abhaengige Risikoskalierung
  - UI-Lock waehrend Rekalibrierung

### 9. NEWS INTELLIGENCE

v4.0:
  - Kein News-Konzept

v5.0-final:
  - Whitelisted Quellen (konfigurierbar)
  - Kein Originaltext im Systemkern (nur Hashes)
  - Impact-Score pro Category
  - Shock-Probability Injection in Systemvertrag
  - News-Regime (QUIET / ACTIVE / HIGH_IMPACT / SHOCK)

### 10. CHART-INTERFACE

v4.0:
  - Keine explizite Chart-Spezifikation
  - Implizit: Preis-Vorhersage + Konfidenz

v5.0-final:
  - Entry Confidence Box (Wahrscheinlichkeitsraum)
  - Exit Risk Corridor (Soft + Hard)
  - Expected Move %
  - Volatility Adjusted Stop
  - Regime Label (ASCII)
  - Strategy Mode Label (ASCII)
  - Meta-Uncertainty Level
  - Verbotene Elemente: BUY/SELL/LONG/SHORT/TAKE PROFIT

---

## MIGRATION VON v4.0 AUF v5.0-final

```
MIGRATION GUIDE:

Schritt 1: assess_build.py auf bestehenden v4-Code anwenden
  -> Was ist REUSE / ADAPT / REWRITE / BUILD?

Schritt 2: Numerische Stabilitaet einbauen (S01-S15)
  -> Alle Clip-Regeln, NaN-Checks, PSD-Erzwingung pruefen

Schritt 3: THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json erstellen
  -> Alle kritischen Schwellenwerte extrahieren und hashen

Schritt 4: Governance-Pipeline aufsetzen
  -> ci_governance_check.py in CI einbinden

Schritt 5: Risk Engine aufbauen (S16-S18)
  -> Neue Module, keine Breaking Changes zu S01-S15

Schritt 6: Intelligence-Stack aufbauen (S21-S25)
  -> Unabhaengig von S01-S15, kann parallel entwickelt werden

Schritt 7: Strategy + Simulation Lab (S26-S28)
  -> Braucht S16-S25 als Input

Schritt 8: Chart-Interface anpassen (S32)
  -> Letzte Schicht: hat keine eigene Logik

Schritt 9: Vollstaendiger Governance-Check
  -> Alle Gates muessen bestehen vor erstem Deployment
```

---

## EMPFEHLUNG

Verwende v5.0-final fuer alle neuen JARVIS-Builds.
v4.0 ist vollstaendig kompatibel als Ausgangspunkt (alle Tools bleiben gueltig).
assess_build.py und update_blueprints.py funktionieren mit beiden Versionen.

v5.0-final ist die institutionell verteidigbare, probabilistisch
korrekte Version. v4.0 war ein notwendiger Meilenstein.

## 3. MERGE-STRATEGIE (Safe Merge Protokoll)

```
SITUATION: Bestehender Code + neuer Blueprint

SCHRITT 1: Assessment
  python assess_build.py ./existing ./blueprints
  -> Generiert: was REUSE, ADAPT, REWRITE, BUILD

SCHRITT 2: Backup
  timestamp=$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S)
  cp -r jarvis jarvis_backup_${timestamp}

SCHRITT 3: Merge per Datei
  IF WORKING:   -> KEEP (keine Aenderung)
  IF INCOMPLETE: -> ADAPT (fehlende Teile ergaenzen)
  IF BROKEN:    -> REPLACE (Backup + neu implementieren)
  IF MISSING:   -> CREATE (vom Blueprint implementieren)

SCHRITT 4: Verifizieren
  python scripts/ci_governance_check.py
  pytest tests/ -v
  python scripts/verify_build_log.py

SCHRITT 5: Deployment nur wenn alle Checks gruen
```

---

## 4. CLAUDE WORKFLOW PRO SESSION

```
1. Lies Blueprint-Datei fuer die Session
2. Lies BUILD STATUS CHECK (falls vorhanden)
3. Erstelle/update Modul in korrektem Ordner
4. Erstelle Tests parallel zur Modul-Struktur
5. Fuehre tests/verify aus
6. Kopiere nach /mnt/user-data/outputs/
7. Melde: "Session XX complete. Files: [liste]"
```

=== ZIP_A FILE: README.md ===
================================================================================
# JARVIS v5.0-final -- Probabilistic Risk Intelligence Platform
## Gehaertet | Institutional Grade | Zero Signal Bot

---

## Was ist JARVIS v5.0-final?

JARVIS ist ein probabilistisches Marktanalyse- und Risiko-Bewertungssystem
mit institutioneller Verteidigbarkeit.

v5.0-final kombiniert:
  - Formalen Systemvertrag (unveraenderlich)
  - Vollstaendige numerische Stabilitaetsdoktrin
  - Hash-gesicherte Schwellenwert-Governance
  - Deployment-Gates als Hard-Exceptions (keine Warnungen)
  - Zero Silent Failure Toleranz
  - Multi-Layer Intelligence Stack (7 Layer)
  - Probabilistic Risk Engine als zentralen Kern
  - Adaptives Strategie-Abstraktionsystem
  - Deterministischen Lernzyklus mit Rollback
  - Professionelles Chart-Interface (keine BUY/SELL)

---

## Formaler Systemvertrag (unveraenderlich)

    J : X(t-k:t) -> D(t)
    D(t) = { mu, sigma^2, Q, S, U, R }

---

## Dateistruktur

    00_INDEX.md                 Navigation + Systemvertrag
    01_INTEGRITY.md             S01: Hash-Chain, Integrity
    02-05_CORE.md               S02-S05: Core Infrastructure
    06-10_MODELS.md             S06-S10: Model Layer
    11-15_FINAL.md              S11-S15: Systems, API, Validation
    16-20_RISK_PLATFORM.md      S16-S18: Risk Engine, Confidence Zones, MTF

## Schnellstart

### Erster Build (kein existierender Code):

    1. Lies 00_INDEX.md
    2. Lies STATUS.json
    3. Beginne mit Session 01 (01_INTEGRITY.md)
    4. Folge Abhaengigkeits-Reihenfolge
    5. Fuehre Governance-Check nach jeder Session aus

### Bestehenden Code integrieren:

    python assess_build.py ./existing_jarvis ./blueprints
    python update_blueprints.py ./existing_jarvis ./blueprints

### Governance-Check:

    python scripts/ci_governance_check.py \
        --manifest config/THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json \
        --ece-results results/ece_per_regime.json \
        --ood-results results/ood_recall.json

---

## Was ist NEU gegenueber v4.0?

    [NEU] Probabilistic Risk Intelligence Platform Identity
    [NEU] Risk Engine als zentraler Kern (S16-S17)
    [NEU] 7-Layer Intelligence Stack (S21-S25)
    [NEU] Adaptive Strategy Abstraction (S26)
    [NEU] Deterministischer Lernzyklus mit Rollback (S27)
    [NEU] Simulation & Strategy Lab: Monte Carlo, Walk-Forward (S28)
    [NEU] Governance & Hardening: Hash-Gates, CI-Block (S31)
    [NEU] Professionelles Chart-Interface (keine BUY/SELL) (S32)
    [NEU] Multi-Timeframe Kalibrierung (S18)
    [NEU] News Intelligence (whitelisted, strukturiert) (S24)
    [NEU] Multi-Broker Data Layer (isoliert) (S25)

    [UPGRADE] Numerische Stabilitaet: systemweit verpflichtend
    [UPGRADE] Governance: Hard Exceptions statt Soft Warnings
    [UPGRADE] Hash-gesicherte Schwellenwerte (THRESHOLD_MANIFEST)

---

## Troubleshooting

### Governance-Fehler:
    Governance-Fehler sind IMMER kritisch.
    Kein Deployment ohne Behebung.
    Logs: data/logs/governance/

### NaN/Inf-Fehler:
    Sind immer Exceptions (nie silent).
    Stack-Trace zeigt genaue Quelle.
    Numerische Stabilitaetsdoktrin anwenden (00_INDEX.md).

### Rollback:
    from jarvis.strategy.deterministic_learning import DeterministicLearningOrchestrator
    orch = DeterministicLearningOrchestrator(...)
    orch.rollback()

# JARVIS v5.0-elite UPGRADE QUICK REFERENCE
## Institution-Grade Enhancements

---

## WHAT WAS UPGRADED

### 1. 11-LAYER ARCHITECTURE (02-05_CORE.md)
**Location:** Beginning of file, before SESSION 02
**What:** Formal layer-by-layer specification with inputs, outputs, failure modes, validation metrics
**Why:** Ensures no cross-layer violations and proper failure handling

### 2. INFORMATION QUALITY (mu) (06-10_MODELS.md)
**Location:** SESSION 08 - Uncertainty Layer
**What:** Regime-adaptive learned weights via cross-validation
**Why:** Replaces heuristics with data-driven optimization

### 3. OOD FORMALIZATION (06-10_MODELS.md)
**Location:** SESSION 10 - OOD Detection
**What:** Ground truth definition, precision/recall metrics, drift tracking
**Why:** Makes OOD detection measurable and verifiable

### 4. MODEL GOVERNANCE (33-34-36_RESEARCH_GOVERNANCE_CERT.md)
**Location:** SESSION 34 - Model Governance Framework
**What:** Complete registry, validation, approval workflow, SR 11-7 compliance
**Why:** Prevents unauthorized deployments, ensures independent validation

### 5. PRODUCTION ENGINEERING (11-15_FINAL.md)
**Location:** Before Pre-Production Checklist
**What:** SLA, circuit breaker, backpressure, auto-scaling, degradation control
**Why:** Makes system production-ready with proper failure handling

### 6. SYSTEM INTERACTION (37_SYSTEM_ADDENDUM.md) **NEW FILE**
**What:** Data flow, control flow, validation gates, mode transitions
**Why:** Documents how all components interact and enforce gates

### 7. FAILURE SIMULATION (37_SYSTEM_ADDENDUM.md) **NEW FILE**
**What:** Flash crash timeline with system response verification
**Why:** Proves system behaves correctly under extreme stress

### 8. CAPITAL ALLOCATION (29-30_CAPITAL_EXECUTION.md)
**Location:** SESSION 29 - Beginning
**What:** Vol targeting, risk budgeting, Kelly criterion, exposure limits
**Why:** Formalizes portfolio mathematics

### 9. SYSTEM METRICS (37_SYSTEM_ADDENDUM.md) **NEW FILE**
**What:** Fragility index, trust score, regime memory
**Why:** Provides system health monitoring

### 10. REALISTIC BUDGET (37_SYSTEM_ADDENDUM.md) **NEW FILE**
**What:** 150k EUR total with breakdown and contingencies
**Why:** Sets realistic expectations for implementation

### 11. COMPLEXITY CONTROL (00_INDEX.md)
**Location:** After Governance Gates
**What:** Explicit rule: no bypassing uncertainty, no weakening gates
**Why:** Prevents shortcuts and silent failures

### 12. CERTIFICATION GATE (00_INDEX.md)
**Location:** Governance Gates section
**What:** ECE, OOD recall, stress detection, Monte Carlo, drawdown, governance approval
**Why:** Blocks deployment unless all conditions met

## KEY FORMULAS ADDED

1. **Volatility Targeting:**
   ```
   position_size = (target_vol / realized_vol) * base_position
   ```

2. **Risk Contributions:**
   ```
   RC_i = w_i * Cov(R_i, R_p) / sigma_p
   ```

3. **Kelly Criterion:**
   ```
   f* = (p*b - q) / b
   Quarter Kelly: f_adj = f* / 4
   ```

4. **Fragility Index:**
   ```
   FI = 0.3*coupling + 0.3*propagation + 0.2*recovery + 0.2*cascade
   ```

5. **Trust Score:**
   ```
   TS = 0.30*cal + 0.25*ood + 0.20*stab + 0.15*risk + 0.10*ops
   ```

# JARVIS v5.0-elite UPGRADE SUMMARY
## Institution-Grade Enhancement - February 2026

---

## OVERVIEW

This document summarizes the comprehensive upgrades applied to the JARVIS v5.0-elite blueprint to achieve institution-grade, mathematically rigorous, and production-realistic standards.

**Upgrade Status:** COMPLETE
**Files Modified:** 7 core files
**Files Created:** 2 new files
**Additions:** ~3,500 lines of formalized documentation
**Approach:** Surgical modifications preserving existing structure

---

## UPGRADE CATEGORIES

### 1. ARCHITECTURE LAYER FORMALIZATION ✓ COMPLETE

**File:** `02-05_CORE.md`
**Location:** Beginning of file (before SESSION 02)

**Added:**
- Formal 11-layer architecture model with strict boundaries
- Per-layer definitions:
  * Inputs
  * Outputs
  * Failure Modes
  * Validation Metrics
  * Hard Stop conditions

**Layers Defined:**
1. Data Ingestion (S03)
2. Feature Preprocessing (S04)
3. State Estimation (S05)
4. Regime Detection (S05)
5. Calibration (S09)
6. Uncertainty Aggregation (S08, S11)
7. OOD Ensemble (S10)
8. Risk Engine (S17)
9. Strategy Abstraction (S26)
10. Degradation Controller (S35)
11. Output Interface (S13)

**Cross-layer Rules:**
- No method may cross layer boundaries
- Explicit failure propagation required
- Validation gates at each layer
- Latency budget per layer (<500ms total P95)

**Index Updated:** `00_INDEX.md` - Added 11-layer architecture section

---

### 2. INFORMATION QUALITY SCORE (mu) SCIENTIFIC HARDENING ✓ COMPLETE

**File:** `06-10_MODELS.md`
**Location:** SESSION 08 (Uncertainty Layer)

**Replaced:** Heuristic weighting with:

**Regime-Adaptive Learned Weights:**
- Cross-validation optimized weights (5-fold Time Series CV)
- Per-regime feature importance via Ridge Regression
- Automatic weight derivation from historical data
- Minimum 100 samples per regime required

**Implementation:**
```python
class InformationQualityEstimator:
    def learn_weights(features, outcomes, regime_labels, n_splits=5)
    def compute_mu(features, regime, data_quality)
    def sensitivity_analysis(regime)
    def weight_stability_check(window_size=1000)
```

**Added:**
- Weight derivation documentation (6-step methodology)
- Sensitivity analysis (per-feature importance tracking)
- Stability across regimes (rolling window std dev)
- Information Gain Optimization (alternative method)

**Metrics:**
- CV Score per regime
- Weight stability score [0, 1]
- Sensitivity scores per feature
- Target: Stability >= 0.7

---

### 3. OOD MEASUREMENT FORMALIZATION ✓ COMPLETE

**File:** `06-10_MODELS.md`
**Location:** SESSION 10 (OOD Detection)

**Added:**

**Ground Truth Definition:**
- Historical crisis labeling methodology
- Known crisis periods (Bitcoin Flash Crash May 2021, Terra/Luna May 2022, FTX Nov 2022, etc.)
- Crisis types: BLACK_SWAN, REGIME_SHIFT, LIQUIDITY_CRISIS, FLASH_CRASH
- Expert verification requirement

**Precision and Recall:**
```python
@dataclass
class OODMetrics:
    true_positives, false_positives, true_negatives, false_negatives
    @property precision, recall, f1_score
```
- Recall >= 90% HARD GATE enforced
- Precision targeting >= 80%

**False Positive Tolerance Policy:**
- DEFENSIVE mode: FPR < 10%
- NORMAL mode: FPR < 5%
- AGGRESSIVE mode: FPR < 2%

**OOD Drift Tracking:**
```python
class OODDriftTracker:
    - Rolling window (1000 samples)
    - Baseline mean/std tracking
    - Drift detection (>2 sigma shift)
    - Magnitude computation
```

---

### 4. MODEL RISK GOVERNANCE EXPANSION ✓ COMPLETE

**File:** `33-34-36_RESEARCH_GOVERNANCE_CERT.md`
**Location:** SESSION 34 (Model Governance)

**Expanded with:**

**Model Registry:**
```python
class ModelRegistry:
    - Model versioning with code/config/dependency hashes
    - Performance metrics (validation, backtest, OOS)
    - Approval workflow
    - Change log per version
    - Risk tier classification (SR 11-7)
```

**Independent Validation Layer:**
```python
@dataclass
class ValidationReport:
    - Conceptual soundness check
    - Implementation correctness
    - Performance adequacy
    - Sensitivity analysis
    - All governance gates status
    - Recommendation (APPROVE/REJECT/CONDITIONAL)
```

**Deployment Controls:**
- Validator must be independent from developer
- All governance gates must pass
- Approval required before deployment
- Status tracking (DEVELOPMENT -> VALIDATION -> APPROVED -> DEPLOYED)

**Rollback Policy:**
```python
def rollback_model(from_version, to_version, reason)
    - Target must be APPROVED or DEPLOYED
    - Suspend current version
    - Re-deploy target version
    - Log reason in change log
```

**Backtest Governance:**
- Walk-forward validation enforced
- Train window >= 365 days
- Test window = 90 days
- Transaction costs >= 1 bps minimum
- Minimum 30 trades in test period

**SR 11-7 Alignment:**
- 10-point compliance checklist
- Three lines of defense
- Model risk rating
- Ongoing monitoring
- Board reporting requirements

**Feature Research Extension:**
- Feature registry with decay tracking
- Automatic feature retirement (<10% importance)
- A/B model testing capability
- Shadow deployment support

---

### 5. PRODUCTION ENGINEERING ADDENDUM ✓ COMPLETE

**File:** `11-15_FINAL.md`
**Location:** Before Pre-Production Checklist

**Added:**

**Operational Stability Layer:**
```python
class StabilityController:
    - StabilityMode (NORMAL, DEGRADED, CRITICAL, EMERGENCY)
    - Circuit breaker (5% error rate threshold)
    - Consecutive failure tracking
    - Mode transition logic
```

**SLA Definition:**
- P50 latency: 100ms
- P95 latency: 200ms
- P99 latency: 500ms
- Availability: 99.9%
- Error rate: 0.1%

**API Backpressure Handling:**
```python
class BackpressureHandler:
    - Max queue size: 1000
    - Reject threshold: 90% utilization
    - Load shedding implementation
    - Rejection rate tracking
```

**Timeout Management:**
- Data fetch: 5s
- Feature compute: 20ms
- Fast path: 50ms
- Deep path: 500ms
- Risk engine: 100ms
- API response: 1s

**Graceful Latency Degradation:**
```python
class GracefulDegradationController:
    - Level 0: Full functionality (99 features)
    - Level 1: Degraded (50 features, no deep path)
    - Level 2: Critical (30 features, fast path only)
    - Level 3: Emergency (cache-only, no predictions)
```

**Resource Scaling Strategy:**
```python
class AutoScaler:
    - Scale-up threshold: 70% CPU, 80% memory
    - Scale-down threshold: 30% CPU
    - Min instances: 2
    - Max instances: 10
    - Cooldown periods: 5min up, 10min down
```

**Failure Escalation Chain:**
- LOW: Log only
- MEDIUM: Alert on-call
- HIGH: Page on-call + escalate to lead
- CRITICAL: All hands + emergency shutdown

**Portfolio Volatility Targeting Formula:**
```python
position_size = (target_vol / realized_vol) * base_position

Risk Parity Extension:
weight_i = (1 / vol_i) / sum_j(1 / vol_j)
```

**Implementation:**

- Max vol cap: 50% (prevents under-leverage)
- Max leverage: 3x

**Risk Budget Allocation Mathematics:**
```python
RC_i = w_i * Cov(R_i, R_p) / sigma_p

class RiskBudgetAllocator:
    def compute_risk_contributions(weights, cov_matrix)
    def optimize_equal_risk_contribution(cov_matrix)
```

**Kelly-Adjusted Cap:**
```python
Full Kelly: f* = (p*b - q) / b
Quarter Kelly: f_adj = f* / 4
Confidence-Scaled: f_adj = f* * confidence
Drawdown-Adjusted: f_adj = f* * (1 - current_dd / max_dd)
```

**Exposure Limit Definitions:**

- Strategy exposure: 40%
- Gross exposure: 80%
- Net exposure: 60%
- Max leverage: 3x
- Crypto exposure: 70%

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
JARVIS Build Assessor
Analysiert bestehenden Code und generiert Assessment-Reports fuer Blueprint-MD-Dateien.
"""

import ast
import json
import re
import subprocess
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
from datetime import datetime
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Dict, List, Optional


@dataclass
class FileStatus:
    path: str
    exists: bool
    lines: int
    last_modified: str
    status: str  # OK, PARTIAL, BROKEN, MISSING


@dataclass
class FunctionStatus:
    name: str
    status: str  # WORKING, BROKEN, INCOMPLETE, MISSING
    line_number: Optional[int]
    has_docstring: bool
    has_type_hints: bool
    has_tests: bool


@dataclass
class SessionAssessment:
    session_id: str
    overall_status: str
    files: List[FileStatus]
    functions: List[FunctionStatus]
    test_coverage: float
    reusable_count: int
    adapt_count: int
    rewrite_count: int
    missing_count: int
    action_plan: List[Dict]
    estimated_time_minutes: int


class BuildAssessor:
    """Analysiert bestehenden Code gegen Blueprint-Specs."""

    def __init__(self, existing_code_path: Path, blueprint_path: Path):
        self.code_path = existing_code_path
        self.blueprint_path = blueprint_path
        self.session_specs = self.load_session_specs()

    def load_session_specs(self) -> Dict:
        """Laedt erwartete Funktionen und Dateipfade fuer alle 15 Sessions."""
        specs = {}

        specs["S01"] = {
            "module": "jarvis/core/integrity_layer.py",
            "functions": [
                "hash_file",
                "verify_file",
                "create_manifest",
                "verify_manifest",
                "init_hash_chain",
                "append_to_chain",
                "verify_chain",
            ],
            "scripts": [
                "scripts/verify_manifest.py",
                "scripts/verify_build_log.py",
                "scripts/update_status.py",
            ],
            "tests": "tests/unit/core/test_integrity_layer.py",
        }

        specs["S02"] = {
            "module": "jarvis/core/logging_layer.py",
            "functions": ["log_event", "query_events", "get_event_stream"],
            "tests": "tests/unit/core/test_logging_layer.py",
        }

        specs["S03"] = {
            "module": "jarvis/core/data_layer.py",
            "functions": ["fetch_market_data", "validate_data", "cache_data", "get_cached"],
            "tests": "tests/unit/core/test_data_layer.py",
        }

        specs["S04"] = {
            "module": "jarvis/core/feature_layer.py",
            "functions": [
                "compute_features",
                "detect_drift",
                "calculate_drift_severity",
                "trigger_response",
            ],
            "tests": "tests/unit/core/test_feature_layer.py",
        }

        specs["S05"] = {
            "module": "jarvis/core/state_layer.py",
            "functions": [
                "detect_regime",
                "estimate_volatility",
                "predict_state",
                "update_state",
            ],
            "tests": "tests/unit/core/test_state_layer.py",
        }

        specs["S06"] = {
            "module": "jarvis/models/fast_path.py",
            "functions": ["predict", "get_uncertainty", "aggregate_fast"],
            "tests": "tests/unit/models/test_fast_path.py",
        }

        specs["S07"] = {
            "module": "jarvis/models/deep_path.py",
            "functions": ["predict", "aggregate_deep", "should_activate_deep_path"],
            "tests": "tests/unit/models/test_deep_path.py",
        }

        specs["S08"] = {
            "module": "jarvis/models/uncertainty.py",
            "functions": [
                "decompose",
                "compute_intervals",
                "compute_aleatoric",
                "compute_epistemic",
            ],
            "tests": "tests/unit/models/test_uncertainty.py",
        }

        specs["S09"] = {
            "module": "jarvis/models/calibration.py",
            "functions": [
                "calibrate",
                "evaluate_calibration",
                "compute_ece_adaptive",
                "compute_reliability_weight",
            ],
            "tests": "tests/unit/models/test_calibration.py",
        }

        specs["S10"] = {
            "module": "jarvis/models/ood_detection.py",
            "functions": [
                "detect_ood",
                "aggregate_ood",
                "handle_unknown_unknown",

                "detect_mahalanobis",
                "detect_wasserstein",
                "detect_ensemble_variance",
            ],
            "tests": "tests/unit/models/test_ood_detection.py",
        }

        specs["S11"] = {
            "module": "jarvis/systems/quality_scorer.py",
            "functions": [
                "compute_quality",
                "calibration_score",
                "confidence_score",
                "stability_score",
                "data_quality_score",
                "regime_confidence_score",
            ],
            "tests": "tests/unit/systems/test_quality_scorer.py",
        }

        specs["S12"] = {
            "module": "jarvis/systems/learning_engine.py",
            "functions": [
                "process_feedback",
                "create_label",
                "detect_bias",
            ],
            "tests": "tests/unit/systems/test_learning_engine.py",
        }

        specs["S13"] = {
            "module": "jarvis/systems/degradation_ctrl.py",
            "functions": ["evaluate_system_health"],
            "tests": "tests/unit/systems/test_degradation_ctrl.py",
        }

        specs["S14"] = {
            "modules": [
                "jarvis/api/routes.py",
                "jarvis/api/models.py",
                "jarvis/api/dependencies.py",
                "jarvis/api/websocket.py",
            ],
            "module": "jarvis/api/routes.py",  # Haupt-Datei fuer Funktions-Analyse
            "functions": ["predict", "feedback", "status", "metrics"],
            "tests": "tests/unit/api/test_routes.py",
        }

        specs["S15"] = {
            "modules": [
                "jarvis/validation/validators.py",
                "jarvis/validation/stress_tests.py",
                "jarvis/validation/metrics.py",
            ],
            "module": "jarvis/validation/validators.py",
            "functions": [
                "test_ece_walk_forward",
                "test_historical_crises",
                "test_synthetic_stress",
                "test_all_degradation_modes",
                "test_latency",
                "test_logging_integrity",
                "test_ablation",
            ],
            "tests": "tests/integration/test_e2e.py",
        }

        return specs

    def assess_session(self, session_id: str) -> SessionAssessment:
        """Fuehrt Assessment fuer eine Session durch."""
        spec = self.session_specs.get(session_id)
        if not spec:
            raise ValueError(f"Unknown session: {session_id}")

        files = self.check_files(spec)
        functions = self.check_functions(spec)
        test_coverage = self.get_test_coverage(spec["tests"])

        reusable = [f for f in functions if f.status == "WORKING"]
        adapt    = [f for f in functions if f.status == "INCOMPLETE"]
        rewrite  = [f for f in functions if f.status == "BROKEN"]
        missing  = [f for f in functions if f.status == "MISSING"]

        action_plan = self.generate_action_plan(reusable, adapt, rewrite, missing)
        estimated_time = self.estimate_time(len(rewrite), len(adapt), len(missing))
        overall = self.determine_overall_status(files, functions)

        return SessionAssessment(
            session_id=session_id,
            overall_status=overall,
            files=files,
            functions=functions,
            test_coverage=test_coverage,
            reusable_count=len(reusable),
            adapt_count=len(adapt),
            rewrite_count=len(rewrite),
            missing_count=len(missing),
            action_plan=action_plan,
            estimated_time_minutes=estimated_time,
        )

    def check_files(self, spec: Dict) -> List[FileStatus]:
        """Prueft ob Dateien existieren (inkl. multi-module Sessions)."""
        files = []

        module_paths = spec.get("modules", [spec.get("module")])
        for module in module_paths:
            if module:
                files.append(self.get_file_status(self.code_path / module))

        for script in spec.get("scripts", []):
            files.append(self.get_file_status(self.code_path / script))

        files.append(self.get_file_status(self.code_path / spec["tests"]))
        return files

    def get_file_status(self, path: Path) -> FileStatus:
        """Ermittelt Status einer einzelnen Datei."""
        if not path.exists():
            return FileStatus(
                path=str(path), exists=False, lines=0,
                last_modified="N/A", status="MISSING"
            )

        lines = self.count_lines(path)
        modified = datetime.fromtimestamp(path.stat().st_mtime).strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M")

        if lines == 0:
            status = "MISSING"
        elif lines < 50:
            status = "PARTIAL"
        else:
            status = "OK"

        return FileStatus(
            path=str(path), exists=True, lines=lines,
            last_modified=modified, status=status
        )

    def count_lines(self, path: Path) -> int:
        """Zaehlt nicht-leere Zeilen in einer Datei."""
        try:
            with open(path) as f:
                return sum(1 for line in f if line.strip())
        except Exception:
            return 0

    def check_functions(self, spec: Dict) -> List[FunctionStatus]:
        """Analysiert implementierte Funktionen via AST."""
        module_path = self.code_path / spec["module"]

        if not module_path.exists():
            return [
                FunctionStatus(
                    name=func, status="MISSING", line_number=None,
                    has_docstring=False, has_type_hints=False, has_tests=False
                )
                for func in spec["functions"]
            ]

        implemented = self.parse_functions(module_path)
        tested = self.get_function_test_coverage(spec["tests"])

        results = []
        for expected_func in spec["functions"]:
            if expected_func in implemented:
                info = implemented[expected_func]
                if not info["has_docstring"] or not info["has_type_hints"]:
                    status = "INCOMPLETE"
                elif not tested.get(expected_func, False):
                    status = "INCOMPLETE"
                else:
                    status = "WORKING"

                results.append(FunctionStatus(
                    name=expected_func,
                    status=status,
                    line_number=info["line"],
                    has_docstring=info["has_docstring"],
                    has_type_hints=info["has_type_hints"],
                    has_tests=tested.get(expected_func, False),
                ))
            else:
                results.append(FunctionStatus(
                    name=expected_func, status="MISSING", line_number=None,
                    has_docstring=False, has_type_hints=False, has_tests=False,
                ))

        return results

    def parse_functions(self, path: Path) -> Dict:
        """Parst Python-Datei und extrahiert Funktions-Metadaten via AST."""
        try:
            with open(path) as f:
                tree = ast.parse(f.read())
        except Exception:
            return {}

        functions = {}
        for node in ast.walk(tree):
            if isinstance(node, ast.FunctionDef):
                functions[node.name] = {
                    "line": node.lineno,
                    "has_docstring": ast.get_docstring(node) is not None,
                    "has_type_hints": self.check_type_hints(node),
                }
        return functions

    def check_type_hints(self, func_node: ast.FunctionDef) -> bool:
        """True wenn alle Parameter (ausser self) und Return annotiert sind."""
        has_return = func_node.returns is not None
        has_args = all(
            arg.annotation is not None
            for arg in func_node.args.args
            if arg.arg != "self"
        )
        return has_return and has_args

    def get_test_coverage(self, test_file: str) -> float:
        """Grobe Coverage-Schaetzung: 1 Testfunktion ~ 10%."""
        test_path = self.code_path / test_file
        if not test_path.exists():
            return 0.0
        try:
            with open(test_path) as f:
                content = f.read()
            count = len(re.findall(r"def test_", content))
            return min(count * 10, 100.0)
        except Exception:
            return 0.0

    def get_function_test_coverage(self, test_file: str) -> Dict[str, bool]:
        """Prueft welche Funktionen durch test_<name>-Muster abgedeckt sind."""
        test_path = self.code_path / test_file
        if not test_path.exists():
            return {}
        try:
            with open(test_path) as f:
                content = f.read()
            return {
                m.group(1): True
                for m in re.finditer(r"def test_(\w+)", content)
            }
        except Exception:
            return {}

    def generate_action_plan(
        self,
        reusable: List[FunctionStatus],
        adapt: List[FunctionStatus],
        rewrite: List[FunctionStatus],
        missing: List[FunctionStatus],
    ) -> List[Dict]:
        """Generiert priorisierten Action Plan."""
        actions = []

        for func in rewrite:
            actions.append({
                "priority": 1,
                "action": "REWRITE",
                "target": func.name,
                "changes": ["rewrite from blueprint (broken)"],
                "time_est": 20,
            })

        for func in adapt:
            reasons = []
            if not func.has_docstring:
                reasons.append("add docstring")
            if not func.has_type_hints:
                reasons.append("add type hints")
            if not func.has_tests:
                reasons.append("add tests")
            actions.append({
                "priority": 2,
                "action": "ADAPT",
                "target": func.name,
                "changes": reasons,
                "time_est": 5 * len(reasons),
            })

        for func in missing:
            actions.append({
                "priority": 3,
                "action": "BUILD",
                "target": func.name,
                "changes": ["implement from blueprint"],
                "time_est": 15,
            })

        return actions

    def estimate_time(self, rewrite_count: int, adapt_count: int, missing_count: int) -> int:
        """Schaetzt Gesamt-Zeit in Minuten."""
        return rewrite_count * 20 + adapt_count * 10 + missing_count * 15

    def determine_overall_status(
        self, files: List[FileStatus], functions: List[FunctionStatus]
    ) -> str:
        """Ermittelt Overall-Status der Session."""
        if all(f.status == "MISSING" for f in files):
            return "NOT_FOUND"

        working = sum(1 for f in functions if f.status == "WORKING")
        total = len(functions)

        if total == 0:
            return "NOT_FOUND"
        if working == total:
            return "COMPLETE"
        if working > total * 0.5:
            return "PARTIAL"
        return "NEEDS_FIX"

    def generate_markdown_report(self, assessment: SessionAssessment) -> str:
        """Generiert Markdown Assessment-Block fuer Einfuegung in MD-Datei."""
        lines = [
            f"## [BUILD STATUS CHECK] - {assessment.session_id}",
            "",
            f"**Generated:** {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')}",
            f"**Overall Status:** {assessment.overall_status}",
            f"**Test Coverage:** {assessment.test_coverage:.1f}%",
            f"**Estimated Time to Complete:** {assessment.estimated_time_minutes} minutes",
            "",
            "---",
            "",
            "### EXISTING CODE ANALYSIS",
            "",
            "**Files Found:**",
        ]

        for file in assessment.files:
            icon = "[OK]" if file.status == "OK" else "[WARN]" if file.status == "PARTIAL" else "[FAIL]"
            lines.append(f"- {icon} `{file.path}` ({file.lines} lines) - {file.status}")

        lines += ["", "**Functions Implemented:**"]
        for func in assessment.functions:
            icon = "[OK]" if func.status == "WORKING" else "[WARN]" if func.status == "INCOMPLETE" else "[FAIL]"
            details = []
            if func.has_docstring:
                details.append("docs")
            if func.has_type_hints:
                details.append("types")
            if func.has_tests:
                details.append("tests")
            detail_str = f" ({', '.join(details)})" if details else ""
            lines.append(f"- {icon} `{func.name}()` - {func.status}{detail_str}")

        lines += [
            "",
            "---",
            "",
            "### REUSABILITY SUMMARY",
            "",
            f"- **Can REUSE (no changes):** {assessment.reusable_count} functions",
            f"- **Can ADAPT (small changes):** {assessment.adapt_count} functions",
            f"- **Must REWRITE (broken):** {assessment.rewrite_count} functions",
            f"- **Must BUILD NEW (missing):** {assessment.missing_count} functions",
            "",
            "---",
            "",
            "### CLAUDE ACTION PLAN",
            "",
        ]

        for action in assessment.action_plan:
            lines.append(f"**Priority {action['priority']} - {action['action']}:**")
            lines.append(f"- {action['target']}: {', '.join(action['changes'])}")
            lines.append(f"  (Est: {action['time_est']} min)")
            lines.append("")

        lines += [
            "---",
            "",
            "### NEXT STEPS FOR CLAUDE",
            "",
            "1. Read existing code in files marked [OK] or [WARN]",
            "2. REUSE functions marked as WORKING without changes",
            "3. ADAPT functions marked as INCOMPLETE (add missing pieces only)",
            "4. BUILD functions marked as MISSING from blueprint",
            "5. Run tests: `pytest tests/ -v`",
            "6. Verify: all functions WORKING, coverage >= 80%",
            "",
            "---",
        ]

        return "\n".join(lines)


def main():
    """Analysiert Code fuer alle Sessions und gibt Reports aus."""
    import sys

    if len(sys.argv) < 3:
        print("Usage: python assess_build.py <existing_code_path> <blueprint_path>")
        sys.exit(1)

    code_path = Path(sys.argv[1])
    blueprint_path = Path(sys.argv[2])

    assessor = BuildAssessor(code_path, blueprint_path)

    all_sessions = [f"S{i:02d}" for i in range(1, 16)]

    for session_id in all_sessions:
        try:
            assessment = assessor.assess_session(session_id)
            report = assessor.generate_markdown_report(assessment)

            print(f"\n{'='*60}")
            print(f"Assessment for {session_id}:")
            print(f"{'='*60}")
            print(report)

            output_file = blueprint_path / f"assessment_{session_id}.md"
            with open(output_file, "w") as f:
                f.write(report)
            print(f"\nSaved to: {output_file}")

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error assessing {session_id}: {e}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

=== ZIP_A FILE: compute_manifest_hash.py ===
================================================================================
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Berechnet und aktualisiert manifest_hash in THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json.
Aufruf: python3 compute_manifest_hash.py config/THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json
"""
import json
import hashlib
import sys
from pathlib import Path

def compute_and_update(manifest_path: str):
    path = Path(manifest_path)
    with open(path) as f:
        data = json.load(f)
    
    thresholds = data.get("thresholds", {})
    computed = hashlib.sha256(
        json.dumps(thresholds, sort_keys=True).encode("utf-8")
    ).hexdigest()
    
    data["manifest_hash"] = computed
    
    with open(path, "w") as f:
        json.dump(data, f, indent=2)
    
    print(f"[OK] manifest_hash berechnet: {computed[:16]}...")
    print(f"[OK] Gespeichert in: {path}")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    if len(sys.argv) < 2:
        print("Usage: python3 compute_manifest_hash.py config/THRESHOLD_MANIFEST.json")
        sys.exit(1)
    compute_and_update(sys.argv[1])

# tests/conftest.py
# Globale Test-Konfiguration fuer JARVIS

import pytest
import numpy as np


@pytest.fixture(autouse=True)
def reset_global_state():
    """
    Setzt GlobalSystemStateController vor jedem Test zurueck.
    Verhindert State-Leaks zwischen Tests (Singleton-Pattern).
    """
    from jarvis.core import global_state as gs
    gs.GlobalSystemStateController._instance = None
    yield
    gs.GlobalSystemStateController._instance = None


@pytest.fixture
def sample_returns():
    """Reproduzierbare Sample-Returns fuer Tests."""
    rng = np.random.RandomState(42)
    return (rng.randn(200) * 0.01).tolist()


@pytest.fixture
def trending_regime_returns():
    """Returns mit klarem Trend (fuer Regime-Tests)."""
    rng = np.random.RandomState(42)
    trend = np.linspace(0.001, 0.003, 100)
    noise = rng.randn(100) * 0.005
    return (trend + noise).tolist()


@pytest.fixture
def shock_regime_returns():
    """Returns mit Schock-Charakteristik."""
    rng = np.random.RandomState(42)
    normal = (rng.randn(80) * 0.01).tolist()
    shock  = (rng.randn(20) * 0.05 - 0.03).tolist()
    return normal + shock
